## Source Text: unaltered below
##

MAT 1:1 Od̠ud̠ul wa̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ ma̠ eghun wa̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Ebraham a̠mite bho̠:
MAT 1:2 Ebraham amar Azi̠ki̠; sa̠ Azi̠ki̠ amar A̠zeko̠pu̠; sa̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠ amar A̠zuda̠ na̠ a̠rumor d̠o̠yo̠;
MAT 1:3 sa̠ A̠zuda̠ amar Ape̠re̠z na̠ Aze̠ra, wa̠ onweni d̠awa aro̠ ma̠ Atama bho̠; sa̠ Ape̠re̠z amar E̠zro̠n; sa̠ E̠zro̠n amar Aram;
MAT 1:4 sa̠ Aram amar Ami̠nadab; sa̠ Ami̠nadab amar Anaso̠n; sa̠ Anaso̠n amar Asalmo̠n;
MAT 1:5 sa̠ Asalmo̠n amar A̠boa̠z wa̠ onweni bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠rehab bho̠; sa̠ A̠boa̠z amar Obe̠di̠, wa̠ onweni bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠rufu bho̠; sa̠ Obe̠di̠ amar Aze̠si̠;
MAT 1:6 sa̠ Aze̠si̠ amar O̠li̠le̠ma A̠devidi; sa̠ A̠devidi amar Aso̠lo̠mo̠n, wa̠ onweni bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ ani̠ ta̠ A̠yuraya bho̠;
MAT 1:7 sa̠ Aso̠lo̠mo̠n amar A̠rihoboa̠m; sa̠ A̠rihoboa̠m amar Abi̠za; sa̠ Abi̠za amar Asaf;
MAT 1:8 sa̠ Asaf amar A̠zehosafat; sa̠ A̠zehosafat amar A̠zoram; sa̠ A̠zoram amar Uzaya;
MAT 1:9 sa̠ Uzaya amar A̠zotam; sa̠ A̠zotam amar Ahaz; sa̠ Ahaz amar E̠zi̠kaya;
MAT 1:10 sa̠ E̠zi̠kaya amar Amanase̠; sa̠ Amanase̠ amar Amo̠n; sa̠ Amo̠n amar A̠zosaya;
MAT 1:11 sa̠ A̠zosaya amar A̠zekonaya na̠ a̠rumor d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ igiel wa̠ ub̠ol awa ka̠ id̠ighom d̠a̠ Ababi̠lo̠n bho̠.
MAT 1:12 Igiel wa̠ na̠ ed̠ighom awa d̠a̠ Ababi̠lo̠n bho̠, sa̠ A̠zekonaya amar A̠seti̠e̠l; sa̠ A̠seti̠e̠l amar A̠zerubabe̠l;
MAT 1:13 sa̠ A̠zerubabe̠l amar Abihud; sa̠ Abihud amar E̠li̠aki̠m; sa̠ E̠li̠aki̠m amar Azo̠;
MAT 1:14 sa̠ Azo̠ amar Azado̠k; sa̠ Azado̠k amar Aki̠m; sa̠ Aki̠m amar E̠li̠ud;
MAT 1:15 sa̠ E̠li̠ud amar E̠li̠aza; sa̠ E̠li̠aza amar Amatan; sa̠ Amatan amar A̠zeko̠pu̠;
MAT 1:16 sa̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠ amar A̠zose̠fu̠ owolom ta̠ A̠meri, wa̠ amar A̠zizo̠s wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠.
MAT 1:17 O̠ku̠a bha̠ eb̠la̠ ramu̠m bho̠, obeton d̠a̠ Ebraham ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ A̠devidi, bha̠ d̠iobh na̠ inya̠ amu̠m; ya̠a̠ obeton d̠a̠ A̠devidi ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ igiel e̠d̠u̠a Ababi̠lo̠n bho̠, bha̠ d̠iobh na̠ inya̠ amu̠m; ya̠a̠ ob̠eton igiel e̠d̠u̠a Ababi̠lo̠n bho̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ igiel ta̠ Akrai̠st, bha̠ d̠iobh na̠ inya̠ amu̠m.
MAT 1:18 Onon agu̠o̠ ubhin u̠mar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st bho̠. A̠zose̠fu̠ a̠sibh A̠meri, onweni D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ obhin ani̠, ya̠a̠ kisa̠ awa ta̠ eten otu bha̠ A̠meri na̠ a̠mumor o̠nyi̠ ola̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠ru.
MAT 1:19 Agu̠o̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ owolom d̠o̠yo̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i o̠ni̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠ko̠ro̠ A̠meri bho̠, sa̠ aru̠ru̠an ogbogina̠ o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ e̠nwo̠ngi̠na.
MAT 1:20 Agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠bhin a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ i̠ru̠an bho̠, sa̠ otileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠mutuma̠ i̠na d̠a̠ amala, a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “A̠zose̠fu̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, ka̠ oghil obhin A̠meri ma̠ o̠ro̠ ani̠ d̠oyom, ezin bho̠ eghun wa̠ i̠na a̠mumor bho̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠ru.
MAT 1:21 I̠na ta̠ amar olobhiri o̠nyi̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠ghol a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s, ezin bho̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠awa.”
MAT 1:22 Eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n imite ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠di̠ar ya̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ owil bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠:
MAT 1:23 “I̠bi̠ghe̠! E̠kar o̠nyani̠ ta̠ a̠mumor amar olobhiri o̠nyi̠, sa̠ ta̠ oghol I̠na ma̠ I̠manu̠e̠l” (a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠zib̠a̠ od̠i na̠ i̠yar”).
MAT 1:24 Igiel wa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ asu̠ma bho̠, sa̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ otileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠ruom i̠na bho̠ sa̠ a̠bhin ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠yel.
MAT 1:25 Ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ okod̠uom d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠meri tu̠tu̠n amar o̠nyi̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠ghol a̠d̠ien D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 2:1 Igiel wa̠ u̠mar A̠zizo̠s, d̠a̠ Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠, bha̠ a̠sora̠n igiel wa̠ E̠ro̠d aro̠ ma̠ o̠li̠le̠ma bho̠, sa̠ iloghodi̠ar i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ agba opuomite ogogo bho̠ iru d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m,
MAT 2:2 sa̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠: “Od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ken O̠li̠le̠ma A̠zu wa̠ u̠mar bho̠? I̠yar u̠bi̠gh e̠ni̠nai̠ny D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ igiel wa̠ a̠b̠etina̠ bho̠ sa̠ i̠yar uru ra̠ okpud̠ia̠n onigha̠ o̠yo̠.”
MAT 2:3 Igiel bho̠ E̠ro̠d amu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ abar bho̠ a̠nyegi i̠na na̠ eb̠la̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m.
MAT 2:4 Sa̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ sa̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ta̠ o̠mar Akrai̠st bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠ken?”
MAT 2:5 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠: “D̠a̠ Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠, ezin bho̠ owil bho̠ age̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠no̠n a̠guri:
MAT 2:6 “ ‘Anwa Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ebhugh A̠zuda̠ bho̠, anwa i̠ki̠r a̠pu d̠a̠ ogbo irileghom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zuda̠ bho̠, ku̠ku̠m eka̠, o̠ni̠ irileghom ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ oyom a̠mite, ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠rileghom a̠nwunom D̠ami̠, Izre̠l.’ ”
MAT 2:7 Sa̠ E̠ro̠d a̠bhelegi ma̠ iloghodi̠ar bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na a̠pura̠n a̠loghom a̠ga̠i obhel wa̠ e̠ni̠nai̠ny bho̠ a̠mite bho̠.
MAT 2:8 Sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠a̠: “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m ka̠ e̠mar epura̠n egboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠. Ka̠ inyin u̠bi̠gh, bha̠ id̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠loghom epa̠, b̠o̠ka̠ ami̠ agi̠ ani̠ ka̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n I̠na.”
MAT 2:9 Awa i̠mu̠gho̠n a̠fugh ta̠ O̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ i̠we̠le̠, sa̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ e̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ e̠ni̠nai̠ny wa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh d̠a̠ opuomite ogogo bho̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠a̠ awa sa̠ awa i̠tu̠o̠no̠m tu̠tu̠n ka̠ amara d̠a̠ anyu̠ esi wa̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠ od̠i bho̠.
MAT 2:10 Sa̠ obhel bho̠ awa i̠bi̠gh e̠ni̠nai̠ny bho̠ sa̠ awa ibhon ologi ma̠ ibom.
MAT 2:11 Sa̠ awa id̠igh d̠a̠ otu bho̠ ka̠ i̠bi̠gh O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ A̠meri onweni bho̠, sa̠ ikpud̠ia̠n I̠na, sa̠ ikpegion a̠rigba̠ i̠di̠ar edim d̠awa inigha̠ I̠na ma̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠: a̠gol na̠ afraki̠nse̠ns na̠ amaya.
MAT 2:12 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠l opa̠n eten imula̠ iyel d̠a̠ ebhugh d̠awa, ezin bho̠ ukikiom awa d̠a̠ amala ma̠a̠ awa omula̠ d̠o̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ E̠ro̠d.
MAT 2:13 Agu̠o̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ otileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ d̠a̠ amala a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “B̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠bhin O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ onweni D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ anu̠r agi̠ d̠a̠ Izipt ka̠ aro̠, tu̠tu̠n anwa ta̠ a̠mula̠ amu̠gho̠n d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠ami̠, ezin bho̠ E̠ro̠d ta̠ abho̠ro̠gh O̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠ ogigh.”
MAT 2:14 Sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ epa̠, a̠bhin O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ onweni D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ugula̠n obha̠ ad̠u̠a agi̠ d̠a̠ Izipt.
MAT 2:15 Sa̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ tu̠tu̠n E̠ro̠d a̠mugh, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzoghod̠iom a̠fugh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ wa̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ owil a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ ibhelegi ma̠ O̠nyi̠ D̠ami̠ d̠a̠ Izipt a̠mutiom.”
MAT 2:16 Igiel bho̠ E̠ro̠d abi̠gh ma̠ iloghodi̠ar bho̠ na̠ egelemeni i̠na bho̠, sa̠ ologi do̠yo̠ a̠gurom, sa̠ ato̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ eb̠la̠ i̠gbara ilobhiri anwi̠i̠ny d̠a̠ Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m na̠ eb̠la̠ eghighira̠ bho̠, ya̠ na̠ ed̠um i̠wal ala ma̠ obhin osor, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠sora̠n a̠ga̠i obhel wa̠ iloghodi̠ar bho̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na bho̠.
MAT 2:17 Onon agu̠o̠ ubhin umuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ya̠ owil A̠zerimaya a̠wa̠ bho̠, ma̠a̠:
MAT 2:18 “U̠mu̠gho̠n o̠gba igbir d̠a̠ Arama, ed̠i na̠ i̠kparakpar ifinigha̠, A̠rese̠l na̠ a̠leghe ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ ola̠ na̠ o̠le̠gh i̠na tu̠tu̠n ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ onima̠ d̠o̠, ezin bho̠ awa na̠ emugughu.”
MAT 2:19 Igiel bho̠ E̠ro̠d a̠mugh bho̠, sa̠ otileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ d̠a̠ amala d̠a̠ Izipt
MAT 2:20 a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “B̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠bhin O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ onweni D̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Izre̠l, ezin bho̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eku ma̠ a̠ghud̠um O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ emugh.”
MAT 2:21 O̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ a̠bhin O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ onweni bho̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Izre̠l.
MAT 2:22 Ya̠a̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n ma̠a̠ Ake̠lo̠s o̠nyi̠ ta̠ E̠ro̠d na̠ a̠rileghom A̠zudia̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ghil o̠gi̠ i̠se̠, sa̠ ukikiom i̠na d̠a̠ amala ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ agba Agalili.
MAT 2:23 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ e̠ma ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Anazare̠t, ma̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠di̠ar ya̠ u̠wo̠l d̠a̠ owil bho̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: “Ta̠ obhelegi I̠na ma̠a̠ ola̠ Anazare̠t.”
MAT 3:1 D̠a̠ igiel bho̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ a̠ru bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ghana A̠zudia̠ ka̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠
MAT 3:2 ma̠a̠: “Itiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin, ezin bho̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠tua̠n.”
MAT 3:3 Onon bha̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ owil Azaya agba a̠gboloma̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Okoroko na̠ a̠si na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ e̠ghana bho̠, na̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠tu̠ghu̠mane̠ ma̠ eten ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, ma̠ eselegi ma̠ reten d̠o̠yo̠.’ ”
MAT 3:4 A̠rukpe ibura̠ ta̠ Azo̠n, bha̠ ubhin ipur e̠nam a̠dol o̠le̠m, sa̠ i̠na akpo̠aghan o̠kara ozu e̠nam a̠kitineni ma̠ ekika̠gh d̠o̠yo̠. Ed̠ia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bha̠ i̠ganw na̠ ame̠ ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ aparapa.
MAT 3:5 Igiel obha̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m na̠ A̠zudia̠ na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh d̠a̠ eghighira̠ Azo̠dan id̠u i̠gi̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 3:6 Sa̠ i̠na a̠wur awa ma̠ amu̠m d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan, agu̠o̠ awa iloghoma̠n i̠karabh d̠awa sa̠ i̠gba imutiom bho̠.
MAT 3:7 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na abi̠gh o̠lo̠gh Rafarisi na̠ Rasadusi na̠ eru ra̠ owura̠ amu̠m bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Inyin anwi̠i̠ny i̠bho̠ru̠bho̠ru̠ i̠karabh i̠di̠ar, a̠nyen a̠kikiom inyin oghil o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ibom i̠gam ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠?
MAT 3:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, imume ma̠ itu ya̠ ta̠ eleriom ma̠a̠ inyin na̠ otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin.
MAT 3:9 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ e̠re̠ma d̠a̠ rologi d̠inyin ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar onwuna̠ ma̠ obom o̠we̠de̠ Ebraham.’ Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin ikputu i̠nye̠n a̠tenemeni ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Ebraham.
MAT 3:10 I̠se̠n, na̠ ologhom oguri ma̠ u̠do̠ d̠a̠ igbolo iriren bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ kerekere oriren ola̠ omum d̠o̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i imuma̠, ta̠ ogu okoton, orobh o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ anya.”
MAT 3:11 “Ya̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ a̠wur inyin amu̠m ma̠ oleriom ma̠a̠ inyin na̠ otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠pu ami̠ na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ ami̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠gi̠o̠n id̠id̠igh agbaka d̠o̠yo̠. I̠na ta̠ a̠bhin E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ na̠ anya a̠wur inyin.
MAT 3:12 I̠na na̠ a̠sibh okporoma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠, ma̠ obhin o̠b̠i̠r o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠ okokod̠i ikpo ed̠ia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ od̠ighom d̠a̠ esi eko bho̠, ya̠a̠ ta̠ anu̠o̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ibhobho bho̠ d̠a̠ anya ola̠ ka̠ od̠im d̠o̠.”
MAT 3:13 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠ sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ Agalili agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan ka̠ ate̠i̠ Azo̠n owur o̠yo̠ amu̠m.
MAT 3:14 Ya̠a̠ Azo̠n na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir o̠ku̠a, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Akpe̠ ku ma̠ anwa ma̠ owur ami̠, bha̠ anwa na̠ a̠ru ku d̠ami̠ ma̠ owur oyom.”
MAT 3:15 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠: “Ma̠ra̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a ma̠ i̠se̠n ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom agu̠o̠ a̠sora̠n o̠ro̠ bho̠.” Sa̠ Azo̠n a̠ma̠ra̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a.
MAT 3:16 Azo̠n owur A̠zizo̠s amu̠m o̠we̠le̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠bhun bho̠ sa̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ a̠gurona̠ sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh ka̠ E̠mu̠gh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠sor akpasan i̠na ka̠ ukpugh osege.
MAT 3:17 Sa̠ okoroko a̠si a̠mite d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ma̠a̠: “Onon o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, wa̠ ami̠ itula̠n ibom bho̠, wa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠bhon ologi na̠ a̠gboloma̠ bho̠.”
MAT 4:1 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠rileghom A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ghana ma̠ eru bho̠ ma̠ o̠d̠agi̠an O̠yo̠.
MAT 4:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ne ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ tu̠tu̠n eruba̠l a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n, sa̠ o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠na.
MAT 4:3 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ad̠agi̠an bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, bha̠ ruome ma̠ ikpo i̠gbaki̠ghe̠ i̠nye̠n etenegia̠n ed̠ia̠n.”
MAT 4:4 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠: “Na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri ma̠a̠: ‘O̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ko obhin d̠o̠ d̠a̠ od̠e ed̠ia̠n ku̠ku̠m a̠d̠um, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ikpo a̠fugh ya̠ na̠ emite d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.’”
MAT 4:5 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠, sa̠ eru bho̠ a̠bhin i̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ka̠ amarame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ asi̠kaka otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
MAT 4:6 sa̠ eru bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ I̠na ma̠a̠: “Agu̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, bha̠ pele ma̠ a̠sor. Ezin bho̠, na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri ma̠a̠: “ ‘I̠na ta̠ a̠ruom itileduom bho̠ ma̠ okponom Oyom, sa̠ ta̠ e̠su̠ar anwa d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa, b̠o̠ka̠ anwa na̠ od̠ighia̠nma̠ ma̠ a̠wel d̠a̠ o̠gbaki̠ghe̠.’”
MAT 4:7 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠: “Na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri nyen ma̠a̠: ‘Ko o̠d̠agi̠an Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom!’”
MAT 4:8 D̠a̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠, sa̠ eru bho̠ a̠bhin I̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu ola̠ amar agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ sa̠ atu̠o̠gho̠m a̠leriom I̠na ma̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠dila̠de irileghom e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ isosorogia̠n d̠awa,
MAT 4:9 sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ I̠na ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ Nyam eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, ka̠ Anwa ikpud̠ia̠n i̠ko̠l ami̠.”
MAT 4:10 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠: “Eru, tene ma̠ ad̠u̠a! Na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri ma̠a̠: ‘Ko̠le̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom ma̠ a̠gir a̠nigha̠ I̠na ku̠ku̠m.’”
MAT 4:11 Sa̠ eru bho̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a. I̠se̠ d̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ iru ra̠ i̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ inigha̠ i̠na.
MAT 4:12 Igiel bho̠ u̠gba unigha̠ I̠na ma̠ na̠ o̠d̠u̠o̠m Azo̠n d̠a̠ ikoli bho̠, sa̠ I̠na ad̠u̠a agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili.
MAT 4:13 Sa̠ i̠na awe̠le̠ ma̠ Anazare̠t agi̠ ka̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ Akapanu̠m d̠a̠ aka abadi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Aze̠bu̠lo̠n na̠ Anaftalai̠,
MAT 4:14 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ta̠ owil Azaya ma̠a̠:
MAT 4:15 “Ebhugh Aze̠bu̠lo̠n na̠ ebhugh Anaftalai̠, d̠a̠ akagara esoroma̠ abadi̠ wa̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ Azo̠dan bho̠, Agalili esi wa̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu na̠ erugh bho̠.
MAT 4:16 A̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ erugh d̠a̠ azi̠m bho̠, na̠ e̠bi̠gh e̠b̠alab̠al ola̠ na̠ awar ibom. Ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh d̠a̠ eghighira̠ okokogh omugh bho̠ eka̠, e̠b̠alab̠al na̠ amu̠o̠m awa.”
MAT 4:17 Ob̠eton obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ o̠gba orile ma̠a̠: “Itiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh, ezin bho̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠tua̠n!”
MAT 4:18 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile agbal Abadi̠ Agalili, sa̠ abi̠gh i̠wal a̠rumor, Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠pita̠ bho̠ na̠ Anduru umor d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ na̠ erobh o̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ abadi̠ bho̠. Awa i̠ku̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠.
MAT 4:19 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠tu̠o̠no̠me̠ Ami̠, sa̠ Ami̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni inyin i̠ku̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠ a̠nwunom.”
MAT 4:20 I̠se̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠we̠le̠ ma̠ i̠gbo̠ d̠awa iten ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m D̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 4:21 O̠d̠u̠a i̠se̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, sa̠ abi̠gh ipa̠n i̠wal a̠rumor, A̠zemsi o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Aze̠bidi na̠ Azo̠n umor d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ologi oghugh na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠awa Aze̠bidi, na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠man i̠gbo̠ d̠awa, sa̠ a̠bhelegi awa.
MAT 4:22 Sa̠ awa i̠we̠le̠ epa̠ ma̠ oghugh bho̠ na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠awa iten ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m D̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 4:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ Agalili atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ru̠gala d̠awa, sa̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba irileghom bho̠, sa̠ a̠koko ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere asu̠nwe̠r na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ a̠nwunom bho̠.
MAT 4:24 Sa̠ o̠du̠ D̠o̠yo̠ asasaragi̠an d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ A̠siria̠, sa̠ awa ibhin eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r a̠d̠ien kere kere rasu̠nwe̠r na̠ i̠nyo̠gho̠nyo̠gh ali̠gam a̠ruzu, na̠ ogbo ya̠ a̠ruru na̠ e̠b̠am, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ena̠ bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ a̠risi ozu na̠ eb̠ogina̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠koko awa.
MAT 4:25 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom d̠a̠ Agalili, na̠ Ebhugh A̠d̠iobh Re̠ma, na̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, na̠ A̠zudia̠, na̠ re̠ma ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠b̠e̠ye̠ma Azo̠dan bho̠, i̠tu̠o̠no̠m I̠na.
MAT 5:1 A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ asi̠n d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ I̠na.
MAT 5:2 Sa̠ i̠na akpato̠n o̠nu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa. Sa̠ agba ma̠a̠:
MAT 5:3 “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ iloghoma̠n ekulom d̠awa d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh bho̠, Ezin bho̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny ola̠ awa.
MAT 5:4 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ bho̠, Ezin bho̠ ta̠ o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠awa!
MAT 5:5 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh ado̠l o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu bho̠, Ezin bho̠ a̠de bho̠ ta̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ awa!
MAT 5:6 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠, o̠ko̠i̠ na̠ ebhiroma̠ orugh ya̠ igielake̠ na̠ ed̠ighi bho̠, Ezin bho̠ ta̠ elegha̠n awa!
MAT 5:7 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekpon igbirigbir bho̠, Ezin bho̠ awa ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ okpon igbirigbir!
MAT 5:8 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ologi i̠b̠ab̠ala bho̠, Ezin bho̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh A̠zib̠a̠!
MAT 5:9 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ emutiom ekima̠ bho̠, Ezin bho̠ ta̠ obhelegi awa ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!
MAT 5:10 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ odin a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ d̠awa na̠ ogbikimeni bho̠, Ezin bho̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny ta̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.”
MAT 5:11 “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin igiel a̠nwunom na̠ erogi inyin, sa̠ na̠ egbikimeni inyin, sa̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere i̠karabh na̠ igunugha̠ na̠ eb̠ologiom inyin ma̠ ebula̠ ami̠.
MAT 5:12 Ibhone ma̠ ologi ma̠ ebo, ezin bho̠ alu̠kpe̠ d̠inyin ibom d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny. Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ awa igbikimeni ma̠ a̠riwil ya̠ id̠ia̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠.”
MAT 5:13 “Inyin ub̠on e̠mara̠nwunom onon, ya̠a̠ ka̠ ub̠on bho̠ osibh mu̠, ka̠ ta̠ od̠ighi eka̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠lisibh bho̠ ta̠ a̠nwe a̠mite? Abar ola̠ ta̠ obhin ogir bo̠mu̠, a̠ten ozu orobh ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠ze̠re̠gi̠.”
MAT 5:14 “Inyin e̠b̠alab̠al e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠. E̠ma ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu ola̠ na̠ anwo̠gi̠na bo̠.
MAT 5:15 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ o̠su̠o̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ ato̠di̠ obhin abafu̠ onin o̠to̠ma okpegiom. Ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠gbam ghan d̠a̠ anyu̠ abar ola̠ u̠marame̠ni̠ ma̠ onigha̠ e̠b̠alab̠al eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu bho̠.
MAT 5:16 D̠a̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, e̠b̠alab̠al d̠inyin amu̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh ib̠eb̠i ogir d̠inyin, sa̠ ta̠ e̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.”
MAT 5:17 “O̠ni̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠ ma̠a̠, Ami̠ iru ma̠ ogbogion Oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi, bo̠d̠o̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ A̠riwil bho̠. Ami̠ iru d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbogion, ya̠a̠ ami̠ iru ma̠ omuzoghod̠iom.
MAT 5:18 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, tu̠tu̠n ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠de onon ta̠ eten e̠d̠u̠a, bebina̠ e̠pe̠re̠pe̠r bo̠d̠o̠ ekpo abar ola̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ ola̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a bo̠ tu̠tu̠n ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠.
MAT 5:19 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠guri d̠a̠ aka ma̠ ekpo abar ola̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ oloko bho̠, sa̠ awe̠le̠man o̠b̠ar na̠ obha̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ta̠ obhelegi i̠na ma̠ wa̠ aki̠r a̠pu d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar ya̠ oloko bho̠ ato̠ bho̠ sa̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a nyen, ta̠ obhelegi i̠na ma̠a̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 5:20 Sa̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, usigimeni ka̠ igielake̠ d̠inyin ipel ita̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠, inyin ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny.”
MAT 5:21 “Inyin o̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠ u̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom igied̠i bho̠ ma̠a̠: ‘Ka̠ ogigh o̠ni̠.’O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gigh o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh ase̠.
MAT 5:22 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ agam i̠gam a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠d̠o̠ u̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ta̠ a̠d̠igh ase̠. O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠d̠o̠ u̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ‘Ema̠!’ ta̠ a̠d̠igh ase̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ikei A̠zu bho̠. O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Ob̠ogoro ema̠,’ bha̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ e̠banya bho̠ a̠sugho.”
MAT 5:23 “Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa a̠bhin abar alu̠kpe̠ d̠oyom agi̠ d̠a̠ enwen alu̠kpe̠ bho̠, sa̠ anwa i̠ru̠ru̠an e̠kal abar ola̠ anwa i̠pi̠o̠m umor d̠oyom,
MAT 5:24 We̠le̠ ma̠ abar alu̠kpe̠ d̠oyom i̠se̠ d̠a̠ ukpo bho̠, ma̠ a̠d̠ia̠ ka̠ a̠tulugia̠n umor d̠oyom ma̠ a̠mutiom ekima̠. I̠se̠ ku ma̠ agi̠ ka̠ akpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ d̠oyom.”
MAT 5:25 “Wia̠ne ma̠ a̠tulugia̠n na̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ anwa na̠ o̠ku̠anan bho̠ d̠a̠ obhel inyin od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ eten, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko obhin d̠o̠ nyam o̠gi̠o̠m ma̠ osobhmase̠ bho̠, sa̠ osobhmase̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠bhin anwa agi̠o̠m o̠du̠o̠ma bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ o̠du̠o̠m anwa d̠a̠ ikoli.
MAT 5:26 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, anwa ko omite d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ tu̠tu̠n ka̠ anwa na̠ akpe̠ kabar kabar d̠a̠ amu̠kpe̠ ebhumase̠ bho̠ amadon.”
MAT 5:27 “Inyin na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n ka̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Ko od̠e ma̠ e̠ma.’
MAT 5:28 Ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠kpon ani̠ebhom sa̠ ibhir okod̠uom, bha̠ na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠ma d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 5:29 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ od̠iom ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam ogir o̠karabh, poko ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠robh. Anwa ma̠ orobh onin esi ozu d̠oyom a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ orobh eb̠la̠ ozu d̠oyom d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠.
MAT 5:30 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam ogir i̠karabh, sobhe ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠robh. Anwa ma̠ orobh onin esi ozu d̠oyom a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ obhin eb̠la̠ ozu d̠oyom ka̠ od̠ighom d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠.”
MAT 5:31 “Na̠ o̠gba oguri ma̠a̠: ‘O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠gbogina̠ ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, bha̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠d̠ire ogbogina̠ ilom.’
MAT 5:32 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠ten ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ ani̠ o̠ni̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠ma, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gbogina̠ ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ od̠e ma̠ e̠ma. Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhin ani̠ ola̠ oku̠a, a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma.”
MAT 5:33 “Inyin o̠mu̠gho̠n nyen, ya̠ u̠gba unigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom igied̠i ma̠a̠: ‘Ko o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ osibh ogua̠n d̠oyom wa̠ anwa igua̠n bho̠, ya̠a̠ sibhe ma̠ ogua̠n wa̠ anwa igua̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.’
MAT 5:34 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ aghaghana inyin ma̠a̠, ko od̠e na̠ od̠e ma̠ i̠zo̠, a̠d̠igh obhin ote̠nai̠ny, ezin bho̠, obha̠ a̠dila̠de irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠;
MAT 5:35 Bo̠d̠o̠ a̠de bho̠, ezin bho̠, obha̠ okpokpolom o̠gbam a̠wel d̠o̠yo̠; bo̠d̠o̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, ezin bho̠, obha̠ e̠ma ta̠ obom O̠li̠le̠ma bho̠.
MAT 5:36 Bo̠d̠o̠, ko obhin e̠mu̠ d̠oyom aghad̠i̠an, ezin bho̠ anwa ko orue d̠o̠ a̠d̠ighi bebina̠ ekpo asi̠ghal ma̠ oten aso̠n, bo̠d̠o̠ oten o̠zu̠zu̠a.
MAT 5:37 Ya̠a̠, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠oyom aro̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Yii, Yii,’ bo̠d̠o̠ ‘E̠e̠nyi̠, E̠e̠nyi̠.’ Ya̠a̠, ka̠ a̠pel o̠ku̠a, bha̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠ru.”
MAT 5:38 “Inyin o̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Na̠ obhin ekpo a̠d̠ien na̠ o̠kpe̠ ma̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien, sa̠ na̠ obhin ob̠ub̠ura̠ na̠ o̠kpe̠ ma̠ ob̠ub̠ura̠.’
MAT 5:39 Ya̠a̠, Ami̠ na̠ aghaghana inyin ma̠a̠, ko owia̠n o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, ka̠ o̠ni̠ ab̠abh anwa d̠a̠ od̠iom ab̠akagba d̠oyom, tiba̠ra̠ ma̠ agba uwed̠i ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na nyen.
MAT 5:40 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan oler onyom iku obhin akapa a̠de d̠oyom, ma̠ra̠ i̠na a̠bhin akapa anyu̠ bho̠ nyen.
MAT 5:41 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠ponoma̠ nyam ma̠ orol a̠dol d̠o̠yo̠ orile amai̠l,bha̠ d̠ighe na̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠rile ma̠ i̠wal amai̠l.
MAT 5:42 Nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠puru nyam abar, sa̠ ka̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠wo̠lo̠ni̠ abar d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom, ko ogineni.”
MAT 5:43 “Inyin o̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Tula̠ne ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ aka d̠oyom bho̠,ma̠ a̠ghel o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ alo̠gh a̠d̠ien anwa bho̠.’
MAT 5:44 Ya̠a̠, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, itula̠ne ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠lo̠gh a̠d̠ien inyin bho̠, ma̠ siseiny enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eku inyin na̠ egbikimeni bho̠,
MAT 5:45 O̠ku̠a sa̠ inyin ta̠ oten anwi̠i̠ny O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠. Ezin bho̠, i̠na na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ ogogo bho̠ na̠ amu̠o̠m id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠, na̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠bha ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠b̠ab̠ala bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh a̠ma̠rugh i̠te̠i̠ bho̠.
MAT 5:46 Ka̠ inyin utula̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ etula̠n inyin bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, asu̠o̠ bho̠ ka̠ ere? Igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh bho̠ eka̠ na̠ erugh o̠ku̠a.
MAT 5:47 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ inyin na̠ obheleghom ogbo ya̠ inyin uloghom bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, ka̠ inyin ugir ere opeleni? Ibhebhia̠nbho̠ eka̠ na̠ erugh o̠ku̠a.
MAT 5:48 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, irughe ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal, ma̠ agu̠o̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ igielake̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal bho̠.”
MAT 6:1 “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ b̠o̠ka̠ ogir ib̠eb̠i d̠inyin i̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ inyin na̠ ogir na̠ oleriom a̠nwunom o̠bi̠gh inyin. Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ inyin ugir o̠ku̠a, bha̠ inyin ko o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 6:2 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, igiel anwa na̠ a̠nwo ma̠ inwo, ko od̠ia̠ ma̠ a̠pughe ma̠ od̠od̠ue ma̠ agu̠o̠ ibhelebhel bho̠ na̠ egir d̠a̠ u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ reten bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠se̠bh awa. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ awa na̠ e̠te̠i̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠awa.
MAT 6:3 Ya̠a̠ anwa, nwo ma̠ inwo ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ekiel agu̠o̠ d̠oyom ko ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠gir,
MAT 6:4 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogir inwo d̠oyom aro̠ d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na, sa̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom wa̠ na̠ abi̠gh d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam.
MAT 6:5 “Igiel inyin na̠ osiseiny, o̠ni̠ ko o̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ibhelebhelbho̠. Ezin bho̠ awa na̠ eba̠ra̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ e̠mara d̠a̠ ru̠gala na̠ d̠a̠ aka reten bho̠ osiseiny, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠bi̠gh awa. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, awa na̠ e̠te̠i̠ epa̠ ma̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠awa eleghemeni.
MAT 6:6 Ya̠a̠ igiel anwa na̠ a̠siseiny, d̠ighe d̠a̠ e̠bhai̠ ma̠ a̠gugi ma̠ egugh bho̠, ma̠ a̠siseiny a̠nigha̠ ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠, sa̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom wa̠ na̠ abi̠gh d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam.
MAT 6:7 O̠ni̠ ko ota̠ba̠ ma̠ a̠fugh d̠a̠ a̠siseiny d̠inyin ma̠ agu̠o̠ ibhebhia̠nbho̠, ya̠ na̠ e̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ ota̠ba̠ a̠fugh d̠a̠ a̠siseiny ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠nagha awa.
MAT 6:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ko orugh agu̠o̠ awa, ezin bho̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin a̠loghom abar wa̠ na̠ akparama inyin bho̠, kisa̠ inyin ta̠ opuru i̠na.
MAT 6:9 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, onon agu̠o̠ inyin ta̠ osiseiny: “ ‘O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, A̠d̠ien d̠oyom aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ e̠tu̠tu̠,
MAT 6:10 Irileghom d̠oyom a̠ru, I̠to̠ d̠oyom e̠ro̠ ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠de onon, Ma̠ agu̠o̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 6:11 Ed̠ia̠n ya̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, Nigha̠ i̠yar ya̠ a̠didon.
MAT 6:12 We̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ i̠karabh d̠i̠yar, Ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh ya̠ ipa̠n ogbo na̠ ed̠ighi i̠yar bho̠.
MAT 6:13 Ko oma̠ra̠ i̠yar omel d̠a̠ ad̠agi̠an, Ya̠a̠, tenemeni i̠yar d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠.’
MAT 6:14 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠, inyin na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh ya̠ a̠nwunom na̠ ed̠ighi inyin, O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠inyin nyen.
MAT 6:15 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ inyin o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh ya̠ a̠nwunom na̠ ed̠ighi inyin bho̠, O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ ka̠ o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin nyen.
MAT 6:16 “Igiel inyin na̠ one ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠ku̠ru̠ru̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ibhelebhel a̠nwunom, ya̠ na̠ egurumeni ma̠ ra̠misigh d̠awa ma̠ oleriom a̠nwunom ma̠ awa na̠ ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, awa na̠ e̠te̠i̠ epa̠ ma̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠awa.
MAT 6:17 Ya̠a̠, igiel anwa na̠ a̠ne ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, titila̠ ma̠ a̠misigh d̠oyom ma̠ a̠sigha̠ ma̠ elo d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ d̠oyom,
MAT 6:18 Agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ko oleriom d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠a̠ anwa na̠ a̠ne ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, ya̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom ku̠ku̠m wa̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ bho̠. Sa̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom wa̠ na̠ abi̠gh d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam.
MAT 6:19 “O̠ni̠ ko okoko ma̠ i̠di̠ar edim d̠inyin d̠a̠ a̠de onon, esi wa̠ ad̠u̠i̠ny na̠ o̠sari̠ ta̠ e̠pi̠e̠gi̠, sa̠ aru̠gba ta̠ eb̠ogion ed̠igh ka̠ eb̠ighogh bho̠.
MAT 6:20 Ya̠a̠, ikoko ma̠ i̠di̠ar edim d̠inyin d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, esi wa̠ ad̠u̠i̠ny bo̠d̠o̠ o̠sari̠ ko o̠pi̠e̠gi̠ d̠o̠, sa̠ aru̠gba ko ob̠ogion d̠o̠ ed̠igh ka̠ eb̠ighogh bho̠.
MAT 6:21 Esi wa̠ i̠di̠ar edim d̠oyom od̠i bho̠, i̠se̠ esi ologi d̠oyom ta̠ aro̠.
MAT 6:22 “Ekpo a̠d̠ien bha̠ ato̠di̠ ozu o̠ni̠. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom aghu̠a, eb̠la̠ ozu d̠oyom ta̠ amar awar.
MAT 6:23 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ekpo ad̠ien d̠oyom na̠ a̠b̠oma̠n, eb̠la̠ ozu d̠oyom ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ azi̠m. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ku̠gba ma̠ e̠b̠alab̠al wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ozu d̠oyom bho̠ na̠ a̠ten azi̠m, o̠ku̠a ka̠ azi̠m bho̠ ta̠ aro̠ eka̠?
MAT 6:24 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom aru̠mu̠ bo̠. Ezin bho̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠ghel odi sa̠ ta̠ a̠tula̠n uwed̠i, bo̠d̠o̠ ta̠ a̠zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoiy a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi, sa̠ ta̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ uwed̠i. O̠ni̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠ ako̠l A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ okpoki.
MAT 6:25 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan a̠ghud̠um d̠inyin ma̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ od̠e, bo̠d̠o̠ abar ola̠ o̠d̠a, bo̠d̠o̠ ipulupul ozu bho̠, na̠ abar ola̠ o̠lagha. A̠ghud̠um na̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar a̠pu ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, sa̠ ozu olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar a̠pu ma̠ ibura̠, ke̠re̠?
MAT 6:26 Ikpone ma̠ ed̠ighom a̠ghud̠um i̠nu̠r ya̠ na̠ e̠bhe̠bh d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠. Awa igbebh d̠o̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ib̠u d̠o̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ikpol d̠o̠ nyen ed̠ia̠n eguri d̠a̠ esi eko, ya̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ na̠ a̠koko awa. Inyin ulei d̠a̠ ma̠ abar opu awa ke̠re̠?
MAT 6:27 A̠nyen inyin ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin d̠a̠ i̠nyo̠gho̠ghan alo̠gho̠m bebina̠ ekud̠i obhel d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠?
MAT 6:28 “Ya̠a̠, inyin na̠ o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan ere na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ ibura̠? I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpon ra̠lele ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ ebhin e̠su̠. Awa igir d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠kparakpar ogir, ikpogh d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar nyen.
MAT 6:29 Ya̠a̠, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ Aso̠lo̠mo̠n eka̠, d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ obura̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ibura̠ ya̠ ibhon ile̠i ita̠ odi i̠se̠.
MAT 6:30 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠buri ma̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ ya̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠didon d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠, sa̠ o̠nyi̠ obhel sa̠ na̠ orobh na̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠, I̠na ka̠ oburi d̠a̠ inyin a̠pu ma̠ o̠ku̠a ke̠re̠? Inyin ogbo ya̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠ bho̠!
MAT 6:31 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ka̠ o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan efugh ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar ta̠ od̠e ma̠ ere?’ Bo̠d̠o̠, ‘Ta̠ o̠d̠a ma̠ ere?’ Bo̠d̠o̠ ‘Ta̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an ere?’
MAT 6:32 Ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n, bha̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ibhebhia̠n bho̠ na̠ ewia̠n o̠te̠i̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠loghom ma̠ a̠bhon inyin o̠te̠i̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠ye̠.
MAT 6:33 Ya̠a̠, abar wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu bho̠, bha̠ iwia̠ne ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ a̠ghud̠um igielake̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ta̠ o̠lo̠gho̠m eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n onigha̠ inyin.
MAT 6:34 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan egboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ elegien ta̠ aro̠. Ezin bho̠, elegien na̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ anyo̠gho̠ghan a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na ta̠ aro̠. Ezin bho̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠wuna̠ ma̠ i̠nyo̠ngho̠yo̠ngh iya̠ o̠yo̠.
MAT 7:1 “Ka̠ o̠bi̠gh a̠nwunom api̠e̠, b̠o̠ka̠ u̠bi̠gh inyin o̠pi̠e̠.
MAT 7:2 A̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ inyin ubhin u̠bi̠gh a̠nwunom u̠pi̠e̠ bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ani̠ inyin o̠pi̠e̠. Sa̠ a̠d̠ien o̠to̠ma wa̠ inyin ubhin u̠to̠ unigha̠ awa bho̠, bha̠ wa̠ ta̠ obhin o̠to̠ onigha̠ inyin bho̠.
MAT 7:3 “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ anwa na̠ abi̠gh o̠taghatagh d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien umor d̠oyom, sa̠ anwa na̠ ologhoma̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ali̠kara wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom bho̠?
MAT 7:4 Anwa ta̠ atu̠n ere a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠oyom ma̠a̠, ‘umor, d̠ighi ami̠ i̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠taghatagh d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom,’ ya̠a̠ ali̠kara od̠i d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom?
MAT 7:5 Anwa obhelebhel o̠ni̠! D̠ia̠ ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ ali̠kara wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom bho̠; i̠se̠ kisa̠ anwa ta̠ amar abi̠gh abar asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠taghatagh wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien umor d̠oyom bho̠.
MAT 7:6 “O̠ni̠ ka̠ onigha̠ ma̠ abar e̠tu̠tu̠ ma̠ a̠sib̠ogho, bo̠d̠o̠ ko orobhod̠i ma̠ ri̠b̠o̠lo̠ ibom a̠b̠ua̠ d̠inyin ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ roporopo, b̠o̠ka̠ ibhin a̠sike d̠awa e̠ze̠re̠gi̠ ed̠iomeni, sa̠ ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ e̠ku̠su̠gi̠ inyin.
MAT 7:7 “Ipuru, sa̠ ta̠ onigha̠ inyin. I̠bho̠ro̠ghane̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh. Ikpukpu, sa̠ ta̠ oguron onigha̠ inyin.
MAT 7:8 Ezin bho̠, ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠puru, ta̠ onigha̠, ola̠ abho̠ro̠ghan ta̠ abi̠gh, ola̠ a̠kpukpu, ta̠ oguron onigha̠.
MAT 7:9 “A̠nyen inyin ola̠ ka̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠puru ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton o̠gbaki̠ghe̠ a̠nigha̠.
MAT 7:10 Bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ a̠puru ma̠ ena̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton o̠karabh abar a̠nigha̠.
MAT 7:11 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ku̠gba ma̠ inyin ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠karabh a̠nwunom bho̠ eloghom agu̠o̠ onigha̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠inyin ib̠ebi̠ i̠di̠ar, a̠dina̠mu ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠. I̠na ta̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠di̠ar ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ipuru I̠na bho̠.
MAT 7:12 Kere kere abar ola̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan ma̠ a̠nwunom egir enigha̠ nyam, gire ani̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a ma̠ a̠nigha̠ awa. Ezin bho̠ onon agu̠o̠ Oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ A̠riwil bho̠ ima̠ra̠.
MAT 7:13 “I̠wo̠le̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ogigo wa̠ a̠kporia̠n bho̠ ma̠ ed̠igh. Ezin bho̠, o̠nu̠ ogigo wa̠ are̠gh bho̠, na̠ eten wa̠ a̠bhela̠ bho̠, na̠ a̠bhin o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ omugh, sa̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom na̠ e̠wo̠l i̠se̠ na̠ ed̠igh.
MAT 7:14 Ya̠a̠, o̠nu̠ ogigo wa̠ na̠ o̠wo̠l na̠ o̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠ a̠kporia̠n, sa̠ eten wa̠ na̠ o̠wo̠l na̠ o̠gi̠ bho̠ eka̠ a̠kporia̠n. Igini a̠nwunom ku̠ku̠m na̠ e̠te̠i̠ na̠ ed̠igh.
MAT 7:15 “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ a̠riwil igunugha̠ ya̠ na̠ eru d̠inyin na̠ ibura̠ ka̠ ro̠nana, ne̠ge̠ i̠gagaman i̠nam.
MAT 7:16 Na̠ obhin imuma̠ d̠awa na̠ olelegi awa. A̠nwunom ikpokpo d̠o̠ ma̠ itu a̠grep d̠a̠ ed̠um ib̠ub̠ulom, bo̠d̠o̠ itu a̠fig d̠a̠ e̠ko̠ko̠.
MAT 7:17 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ob̠eb̠i oriren na̠ a̠mum ib̠eb̠i itu, ya̠a̠ o̠karabh oriren na̠ a̠mum i̠karabh itu.
MAT 7:18 Ob̠eb̠i oriren na̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠mum i̠karabh itu, obha̠ agu̠o̠ o̠karabh oriren eka̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠mum ib̠eb̠i itu.
MAT 7:19 Kere kere oriren ola̠ omum d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i otu ta̠ ogu o̠gu̠ro̠m, sa̠ ta̠ orobh o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠.
MAT 7:20 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ta̠ obhin imuma̠ d̠awa olelegi awa.
MAT 7:21 “Ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhelegi Ami̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, Wa̠nwuna̠,’ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny, ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ igir i̠to̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 7:22 D̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠go̠ya ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, Wa̠nwuna̠, i̠yar ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien d̠oyom o̠gba ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠, obhin a̠d̠ien d̠oyom oze ma̠ a̠ruru, obhin a̠d̠ien d̠oyom ogir a̠d̠izo ilologia̠n, ke̠re̠?’
MAT 7:23 Yaa̠, ami̠ ta̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, ‘Obhel ola̠ ami̠ iloghom inyin bo̠, itene ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a, inyin ogbo ya̠ irugh i̠te̠i̠.’
MAT 7:24 “Kere kere o̠ni̠ ola̠ amu̠gho̠n atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠ami̠ i̠nye̠n, sa̠ a̠rugh o̠ku̠a, bha̠ ta̠ obhin o̠tu̠o̠m ologhobar o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lo ma̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠.
MAT 7:25 Sa̠ igiel a̠d̠io bho̠ alo̠bh bho̠, sa̠ ra̠d̠igho bho̠ iru bho̠, sa̠ rogim bho̠ igim i̠dama ma̠ otu bho̠, otu bho̠ na̠ omel d̠o̠. Ezin bho̠, o̠di̠o̠ma bho̠ bo̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma.
MAT 7:26 Ya̠a̠, ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ola̠ amu̠gho̠n atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠ami̠ i̠nye̠n, sa̠ ogir d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a, bha̠ ta̠ obhin o̠tu̠o̠m ema̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lo ma̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ i̠si̠sar bho̠.
MAT 7:27 Sa̠ igiel a̠d̠io bho̠ alo̠bh bho̠, sa̠ ra̠d̠igho bho̠ iru bho̠, sa̠ rogim bho̠ igim, i̠dama ma̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ otu bho̠ a̠mel a̠tutughud̠ia̠n. Abu̠gh emel!”
MAT 7:28 Sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠, igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠kunugiom atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ ro̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 7:29 Ezin bho̠ i̠na atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠, sa̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ inwegia̠n ita̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠.
MAT 8:1 Igiel bho̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu a̠sor bho̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAT 8:2 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh a̠ru ra̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Wa̠nwuna̠! Ku̠gba ma̠ Anwa ta̠ a̠ma̠ra̠, bha̠ koko ami̠ ma̠ ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠.”
MAT 8:3 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠selegheni epa̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠kula̠n i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ a̠ma̠ra̠, b̠ab̠ala” Ogbo na̠ onin sa̠ a̠d̠um d̠a̠ asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh bho̠
MAT 8:4 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠: “Bi̠ghe̠! Ko o̠gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ gi̠e̠ ka̠ a̠leriom ozu d̠oyom okur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠ akpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ wa̠ A̠mozizi a̠ruom bho̠, ma̠ oleriom ma̠ anwa na̠ a̠d̠um.”
MAT 8:5 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ Akapanu̠m bho̠, sa̠ odi we̠mu̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham A̠rom a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ i̠na, sa̠ ale̠gh i̠na
MAT 8:6 a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Wa̠nwuna̠, ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠ami̠ na̠ anwe̠r a̠b̠ogina̠ d̠a̠ otu sa̠ na̠ abi̠gh ibom ali̠gam a̠ruzu.”
MAT 8:7 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠koko i̠na.”
MAT 8:8 Sa̠ we̠mu̠ e̠gham bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠: “Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ ilei d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ od̠ighom oyom d̠a̠ ekpukpu i̠galaga otu d̠ami̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, fughe ma̠ i̠na a̠d̠um, sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠um.
MAT 8:9 Ami̠ eka̠ bha̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠, sa̠ ami̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon igboloma̠ ma̠ ogbo e̠gham ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ekpukpu d̠ami̠ bho̠. Ka̠ ami̠ iruom o̠ni̠ onon ma̠a̠, ‘Gi̠e̠,’ sa̠ ta̠ agi̠; ka̠ ami̠ iruom opa̠n o̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Tue,’ sa̠ ta̠ a̠ru. Ka̠ ami̠ iruom ogoni d̠ami̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Gire ma̠ abar onon,’ sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠gir.”
MAT 8:10 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ a̠b̠a̠gha̠gha̠, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m I̠na bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ami̠ ta̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠ abu̠gh o̠ko̠no̠n d̠a̠ Izre̠l.
MAT 8:11 Sa̠ Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ agba opuomite na̠ osor ogogo bho̠, ra̠ ed̠igh na̠ Ebraham, na̠ Azi̠ki̠, na̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ akpata od̠e d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 8:12 Ya̠a̠ ta̠ oze ma̠ idi anwi̠i̠ny Izre̠l ya̠a̠, nab̠o̠, awa anwi̠i̠ny irileghom bho̠, ka̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ obom azi̠m, esi ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠.”
MAT 8:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Gi̠e̠! A̠mite a̠nigha̠ nyam agu̠o̠ anwa ima̠ra̠ bho̠.” Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠d̠um onin obhel obha̠.
MAT 8:14 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠pita̠, sa̠ abi̠gh o̠yo̠go̠-onweni ta̠ A̠pita̠ d̠a̠ e̠mana asu̠nwe̠r ola̠ amu̠m o̠bhi̠i̠y na̠ a̠sibh sa̠ na̠ a̠bhin igiri.
MAT 8:15 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kula̠n agu̠o̠ ani̠ bho̠, sa̠ amu̠m-o̠bhi̠i̠y bho̠ ad̠u̠a, sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ed̠ia̠n aki̠o̠m i̠na i̠na.
MAT 8:16 Ate̠i̠ a̠dule, sa̠ ibhinogh a̠d̠izo ogbo ya̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ enyegi iru d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠mulughuom a̠ze ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ asi̠ghe̠gi̠ na̠ ekpo a̠fugh, sa̠ a̠koko ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠ bho̠ a̠d̠umeni,
MAT 8:17 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ya̠ owil Azaya a̠wa̠ bho̠, ma̠a̠: “I̠na asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ rasu̠nwe̠r d̠a̠ a̠ruzu d̠i̠yar, sa̠ a̠rol a̠dol rasu̠nwe̠r d̠i̠yar.”
MAT 8:18 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh agu̠o̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom na̠ eko i̠na ekiton bho̠, sa̠ a̠ruom ma̠ o̠b̠e̠i̠y d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠.
MAT 8:19 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ Atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ ta̠ atu̠o̠no̠m anwa agi̠ kesi kesi ola̠ anwa na̠ agi̠.”
MAT 8:20 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Rududu enwuna̠ ma̠ iyol ya̠ awa na̠ erugh, sa̠ i̠nu̠r anyu̠ eka̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ a̠rutu; ya̠a̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ od̠igh ola̠ ob̠enegiom e̠mu̠.”
MAT 8:21 Sa̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, d̠ighi ami̠ id̠ia̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ id̠i ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠.”
MAT 8:22 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Tu̠o̠no̠me̠ ku ami̠, ma̠ awe̠le̠man imumugh a̠nwunom bho̠, ed̠i ma̠ imumugh d̠awa.”
MAT 8:23 Sa̠ I̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi oghugh sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan D̠o̠yo̠ id̠igh ani̠.
MAT 8:24 Sa̠ o̠gagaman ogim a̠gim awai̠ d̠a̠ abadi̠ bho̠ ma̠ ola̠ ipoka̠na̠n amu̠m id̠u id̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠, ma̠ owie, ya̠a̠ I̠na na̠ okod̠u.
MAT 8:25 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠su̠me̠ni̠ I̠na ifugh ma̠a̠: “Wa̠nwuna̠, tenemeni i̠yar! A̠d̠ugh na̠ a̠bhin i̠yar!”
MAT 8:26 Sa̠ awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠: “Inyin u̠tu̠n ere na̠ oghil a̠rugugu? Inyin a̠nwunom ya̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠!” Sa̠ I̠na a̠b̠etina̠ a̠mulughuom ogim bho̠ na̠ abadi̠ bho̠, sa̠ ilia̠ i̠ro̠ to̠i̠ny.
MAT 8:27 Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠, ifugh ma̠a̠, “Onon ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠, ma̠ ola̠ ogim na̠ abadi̠ eka̠ na̠ e̠nagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ D̠o̠yo̠ bho̠?”
MAT 8:28 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠be̠i̠ d̠a̠ agba ebhugh Agadara bho̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠pel a̠bhun. Sa̠ i̠wal ilobhiri a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ enyegi i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠karabh esi bho̠ iru ra̠ i̠damaghan i̠na. Awa i̠bho̠ru̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠, a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ a̠mon ate̠i̠, orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠wo̠l esi bho̠ oten.
MAT 8:29 Awa i̠bi̠gh i̠na sa̠ imulughu ifugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ere d̠a̠ a̠ruzu d̠i̠yar? Anwa iru ma̠ i̠se̠n ma̠ o̠nyo̠gho̠gh i̠yar kisa̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ ekunuguma̠ obhel bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAT 8:30 Igiel obha̠, obom o̠lo̠gh roporopo na̠ ed̠e ma̠ esi ola̠ osigima̠ d̠o̠ awa.
MAT 8:31 Sa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ i̠le̠gh i̠na ifugh ma̠a̠: “Agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ a̠ze i̠yar na̠ asi̠ghe̠ bho̠, bha̠ ruome i̠yar o̠gi̠ ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ruzu roporopo bho̠.”
MAT 8:32 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Imite ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a!” Sa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ imite i̠gi̠ ka̠ id̠igh d̠a̠ roporopo bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh roporopo bho̠ igbudon ighil isor d̠a̠ a̠gbo bho̠, ka̠ i̠bhu̠ghu̠d̠i̠an imugughu d̠a̠ abadi̠ bho̠.
MAT 8:33 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekponom roporopo bho̠ ikpo ma̠ eghil i̠d̠u̠a, i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ka̠ i̠gba ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imutuma̠ ma̠ i̠wal ilobhiri a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ enyegi bho̠.
MAT 8:34 Obha̠ abar! Sa̠ eb̠la̠ e̠ma bho̠ id̠ua̠n i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ ima̠ra̠nua̠n i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠ oten o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ebhugh d̠awa.
MAT 9:1 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh ab̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ bho̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 9:2 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠misi bho̠, sa̠ idi a̠nwunom irol o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠b̠ogina̠ d̠a̠ ozu d̠a̠ a̠kporokporo ibhin ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠zizo̠s. Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh e̠mi̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠awa bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, kpo̠ ma̠ a̠luzu, na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠oyom onigha̠ nyam.”
MAT 9:3 Sa̠ idi ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ id̠igh i̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ epura̠n d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa ma̠a̠, “Onon a̠fugh i̠basi̠ ola̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAT 9:4 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠loghom i̠ru̠ru̠an d̠awa, sa̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ inyin na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an i̠karabh d̠a̠ rologi d̠inyin?
MAT 9:5 Oken wa̠ a̠b̠ur a̠pu ma̠ ofugh bho̠, ‘Na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠oyom onigha̠ nyam,’ bo̠d̠o̠, ‘B̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠rile’?
MAT 9:6 Ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan ma̠a̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh a̠nwunom d̠a̠ a̠de onon.” Sa̠ i̠na akparame̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ukula̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “B̠etina̠, ma̠ a̠b̠eton a̠kporokporo d̠oyom ma̠ a̠ten a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom.”
MAT 9:7 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠b̠ogina̠ bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 9:8 Igiel bho̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠bi̠gh abar wa̠ a̠mite bho̠, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa, sa̠ i̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠limon ya̠ o̠ku̠a bho̠.
MAT 9:9 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠d̠igh erile bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh o̠ni̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Amatiu, ka̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ e̠fe̠m ogun otua̠-ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhelegi a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Tu̠o̠no̠me̠ ami̠.” Sa̠ Amatiu a̠b̠etina̠ epa̠ atu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAT 9:10 Sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na od̠i d̠a̠ akpata od̠e d̠a̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠izo igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh iru ra̠ id̠igh na̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ id̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n.
MAT 9:11 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠bi̠gh bho̠, sa̠ ipura̠n ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere, ka̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin na̠ a̠d̠ed̠ia̠n igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠ka̠rabh?”
MAT 9:12 O̠mu̠gho̠n a̠pura̠n onon, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ogbo ya̠ a̠ruzu i̠ghu̠a bho̠ i̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ owil, ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r bho̠.
MAT 9:13 I̠se̠n, i̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ e̠tu̠ghan ezin abar wa̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Ami̠ iba̠ra̠ ku ma̠ okpon igbirigbir, ya̠a̠ o̠kpe̠ alu̠kpe̠ d̠o̠.’ Ezin bho̠ ami̠ iru d̠o̠ ma̠ ra̠ olebh ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom, ya̠a̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.”
MAT 9:14 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Azo̠n iru ra̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere wa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠mar na̠ one ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, ya̠a̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom ine ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ bho̠?”
MAT 9:15 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ogbo erogh bho̠ ta̠ e̠tu̠n ere e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ obhel wa̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ od̠i na̠ awa bho̠? Ya̠a̠, igiel na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa, sa̠ awa ta̠ ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠ye̠.
MAT 9:16 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin o̠go̠go̠ra̠ omom ukpe na̠ ab̠ad̠i̠ ma̠ opupu akapa bo̠. Ezin bho̠, esi wa̠ u̠b̠ad̠i bho̠ ta̠ a̠puruna̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ akapa bho̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ agu̠an a̠peleni ma̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ bho̠.
MAT 9:17 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ko o̠lo̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ imom a̠min d̠a̠ opupu akana ozu e̠nam, bo̠d̠o̠ bha̠ akana ozu e̠nam bho̠ ta̠ a̠pol, sa̠ a̠min bho̠ ta̠ ezugia̠n ebhe, sa̠ akana bho̠ ta̠ api̠an. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, na̠ o̠lo̠gh imom a̠min d̠a̠ imom rakana ozu e̠nam, sa̠ i̠wal a̠yi ta̠ ed̠um ebia̠.”
MAT 9:18 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ agba ma̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ irileghom u̠gala A̠zu bho̠ a̠ru, sa̠ a̠mel a̠kpud̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “I̠se̠n i̠se̠n kisa̠ ekpo epobh o̠nyani̠ d̠ami̠ a̠sobha̠n. O̠ku̠a eka̠, tue ra̠ agbam agu̠o̠ d̠oyom d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um.”
MAT 9:19 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠etina̠, sa̠ I̠na na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAT 9:20 Sa̠ odi ani̠ ola̠, na̠ a̠lei d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) ala ya̠ asi̠ na̠ e̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ ozu, awo̠l d̠a̠ aman ka̠ a̠kula̠n esi wa̠ u̠labh akapa d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
MAT 9:21 ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠fugh d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠: “Ka̠ ami̠ irue ikula̠n akapa d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠um.”
MAT 9:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠tiba̠ra̠ abi̠gh i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠nyani̠ d̠ami̠, ologi d̠oyom akpo̠, ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠umeni nyam.” Sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠d̠um onin igiel obha̠.
MAT 9:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ otu o̠ni̠ irileghom bho̠ sa̠ abi̠gh ogbo ya̠ na̠ epughe ma̠ o̠za na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ko̠ro̠ na̠ eleghe.
MAT 9:24 Sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Itene ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a. O̠gbara o̠nyani̠ bho̠ na̠ omugh d̠o̠, i̠na na̠ a̠kod̠u a̠kod̠ua̠.” Sa̠ awa i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na.
MAT 9:25 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ze ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ a̠mutiom bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh agi̠ ka̠ a̠sibh agu̠o̠ o̠gbara o̠nyani̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠.
MAT 9:26 Sa̠ o̠du̠ abar onon asasaragi̠an d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh bho̠.
MAT 9:27 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠d̠igh erile bho̠, sa̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom ikpom a̠rid̠ien i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na, imulughu i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone i̠yar igbirigbir!”
MAT 9:28 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi otu bho̠, sa̠ a̠nwunom ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin oma̠ra̠ ma̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠gir abar onon ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Yii, Wa̠nwuna̠.”
MAT 9:29 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na a̠kula̠n a̠rid̠ien d̠awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Aro̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin agu̠o̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin od̠i bho̠.”
MAT 9:30 Sa̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa i̠kpagi̠na. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s anyagh ra̠to d̠awa ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ ko od̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠loghom.”
MAT 9:31 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ awa ibhin o̠du̠ ogir ilologia̠n ta̠ A̠zizo̠s i̠gba i̠sasaragi̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh obha̠.
MAT 9:32 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠d̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠, sa̠ ubhin o̠ni̠ ola̠ eru na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ emua̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na.
MAT 9:33 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ze ma̠ eru bho̠ asi̠ghe̠, sa̠ emua̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ake̠ ma̠ ofugh abar, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ ifugh ma̠a̠: “Abar ola̠ o̠ko̠no̠n ta̠ od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ Izre̠l.”
MAT 9:34 Ya̠a̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠: “I̠na na̠ a̠bhin a̠limon ta̠ eru na̠ a̠ze ma̠ a̠ruru.”
MAT 9:35 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ ibom re̠ma a̠ten i̠gbara re̠ma, atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ru̠gala d̠awa, sa̠ a̠b̠om okpokpo ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba irileghom bho̠, sa̠ a̠koko ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere rasu̠nwe̠r na̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ali̠gam a̠ruzu.
MAT 9:36 Obhel bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ igbirigbir awa id̠ighi i̠na. Ezin bho̠, ali̠gam a̠ruzu d̠awa na̠ ebuiy ka̠ e̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ na̠ e̠tabh awa, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ro̠nana ya̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ okponom.
MAT 9:37 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠: “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ed̠ia̠n ya̠ ob̠u bho̠ eb̠uiy, ya̠a̠, ogbo ogir bho̠ ib̠uiy d̠o̠.
MAT 9:38 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, isiseinye ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ib̠ua̠ bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ afi̠ri̠ma ma̠ ogbo ogir alo̠gho̠m d̠a̠ ogir ob̠u ed̠ia̠n d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAT 10:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kokod̠i d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ a̠limon ola̠ ebhin oze i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh o̠si̠ghe̠gi̠ na̠ okoko a̠d̠ien kerekere rasu̠nwe̠r na̠ kerekere a̠d̠ien ali̠gam a̠ruzu.
MAT 10:2 I̠nye̠n bha̠ a̠rid̠ien a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo ogir bho̠. O̠pu̠r bho̠ bha̠ Asai̠mo̠n, wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠pita̠ bho̠, na̠ Anduru umor d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ A̠zemsi o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Aze̠bidi na̠ Azo̠n umor d̠o̠yo̠,
MAT 10:3 A̠filip na̠ Abatolomio, Ato̠mo̠si̠ na̠ Amatiu ogun ma̠ otua̠ ebhugh bho̠, A̠zemsi o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Ali̠fi̠o̠s na̠ Atadi̠o̠s,
MAT 10:4 Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ A̠kenan bho̠, na̠ A̠zuda̠s o̠nyi̠ ta̠ I̠skari̠o̠t, wa̠ ra̠ a̠wol I̠na bho̠.
MAT 10:5 D̠iobh na̠ i̠wal i̠nye̠n bha̠ ya̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠limon sa̠ a̠du a̠mutiom bho̠. Kisa̠ i̠na a̠du awa a̠mutiom, i̠na a̠kikiom awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ ka̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Ibhebhia̠n bho̠, ka̠ od̠igh nyen d̠a̠ e̠ma Asameria̠.
MAT 10:6 Ya̠a̠ i̠gi̠e̠ ku̠ d̠a̠ ro̠nana ebhugh Izre̠l ya̠ na̠ ebhe bho̠.
MAT 10:7 I̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ ob̠om okpokpo ma̠a̠: ‘Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠tua̠n.’
MAT 10:8 Ikoko ma̠ ogbo asu̠nwe̠r, ib̠egione ma̠ imumugh a̠nwunom, i̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh, ize ma̠ a̠ruru ma̠ e̠si̠ghe̠gi̠. Inyin u̠te̠i̠ i̠kpo̠, inigha̠ nyen i̠kpo̠.
MAT 10:9 “O̠ni̠ ka̠ o̠b̠ar na̠ okpoki, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ka̠ o̠kpo̠a ma̠ o̠kara ikpoki d̠inyin,
MAT 10:10 a̠d̠igh e̠kpa e̠gi̠, bo̠d̠o̠ akapa onwegina̠, bo̠d̠o̠ agbaka bo̠d̠o̠ okpeti i̠ki̠ani̠. O̠ni̠ ogir bho̠ akpe̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n ogir d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 10:11 Ke̠ma ke̠ma ola̠ inyin ud̠igh, ipura̠ne ma̠ wa̠ a̠sora̠n d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ma̠ esul e̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ tu̠tu̠n inyin ta̠ o̠d̠u̠a.
MAT 10:12 Id̠ighe ma̠ ebheleguma̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu bho̠.
MAT 10:13 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu bho̠ a̠d̠ighom inyin, bha̠ ekima̠ d̠inyin a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu bho̠. Ya̠a̠ ku̠gba ma̠ awa id̠ighom d̠o̠ inyin, bha̠ ekima̠ d̠inyin a̠mula̠ aro̠ na̠ inyin.
MAT 10:14 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ o̠da d̠o̠ inyin a̠bhin, bo̠d̠o̠ na̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin, bha̠ ikpukpu ma̠ ibhugh d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠a a̠sike d̠inyin ma̠ esorogi d̠a̠ otu bho̠ bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ma̠ eten e̠d̠u̠a.
MAT 10:15 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠, ta̠ okpon igbirigbir Aso̠do̠m na̠ A̠gomora opu ma̠ e̠ma obha̠.
MAT 10:16 “Iloghome! Ami̠ na̠ a̠du inyin na̠ a̠mutiom na̠ a̠limon, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ro̠nana d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io i̠gagaman i̠nam. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, inwuna̠ ma̠ eloghom abar ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠karabh i̠di̠ar, ya̠a̠ ikima̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ rukur osege.
MAT 10:17 Iloghoma̠ne ma̠a̠; a̠nwunom ta̠ eb̠ologh inyin e̠gi̠o̠m d̠a̠ ri̠gada ase̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gu̠ro̠gh inyin d̠a̠ ru̠gala d̠awa.
MAT 10:18 Sa̠ ta̠ edin ami̠ ebhin inyin e̠gi̠o̠m Aru̠li̠le̠ma, na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rebhugh bho̠, sa̠ obha̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ onigha̠ awa, na̠ ogbo ya̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
MAT 10:19 Ya̠a̠ igiel ib̠eton inyin unigha̠ awa, o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan egboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gba o̠nu̠, bo̠d̠o̠ iya̠ o̠gba, ezin bho̠ ta̠ onigha̠ inyin onin obhel obha̠ ma̠ iya̠ o̠gba.
MAT 10:20 Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ ko ofugh d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin ta̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ d̠inyin agba.
MAT 10:21 Sa̠ umor ta̠ a̠wol umor ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ ogigh, sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ ta̠ a̠wol o̠nyi̠, sa̠ anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ ewia̠n ro̠we̠de̠ ma̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ awa.
MAT 10:22 Sa̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠din a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ alo̠gh inyin a̠d̠ien, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ne ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ten.
MAT 10:23 Sa̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ ogbikimeni inyin d̠a̠ odi e̠ma, bha̠ ighile ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n e̠ma. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, inyin ka̠ orue d̠o̠ orile d̠a̠ re̠ma Izre̠l e̠b̠e̠i̠, kisa̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠ru.
MAT 10:24 O̠ni̠ atu̠ghan na̠ opu d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ e̠bana opu d̠o̠ ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ i̠na bho̠.
MAT 10:25 A̠sora̠n o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan bho̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ ka̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ e̠bana bho̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ ka̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠. Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ na̠ obhelegi ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ ma̠ Abe̠lzibul, ere wa̠ ka̠ obhelegi d̠o̠ ma̠ eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ola̠ a̠gurom a̠pu ma̠ o̠ku̠a bho̠?
MAT 10:26 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ko oghil awa, ezin bho̠ abar ola̠ ukpegi ola̠ ko omite d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠ma bo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ola̠ odi d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ola̠ ko ologhom d̠o̠ bo̠.
MAT 10:27 Abar ola̠ ami̠ i̠gba inigha̠ inyin d̠a̠ azi̠m, bha̠ i̠gba ma̠ emutiom d̠a̠ e̠b̠alab̠al, sa̠ abar ola̠ ami̠ ibhobhola̠ inigha̠ inyin d̠a̠ a̠to, ib̠ome ma̠ okpokpo ma̠ e̠gba ma̠ e̠sasaragi̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ a̠rutu.
MAT 10:28 Ko oghil ogbo ya̠ na̠ egigh ipulupul ozu bho̠, ya̠a̠ ko orue d̠o̠ egigh eloghoma̠n ozu bho̠. Ya̠a̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, ighile ku ma̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠rue api̠e̠gi̠ ma̠ eloghoma̠n ozu bho̠, na̠ ipulupul ozu bho̠, d̠a̠ e̠banya bho̠.
MAT 10:29 Uwol d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠wal ro̠gi̠e̠ ta̠ egule ma̠ ape̠ni̠ ke̠re̠? Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, odi i̠se̠ na̠ omel d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠de ma̠ ola̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin ko ologhom d̠o̠.
MAT 10:30 Ya̠a̠, ikpo asi̠ghal e̠mu̠ d̠inyin bho̠ eka̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠loghom o̠nu̠ o̠wal bho̠.
MAT 10:31 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu; inyin ulei abar opu, ma̠ o̠lo̠gh ro̠gi̠e̠ ta̠ egule.
MAT 10:32 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ agba ami̠ a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠nwunom, obha̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ ta̠ agba ani̠ i̠na a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠misigh O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 10:33 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ aku̠a ami̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠nwunom, obha̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ ta̠ aku̠a ani̠ i̠na d̠a̠ a̠misigh O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.”
MAT 10:34 “O̠ni̠ ko o̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠a̠, ami̠ iru ra̠ omutiom ekima̠ onigha̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon, ya̠a̠ ami̠ ibhin alapogidia̠ru.
MAT 10:35 Ezin bho̠, ami̠ iru ma̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n, “ ‘O̠nyi̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠we̠de̠, sa̠ o̠nyani̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n onweni, sa̠ o̠yo̠go̠-o̠nyani̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠yo̠go̠-onweni,
MAT 10:36 sa̠ ogbo a̠ghisia̠n o̠ni̠ ta̠ e̠lo̠gh a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠ bho̠.’
MAT 10:37 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠tula̠n onweni bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ a̠pu ami̠, na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠ami̠. Sa̠ ola̠ a̠tula̠n o̠nyani̠ o̠nyi̠ bo̠d̠o̠ olobhiri o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠pu ami̠ eka̠, na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠ami̠.
MAT 10:38 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ orol d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren d̠o̠yo̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠, o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠ami̠.
MAT 10:39 O̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠kighom a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ atu̠n ami̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um.”
MAT 10:40 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ ada inyin a̠bhin, bha̠ ada ami̠ a̠bhin. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ada ami̠ a̠bhin, ada ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ruom ami̠ bho̠ a̠bhin nyen.
MAT 10:41 O̠ni̠ ola̠ ada ma̠ owil a̠bhin d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ owil bho̠, ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠d̠ien amu̠kpe̠ ya̠ owil na̠ ate̠i̠ bho̠. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ada ma̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ bho̠, ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠d̠ien amu̠kpe̠ ya̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ na̠ ate̠i̠ bho̠.
MAT 10:42 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠ami̠ wa̠ aki̠r a̠pu bho̠ eka̠ ma̠ okpa̠ko eb̠ob̠okum amu̠m, ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAT 11:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠kikiom d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ awe̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠, ka̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma ya̠ itua̠n bho̠.
MAT 11:2 Igiel bho̠ Azo̠n aro̠ d̠a̠ ikoli amu̠gho̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ Akrai̠st na̠ a̠gir bho̠, sa̠ a̠ruom ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠,
MAT 11:3 ka̠ opura̠n o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Anwa o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠ ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ i̠yar ogon opa̠n o̠ni̠?”
MAT 11:4 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ Azo̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh bho̠, sekina̠ ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠.
MAT 11:5 Ogbo ya̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠, na̠ e̠bi̠gh esi, a̠rukula̠ bho̠ na̠ erile, ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh bho̠ na̠ okoko o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠, remua̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n abar, imumugh a̠nwunom na̠ ob̠egion, sa̠ na̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠.
MAT 11:6 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ o̠tu̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ rogir ya̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠gir bho̠ a̠ghel ami̠.”
MAT 11:7 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ o̠gba i̠di̠ar ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ Azo̠n owurma̠mu̠m bho̠ onigha̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Inyin u̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠, ka̠ inyin u̠ru̠ru̠an o̠bi̠gh ere? Ikpoko ya̠ na̠ eduka̠ d̠a̠ o̠fe̠gu̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 11:8 Ku̠gba ma o̠ku̠a d̠o̠, ka̠ inyin u̠ru̠ru̠an ka̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bura̠ ma̠ ibura̠ e̠no̠gho̠man ke̠re̠? Iloghome ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ebura̠ ma̠ ibura̠ e̠no̠gho̠man, na̠ erugh d̠a̠ rogigo Aru̠li̠le̠ma!
MAT 11:9 Ya̠a̠, inyin u̠tu̠n ka̠ o̠bi̠gh ere o̠gi̠? Owil ke̠re̠? Yii, owil ga̠i, ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠pu ma̠ owil.
MAT 11:10 Onon o̠ni̠ wa̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ruom o̠ni̠ a̠duom d̠ami̠ ma̠ od̠ia̠ o̠gi̠ kisa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠ru, ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man eten d̠oyom ob̠a̠ra̠.’
MAT 11:11 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ anwani̠ i̠maragi̠ bho̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ma̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ ta̠ omite d̠o̠; ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ aki̠r a̠pu d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny bho̠, abu̠gh a̠pu i̠na.”
MAT 11:12 Ob̠eton d̠a̠ amu̠m ta̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ ra̠ o̠te̠i̠ i̠se̠n, irileghom ote̠nai̠ny na̠ asu̠ ma̠ onyen o̠kparakpar agu̠o̠, sa̠ i̠kparakpar a̠nwunom ku̠ku̠m na̠ ewia̠n na̠ e̠te̠i̠.
MAT 11:13 Kisa̠ Azo̠n ta̠ a̠ru, eb̠la̠ a̠riwil bho̠ ewa̠ sa̠ oloko bho̠ eka̠ agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ irileghom bho̠.
MAT 11:14 Sa̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ inyin ta̠ o̠da ma̠ asu̠gbagba d̠ami̠ obhin, bha̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, i̠na I̠lai̠za wa̠ a̠riwil bho̠ iwa̠ ma̠a̠ ta̠ a̠ru bho̠.
MAT 11:15 “Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to, anagha o!”
MAT 11:16 “I̠se̠n, ka̠ ta̠ obhin amu̠m onon atu̠o̠m ere? Awa od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny, ya̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ egbolom a̠b̠ua̠, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠kele ma̠ odi ma̠a̠:
MAT 11:17 “‘I̠yar upughe ma̠ od̠od̠ue onigha̠ inyin, ya̠a̠ inyin u̠ghe̠r d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠gba, I̠yar u̠mo̠r aso̠r ekulom, ya̠a̠ inyin u̠ku̠nu̠ d̠o̠.’
MAT 11:18 Azo̠n a̠ru bho̠, na̠ od̠e d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, na̠ o̠d̠a d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠min nyen, sa̠ inyin u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Eru na̠ ab̠am.’
MAT 11:19 O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ a̠ru bho̠, na̠ a̠d̠e na̠ ad̠a, sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠bi̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠d̠o̠gho̠d̠o̠gh na̠ o̠d̠a ma̠ a̠min onon, wa̠ na̠ a̠rologha̠n igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠.’ Yaa̠, od̠ighi i̠di̠ar o̠ni̠ na̠ eleriom eloghom abar o̠ni̠ bho̠.”
MAT 11:20 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ osugi re̠ma ya̠ i̠na a̠gir ibom ilologia̠n bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ otiba̠ra̠.
MAT 11:21 “Ekulom inyin a̠nwunom A̠kora̠zin! Ekulom inyin a̠nwunom Abe̠tsai̠da! Ezin bho̠, ilologia̠n ya̠ ugir unigha̠ inyin bho̠ ma̠ ugir onigha̠ ma̠ Ataya na̠ Asi̠do̠n nab̠o̠, awa ka̠ i̠lo̠gi̠an akapa i̠ku̠nu̠, sa̠ ka̠ ibhugha̠ ma̠ i̠ru̠ru̠ etiba̠ra̠ ka̠ ob̠om igiel.
MAT 11:22 O̠ku̠a eka̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ta̠ okpon igbirigbir Ataya na̠ Asi̠do̠n opu inyin d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠.
MAT 11:23 Ya̠a̠, inyin a̠nwunom Akapanu̠m, ta̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ke̠re̠? E̠nyi̠, ta̠ orobh inyin osoroni d̠a̠ ekud̠um a̠de imumugh bho̠. Ezin bho̠, ilologia̠n ya̠ ugir unigha̠ inyin bho̠, ma̠a̠ ugir d̠a̠ e̠ma Aso̠do̠m nab̠o̠, e̠ma bho̠ ka̠ i̠ro̠ ate̠i̠ a̠didon.
MAT 11:24 O̠ku̠a eka̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ta̠ okpon igbirigbir a̠nwunom Aso̠do̠m opu inyin d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠.”
MAT 11:25 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ ase̠bh anwa O̠we̠de̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠de. Ezin bho̠ anwa i̠wo̠gi̠o̠m i̠nye̠n iloghodi̠ar bho̠ sekina̠ iloghod̠ire bho̠, sa̠ anwa ileriom kuma̠ ogbo ya̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠d̠iar bho̠.
MAT 11:26 Ya̠ga̠i, a̠sora̠n O̠we̠de̠. Ezin bho̠, a̠d̠igh anwa ma̠ ologi ma̠ o̠to̠ oguri o̠ku̠a.
MAT 11:27 “O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar. O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠loghom O̠nyi̠ bho̠ bo̠, a̠ten O̠we̠de̠ bho̠. Obha̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠loghom O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, a̠ten O̠nyi̠ bho̠, na̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠ ato̠ ma̠ obhin O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ oleriom.
MAT 11:28 “Itue d̠ami̠, eb̠la̠ inyin ya̠ a̠ruzu na̠ edughogh, sa̠ a̠dol na̠ e̠ne̠mu̠o̠m bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin osira̠ epobh.
MAT 11:29 Ib̠etone ma̠ a̠dol d̠a̠ ami̠ ma̠ erol, ma̠ e̠tu̠ghan d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠, ezin bho̠ ami̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ ologi ekima̠ na̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi, sa̠ reloghoma̠n a̠ruzu d̠inyin ta̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ ekima̠.
MAT 11:30 Ezin bho̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m ami̠ ob̠ub̠ura̠n abar, sa̠ a̠dol d̠ami̠ a̠bhobhogh.”
MAT 12:1 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ ari̠si̠ i̠bu̠kpa ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠, ya̠a̠ o̠ko̠i̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ ob̠oghi itu i̠bu̠kpa bho̠ o̠kpi̠r od̠e.
MAT 12:2 Igiel bho̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠bi̠gh bho̠, sa̠ ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Bi̠ghe̠, ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom na̠ egir abar ola̠ oloko bho̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ogir d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh bho̠”
MAT 12:3 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ A̠devidi a̠gir igiel bho̠ o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠na sekina̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 12:4 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu akpu̠ru̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ abe̠re̠di̠ ya̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ i̠na, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ od̠e, ya̠ i̠ro̠ inigha̠ ma̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ku̠ku̠m bho̠.
MAT 12:5 Bo̠d̠o̠, inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ d̠a̠ oloko bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ rokur i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠pi̠o̠gho̠m A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠, ya̠a̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ awa esor oloko bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 12:6 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, abar ola̠ a̠pu ma̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n.
MAT 12:7 I̠se̠ ma̠ inyin uloghom ezin abar wa̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠: ‘Ami̠ iba̠ra̠ kuma̠ okpon igbirigbir, ya̠ i̠ko̠l d̠o̠,’ nab̠o̠, inyin ka̠ usobh d̠o̠ ma̠ ase̠ obhumeni ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ o̠pi̠o̠gho̠m d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAT 12:8 Ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠.”
MAT 12:9 A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ sa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ u̠gala A̠zu bho̠,
MAT 12:10 sa̠ abi̠gh o̠ni̠ ola̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ na̠ akpari̠an. Sa̠ awa ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “A̠sora̠n okoko o̠ni̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠ ke̠re̠?” Awa ipura̠n o̠ku̠a bo̠ka̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh e̠kal ola̠ obhin oler o̠yo̠.
MAT 12:11 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “A̠nyen o̠ni̠ inyin ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ o̠nana, sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ a̠mel a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ogugua̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ka̠ o̠gi̠o̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ka̠ a̠sibh a̠mutiom?
MAT 12:12 O̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ na̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar a̠pu ma̠ o̠nana ke̠re̠? O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, a̠sora̠n ogir ib̠eb̠i ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh.”
MAT 12:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Selegheni ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom.” Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠selegheni, sa̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ a̠bhon aro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ uwed̠i.
MAT 12:14 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a ka̠ i̠mimia̠n igboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogigh o̠yo̠.
MAT 12:15 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠loghoma̠n sa̠ ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m I̠na, sa̠ a̠koko ma̠ eb̠la̠ awa.
MAT 12:16 Sa̠ a̠kikiom awa ma̠a̠ od̠ighi̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ eloghom ya̠ igboloma̠ I̠na.
MAT 12:17 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ta̠ owil Azaya bho̠ ma̠a̠:
MAT 12:18 “Obha̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠ami̠ wa̠ ami̠ i̠so̠n bho̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ ami̠ itula̠n bho̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠bhonomeni ma̠ ologi d̠ami̠ bho̠; Ami̠ ta̠ alo̠gh E̠mu̠gh d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠sobh a̠ga̠i ase̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ rebhugh bho̠.
MAT 12:19 I̠na ko o̠b̠u̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠b̠e̠m, bo̠d̠o̠ omulughu izul, o̠ni̠ ko o̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ okoroko d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ reten bho̠.
MAT 12:20 I̠na ko onwinigi d̠o̠ ma̠ ikpoko ya̠ na̠ e̠nyu̠bhi̠an, sa̠ i̠na ko od̠imigi d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠tani̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ od̠im nyen, tu̠tu̠n i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ a̠sobh ase̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom.
MAT 12:21 Sa̠ rebhugh bho̠ ta̠ eb̠em ologi d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAT 12:22 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠ sa̠ idi a̠nwunom ibhin o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh na̠ anyo̠gho̠gh, ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ emua̠ ola̠ a̠rid̠ien na̠ eb̠omia̠n nyen, iruom i̠na. Sa̠ i̠na a̠koko ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ake̠ ma̠ ofugh abar, o̠bi̠gh esi.
MAT 12:23 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ na̠ epupura̠n ma̠a̠, “Onon ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi ke̠re̠?”
MAT 12:24 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ a̠bhin a̠limon ta̠ Abe̠lzibul, we̠mu̠ a̠ruru bho̠ na̠ a̠ze ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh.”
MAT 12:25 Ya̠a̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠loghom i̠ru̠ru̠an d̠awa bho̠, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ola̠ aru̠gi̠an na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ ago̠gu̠an a̠mel, sa̠ e̠ma bo̠d̠o̠ eghun otu ola̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ko o̠mara d̠o̠ gigiribh.
MAT 12:26 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ Eru bho̠ na̠ a̠ze ma̠ Eru bho̠ na̠ asi̠ghe̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ aru̠gi̠an! O̠ku̠a ka̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ amara gigiribh?
MAT 12:27 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠limon ta̠ Abe̠lzibul na̠ a̠ze ma̠ a̠ruru na̠ asi̠ghe̠gi̠, ka̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠inyin na̠ e̠bhin ere na̠ eze na̠ e̠si̠ghe̠gi̠? D̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, awa ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ isobhmase̠ d̠inyin.
MAT 12:28 Ya̠a̠, agu̠o̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin E̠mu̠gh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ze ma̠ a̠ruru na̠ asi̠ghe̠gi̠ bho̠, bha̠ iloghome ma̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ inyin.
MAT 12:29 “Bo̠d̠o̠, ka̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu omomona̠n ka̠ a̠ghumi ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠, a̠sigimeni ka̠ na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ abhad̠i̠ ma̠ omomona̠n bho̠, i̠se̠ kisa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue amar afo̠i̠ny otu omomona̠n bho̠.
MAT 12:30 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ri̠la d̠o̠ na̠ ami̠, na̠ a̠wia̠n ami̠; sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ na̠ ami̠ okokod̠ia̠n bho̠, na̠ asasaragi̠.
MAT 12:31 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠karabh ya̠ o̠ni̠ a̠gir na̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ ya̠ o̠ni̠ a̠fugh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠, ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man; ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, ko o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠.
MAT 12:32 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠, ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠na, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, ka̠ o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ i̠na, a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ amu̠m onon, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.
MAT 12:33 “Ku̠gba ma̠ anwa amar a̠koko ma̠ oriren ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠bhon, bha̠ itu oriren bho̠ obhon, ya̠a̠ ku̠gba ma̠ anwa na̠ amar d̠o̠ a̠koko ma̠ oriren bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠bhon, bha̠ itu oriren bho̠ ko obhon d̠o̠ nyen. Ezin bho̠ na̠ obhin otu bho̠ na̠ ologhom oriren bho̠.
MAT 12:34 Anwi̠i̠ny i̠bho̠ru̠bho̠ru̠ i̠karabh i̠di̠ar. Inyin ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠ ta̠ ed̠ighi eka̠ efugh ib̠eb̠i a̠fugh. Ezin bho̠, a̠d̠ien i̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠ni̠ a̠kokod̠i a̠muzoghod̠i d̠a̠ ologi bho̠, i̠ye̠ bha̠ iya̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠fugh bho̠.
MAT 12:35 O̠ni̠ wa̠ ob̠eb̠i ologi bho̠, na̠ a̠mutioghom ib̠eb̠i i̠di̠ar d̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i ya̠ a̠kpol d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠; sa̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠, na̠ a̠mutioghom i̠karabh i̠di̠ar d̠a̠ i̠karabh ya̠ a̠kpol d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
MAT 12:36 I̠se̠n, bha̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, kere kere a̠fugh i̠te̠i̠, ya̠ a̠nwunom ifugh bha̠ ta̠ obhin osobh ase̠ onigha̠ awa d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠.
MAT 12:37 Ezin bho̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien a̠fugh d̠oyom sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠bhin eyel ase̠, sa̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠fugh d̠oyom sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠bhin ebhum ase̠.”
MAT 12:38 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ idi i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠ ifugh inigha̠ I̠na ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni, i̠yar na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠bi̠gh elegh d̠a̠ ozu D̠oyom.”
MAT 12:39 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠: “Amu̠m i̠basi̠ ola̠ oghila̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ a̠puru ma̠ elegh; ya̠a̠ elegh ola̠ ta̠ oleriom i̠na bo̠, a̠ten elegh ta̠ owil A̠zona̠.
MAT 12:40 Onin agu̠o̠ wa̠ A̠zona̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ okurogh obom ena̠ ma̠ i̠sar etita̠n na̠ i̠sar a̠d̠ugula̠n bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ologi a̠de bho̠ ma̠ i̠sar etita̠n na̠ i̠sar a̠d̠ugula̠n.
MAT 12:41 D̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠, a̠nwunom A̠ninive ta̠ e̠mara e̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ ebhumeni ma̠ amu̠m onon; ezin bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n okpokpo ta̠ A̠zona̠, sa̠ itiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠awa. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ma̠ A̠zona̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n!
MAT 12:42 D̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠, O̠li̠la ani̠ebhom ebhugh Ase̠ba ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ agba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ ebhumeni ma̠ amu̠m onon; ezin bho̠, i̠na ad̠u̠a ma̠ esi egbeiny a̠ru ra̠ anagha ma̠ eloghom abar ta̠ Aso̠lo̠mo̠n. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ma̠ Aso̠lo̠mo̠n od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n!
MAT 12:43 “Igiel o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠, sa̠ na̠ ada na̠ agi̠ na̠ ada na̠ a̠ru ma̠ a̠risisi ya̠ aghi̠ghi̠ra ma̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh esi ola̠ a̠sora̠n od̠igh o̠ro̠. Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠a̠ na̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠,
MAT 12:44 sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ otu wa̠ ami̠ i̠d̠u̠a bho̠.’ Igiel i̠na a̠misi sa̠ abi̠gh ma̠a̠, otu bho̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bo̠, na̠ o̠mar ogber oselegi ma̠ i̠di̠ar,
MAT 12:45 i̠se̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin ipa̠n od̠ua̠l i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh ya̠ i̠bho̠ru̠ ipu i̠na ma̠ o̠b̠aragu̠ma o̠yo̠, sa̠ awa ta̠ ka̠ ed̠igh erugh d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠ bho̠. Sa̠ e̠do̠lo̠ghu̠ma o̠ni̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠gurom a̠pu ma̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠pu̠r igiel bho̠. Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ nyen d̠a̠ o̠karabh amu̠m onon.”
MAT 12:46 Agu̠o̠ i̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠fugh na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ onweni na̠ a̠rumor d̠o̠yo̠ iru ra̠ i̠mara d̠a̠ etire na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an o̠yo̠.
MAT 12:47 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Bi̠ghe̠, onweni d̠oyom na̠ a̠rumor d̠oyom na̠ e̠mara d̠a̠ etire na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠ghan ofugha̠n onyom.”
MAT 12:48 Sa̠ awo̠ran o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “A̠nyen oweni d̠ami̠, ya̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nyen a̠rumor d̠ami̠?”
MAT 12:49 Sa̠ i̠na a̠selegheni ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ atu̠o̠m ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Onweni d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠rumor d̠ami̠ bha̠ ogbo iya̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠.
MAT 12:50 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠to̠ ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠, bha̠ umor d̠ami̠, na̠ u̠marani̠ d̠ami̠, na̠ onweni d̠ami̠.”
MAT 13:1 D̠a̠ onin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mite d̠a̠ otu bho̠ agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ aka abadi̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:2 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom iko i̠na ikiton ma̠ ola̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠pel a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠mara d̠a̠ egbolom.
MAT 13:3 Sa̠ agba ma̠ a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar a̠nigha̠ awa d̠a̠ ra̠sidogh ma̠a̠: “I̠nagha o! Ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ ogbebh ed̠ia̠n.
MAT 13:4 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠kpo ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠ asar bho̠, sa̠ idi imel d̠a̠ eten, sa̠ i̠nu̠r bho̠ iru ra̠ ikpokpoiny id̠e i̠mado̠n.
MAT 13:5 Ya̠a̠ idi sa̠ imel d̠a̠ a̠de o̠gbe̠o̠ma, esi ola̠ o̠do̠gho̠l bho̠ okud̠um d̠o̠. Sa̠ i̠rabh epa̠ ma̠ o̠su̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠do̠gho̠l bho̠ okud̠um d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:6 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ ogogo a̠mite bho̠, sa̠ i̠nyu̠n i̠ghaghara d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ i̠ki̠ka o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:7 Sa̠ idi imel d̠a̠ e̠ku̠ko̠ ib̠ub̠ulom, sa̠ e̠ku̠ko̠ ib̠ub̠ulom bho̠ i̠su̠ ikpegiom ed̠ia̠n bho̠ i̠bhu̠ghu̠d̠i̠ i̠ze̠gi̠.
MAT 13:8 Sa̠ idi imel d̠a̠ ob̠eb̠i a̠de, sa̠ imum imuma̠ ya̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100) a̠bin, idi e̠rabharabh (60) a̠bin, sa̠ idi imum a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh (30) a̠bin i̠se̠.
MAT 13:9 Wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to, anagha o!”
MAT 13:10 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ anwa na̠ a̠rogha̠n a̠sidogh na̠ a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠?”
MAT 13:11 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ inyin bha̠ na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ologhom i̠di̠ar e̠wo̠gi̠na irileghom ote̠nai̠ny; ya̠a̠ unigha̠ ani̠ d̠o̠ awa.
MAT 13:12 I̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ o̠lo̠gho̠m o̠gbam, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠b̠utu, ya̠a̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, ta̠ o̠wo̠r nyen ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:13 Ami̠ idin o̠ku̠a na̠ a̠bhin a̠sidogh na̠ a̠fugha̠n awa: “Ezin bho̠ ta̠ ekpon, ya̠a̠ ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠. Awa ta̠ e̠nagha, ya̠a̠ awa ko o̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠ e̠mu̠gho̠nyan nyen.”
MAT 13:14 Sa̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom onigha̠ awa ma̠ iwowa̠ ta̠ Azaya ma̠a̠: “ ‘D̠a̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n bha̠ ta̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n sa̠ ko o̠mu̠gho̠nya̠n d̠o̠; d̠a̠ o̠bi̠gh bha̠ ta̠ e̠bi̠gh, ya̠a̠ ko olelegi d̠o̠.
MAT 13:15 Na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n; sa̠ na̠ ob̠ulugi ma̠ ra̠to d̠awa, sa̠ na̠ okpegi ma̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa, ma̠ ola̠ awa ibhin d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa e̠bi̠gh abar, sa̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠ na̠ ra̠to d̠awa, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ka̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ eloghoma̠n eten.’
MAT 13:16 Ya̠a̠, na̠ otutumeni inyin ogbo ya̠ a̠rid̠ien bho̠ na̠ e̠bi̠gh esi bho̠, sa̠ ra̠to bho̠ na̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠.
MAT 13:17 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠d̠izo a̠riwil na̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom e̠mar e̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠, na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠.
MAT 13:18 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠nagha ma̠ ezin a̠sidogh ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.
MAT 13:19 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ amu̠gho̠n a̠duom irileghom bho̠, sa̠ i̠na o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠, bha̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ ugbebh d̠a̠ ologi o̠ni̠ bho̠. I̠nye̠n bha̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ imel d̠a̠ eten bho̠.
MAT 13:20 Ya̠a̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ imel d̠a̠ a̠de o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠, bha̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba bho̠, sa̠ i̠da epa̠ ibhin d̠a̠ a̠libhon ologi.
MAT 13:21 Ya̠a̠ isi d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠ka iya̠ awa, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ ekud̠i obhel, sa̠ imel i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ igiel ali̠gam a̠ruzu bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ uponoma̠ awa d̠a̠ ebula̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠.
MAT 13:22 Sa̠ iya̠ imel d̠a̠ ed̠um ib̠ub̠ulom bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba bho̠, sa̠ i̠nyo̠gho̠nyo̠gh e̠mara̠nwunom na̠ e̠ralma ogbo e̠li̠la i̠vi̠mo̠m asu̠gbagba bho̠, sa̠ awa orue d̠o̠ ma̠ omum itu.
MAT 13:23 Ya̠a̠, ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ imel d̠a̠ ob̠eb̠i a̠de bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba bho̠ sa̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan bho̠, sa̠ imum itu ga̠i, idi i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100), sa̠ idi e̠rabharabh (60), sa̠ idi a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh (30) a̠bin i̠se̠, d̠a̠ ikpo ya̠ ubhin ugbebh bho̠.”
MAT 13:24 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh opa̠n a̠sidogh a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gbebh ib̠eb̠i ikpo ed̠ia̠n d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 13:25 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ekod̠u bho̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ agi̠ ka̠ alo̠gi̠o̠gho̠m ib̠utula d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io i̠bu̠kpa bho̠ sa̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a.
MAT 13:26 Sa̠ igiel i̠mu̠nu̠mu̠n i̠bu̠kpa bho̠ i̠rabh imite bho̠, sa̠ ib̠utula bho̠ eka̠ i̠rabh imite.
MAT 13:27 “Sa̠ aru̠bana bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ o̠si̠ bho̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, ‘We̠mu̠, wokuma̠ ugbebh ib̠eb̠i ikpo i̠bu̠kpa d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠oyom? O̠ku̠a ka̠ ib̠utula i̠wo̠l d̠a̠ a̠ken emite?’
MAT 13:28 “Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien a̠gir o̠ku̠a.’ “Sa̠ aru̠bana bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar o̠gi̠ ka̠ ob̠ugion o̠si̠ghe̠gi̠ ke̠re̠?’
MAT 13:29 “Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘E̠e̠nyi̠, bo̠ka̠ inyin u̠b̠aram na̠ i̠bu̠kpa bho̠ ob̠ugion na̠ ib̠utula bho̠.
MAT 13:30 Ima̠ra̠ i̠wal a̠yi e̠su̠ emum itu. Sa̠ d̠a̠ igiel ob̠u ed̠ia̠n bho̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠ruom ogbo ob̠u ed̠ia̠n bho̠, ma̠ ed̠ia̠ eb̠ugion ib̠utula bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ to okokod̠i o̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ o̠bhu̠gi̠ orobh. Ya̠a̠ ta̠ okokod̠i ma̠ i̠bu̠kpa bho̠ okpol d̠a̠ esi eko d̠ami̠.’ ”
MAT 13:31 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh opa̠n a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an ekpo amu̠stad ola̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin a̠gbebh d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 13:32 Eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na aki̠r a̠pu d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ikpo ya̠ na̠ ogbebh bho̠ eka̠, igiel na̠ asu̠ abu̠gh, bha̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ a̠mobobh na̠ e̠su̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠ten oriren, ma̠ ola̠ i̠nu̠r anyu̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ elo ma̠ a̠rutu d̠a̠ i̠gha bho̠.”
MAT 13:33 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh opa̠n a̠sidogh ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠nyi̠ki̠kara a̠yist ya̠ ani̠ebhom a̠bhin alo̠gh d̠a̠ o̠to̠ma̠ i̠sar-abafu̠ ed̠ia̠n ibhugh, sa̠ iwubhmeni ma̠ eb̠la̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.”
MAT 13:34 A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠sidogh a̠fugh eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠. Sa̠ bebina̠ abar ola̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ola̠ i̠na obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠sidogh a̠fugh na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
MAT 13:35 O̠ku̠a bho̠ i̠nye̠n imuzoghod̠iom abar wa̠ owil bho̠ a̠wa̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ ta̠ akpato̠n o̠nu̠ d̠ami̠ a̠rogh ra̠sidogh, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ agba ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na a̠mutiom, ka̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠.”
MAT 13:36 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠gbogion a̠kokod̠ia̠n bho̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na ifugh ma̠a̠, “Gba ma̠ ezin a̠sidogh ib̠utula ya̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ bho̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar.”
MAT 13:37 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠gbebh ib̠eb̠i ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠ bha̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠.
MAT 13:38 O̠si̠ bho̠ bha̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, ib̠eb̠i ikpo bho̠ bha̠ anwi̠i̠ny irileghom bho̠, ya̠a̠ ib̠utula bho̠ bha̠ anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:39 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien wa̠ a̠gbebh ib̠utula̠ bho̠ bha̠ eru bho̠. Ib̠ua̠ bho̠ bha̠ ekunuguma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ ogbo ob̠u bho̠ bha̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAT 13:40 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, agu̠o̠ ta̠ ob̠ugion ib̠utula bho̠ okokod̠i o̠bhu̠gi̠ bho̠, obha̠ bha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom.
MAT 13:41 O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠ruom itileduom d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠si̠ghe̠gi̠ d̠a̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠kpo̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠le̠ge̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ ogir i̠karabh bho̠, na̠ eb̠la̠ idighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠.
MAT 13:42 Sa̠ ta̠ erobhod̠i awa e̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠, d̠a̠ esi wa̠ ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠ od̠i bho̠.
MAT 13:43 Igiel obha̠, ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ e̠war agu̠o̠ ogogo bho̠ d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠awa. Wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ra̠to, amar anagha o!
MAT 13:44 “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an i̠di̠ar edim ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na d̠a̠ o̠si̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ agi̠ ka̠ abi̠gh, sa̠ a̠puta̠ awo̠gi̠. Sa̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ ibo bho̠, sa̠ ad̠u̠a ka̠ a̠wol eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhin a̠gho ma̠ egbolom o̠si̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:45 “O̠lo̠gho̠m i̠se̠, irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠ni̠ a̠b̠ua̠ ola̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a ma̠ esi na̠ a̠ten esi na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan ib̠eb̠i i̠b̠o̠lo̠.
MAT 13:46 Sa̠ ka̠ abi̠gh odi o̠b̠o̠lo̠ obom a̠b̠ua̠, sa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠wol eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhin a̠gho ma̠ o̠b̠o̠lo̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:47 “O̠lo̠gho̠m i̠se̠, irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠gbo̠ ola̠ usoroni d̠a̠ abadi̠ sa̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ina̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ isin.
MAT 13:48 Igiel bho̠ ina̠ bho̠ isin o̠gbo̠ bho̠ imuzo bho̠, sa̠ i̠ku̠mi̠ku̠ bho̠ ikpor o̠gbo̠ bho̠ ibhuneni d̠a̠ egbolom, sa̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de i̠so̠n ib̠eb̠i i̠na bho̠ i̠lo̠gi̠ d̠a̠ egunu, ya̠a̠ i̠karabh bho̠, sa̠ awa irobhod̠i.
MAT 13:49 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠. Itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ e̠so̠n id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ib̠eb̠i bho̠,
MAT 13:50 sa̠ ta̠ erobhodi awa e̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya bho̠, d̠a̠ esi wa̠ ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠ od̠i bho̠.
MAT 13:51 “Inyin o̠mu̠gho̠nyan eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Yii.”
MAT 13:52 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ola̠ ada ma̠ atu̠ghan irileghom ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ a̠bhin, bha̠ agu̠b̠an o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ a̠mutioghom imom na̠ igba̠iny i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na alo̠gi̠ a̠guri d̠a̠ igba̠ i̠d̠i̠ar edim d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.”
MAT 13:53 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rogh a̠sidogh i̠nye̠n awe̠le̠ bho̠.
MAT 13:54 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa d̠a̠ u̠gala d̠awa, ma̠ ola̠ awa ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠. Sa̠ awa na̠ epupura̠n ma̠a̠, “Eloghom abar onon na̠ a̠d̠ien ilologia̠n i̠nye̠n ka̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠ken eru?”
MAT 13:55 “Onon O̠nyi̠ ta̠ o̠du̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Oweni d̠o̠yo̠ ubhelegi d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠meri ke̠re̠? Sa̠ a̠rumor d̠o̠yo̠ bha̠ A̠zemsi na̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ na̠ Asai̠mo̠n na̠ A̠zud d̠o̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 13:56 Eb̠la̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠ na̠ i̠yar i̠se̠n ke̠re̠? O̠ku̠a ka̠ eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠ken eru?”
MAT 13:57 Sa̠ rologi d̠awa igurom d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠. Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ owil o̠tu̠o̠m abar d̠a̠ e̠ma d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ eghun otu wa̠ i̠na a̠mite bho̠.”
MAT 13:58 Ebula̠ agu̠o̠ awa od̠umom d̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ogir d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠izo ilologia̠n i̠se̠.
MAT 14:1 Igiel bho̠ E̠ro̠d we̠mu̠ irileghom odi agba ebhugh bho̠, amu̠gho̠n o̠du̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠,
MAT 14:2 sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Onon ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ Azo̠n Owurmamu̠m bho̠; i̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh! Obha̠ ezin bho̠ ra̠limon i̠nye̠n na̠ i̠kpasan i̠na bho̠.”
MAT 14:3 Ezin bho̠ E̠ro̠d a̠b̠ol Azo̠n, sa̠ adu̠o̠m d̠a̠ ikoli ma̠ ebula̠ E̠ro̠di̠as ani̠ ta̠ A̠filip umor d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 14:4 Ezin bho̠ Azo̠n a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠: “Na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ nyam ma̠ obhin E̠ro̠di̠as ani̠.”
MAT 14:5 Sa̠ E̠ro̠d abho̠ro̠gh ogigh Azo̠n, ya̠a̠ i̠na a̠ghil a̠nwunom bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa eloghom ma̠ Azo̠n owil.
MAT 14:6 D̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ e̠yal i̠mara ta̠ E̠ro̠d, sa̠ o̠nyani̠ ta̠ E̠ro̠di̠as aghe̠r d̠a̠ a̠misigh ogbo o̠d̠e̠ bho̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠igh ologi ma̠ E̠ro̠d.
MAT 14:7 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ E̠ro̠d a̠sibhigha̠ a̠gua̠n onigha̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ kere kere abar ola̠ ta̠ a̠puru i̠na.
MAT 14:8 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠pura̠n onweni d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠puru bho̠, sa̠ oweni d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ruom i̠na ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠gba onigha̠ E̠ro̠d ma̠a̠, “Nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n i̠se̠n e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n Owurmamu̠m bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠kpa imobh.”
MAT 14:9 Sa̠ o̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ a̠b̠ogina̠, ya̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠zo̠ bho̠ na̠ ogbo o̠d̠e̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom awa ma̠ onigha̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ i̠na a̠puru bho̠.
MAT 14:10 Sa̠ i̠na ato̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ osobh e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n d̠a̠ ologi ikoli bho̠.
MAT 14:11 Sa̠ awa irol e̠mu̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠kpa imobh ra̠ inigha̠ ma̠ o̠gbara o̠nyani̠ bho̠, sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ a̠bhin ka̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠.
