MAT 14:12 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Azo̠n i̠gi̠ ka̠ irol ekuna̠ bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a ka̠ id̠i, sa̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 14:13 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠n abar wa̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ Azo̠n bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ku̠ku̠m a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh sa̠ ad̠u̠a agi̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ aro̠ kukunum. Sa̠ agu̠o̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ re̠ma d̠awa i̠wo̠l ya̠ a̠wel i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAT 14:14 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠bhun d̠a̠ egbolom bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom sa̠ igbirigbir awa id̠ighi i̠na, sa̠ a̠koko ma̠ ogbo asu̠nwe̠r ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠.
MAT 14:15 Igiel bho̠ a̠d̠io na̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Onon esi ola̠ od̠i kukunum, ya̠a̠ obhel na̠ a̠ten. Ruome ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma bho̠ ka̠ eghoyogh ed̠ia̠n ya̠ awa ta̠ ed̠e.”
MAT 14:16 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ awa ma̠ o̠d̠u̠a. Inigha̠ awa ma̠ abar od̠e.”
MAT 14:17 Sa̠ i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar unwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar esi onon, a̠ten ogho ikpokpogh abre̠di̠ na̠ i̠wal ikpo ina̠.”
MAT 14:18 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ibhine ma̠ eru ma̠ i̠se̠n.”
MAT 14:19 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin ogho ikpokpogh abre̠di̠ bho̠ na̠ i̠wal ikpo ina̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠tutumeni ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠pupugion a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠ru̠gi̠ iinigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠.
MAT 14:20 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa id̠e, sa̠ ilegha̠n ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠, sa̠ ikokod̠i ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r ya̠ isughia̠n bho̠ imuzoghod̠i d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) a̠rukpuom.
MAT 14:21 Aro̠ ka̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala (5,000) ilobhiri a̠nwunom id̠e. U̠wal ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwani̠ na̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny ya̠ id̠e ani̠ bho̠.
MAT 14:22 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠nugi ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh ed̠ia̠ eb̠etina̠ na̠ i̠na i̠b̠e̠i̠y d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na ta̠ aro̠ a̠b̠a̠ra̠ tu̠tu̠n ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ oyeleghu o̠mado̠n.
MAT 14:23 Igiel bho̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ eyeleghu bho̠, sa̠ i̠na asi̠n d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu ka̠ a̠siseiny tu̠tu̠n a̠d̠io a̠kpegi, sa̠ i̠na ku̠ku̠m aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAT 14:24 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, oghugh bho̠ na̠ agi̠ ma̠ egbeiny d̠a̠ obodo bho̠, sa̠ opoka̠n amu̠m bho̠ na̠ a̠b̠oroghom awa, ezin bho̠ ogim bho̠ na̠ a̠gim na̠ adama awa.
MAT 14:25 Igiel bho̠ ate̠i̠ obhel ogir wa̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa.
MAT 14:26 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠bi̠gh agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m bho̠, sa̠ rologi d̠awa ikpoyogh, sa̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “Obha̠ e̠mu̠gh o,” sa̠ ikpo ma̠ izul d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠rugugu.
MAT 14:27 Ogbo na̠ onin, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠kpo̠ ma̠ ologi. O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu. Ami̠!”
MAT 14:28 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ku̠gba ma̠ anwa na̠ agu̠o̠ ga̠i, bha̠ ruome ami̠ ma̠ orile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m bho̠ oru d̠oyom.”
MAT 14:29 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Tue.” Sa̠ A̠pita̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠ a̠sor a̠rile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m bho̠ na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 14:30 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na abi̠gh e̠mi̠ ogim bho̠, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh i̠na, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ od̠in, sa̠ i̠na a̠mulughu a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, tenemeni ami̠.”
MAT 14:31 Ogbo na̠ onin, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠o̠m agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠sibh i̠na sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠, ologi d̠oyom na̠ a̠kpo ma̠ ere?”
MAT 14:32 Sa̠ i̠wal awa ipel id̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠, sa̠ ogim bho̠ a̠lia̠.
MAT 14:33 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠ ikpud̠ia̠n inigha̠ i̠na d̠a̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi, sa̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, anwa O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAT 14:34 Sa̠ awa i̠b̠e̠i̠ ka̠ isul d̠a̠ Age̠ne̠sare̠t.
MAT 14:35 Sa̠ a̠nwunom e̠ma bho̠ ilelegi i̠na, sa̠ iruom ka̠ obhinogh eb̠la̠ ogbo asu̠nwe̠r d̠a̠ eghighira̠ bho̠ oru d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 14:36 Sa̠ awa i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠ i̠na a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ ogbo asu̠nwe̠r bho̠ ma̠ okula̠n bebina̠ esi bho̠ u̠labh akapa d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ ikula̠n bho̠ id̠um i̠man.
MAT 15:1 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m i̠gi̠ ka̠ ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠,
MAT 15:2 “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ od̠ud̠ul ibom ro̠we̠de̠ bho̠? Awa ititila̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa kisa̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n!”
MAT 15:3 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠a̠, inyin eka̠ ka̠ inyin na̠ odin ere na̠ obhin d̠a̠ od̠ud̠ul d̠inyin na̠ okpon oloko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠?
MAT 15:4 Ezin bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom’sa̠ ‘O̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ta̠ ogigh.’
MAT 15:5 Ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, o̠kpe̠ bo̠ ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na ka̠ ibhin alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠ ma̠ iya̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAT 15:6 Sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ozuruna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠. O̠ku̠a bha̠ inyin na̠ ogbogion oloko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m ratu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin.
MAT 15:7 Inyin ibhelebhel! A̠sora̠n ga̠i ya̠ Azaya a̠wa̠ a̠gboloma̠ inyin bho̠ ma̠a̠,
MAT 15:8 “ ‘A̠nwunom i̠nye̠n na̠ ebhin aru̠nu̠ d̠awa na̠ ebuom ami̠, ya̠a̠ rologi d̠awa isigima̠ ami̠.
MAT 15:9 Awa na̠ e̠ko̠l ami̠ ma̠ obhubho i̠kpo̠, sa̠ na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ agu̠o̠ roloko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.’ ”
MAT 15:10 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kokod̠i ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠nagha, ma̠ e̠mu̠gho̠nyan o!
MAT 15:11 Abar wa̠ na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ d̠o̠, ma̠ wa̠ na̠ api̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ abar wa̠ na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ bho̠ na̠ api̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.”
MAT 15:12 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa a̠loghom ma̠a̠ rologi Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ egurom ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAT 15:13 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Kere kere oriren ola̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ogbebh d̠o̠, ta̠ ob̠uron.
MAT 15:14 I̠we̠le̠mane̠ awa, ogbo ya̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi na̠ erileghom ogbo ya̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi. Sa̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi a̠rileghom o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi, i̠wal awa ta̠ emel ed̠igh d̠a̠ ogugua̠.”
MAT 15:15 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Gba ma̠ ezin a̠sidogh onon asi̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar.”
MAT 15:16 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠se̠n eka̠ bha̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ nyen ke̠re̠?”
MAT 15:17 “Inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠a̠, kere kere abar ola̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ na̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ okurogh, sa̠ na̠ a̠tenegia̠n ati̠n ma̠ ola̠ na̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ orobh ke̠re̠?
MAT 15:18 Ya̠a̠, i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ na̠ emite bho̠, i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ekpo ologi bho̠ emite eru, i̠ye̠ bha̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAT 15:19 Ezin bho̠, d̠a̠ ekpo ologi bho̠, bha̠ esi i̠karabh i̠ru̠ru̠an ya̠ ogigh o̠ni̠, na̠ orile isorogi,od̠e e̠ma, ob̠igh a̠b̠igh, o̠gba onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠, o̠gba o̠ni̠ o̠pi̠e̠ na̠ emite na̠ eru bho̠.
MAT 15:20 I̠nye̠n bha̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠we̠le̠man otitila̠ agu̠o̠ kisa̠ od̠e ed̠ia̠n na̠ o̠pi̠e̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.”
MAT 15:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ agba Ataya na̠ Asi̠do̠n.
MAT 15:22 I̠se̠ sa̠ ani̠ ola̠ ebhugh A̠kenan a̠mite a̠ru ra̠ a̠leghe ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir! Eru na̠ ab̠am o̠nyani̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ o̠kparakpar agu̠o̠.”
MAT 15:23 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s na̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠ i̠na bebina̠ abar. Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ze i̠na ma̠ asi̠ghe̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠leghe na̠ atu̠o̠no̠m i̠yar.”
MAT 15:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ani̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Uruom d̠o̠ ami̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠n ipa̠n ogbo oru, ya̠a̠ uruom ami̠ ma̠ oru d̠a̠ ro̠nana ya̠ na̠ ebhe bho̠, d̠a̠ a̠nwunom Izre̠l.”
MAT 15:25 Sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n a̠nigha̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, lo̠ghe̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠.”
MAT 15:26 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ orobh ed̠ia̠n i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ onigha̠ a̠sib̠ogho.”
MAT 15:27 Sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ga̠i, Wa̠nwuna̠. Ya̠a̠, anwi̠i̠ny a̠sib̠ogho bho̠ eka̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ akpata od̠e ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ awa na̠ emeleghu bho̠.”
MAT 15:28 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ani̠ bho̠, alu̠bu̠gh ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom! A̠mite ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠gh bho̠.” Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠d̠um epa̠ d̠a̠ ogbo obhel obha̠.
MAT 15:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ aka abadi̠ Agalili sa̠ asi̠n d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de.
MAT 15:30 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom iru d̠o̠yo̠. Awa i̠b̠ar na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠ikighu ma̠ re̠gha, ogbo ikpom a̠rid̠ien, a̠rukula̠, remua̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere a̠d̠izo rasu̠nwe̠r ka̠ iguri d̠a̠ aka a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠koko awa.
MAT 15:31 Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ awa i̠bi̠gh bho̠. Remua̠ bho̠ na̠ efugh a̠fugh, ogbo ya̠ na̠ eb̠ogina̠ bho̠ na̠ okoko od̠umeni, sa̠ a̠rukula̠ bho̠ na̠ erile, sa̠ a̠nwunom ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠ na̠ e̠bi̠gh esi. Sa̠ awa itutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Izre̠l.
MAT 15:32 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kokod̠i ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Igbirigbir o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ed̠ighi ami̠. Ezin bho̠ onon oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ na̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ ami̠ sa̠ bebina̠ abar ola̠ ta̠ ed̠e bo̠. Ya̠a̠, ami̠ i̠bho̠ro̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ oruom awa ta̠ eyel o̠ko̠i̠, b̠o̠ka̠ awa i̠fu̠mu̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠.”
MAT 15:33 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ a̠ken ikpokpogh abre̠di̠ ya̠ ta̠ elei onigha̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n, d̠a̠ esi ola̠ od̠i kukunum o̠ko̠no̠n?”
MAT 15:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin unwuna̠ i̠ni̠ ikpokpogh abre̠di̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Od̠ua̠l ikpokpogh abre̠di̠, na̠ o̠nyi̠ki̠kara i̠gbara ikpo ina̠.”
MAT 15:35 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ awa e̠ro̠ ma̠a̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ a̠de.
MAT 15:36 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin od̠ua̠l ikpogh abre̠di̠ bho̠ na̠ ina̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ali̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠pupugion a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ ma̠ o̠ru̠gi̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠.
MAT 15:37 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa id̠e ilegha̠n, sa̠ ikpokpo ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r ya̠ isughia̠n bho̠ i̠lo̠gi̠ imuzoghod̠i ma̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rukpuom.
MAT 15:38 Ogbo ya̠ id̠e ma̠ abre̠di̠ bho̠, bha̠ d̠iobh o̠ni̠r (4,000) ilobhiri. U̠wal ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ranwani̠ na̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny.
MAT 15:39 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ oten oyeleghu, sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Amagadan.
MAT 16:1 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ Rasadusi bho̠ iru ra̠ o̠d̠a A̠zizo̠s okpon, sa̠ ipuru ma̠ i̠na a̠leriom awa ma̠ elegh d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 16:2 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Igiel o̠b̠u̠ghu̠bu̠gh bho̠ ab̠am agu̠o̠ ododo ma̠ a̠dule, sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘E̠mu̠ a̠d̠io bho̠ ta̠ a̠bhon.’
MAT 16:3 Ya̠a̠ ka̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ ab̠am agu̠o̠ ododo sa̠ ade̠bh ad̠i̠ro̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘E̠mu̠ a̠d̠io bho̠ ko obhon d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠didon.’ Inyin na̠ orue na̠ obhin o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ na̠ ologhom agu̠o̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠io bho̠ ta̠ aro̠, ya̠a̠ inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan elegh wa̠ robhel ekunuguma̠ bho̠.
MAT 16:4 Amu̠m i̠basi̠ ola̠ oghila̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ a̠puru ma̠ oleriom o̠yo̠ ma̠ elegh, ya̠a̠ elegh ola̠ ta̠ oleriom bo̠, a̠ten elegh ta̠ A̠zona̠.” Sa̠ i̠na awe̠le̠ awa a̠ten ad̠u̠a.
MAT 16:5 Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ na̠ i̠b̠e̠i̠y d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa iloghoma̠n ma̠a̠ awa na̠ eweletia̠n o̠b̠ar na̠ abre̠di̠ obhin o̠gi̠.
MAT 16:6 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kikiom awa ma̠a̠, “Ilelegi, ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ a̠yist ta̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ Rasadusi bho̠.”
MAT 16:7 Sa̠ awa ibhin a̠kikiom bho̠ id̠ighom d̠a̠ i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ i̠yar obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ abre̠di̠ oru bho̠.”
MAT 16:8 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠nyan abar wa̠ awa na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an bho̠, sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Inyin ogbo ya̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠! Inyin udin ere na̠ o̠ku̠anan na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ abre̠di̠ bho̠?
MAT 16:9 I̠se̠n eka̠ bha̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠, bo̠d̠o̠ inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an, ma̠ o̠nu̠ o̠wal a̠rukpuom i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r abre̠di̠ ya̠ ipel d̠a̠ ogho ikpokpogh abre̠di̠ ya̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala (5,000) a̠nwunom id̠e bho̠, ke̠re̠?
MAT 16:10 Bo̠d̠o̠ o̠nu̠ o̠wal a̠rukpuom ya̠ u̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ od̠ua̠l ikpokpogh abre̠di̠ ya̠ d̠iobh o̠ni̠r (4,000) a̠nwunom id̠e sa̠ ipel bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 16:11 Eka̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ ami̠ ifugh d̠o̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ abre̠di̠? Ya̠a̠ ikpona̠ ma̠ a̠yist Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ Rasadusi bho̠!”
MAT 16:12 I̠se̠ kisa̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠nyan ma̠a̠, i̠na na̠ ofugh d̠o̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ a̠yist abre̠di̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ta̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ Rasadusi bho̠.
MAT 16:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh A̠sizeria̠ d̠a̠ A̠filipai̠, sa̠ a̠pura̠n ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠nwunom na̠ e̠gba ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ka̠ a̠nyen?”
MAT 16:14 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Idi na̠ e̠gba ma̠ anwa Azo̠n Owurmamu̠m bho̠, ipa̠n sa̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ anwa I̠lai̠za, ipa̠n ogbo sa̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ anwa A̠zerimaya, bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ awa a̠riwil bho̠.”
MAT 16:15 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠ ami̠ ka̠ a̠nyen?”
MAT 16:16 Sa̠ Asai̠mo̠n A̠pita̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa Akrai̠st, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠.”
MAT 16:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “E̠b̠e̠l oyom Asai̠mo̠n, o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zona̠. Ipulupul na̠ asi̠ i̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na onon emutiom enigha̠ nyam, ya̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 16:18 Sa̠ ami̠ na̠ ka̠ ab̠aram na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, anwa A̠pita̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠lo ma̠ aso̠si̠ d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma onon, sa̠ ra̠limon a̠d̠ugh ko orue d̠o̠ e̠ne̠gi̠me̠ni̠ i̠na.
MAT 16:19 Ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ri̠sabi̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny, sa̠ kere kere abar ola̠ anwa i̠bhad̠i̠ d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠ na̠ o̠bhad̠i̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, sa̠ ola̠ anwa i̠ko̠gi̠o̠n d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠, na̠ o̠ko̠gi̠o̠n d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.”
MAT 16:20 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠ sa̠ i̠na aghaghana ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ma̠ awa o̠gba d̠o̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠na Akrai̠st bho̠.
MAT 16:21 Ob̠eton d̠a̠ igiel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ o̠gba o̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ inigha̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ akpe̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, ka̠ o̠bi̠gh a̠d̠izo ali̠gam a̠ruzu d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ikei bho̠, na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ ogbo-atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, sa̠ awa ta̠ egigh I̠na, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.
MAT 16:22 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠bhin i̠na a̠ten d̠a̠ aka, sa̠ a̠bhin o̠gagaman okoroko a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ko ofugh o̠ku̠a. A̠zib̠a̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ e̠tu̠tu̠! Abar ola̠ o̠ku̠a omutuma̠ d̠o̠ nyam!”
MAT 16:23 Sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ awo̠ran A̠pita̠ ma̠a̠, “Eru, tene d̠a̠ aman d̠ami̠! Anwa na̠ ad̠agi̠an ka̠ ami̠, ezin bho̠ anwa na̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠o̠m abar, ya̠a̠ ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠.”
MAT 16:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ e̠ral o̠tu̠o̠no̠m ami̠, a̠ghel ozu d̠o̠yo̠, a̠rol e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren d̠o̠yo̠, atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠.
MAT 16:25 O̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh otenemeni a̠ghud̠um e̠mara̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ atu̠n ami̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um e̠mara̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um.
MAT 16:26 Ya̠a̠ a̠kere asu̠o̠, wa̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ ka̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, a̠dinom a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠? Bo̠d̠o̠, ka̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ere aru̠r a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠?
MAT 16:27 Ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ a̠ru na̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠, seki̠na̠ itileduom d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ta̠ akpe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ ya̠ ilegha̠n ya̠ i̠na a̠gir bho̠.
MAT 16:28 “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, idi inyin ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠, ka̠ omugh d̠o̠ tu̠tu̠n ta̠ e̠bi̠gh eruoma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ d̠a̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAT 17:1 Odin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin A̠pita̠, na̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n umor d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠bhin awa a̠bhun d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu esi ola̠ awa ku̠ku̠m i̠ro̠.
MAT 17:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠nwegina̠ ma̠ ozu d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠awa, sa̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠ amu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogogo bho̠, sa̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ i̠war agu̠o̠ e̠b̠alab̠al.
MAT 17:3 Sa̠ A̠mozizi na̠ I̠lai̠za imite d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠awa na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an i̠na.
MAT 17:4 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ya̠ a̠bhon agu̠o̠ i̠yar od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠! Ku̠gba ma̠ ta̠ a̠sora̠n bha̠, d̠ighi ami̠ igim i̠sar a̠rutu akpu̠ru̠ ma̠ esi onon: odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ oyom, ya̠a̠ odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ A̠mozizi, sa̠ odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ I̠lai̠za.”
MAT 17:5 I̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠fugh, sa̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ a̠kpegiom awa. Sa̠ okoroko ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ a̠si a̠mite ma̠a̠, “Onon O̠nyi̠ etula̠n d̠ami̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠gir ya̠ na̠ ed̠igh ami̠ ma̠ ologi bho̠. I̠nagha i̠na!”
MAT 17:6 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n okoroko bho̠, sa̠ ibom a̠rugugu isibh awa, sa̠ imel ib̠obhia̠n.
MAT 17:7 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ru ra̠ a̠kula̠n awa a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ib̠egina̠, o̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu.”
MAT 17:8 Sa̠ awa ib̠egion ra̠misigh d̠awa, ya̠a̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ a̠ten i̠na A̠zizo̠s ku̠ku̠m.
MAT 17:9 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ esor d̠a̠ igu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s anyagh ra̠to d̠awa agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko o̠gba ma̠ aghi̠m bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, tu̠tu̠n O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh.”
MAT 17:10 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ i̠tu̠n ere na̠ e̠gba ma̠ I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠ru?”
MAT 17:11 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠ru ga̠i, sa̠ ta̠ atu̠ghu̠man eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar.
MAT 17:12 Ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ I̠lai̠za na̠ a̠ru a̠ten, ya̠a̠ a̠nwunom ilelegi d̠o̠ i̠na, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, awa irughom i̠na ma̠ iya̠ awa i̠to̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa. Obha̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n nyen O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ma̠ ogbika̠ d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa.”
MAT 17:13 I̠se̠ kisa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠na a̠fugh na̠ a̠gboloma̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠ ma̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠.
MAT 17:14 Sa̠ awa iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠ru d̠o̠yo̠ ra̠ a̠kpuluma̠n a̠nigha̠ i̠na.
MAT 17:15 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, kpone ma̠ igbirigbir o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ena̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠nyegi i̠na. A̠d̠izo robhel na̠ a̠robh i̠na na̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ anya, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m.
MAT 17:16 Sa̠ ami̠ ibhin i̠na iruom ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom, ya̠a̠ awa irue d̠o̠ ma̠ okoko o̠yo̠.”
MAT 17:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Sei, amu̠m ola̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠to̠, ya̠ na̠ erugh ado̠l i̠te̠i̠! Ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ na̠ inyin a̠bia̠ eka̠? Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ne ma̠ ado̠l d̠inyin ka̠ ate̠i̠ eka̠? Ibhine ma̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠ eruom ami̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n.”
MAT 17:18 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ab̠ab̠agi̠na ma̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠, sa̠ a̠mite ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyi̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠um epa̠ ma̠ onin obhel obha̠.
MAT 17:19 I̠se̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s d̠a̠ a̠d̠ukun ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar orue d̠o̠ ma̠ oze o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ o̠si̠ghe̠?”
MAT 17:20 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin bho̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin ta̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ agba ma̠a̠, ka̠ inyin u̠te̠i̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ ola̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ ekpo oriren amu̠stad sa̠ inyin ufugh unigha̠ ma̠ igu onon ma̠a̠, ‘B̠etina̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ebha̠,’ sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠. Abar ola̠ ta̠ akpar a̠pu inyin ogir ka̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.”
MAT 17:21 Ya̠a̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ a̠siseiny na̠ one o̠ko̠i̠ bo̠d̠o̠, ola̠ o̠ko̠no̠n ko orue d̠o̠ ad̠u̠a.
MAT 17:22 D̠a̠ igiel bho̠ awa inwe ikokod̠ia̠n d̠a̠ Agalili bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Na̠ a̠tua̠n igiel ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ob̠eton o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de a̠limon.
MAT 17:23 Sa̠ awa ta̠ egigh i̠na, sa̠ d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh.” Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ id̠igh ibom i̠ku̠nu̠.
MAT 17:24 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ awa id̠igh d̠a̠ Akapanu̠m bho̠, sa̠ igunmotua̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠pita̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin na̠ a̠tua̠gha̠n otua̠ okpoki i̠wal e̠mu̠ a̠d̠uma̠ ogir bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAT 17:25 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Yii,” i̠na na̠ akpe̠, ya̠a̠ igiel i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi otu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awalama a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Asai̠mo̠n, anwa i̠bi̠gh eka̠? Aru̠lala e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ esobh otua̠ na̠ enigha̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠awa ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ na̠ egun d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ risoloma̠?”
MAT 17:26 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ risoloma̠.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a sa̠ anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ id̠igh ani̠ d̠o̠.
MAT 17:27 Ya̠a̠, agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko o̠gamame̠ni̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ rologi d̠awa, bha̠ sore d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y ka̠ ato̠ri̠ ma̠ amu̠kpabh, sa̠ o̠pu̠r ena̠ wa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠kor bho̠, bha̠ b̠etone ma̠ akpato̠n o̠nu̠ bho̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ abi̠gh okpoki. Bhine ma̠ ka̠ a̠tua̠ ma̠ a̠bin d̠ami̠ na̠ ita̠ oyom.”
MAT 18:1 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iru ra̠ ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “A̠nyen o̠ni̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny bho̠?”
MAT 18:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ ra̠ amarame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa.
MAT 18:3 Sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ka̠ rologi d̠inyin onwegia̠n d̠o̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ita̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny, inyin ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 18:4 Ezin bho̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ aki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ onon, bha̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 18:5 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠d̠ighom o̠nyi̠ ola̠ o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠, bha̠ a̠d̠ighom ami̠.
MAT 18:6 “Ali̠gam ta̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠kpu̠o̠m o̠gbe̠o̠ma d̠a̠ orum bho̠ ud̠ineni d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io abadi̠, ta̠ a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ uta̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ odi okubh o̠nyi̠ d̠a̠ anwi̠i̠ny i̠nye̠n ya̠ ima̠ra̠ ami̠ bho̠ ma̠ omel od̠igh d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
MAT 18:7 Olo a̠leghe ma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom d̠a̠ ebula̠ rad̠agi̠an ya̠ na̠ ed̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom na̠ egir i̠karabh. Rad̠agi̠an ya̠ o̠ku̠a ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ omite, ya̠a̠ olo a̠leghe ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ad̠agi̠an ta̠ e̠wo̠l d̠o̠yo̠ emite bho̠!
MAT 18:8 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ agu̠o̠ bo̠d̠o̠ a̠wel d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam ogir i̠karabh, sobhe ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠robh. Anwa ma̠ obhin ekud̠i agu̠o̠, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠ro̠ ukula̠ ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠oyom bo̠d̠o̠ a̠sike d̠oyom olegha̠n, sa̠ ta̠ orobh anwa o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ anya wa̠ ko od̠im d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAT 18:9 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam ogir i̠karabh, poko ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠robh. Anwa ma̠ obhin onin ekpo a̠d̠ien od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ anwa ma̠ onwuna̠ i̠wal ikpo a̠rid̠ien, sa̠ ta̠ orobh anwa o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ogugua̠ anya.
MAT 18:10 “I̠bi̠ghe̠, o̠ni̠ ko okpon bebina̠ onin d̠a̠ ikubh anwi̠i̠ny i̠nye̠n egurumeni. Ezin bho̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠awa na̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ obhel d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 18:11 Ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ a̠ru ra̠ otenemeni ogbo ya̠ na̠ ebhe bho̠.
MAT 18:12 “Inyin u̠bi̠gh eka̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100) ro̠nana, sa̠ odi d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa a̠bhe, i̠na ka̠ o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ d̠iobh na̠ esugho (99) bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠rugugum bho̠, agi̠ ka̠ abho̠ro̠ghan wa̠ a̠bhe bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 18:13 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na abi̠gh, ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bo a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nana wa̠ a̠bhe bho̠ a̠pu ma̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ d̠iobh na̠ esugho (99) ya̠ obhe d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAT 18:14 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ od̠i, bo̠ d̠a̠ ologi O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ ma̠ odi o̠nyi̠ d̠a̠ ikubh anwi̠i̠ny i̠nye̠n omugh.
MAT 18:15 “Ku̠gba ma̠a̠, umor d̠oyom a̠d̠ighi nyam ma̠ i̠karabh, gi̠e̠ ka̠ agba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ esi ola̠ i̠wal inyin ku̠ku̠m od̠i. Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na anagha nyam, bha̠ anwa na̠ a̠mula̠ ate̠i̠ umor d̠oyom.
MAT 18:16 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ nyam, bha̠ barame̠ na̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ bo̠d̠o̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh ani̠. I̠wal bo̠d̠o̠ i̠sar ronyob̠a̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ na̠ e̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ iku.
MAT 18:17 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠, bha̠ gba d̠a̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n bho̠. Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠kikiom a̠kokod̠ia̠n bho̠ nyen, bha̠ ibhine i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ obhebhia̠n bo̠d̠o̠ ogun ma̠ otua̠ ebhugh.
MAT 18:18 “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, kerekere abar ola̠ u̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠, na̠ o̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, sa̠ kerekere abar ola̠ u̠ko̠gi̠o̠n d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠, na̠ o̠ko̠gi̠o̠n d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 18:19 “O̠lo̠gho̠m i̠se̠, ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠ inyin enwuna̠ ma̠ onin ologi d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠ egboloma̠ kerekere abar, O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ a̠muzughod̠iom a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ ya̠ ipuru bho̠.
MAT 18:20 Ezin bho̠, esi ola̠ i̠wal bo̠d̠o̠ i̠sar o̠ni̠ ibhin a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ ikokod̠ia̠n, ami̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa.”
MAT 18:21 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, i̠ni̠ igiel ya̠ ka̠ umor d̠ami̠ a̠d̠ighi ami̠ ma̠ i̠karabh sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠man a̠nigha̠ bho̠? Agu̠o̠ od̠ua̠l igiel ke̠re̠?”
MAT 18:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, od̠ua̠l (7) igiel d̠o̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, od̠ua̠l (7) igiel ta̠ e̠rabharabh na̠ d̠iobh (70).
MAT 18:23 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠li̠le̠ma ola̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ okpon o̠wal ikpoki ogir ta̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 18:24 Agu̠o̠ i̠na ake̠ na̠ a̠kpon bho̠, sa̠ ubhin o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠d̠igh i̠na ma̠ o̠mu̠gh a̠d̠usubh na̠ ogho o̠ni̠r (10,000) ami̠na.
MAT 18:25 Ya̠a̠, agu̠o̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠kpe̠ bho̠ sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠ruom ma̠ owol i̠na, na̠ ani̠ bho̠, na̠ anwi̠i̠ny bho̠, na̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠o̠yo̠ obhin o̠kpe̠.
MAT 18:26 “Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠mel a̠de a̠kpud̠ia̠n i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Kpone ami̠ igbirigbir ma̠ a̠ne ma̠ ekud̠i obhel, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam kerekere abar.’
MAT 18:27 Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠kpon igbirigbir ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠, sa̠ awe̠le̠man i̠na a̠gbogion o̠mu̠gh bho̠.
MAT 18:28 “Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu obha̠ ad̠u̠a sa̠ abi̠gh odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu ola̠ a̠d̠igh o̠mu̠gh i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠dusubh (100) a̠dinari̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠ghinigia̠n i̠na, adu̠ ma̠ e̠d̠o̠gh bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Kpe̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠mu̠gh ya̠ anwa na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠!’
MAT 18:29 “Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ na̠ i̠na na̠ ogir bho̠, a̠mel d̠a̠ a̠de ale̠gh i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Kpone ami̠ igbirigbir ma̠ a̠ne ma̠ ekud̠i obhel, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam kerekere abar.’
MAT 18:30 “Ya̠a̠, i̠na na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, a̠b̠ol i̠na ka̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ ikoli tu̠tu̠n akpe̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠mu̠gh bho̠.
MAT 18:31 Igiel bho̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu iyed̠i i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠kakanyi̠gha ma̠ ibom, sa̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠awa ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠.
MAT 18:32 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠lebh i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa obom o̠karabh ob̠a̠ra̠motu. Ami̠ i̠tu̠n agu̠o̠ anwa i̠le̠gh ami̠ bho̠ awe̠le̠man eb̠la̠ i̠mu̠gh d̠oyom.
MAT 18:33 Na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ nyam nyen okpon igbirigbir ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ na̠ anwa na̠ ogir bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ ikpon anwa ma̠ igbirigbir bho̠ ke̠re̠?’
MAT 18:34 Sa̠ ologi ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠ agam sa̠ a̠bhin i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ egbikimeni ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠, tu̠tu̠n ta̠ akpe̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠mu̠gh bho̠ amado̠n.
MAT 18:35 “Obha̠ agu̠o̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi nyen, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ inyin na̠ obhin d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ awe̠le̠man i̠karabh umor d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAT 19:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kunugiom atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ Agalili agi̠ d̠a̠ Azo̠dan agba ebhugh A̠zudia̠.
MAT 19:2 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na, sa̠ i̠na a̠koko awa ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAT 19:3 Sa̠ idi Rafarisi iru d̠o̠yo̠ ra̠ i̠d̠a i̠na ikpon ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ezin ola̠ a̠sora̠n o̠ni̠ ma̠ odin oze ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ od̠i ke̠re̠?”
MAT 19:4 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠a̠, uwa̠ ale̠m awa d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, ale̠m awa ma̠ o̠ya na̠ olobhiri ke̠re̠?
MAT 19:5 Sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, o̠ni̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ na̠ oweni d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ akpabhan ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠wal awa ta̠ eten onin ozu ku̠ku̠m?’
MAT 19:6 Sa̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ko onwuna̠ mu ma̠ ozu ola̠ o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ i̠wal awa, ya̠a̠ onin ozu ku̠ku̠m. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠di̠ar iya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ atu̠lo̠m a̠guri onin bho̠, o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n d̠o̠.”
MAT 19:7 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ku̠a ka̠ A̠mozizi a̠din ere agba ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ire ogbogina̠ ilom a̠bhin a̠ze i̠na.”
MAT 19:8 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “A̠mozizi a̠din rab̠agh e̠mu̠ d̠inyin a̠ma̠ra̠ inyin ozegi ranwani̠ d̠inyin. Ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠.
MAT 19:9 Ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gbogina̠ ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, a̠sigimeni d̠a̠ ebula̠ ari̠gi̠, sa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin opa̠n ani̠, bha̠ a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma.”
MAT 19:10 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ e̠do̠lo̠ghu̠ma ta̠ ani̠ na̠ owolom od̠i ma̠ o̠ko̠no̠n, sa̠ o̠we̠le̠man o̠walan ilom ta̠ a̠bhon a̠pu.”
MAT 19:11 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ko orue d̠o̠ ada ma̠ ikpo a̠fugh i̠nye̠n a̠bhin, ya̠a̠, ogbo ya̠ na̠ o̠to̠ onigha̠ bho̠ ku̠ku̠m.
MAT 19:12 Ezin bho̠, ugiri ma̠ idi ka̠ d̠a̠ okurogh onweni ma̠ o̠ro̠ ibhogha̠n ilobhiri kisa̠ u̠maragi̠, ya̠a̠ idi sa̠ a̠nwunom ibhoghi itenemeni ma̠ ibhogha̠n ilobhiri, idi sa̠ awa na̠ agu̠o̠ isibhom ozu iten ibhogha̠n ilobhiri d̠a̠ ebula̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny. O̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠rue ada ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠nye̠n a̠bhin bho̠, bha̠ ada a̠bhin!”
MAT 19:13 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ a̠nwunom ibhin i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny iru d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠gbam agu̠o̠ otutumeni, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ikigima̠ awa.
MAT 19:14 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ima̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ eru d̠ami̠, o̠ni̠ ko okigima̠ awa, ezin bho̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny aro̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa.”
MAT 19:15 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ agbam awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ awe̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh erile ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAT 19:16 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠-atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠gir a̠kere ob̠eb̠i abar ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠?”
MAT 19:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa i̠tu̠n ere na̠ a̠pura̠n ami̠ ma̠ ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i? A̠zib̠a̠ ku̠ku̠m ob̠eb̠i. Ya̠a̠, agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠, bha̠ koko ma̠ roloko bho̠.”
MAT 19:18 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Iken?” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “ Ko ogigh o̠ni̠, ko od̠e ma̠ e̠ma, ko ob̠igh a̠b̠igh, ko o̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠,
MAT 19:19 ‘zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom,’ ma̠ ‘a̠tula̠n o̠ni̠ wa̠ d̠a̠ aka d̠oyom ma̠ agu̠o̠ ozu d̠oyom.’”
MAT 19:20 Sa̠ okubh o̠ni̠ bho̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠koko ma̠ eb̠la̠ roloko i̠nye̠n. Abar wa̠ a̠sughonom ami̠ ma̠ ogir bho̠, ka̠ ere?”
MAT 19:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan obhon olegha̠n bho̠, gi̠e̠ ka̠ a̠wol eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠oyom ma̠ a̠bhin a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ ate̠i̠ e̠li̠la d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, ma̠ a̠ru ra̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠.”
MAT 19:22 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ okubh o̠ni̠ bho̠ amu̠gho̠n e̠kal onon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na aku̠ru̠ru̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a, ezin bho̠ i̠na obom o̠li̠la.
MAT 19:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ akpar ibom ma̠ o̠li̠la ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny!
MAT 19:24 Ami̠ na̠ abaram na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, e̠nam-a̠dol o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ oyol anu̠ga oten ta̠ a̠b̠ur a̠pu ma̠ o̠li̠la o̠ni̠ ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAT 19:25 Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ ma̠ ibom ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ a̠nyen ta̠ a̠rue ate̠i̠ itenemeni?”
MAT 19:26 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kimeni a̠kpon awa agba ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠, bho̠ onon ka̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠mite, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠, bha̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar eb̠ur.”
MAT 19:27 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Bi̠ghe̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠we̠le̠man eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠i̠yar na̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m anwa. Ere wa̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ bho̠?”
MAT 19:28 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m ami̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ omom amu̠m bho̠, ma̠ igiel O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ i̠kasi̠ a̠dila̠de isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, inyin eka̠ ta̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) ri̠kasi̠ erileghom d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) roghol Izre̠l.
MAT 19:29 Sa̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ awe̠le̠man eghunotu, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠rumor, bo̠d̠o̠ aru̠marani̠, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠, bo̠d̠o̠ onweni, bo̠d̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny, bo̠d̠o̠ ari̠si̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ ami̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ ate̠i̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100) o̠gbam, sa̠ ta̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠.
MAT 19:30 Ya̠a̠, a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠pu̠r i̠se̠n bho̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ u̠man, sa̠ a̠d̠izo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ u̠man i̠se̠n bho̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠pu̠r.
MAT 20:1 “Ta̠ obhin irileghom ote̠nai̠ny o̠tu̠o̠m o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei a̠grep, sa̠ a̠mite ma̠ ad̠i̠ro̠ ka̠ ako̠ ma̠ ogbo ogir agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ egir d̠a̠ a̠lei a̠grep d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 20:2 Sa̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠nyan na̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ ma̠ o̠kpe̠ o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ onin a̠dinari̠ ma̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ a̠lei d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 20:3 “Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ esugho obhel ma̠ asi̠ro̠, sa̠ abi̠gh ipa̠n a̠nwunom ka̠ i̠mara d̠a̠ egbolom a̠b̠ua̠ ya̠a̠ abar ogir bo̠.
MAT 20:4 Sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin eka̠ i̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠ sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠kpon ya̠ i̠kpe̠ akpe̠ inyin.’
MAT 20:5 Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ epa̠. “Sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal obhel na̠ d̠a̠ i̠sar obhel d̠a̠ etita̠n a̠gir onin agu̠o̠.
MAT 20:6 Sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ ogho obhel d̠a̠ a̠dule ka̠ ami̠nana ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ e̠mara, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ezin ka̠ ere ma̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ o̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠n eb̠la̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, ugir d̠o̠ abar?’
MAT 20:7 “Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhin i̠yar ogir bo̠.’ Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom awa ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin eka̠ i̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠.’
MAT 20:8 “Sa̠ agu̠o̠ a̠d̠io na̠ a̠gul bho̠, sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ a̠ruom we̠mu̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ ogbo od̠ighi bho̠ akpe̠gi̠ awa ma̠ ya̠ awa igir bho̠, sa̠ ake̠ d̠a̠ ya̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ akpe̠ ka̠ a̠kunugiom d̠a̠ i̠pu̠r bho̠.
MAT 20:9 “Sa̠ i̠na akpe̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ iru d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ onin obhel bho̠, o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ onin a̠dinari̠.
MAT 20:10 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ ib̠on iru bho̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ i̠na ta̠ o̠kpe̠ a̠wa opeleni ma̠ o̠ku̠a, ya̠a̠ u̠kpe̠ awa nyen o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ onin a̠dinari̠.
MAT 20:11 Awa i̠da ibhin, sa̠ i̠go̠ya inigha̠ ma̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠,
MAT 20:12 ma̠a̠, ‘I̠nye̠n ya̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ igir onin awa-obhel ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ u̠kpe̠ awa na̠ i̠yar onin agu̠o̠, ogbo ya̠ ugir etita̠n a̠d̠io ub̠ogina̠ bho̠ sa̠ u̠nu̠nu̠an e̠si̠so̠ ogogo bho̠.’
MAT 20:13 “Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran odi awa ma̠a̠, ‘A̠tologha̠n, o̠karabh ola̠ ami̠ d̠ighi nyam bo̠. U̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ akpe̠gi̠an onin a̠dinari̠ ke̠re̠?
MAT 20:14 Bhine ma̠ otoyom ma̠ ad̠u̠a, ami̠ i̠kpe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon wa̠ a̠ru ma̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ nyen.
MAT 20:15 Bo̠d̠o̠, na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ ami̠ ma̠ obhin ya̠ ologi d̠ami̠ ogir ogboloma̠ i̠di̠ar d̠ami̠ ke̠re̠? Bo̠d̠o̠, anwa na̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ obom ekpo a̠d̠ien na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ ya̠ ami̠ i̠ne̠ghe̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠?’
MAT 20:16 “Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠, iya̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ ta̠ eten i̠pu̠r, sa̠ i̠pu̠r bho̠ ta̠ eten iya̠ o̠gu̠man.”
MAT 20:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh erile ma̠ obhun o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, sa̠ a̠bhin d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ a̠d̠ukun, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠,
MAT 20:18 “I̠bi̠ghe̠, i̠yar na̠ obhun o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, sa̠ ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ sa̠ ta̠ esobh ase̠ omugh ebhumeni i̠na.
MAT 20:19 Ta̠ ob̠eton i̠na o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ibhebhia̠n bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ e̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gu̠ro̠gh i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ e̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren egigh, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠!”
MAT 20:20 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ onweni anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ Aze̠bidi a̠ru na̠ i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ ra̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n i̠na ma̠ opuru abar.
MAT 20:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa iru ra̠ opuru ere?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ma̠ra̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠, d̠a̠ irileghom d̠oyom, i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny d̠ami̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, odi d̠a̠ od̠iom, ya̠a̠ uwed̠i d̠a̠ ekiel d̠oyom.”
MAT 20:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ inyin na̠ a̠puru bho̠. Inyin ta̠ orue o̠d̠a ma̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ okpa̠ko wa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ o̠d̠a bho̠ ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar ta̠ orue.”
MAT 20:23 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠ga̠i, inyin ta̠ o̠d̠a d̠a̠ okpa̠ko d̠ami̠, ya̠a̠ o̠ro̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom d̠ami̠ na̠ d̠a̠ ekiel d̠ami̠, bo̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠ami̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠guri a̠sisa̠n bho̠.”
MAT 20:24 Igiel bho̠ d̠iobh iyed̠i i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gam inigha̠ ma̠ i̠wal a̠rumor bho̠.
MAT 20:25 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kokod̠i awa agba ma̠a̠, “Inyin ologhom ma̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erileghom ibhebhia̠n bho̠ na̠ eponoma̠ awa, sa̠ ibom a̠nwunom bho̠, bha̠ ya̠ awa i̠to̠ ya̠ iten.
MAT 20:26 Ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠bu̠gh d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin bho̠, aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠inyin.
MAT 20:27 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠inyin bho̠, aro̠ ma̠ e̠bana d̠inyin:
MAT 20:28 ma̠ agu̠o̠ bha̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ oru d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ ogir e̠bana onigha̠ i̠na bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na a̠ru ma̠ o̠ro̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu onigha̠ a̠nwunom na̠ onigha̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ obhin o̠ta a̠d̠izo ogbo.”
MAT 20:29 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ Aze̠riko bho̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAT 20:30 I̠wal a̠nwunom ikpom a̠rid̠ien i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ aka eten bho̠. Igiel bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠ten bho̠, sa̠ awa ikele ifugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone i̠yar igbirigbir!”
MAT 20:31 Ya̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠ghaghana awa, ma̠ awa e̠ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m. Ya̠a̠, awa i̠lo̠gh kuma̠ e̠mi̠ emulughu ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone i̠yar igbirigbir!”
MAT 20:32 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s amara, sa̠ a̠bhelegi awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan ami̠ ma̠ ogir ere onigha̠ inyin?”
MAT 20:33 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, i̠yar na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠bi̠gh abar.”
MAT 20:34 Sa̠ igbirigbir awa id̠ighi ma̠ A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ i̠na a̠kula̠n a̠rid̠ien d̠awa, sa̠ d̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ awa inwe i̠bi̠gh abar, sa̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAT 21:1 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ etua̠n A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠, sa̠ i̠gbari̠ d̠a̠ igu Roliv d̠a̠ e̠ma Abe̠tfagi̠. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom a̠duom i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 21:2 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma wa̠ a̠sumogha̠n inyin bho̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh okubh ado̠ki̠ ola̠ u̠kpu̠o̠m na̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠. I̠ko̠gi̠o̠ne̠ awa ma̠ ebhin eruom ami̠.
MAT 21:3 Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠pura̠n inyin abar, i̠wo̠rane̠ ma̠a̠, Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan orughom, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin.”
MAT 21:4 Eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n imite ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ omuzughod̠iom iwowa̠ ya̠ owil bho̠ a̠wa̠ bho̠, ma̠a̠:
MAT 21:5 “I̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ O̠nyani̠ ta̠ Azayo̠n ma̠a̠, ‘Kpone, O̠li̠le̠ma d̠oyom na̠ a̠ru d̠oyom, ti̠to̠i̠ny d̠a̠ anyu̠ ado̠ki̠, olobhiri o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠, e̠nam a̠dol.’ ”
MAT 21:6 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ igir agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom awa bho̠.
MAT 21:7 Sa̠ awa ibhin ado̠ki̠ bho̠ na̠ olobhiri o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠ iru, sa̠ ibhin rakapa d̠awa i̠de̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ rado̠ki̠ bho̠, ma̠ A̠zizo̠s od̠igh orile.
MAT 21:8 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠de̠de̠gi̠ ma̠ ibom rakapa d̠awa d̠a̠ eten bho̠, sa̠ ipa̠n a̠nwunom isobhi ma̠ igologo a̠d̠e ibhin i̠de̠de̠gi̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠.
MAT 21:9 Sa̠ ro̠lo̠gh ogele i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ na̠ d̠a̠ aman d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ imulughu ma̠a̠, “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̱ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi!” “E̠no̠gho̠man na̠ e̠te̠i̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.” “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, wa̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ a̠pu bho̠!”
MAT 21:10 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, sa̠ eb̠la̠ e̠ma bho̠ na̠ a̠nye̠ge̠re̠, sa̠ na̠ epura̠n ma̠a̠, “Onon ka̠ a̠nyen?”
MAT 21:11 Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Onon owil A̠zizo̠s, wa̠ Anazare̠t d̠a̠ Agalili bho̠.”
MAT 21:12 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠zegi ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eb̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠b̠ua̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠kpululeni ma̠ rakpata ogbo ya̠ na̠ enwegi ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ na̠ i̠kasi̠ ta̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ewod̠i ma̠ ukpugh osege bho̠.
MAT 21:13 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri ma̠a̠, ‘Otu d̠ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ otu a̠siseiny,’ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ otenemeni ma̠ ‘E̠fe̠m aru̠gba.’”
MAT 21:14 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien na̠ a̠rukula̠ bho̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠koko awa.
MAT 21:15 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ roloko bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ilologia̠n ya̠ na̠ emite bho̠, na̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ na̠ emulughu d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠a̠, “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̱ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi,” sa̠ rologi d̠awa igurom.
MAT 21:16 Sa̠ awa ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ amu̠gho̠n ya̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ efugh bho̠ ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Yii, inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠a̠, “ ‘D̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ e̠mam, bha̠ esi itutumeni d̠oyom na̠ e̠d̠u̠a na̠ eru’?”
MAT 21:17 Sa̠ i̠na awe̠le̠ awa ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠tani̠ ka̠ a̠kod̠u ab̠al.
MAT 21:18 Ad̠i̠ro̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠mula̠ na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ na̠ o̠ko̠i̠.
MAT 21:19 Sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh oriren a̠fig ola̠ a̠tua̠n eten bho̠, sa̠ a̠rile ka̠ ate̠i̠ bha̠ na̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ abar d̠a̠ eb̠o, a̠ten ra̠to ku̠ku̠m. Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Otu omite mu d̠oyom tu̠tu̠n ka̠ id̠ud̠ul!” Sa̠ oriren a̠fig bho̠ aghi̠ghi̠ra epa̠.
MAT 21:20 Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠bi̠gh bho̠, sa̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Eka̠ ma̠ ola̠ oriren a̠fig bho̠ aghi̠ghi̠ra epa̠ ma̠ ogbo na̠ onin bho̠?”
MAT 21:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ka̠ inyin unwuna̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ ola̠ o̠gba d̠o̠ i̠wal, inyin ko ogir d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ ugir ugboloma̠ ma̠ a̠fig bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, ya̠a̠ ka̠ inyin ufugh unigha̠ ma̱ igu onon eka̠, ma̠a̠, ‘B̠etina̠ ka̠ a̠mel d̠a̠ abadi̠,’ sa̠ ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
MAT 21:22 Sa̠ kerekere abar ola̠ inyin ubhin d̠a̠ a̠siseiny upuru, sa̠ inyin uma̠ra̠, bha̠ inyin ta̠ o̠te̠i̠.”
MAT 21:23 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei a̠nwunom bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠kere a̠limon wa̠ anwa na̠ a̠bhin na̠ a̠gir i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ a̠nyen a̠nigha̠ nyam a̠limon onon bho̠?”
MAT 21:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ opura̠n inyin ipura̠n nyen. Ku̠gba ma̠ inyin o̠wo̠ran ami̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ agba a̠nigha̠ inyin nyen a̠d̠ien a̠limon wa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠.
MAT 21:25 Owura̠ amu̠m ta̠ Azo̠n ka̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠ken a̠ru? D̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠?” Sa̠ awa ibhin id̠igh d̠a̠ i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ifugh ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ i̠yar u̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘D̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny,’ sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ku̠a ka̠, ezin ka̠ ere wa̠ i̠yar oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ i̠na bho̠?’
MAT 21:26 Ya̠a̠ ka̠ i̠yar u̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠,’ ya̠a̠ i̠yar na̠ oghil a̠nwunom bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa ibhin ma̠ Azo̠n owil.”
MAT 21:27 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “I̠yar uloghom d̠o̠.” Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ko o̠gba d̠o̠ nyen a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠d̠ien a̠limon wa̠ Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠.
MAT 21:28 “Inyin u̠bi̠gh ani̠ eka̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ odi o̠ni̠. Odi o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny, sa̠ a̠ruom o̠pu̠r o̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠ ka̠ a̠gir a̠didon.’
MAT 21:29 “Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠,’ ya̠a̠ a̠tepa̠, sa̠ a̠nwe ma̠ ologi agi̠.
MAT 21:30 “Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ bho̠ ate̠i̠ uwed̠i agba ma̠ onin agu̠o̠. Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ a̠ma̠ra̠,’ ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠gi̠ d̠o̠.
MAT 21:31 “Oken d̠a̠ i̠wal awa a̠gir i̠to̠ ta̠ o̠we̠de̠ bho̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠pu̠r bho̠.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, rogunma̠otua̠ bho̠ na̠ id̠eme̠ma bho̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠inyin ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAT 21:32 Ezin bho̠ Azo̠n a̠ru ra̠ oleriom inyin agu̠o̠ orugh a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠, ya̠a̠ inyin uma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ i̠na. Ya̠a̠ rogunma̠otua̠ bho̠ na̠ id̠eme̠ma bho̠ ema̠ra̠ i̠na. Sa̠ eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ inyin u̠bi̠gh ya̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠ itiba̠ra̠ bho̠ eka̠, inyin uloghoma̠n d̠o̠ oma̠ra̠ i̠na otiba̠ra̠.
MAT 21:33 “I̠nagha ma̠ opa̠n a̠sidogh: O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu aro̠, sa̠ a̠gbebhegh a̠grep d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ a̠ko a̠kiton a̠lei bho̠. Sa̠ a̠gbo ma̠ esi ola̠ o̠fi̠d̠igi̠ itu bho̠, sa̠ a̠lo ma̠ otu ipoiny. Sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ esi bho̠ ma̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei ma̠ o̠ko̠ orughom, sa̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠.
MAT 21:34 Ate̠i̠ obhel o̠ku̠ imuma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ikponom ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ka̠ obhin a̠bin imuma̠ bho̠.
MAT 21:35 “Sa̠ ikponom ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ikighom rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠mar id̠ul odi, sa̠ igigh opa̠n, sa̠ irobhod̠i ma̠ uwed̠i.
MAT 21:36 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠ruom ipa̠n rob̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ ib̠uiy ipu ma̠ i̠pu̠r bho̠. Sa̠ igir onin agu̠o̠ igboloma̠ awa.
MAT 21:37 D̠a̠ okunugiom, sa̠ a̠ruom o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ awa. Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ta̠ eghila̠n o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠.’
MAT 21:38 “Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ a̠gbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠, sa̠ imimia̠n ma̠a̠, ‘Onon uwa̠ ta̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ad̠i̠a bho̠, id̠ighi ta̠ ogigh i̠na, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠d̠i̠ar do̠yo̠ eten iyiyar.’
MAT 21:39 Sa̠ ikighom i̠na, inuoghom i̠na imutiom d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ igigh i̠na.”
MAT 21:40 “Igiel wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru, ta̠ a̠gir eka̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ikponom ma̠ a̠lei bho̠?”
MAT 21:41 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠na ta̠ amar a̠kunugi ma̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ma̠ ipa̠n i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei ya̠ ta̠ enigha̠ gha̠n i̠na ma̠ a̠bin imuma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ akpe̠ bho̠.”
MAT 21:42 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ikputu wa̠ ilo ma̠ a̠rutu ighel bho̠, na̠ a̠ten e̠ko̠ otu bho̠, Onon ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠mite, sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠i̠yar, sa̠ a̠bhon o̠bi̠gh’?
MAT 21:43 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ta̠ o̠wo̠r inyin irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ obhin onigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ta̠ emum ib̠eb̠i itu.
MAT 21:44 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠melema̠ ma̠ ikputu onon ta̠ a̠tutughud̠ia̠n, sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ i̠na a̠mel a̠bhum sa̠ i̠na ta̠ agbe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠tutughud̠i.”
MAT 21:45 Igiel bho̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n a̠sidogh d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ iloghoma̠n ma̠ a̠rogh a̠sidogh bho̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.
MAT 21:46 Sa̠ awa i̠ru̠ru̠an ob̠ol o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ ighil a̠nwunom bho̠, ezin bho̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ibhin ma̠ i̠na owil.
MAT 22:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s alo̠gho̠m opa̠n a̠sidogh a̠rogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠,
MAT 22:2 “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny agu̠b̠an o̠li̠le̠ma ola̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n o̠d̠e̠ erogh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 22:3 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ obhelegi eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ u̠tu̠n o̠d̠e̠ erogh ulebh bho̠, ya̠a̠ awa i̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ oru.
MAT 22:4 “Sa̠ i̠na a̠puta̠ a̠ruom ipa̠n rob̠a̠ra̠motu, agba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ulebh bho̠ ma̠a̠: I̠bi̠ghe̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n ed̠ia̠n bho̠ amado̠n. Na̠ ogigh rodughuna̠ na̠ rovi i̠nu̠m d̠ami̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ na̠ elegha̠n. Itue d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ erogh bho̠.’
MAT 22:5 “Ya̠a̠, awa ibhin d̠o̠ e̠tu̠o̠m abar, sa̠ iten i̠d̠u̠a; odi agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ uwed̠i agi̠ d̠a̠ esi a̠b̠ua̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 22:6 Sa̠ ipa̠n isibh rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠, irughom i̠te̠i̠ sa̠ i̠ze̠gi̠ awa.
MAT 22:7 Sa̠ ologi o̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ a̠gurom, sa̠ a̠ruom ogbo e̠gham d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ okunugi i̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠, na̠ o̠bhu̠gi̠ e̠ma d̠awa osoroni.
MAT 22:8 “Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘O̠d̠e̠ erogh bho̠ na̠ a̠lei, ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ ulebh bho̠ i̠bi̠gh ma̠ i̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ awa ma̠ oru.
MAT 22:9 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ reten bho̠, ma̠ elebh ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ inyin u̠manana ma̠ oru d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ erogh bho̠.’
MAT 22:10 Sa̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ imite i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ reten bho̠ ka̠ ikokod̠i ma̠ ogbo ya̠ awa i̠manana bho̠, a̠d̠igh i̠karabh na̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ imuzo d̠a̠ obom ogbo otu erogh bho̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ rakpata od̠e.
MAT 22:11 “Sa̠ o̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ a̠d̠igh okpon ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ rakpata od̠e bho̠, sa̠ abi̠gh o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠lagha d̠o̠ ma̠ ibura̠ erogh e̠yal bho̠.
MAT 22:12 Sa̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘A̠tologha̠n, anwa id̠ighi eka̠ a̠d̠igh esi onon, ma̠ ola̠ anwa onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ibura̠ e̠yal erogh bho̠?’ Ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ owuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ o̠wo̠ran.
MAT 22:13 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ o̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ a̠ruom rob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠bhad̠i̠ ma̠ a̠sike na̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ enuwoghom i̠na ka̠ ed̠ighom d̠a̠ obom azi̠m. I̠se̠ esi ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠ od̠i.’
MAT 22:14 “Ezin bho̠ ubhelegi ma̠ iya̠ ib̠uiy, ya̠a̠ ta̠ o̠so̠n o̠nyi̠ki̠kara a̠nwunom obhin.”
MAT 22:15 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a ka̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan agu̠o̠ obhin d̠a̠ asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠ o̠kpati̠ ob̠ol o̠yo̠.
MAT 22:16 Sa̠ awa iruom ogbo atu̠ghan d̠awa na̠ ita̠ E̠ro̠d ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ opura̠n ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠yar ologhom ma̠ anwa na̠ amar a̠rugh d̠a̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i, sa̠ anwa na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ eten ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ga̠i, anwa na̠ okpon d̠o̠ bebina̠ o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh, sa̠ anwa obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ imitia̠n o̠ni̠ atu̠o̠m abar.
MAT 22:17 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, anwa i̠bi̠gh eka̠? A̠sora̠n otua̠ otua̠-ebhugh onigha̠ A̠siza̠ ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠?”
MAT 22:18 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s abi̠gho̠m ipesi d̠awa sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Sa̠ ibhelebhel, ere wa̠ inyin na̠ o̠d̠agi̠an ami̠ bho̠?
MAT 22:19 Ileriome ami̠ ma̠ okpoki otua̠ bho̠.” Sa̠ awa imutiom a̠dinari̠.
MAT 22:20 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Onon ka̠ a̠misigh ta̠ a̠nyen, sa̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ a̠nyen?”
MAT 22:21 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠siza̠.” Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, inigha̠ ma̠ A̠siza̠ ma̠ ita̠ A̠siza̠, ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ita̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAT 22:22 Agu̠o̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ awa ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ i̠we̠le̠man i̠na iten i̠d̠u̠a.
MAT 22:23 D̠a̠ onin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, sa̠ Rasadusi bho̠, ogbo ya̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh odi bho̠, i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠,
MAT 22:24 “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, A̠mozizi agba ma̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠mugh ya̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠, umor bho̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ b̠o̠ka̠ amar o̠nyi̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na.
MAT 22:25 I̠se̠n bha̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor e̠ro̠ na̠ i̠yar, sa̠ o̠pu̠r bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠, sa̠ a̠mugh awe̠le̠man ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 22:26 Sa̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a ma̠ oleghemeni i̠wal bho̠ na̠ oleghemeni i̠sar bho̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ oleghemeni od̠ua̠l bho̠.
MAT 22:27 D̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠, sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ eka̠ a̠mugh.
MAT 22:28 O̠ku̠a ka̠, d̠a̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ ka̠ i̠na ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ani̠ ta̠ a̠nyen, ma̠ agu̠o̠ eb̠la̠ od̠ua̠l awa na̠ ebhin i̠na bho̠?”
MAT 22:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠ru̠an o̠pi̠e̠, ezin bho̠ inyin u̠mo̠gho̠yan d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, a̠d̠igh a̠limon ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAT 22:30 D̠a̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ o̠walan ilom bo̠, unigha̠nom d̠o̠ nyen anwi̠i̠nyan, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
MAT 22:31 Ya̠a̠, ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh imumugh bho̠, inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba a̠nigha̠ inyin bho̠ ma̠a̠,
MAT 22:32 ‘Ami̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Ebraham na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Azi̠ki̠ na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠ ke̠re̠’? I̠na A̠zib̠a̠ imumugh d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠.”
MAT 22:33 Igiel bho̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ ma̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
MAT 22:34 Igiel bha̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠kpegi ma̠ aru̠nu̠ Rasadusi bho̠, sa̠ awa ikokod̠ia̠n ani̠.
MAT 22:35 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, a̠pura̠n o̠d̠agi̠an o̠yo̠, ma̠a̠:
MAT 22:36 “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, oloko oken wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ oloko bho̠?”
MAT 22:37 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠: “ ‘Tula̠ne ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom na̠ eb̠la̠ ekpo ologi d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ eloghoma̠n ozu d̠oyom, na̠ ebla̠ ologi d̠oyom.’
MAT 22:38 Onon o̠pu̠r oloko bho̠ sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu bho̠.
MAT 22:39 Oleghemeni i̠wal bho̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠pu̠r bho̠: ‘Tula̠ne ma̠ o̠ni̠etua̠n d̠oyom ma̠ agu̠o̠ ozu d̠oyom.’
MAT 22:40 Eb̠la̠ roloko bho̠ na̠ a̠riwil bho̠, u̠ke̠ri̠ d̠a̠ i̠wal roloko i̠nye̠n.”
MAT 22:41 Igiel bho̠ Rafarisi bho̠ ikokod̠ia̠n bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠:
MAT 22:42 “Inyin na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an eka̠ na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st? I̠na ka̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ a̠nyen?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi.”
MAT 22:43 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠: “O̠ku̠a ka̠ ere wa̠ igiel E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠d̠igh A̠devidi bho̠ sa̠ a̠bhelegi I̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠’? Sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠,
MAT 22:44 “ ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠: “Ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ tu̠tu̠n ami̠ ta̠ a̠soroni ma̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom a̠tenemeni ma̠ okpokpolom o̠gbam a̠sike d̠oyom.” ’
MAT 22:45 Ku̠gba ma̠ A̠devidi a̠bhelegi i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠,’ ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠?”
MAT 22:46 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠rue ma̠ o̠wo̠ran o̠yo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ omula̠ opura̠n o̠yo̠ ma̠ abar na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, ob̠eton a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠.
MAT 23:1 Igiel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ogbo ogir d̠o̠yo̠,
MAT 23:2 ma̠a̠: “I̠tu̠ghe̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ i̠kasi̠ ta̠ A̠mozizi.
MAT 23:3 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, kerekere abar ola̠ awa iruom inyin, igire. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ko orugh agu̠o̠ awa, ezin bho̠, awa na̠ e̠gba ma̠ ipa̠n na̠ egir ipa̠n.
MAT 23:4 Awa na̠ e̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ ma̠ ra̠dol ya̠ i̠mu̠mo̠r ipu ma̠ a̠nwunom orol na̠ e̠gbam d̠a̠ ro̠kpalma a̠nwunom, ya̠a̠ awa ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ bebina̠ ad̠u̠nu̠ agu̠o̠ d̠awa ma̠ od̠igh orol.
MAT 23:5 “Eb̠la̠ ogir ya̠ awa na̠ egir bho̠, bha̠ na̠ egir agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ elelegi awa. Awa na̠ e̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ robhurugho o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ a̠siseiny d̠awa, sa̠ na̠ eweghemeni ma̠ i̠sabh akapa d̠awa.
MAT 23:6 Awa iba̠ra̠ ma̠ ri̠kasi̠ edim d̠a̠ rakpata o̠d̠e̠ na̠ ra̠dila̠de edim d̠a̠ a̠rutu u̠gala A̠zu,
MAT 23:7 sa̠ iba̠ra̠ ma̠ ipeleguma̠ itum d̠a̠ a̠risisi a̠b̠ua̠, na̠ a̠nwunom obhelegi awa ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.’
MAT 23:8 “Ya̠a̠, obhelegi d̠o̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.’ Onin o̠ni̠ ku̠ku̠m O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin, ya̠a̠ eb̠la̠ inyin a̠rumor.
MAT 23:9 Ko obhelegi ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, ‘O̠we̠de̠’ i̠se̠n a̠de onon. Ezin bho̠ inyin unwuna̠ ma̠ onin O̠we̠de̠ ku̠ku̠m, ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
MAT 23:10 Obhelegi d̠o̠ inyin ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ezin bho̠ Akrai̠st ku̠ku̠m bha̠ O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin.
MAT 23:11 O̠ni̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin bho̠, aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠inyin.
MAT 23:12 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ abu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ta̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ aki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ta̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
MAT 23:13 “Olo a̠leghe inyin i̠tu̠ghe̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠, Ribhelebhel! Ezi̠n bho̠, inyin na̠ ogugi ma̠ o̠nu̠ otu irileghom ote̠nai̠ny na̠ okigima̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠inyin bho̠. Inyin ud̠igh d̠o̠ sa̠ inyin na̠ okigima̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ od̠i̠gh bho̠ ma̠ od̠igh.
MAT 23:14 Olo a̠leghe inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ roloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠, Ribhelebhel! Inyin na̠ oponoma̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠ na̠ o̠wo̠ro̠gh i̠di̠ar, sa̠ inyin na̠ osiseiny iwewegh a̠siseiny b̠o̠ka̠ olelegi inyin. Ta̠ o̠gu̠r inyin agu̠o̠ i̠zagba ola̠ abu̠gh ibom.”
MAT 23:15 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠. Ribhelebhel! Inyin na̠ o̠d̠u̠a ma̠ esi na̠ oten esi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠te̠i̠ bebina̠ o̠ni̠, sa̠ ka̠ inyin na̠ o̠te̠i̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ omula̠ na̠ od̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ten o̠nyi̠ e̠banya ola̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh a̠pu inyin i̠wal igiel.
MAT 23:16 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin, ogbo ikpom a̠rid̠ien ya̠ na̠ erileghom ipa̠n ogbo! Inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aghad̠i̠an, bha̠ o̠kpe̠ bo̠. Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin a̠gol wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ aghad̠i̠an, bha̠ i̠na na̠ ako̠man.’
MAT 23:17 Rema̠! Ogbo ikpom a̠rid̠ien! Oken abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ i̠wal a̠yi: a̠gol bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠worogi ma̠ a̠gol bho̠?
MAT 23:18 Inyin na̠ o̠gba nyen ma̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin enwen alu̠kpe̠ bho̠ aghad̠i̠an, ma̠ o̠kpe̠ bo̠. Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin e̠ne̠ghe̠ wa̠ u̠gbam d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠ aghad̠i̠an bha̠ na̠ ako̠man.
MAT 23:19 Ogbo ikpom a̠rid̠ien, oken abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ i̠wal a̠yi: enigha̠ bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ enwen bho̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠worogi ma̠ enigha̠ bho̠?
MAT 23:20 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠bhin enwen bho̠ aghad̠i̠an bho̠, ab̠aram na̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ u̠gbam d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠ aghad̠i̠an.
MAT 23:21 Sa̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠bhin otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aghad̠i̠an bho̠, a̠bhin otu bho̠ na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ ologi bho̠ aghad̠i̠an.
MAT 23:22 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhin ote̠nai̠ny aghad̠i̠an, bha̠ a̠bhin a̠dila̠de irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ i̠na wa̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ i̠kasi̠ irileghom bho̠ aghad̠i̠an.
MAT 23:23 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠, Ribhelebhel! Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ obhin aghan-od̠od̠ua̠ na̠ u̠ki̠a na̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere i̠gho̠gho̠ a̠mubobh, na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ a̠bin d̠a̠ a̠d̠iobh atu̠gi̠, ya̠a̠ inyin ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ilei abar ipu d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ o̠tu̠o̠m abar. A̠ma̠rugh igielake̠, na̠ okpon igbirigbir, na̠ onwuna̠ ologi ima̠ra̠. Akpe̠ inyin ogir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ko o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ ogir i̠di̠ar iyed̠i nyen.
MAT 23:24 Ogbo ikpom a̠rid̠ien! Inyin na̠ omurugha̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠mi̠n e̠nam-a̠dol.
MAT 23:25 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠. Ribhelebhel! Ezin bho̠ inyin na̠ otitol aman okpa̠ko bho̠, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ ologi bho̠ bha̠ a̠ponoma̠, na̠ o̠ku̠ku̠, na̠ i̠karabh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar imuzo.
MAT 23:26 Rafarisi ikpom a̠rid̠ien! Id̠ia̠ ma̠ etitol eb̠la̠ ologi okpa̠ko bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ aman bho̠ eka̠ ta̠ ab̠ab̠ala.
MAT 23:27 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠. Ribhelebhel! Ezin bho̠ inyin u̠gu̠b̠an ranyu̠ od̠i ya̠ u̠mar u̠lo̠ sa̠ na̠ ekil d̠a̠ etire, sa̠ i̠gu̠b̠an ya̠ ibhon ibom d̠a̠ ologi. Ne̠ge̠ bha̠ i̠kpo̠kpo̠ imumugh a̠nwunom na̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere i̠gho̠ro̠gho̠r emuzo d̠a̠ ologi.
MAT 23:28 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ inyin eka̠ u̠gu̠b̠an ogbo ya̠ i̠b̠ab̠ala d̠a̠ anyu̠, sa̠ na̠ erugh a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠, ya̠a̠, ado̠l ibhelebhel na̠ a̠ma̠rugh i̠te̠i̠ imuzo d̠a̠ aghud̠um d̠inyin.
MAT 23:29 “Itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ inyin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠. Ribhelebhel! Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ ob̠olob̠ol ranyu̠od̠i a̠riwil bho̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ oburi ma̠ ranyu̠od̠i ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠.
MAT 23:30 Sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar umite d̠a̠ amu̠m igba̠iny ro̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar nab̠o̠, i̠yar ka̠ ud̠igh ani̠ d̠o̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠riwil bho̠.’
MAT 23:31 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, inyin agu̠o̠ ud̠igh onyob̠a̠ ebhum ase̠ d̠inyin, ma̠a̠, inyin anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠riwil bho̠.
MAT 23:32 Inyin eka̠ i̠gi̠o̠me̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, ma̠ emuzoghod̠iom ogir ya̠ igba̠iny ro̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin i̠ke̠ bho̠!
MAT 23:33 “I̠karabh i̠di̠ar! Anwi̠i̠ny i̠bho̠ru̠bho̠ru̠ i̠karabh i̠di̠ar! Inyin ta̠ od̠ighi eka̠ omiza̠n osobh ase̠ e̠ba anya bho̠?
MAT 23:34 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠ruom a̠riwil, na̠ iloghom ma̠ i̠di̠ar, na̠ ogbo i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ na̠ a̠ruom inyin. Inyin ta̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ idi awa, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠du̠gi̠ ma̠ idi o̠ze̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh idi d̠a̠ ru̠gala d̠inyin, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠d̠u̠a ma̠ e̠ma oten e̠ma ozegi awa.
MAT 23:35 D̠a̠ ebul o̠ku̠a, eb̠la̠ asi̠ ta̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom ya̠ uzu d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ d̠inyin, ob̠eton d̠a̠ asi̠ ta̠ ob̠eb̠i Ebe̠l ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ asi̠ ta̠ Azakaraya o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Abarakaya wa̠ igigh d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ enwen i̠ko̠l bho̠.
MAT 23:36 Ya̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite d̠a̠ amu̠m onon.
MAT 23:37 “A̠zeruse̠le̠m, A̠zeruse̠le̠m, anwa wa̠ na̠ aze̠ ma̠ a̠riwil bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠robhod̠i ma̠ ogbo ya̠ uruom oru d̠oyom bho̠. Ya̠a̠ i̠ni̠ igiel, ka̠ na̠ ebhir ami̠ ma̠ okokod̠i eb̠la̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠oyom oguri onin esi, ma̠ agu̠o̠ e̠nu̠r-e̠ma na̠ a̠bhin rapu̠ba d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠ghughuom anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ anwa na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠.
MAT 23:38 Ya̠ga̠i, na̠ o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ otu d̠oyom oguri ma̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠.
MAT 23:39 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ob̠eton i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, inyin ko o̠bi̠gh mu̠ ami̠ tu̠tu̠n inyin ta̠ ofugh ma̠a̠, ‘Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.’”
MAT 24:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠mite na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iru ra̠ i̠tu̠o̠gho̠m inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ eloma̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
MAT 24:2 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n? Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, ekpo ikputu ola̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ ta̠ opa̠n ola̠ ko ob̠ogion d̠o̠ bo̠.”
MAT 24:3 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ igu Roliv bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iru d̠o̠yo̠ ra̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “Gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, a̠kere obhel wa̠ i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite bho̠, na̠ ere wa̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ elegh eruoma̠ d̠oyom na̠ ekunuguma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠?”
MAT 24:4 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ko ogelemeni d̠o̠ inyin.
MAT 24:5 A̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhin a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ eru, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ Akrai̠st,’ sa̠ ta̠ egelemeni ma̠ a̠d̠izo ogbo.
MAT 24:6 Inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n i̠mu̠mu̠gho̠n re̠gham, o̠ni̠ okpa̠ra̠numa̠ d̠o̠. I̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠ku̠a ta̠ emite, ya̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ obhel bho̠ ta̠ olei d̠o̠.
MAT 24:7 Ebhugh ta̠ ewia̠n ebhugh, sa̠ irileghom ta̠ ewia̠n irileghom. Ibom ro̠ko̠i̠ ta̠ esor, sa̠ ra̠de ta̠ enyegia̠n eb̠omia̠n ekurubh, d̠a̠ a̠d̠izo a̠risi.
MAT 24:8 Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n kisa̠ ob̠eton ali̠gam a̠ruzu bho̠.
MAT 24:9 “Igiel o̠ku̠a, ta̠ ob̠eton inyin onigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ta̠ e̠ni̠ni̠gi̠o̠m inyin, sa̠ ta̠ egigh inyin, sa̠ eb̠la̠ ibhebhia̠n bho̠ ta̠ e̠lo̠gh inyin a̠d̠ien d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠.
MAT 24:10 Igiel o̠ku̠a, a̠d̠izo ogbo ta̠ emel e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠, sa̠ odi ta̠ a̠luom odi, sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠lo̠gi̠an a̠rid̠ien,
MAT 24:11 sa̠ a̠d̠izo a̠riwil igunugha̠ ta̠ emite egelemeni ma̠ a̠d̠izo ogbo.
MAT 24:12 Sa̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ a̠ma̠rugh i̠te̠i̠ ta̠ a̠kpegiom a̠nwunom bho̠, etula̠n ta̠ aki̠r d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠d̠izo ogbo.
MAT 24:13 Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ne ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ten.
MAT 24:14 Sa̠ ta̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba irileghom bho̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ta̠ amu̠gho̠n, sa̠ ekunuguma̠ obhel bho̠ ta̠ a̠lei.
MAT 24:15 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ka̠ abar ola̠ omitegha̠n d̠o̠ na̠ a̠mite amara d̠a̠ esi e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠d̠i̠ar na̠ e̠pi̠e̠gi̠an, ma̠ agu̠o̠ owil Adani̠e̠l a̠wa̠ bho̠ (o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠sen bho̠ amu̠gho̠nyan),
MAT 24:16 bha̠, ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠, eghil ebhun d̠a̠ rebhugh ya̠ i̠gi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ bho̠.
MAT 24:17 O̠ni̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu bho̠ osor d̠o̠ ka̠ a̠bhin abar d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 24:18 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ od̠ighi bho̠ omula̠ d̠o̠ ka̠ a̠bhin ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 24:19 Ya̠a̠ ekulom anwani̠ a̠rughun na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ enigha̠ ma̠ amu̠mam bho̠, d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠ye̠,
MAT 24:20 Isiseinye ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠inyin ko osora̠n d̠o̠ d̠a̠ obhel a̠d̠igho, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠.
MAT 24:21 Ezin bho̠, ka̠ a̠sora̠n d̠a̠ igiel ola̠ o̠ku̠a, ali̠gam a̠ruzu bho̠ ta̠ a̠peleni ka̠ ate̠i̠ esi ola̠, ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ abar ola̠ oku̠a ta̠ od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ a̠mite ma̠ obhin d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ ra̠ o̠te̠i̠ i̠se̠n, ya̠ ko omite mu nyen.
MAT 24:22 “Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠a̠, ukperemeni d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel bho̠, bebina̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠miza̠n a̠d̠um bo̠. Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ o̠so̠n bho̠, ta̠ okperemeni ma̠ obhel obha̠.
MAT 24:23 Igiel o̠ku̠a, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ‘Bi̠ghe̠, Akrai̠st od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n!’ Bo̠d̠o̠, ‘Od̠i ma̠ ebha̠!’ O̠ni̠ ko od̠umom.
MAT 24:24 Ra̠krai̠st igunugha̠ na̠ a̠riwil igunugha̠ ta̠ emite sa̠ ta̠ eleriom ibom relegh na̠ ogir ilologia̠n, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠b̠ur nab̠o̠, ka̠ igelemeni nyen ogbo ya̠ na̠ o̠so̠n bho̠.
MAT 24:25 I̠bi̠ghe̠! Ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ agba a̠nigha̠ inyin.
MAT 24:26 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ‘I̠bi̠ghe̠, od̠i d̠a̠ e̠ghana bho̠,’ ko o̠gi̠ ka̠ e̠bi̠ghan; bo̠d̠o̠, ‘I̠bi̠ghe̠, od̠i d̠a̠ e̠bhai̠, esi e̠wo̠gi̠na’ ko oma̠ra̠.
MAT 24:27 Ezin bho̠, agu̠o̠ i̠me̠me̠gi̠na agbararan, ka̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ opu omite ogogo bho̠, sa̠ na̠ awar na̠ a̠misi d̠a̠ osor ogogo bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ eruoma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠.
MAT 24:28 Kesikesi ola̠ e̠b̠u̠re̠ od̠i, obha̠ esi ro̠de̠le̠ bho̠ na̠ ekokod̠ia̠n bho̠.
MAT 24:29 “Ali̠gam a̠ruzu ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠n ma̠ oten ku̠ku̠m bha̠, “ ‘Ogogo bho̠ o̠zu̠, sa̠ uwetere bho̠ ko o̠mu̠ mu̠; re̠ni̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny emeleghu, sa̠ ra̠limon ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ re̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ enyegia̠n.’
MAT 24:30 “D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ elegh O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny, sa̠ eb̠la̠ rebhugh e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ ed̠igh i̠ku̠nu̠. Sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh ka̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠ugh ote̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠limon na̠ ibom isosorogia̠n.
MAT 24:31 Sa̠ ta̠ a̠ruom itileduom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ opughe od̠od̠ue obom oghur, sa̠ ta̠ ekokod̠i ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n d̠a̠ inya̠ re̠ku̠l bho̠, obeton d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ odi agba a̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ esumogha̠n bho̠.
MAT 24:32 “I̠tu̠ghane̠ ma̠ a̠sidogh oriren a̠fig bho̠: Igiel bha̠ i̠gha na̠ edugh na̠ a̠nwegina̠ ma̠ a̠to, bha̠ inyin ologhom ma̠ a̠kozogh na̠ a̠tua̠n.
MAT 24:33 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ od̠i nyen, igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, iloghome ma̠ obhel bho̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠a agu̠o̠, na̠ a̠misi d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ otu.
MAT 24:34 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, amu̠m onon ka̠ oten d̠o̠ a̠munia̠n kisa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite.
MAT 24:35 A̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny ta̠ eten e̠d̠u̠a, ya̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠ami̠ ko oten d̠o̠ e̠d̠u̠a.
MAT 24:36 “Ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ologhom a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠ na̠ obhel bho̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠loghom bo̠, a̠d̠igh itileduom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠, a̠d̠igh O̠nyi̠ bho̠. O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ ku̠ku̠m a̠loghom.
MAT 24:37 Agu̠o̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ obhel ta̠ A̠nua̠ bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ eruoma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠.
MAT 24:38 Ezin bho̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ obhel bho̠, kisa̠ obom amu̠m a̠d̠igho bho̠ a̠ru bho̠, a̠nwunom na̠ ed̠e na̠ e̠d̠a, na̠ ebhinogh ranwani̠ na̠ enigha̠nom ra̠nwi̠i̠nyan, tu̠tu̠n d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ A̠nua̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi obom oghugh bho̠;
MAT 24:39 sa̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ ta̠ emite tu̠tu̠n obom amu̠m a̠d̠igho bho̠ a̠ru, sa̠ aze̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠. Obha̠ agu̠o̠ eruoma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠ nyen.
MAT 24:40 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, i̠wal o̠ni̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠, ta̠ obhin odi sa̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ uwed̠i.
MAT 24:41 I̠wal anwani̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ esi o̠gbe̠ ed̠ia̠n na̠ e̠gbe̠ ma̠ ed̠ian, sa̠ ta̠ obhin odi o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ uwed̠i.
MAT 24:42 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, igone, ezin bho̠ inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠inyin ta̠ a̠ru bho̠.
MAT 24:43 I̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar onon. Ku̠gba ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ a̠loghom obhel wa̠ o̠gba bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru bho̠ nab̠o̠, i̠na ka̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ omom a̠kigima̠ ma̠ o̠gba bho̠ ma̠ ob̠om otu bho̠ od̠igh.
MAT 24:44 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, inyin eka̠ ikokod̠ia̠ne, ezin bho̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠ru ma̠ obhel ola̠ inyin o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠.
MAT 24:45 “I̠se̠, ka̠ a̠nyen a̠ga̠i ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ a̠loghom abar bho̠, ola̠ wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠sibh, ma̠ okponom rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ onigha̠ awa ma̠ ed̠ia̠n d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ akpe̠ bho̠?
MAT 24:46 E̠b̠e̠l ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ ka̠ wa̠nwuna̠ i̠na bho̠ a̠ru, sa̠ ta̠ abi̠gh ma̠ i̠na na̠ amar na̠ a̠gir bho̠.
MAT 24:47 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton eb̠la̠ e̠li̠la d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ okponom.
MAT 24:48 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu obha̠ ma̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠, sa̠ aru̠ru̠an d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ ta̠ a̠bia̠ ma̠ oru,’
MAT 24:49 sa̠ ake̠ ma̠ od̠ulogh rob̠a̠ra̠motu iyed̠i, sa̠ na̠ a̠d̠e na̠ ad̠a na̠ ro̠d̠amin.
MAT 24:50 Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ i̠na o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠, na̠ obhel ola̠ i̠na ologhoma̠n d̠o̠.
MAT 24:51 Sa̠ ta̠ agu̠r i̠na ma̠ obom agu̠o̠ i̠zagba, sa̠ ta̠ alo̠gh i̠na d̠a̠ agba ibhelebhel bho̠: i̠se̠ esi bho̠ ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠ od̠i.
MAT 25:1 “O̠ku̠a bha̠, ta̠ obhin irileghom ote̠nai̠ny o̠tu̠o̠m d̠iobh re̠kar anwi̠i̠nyan ya̠ ibhin rato̠di̠ d̠awa imite ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠bi̠ghan o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠.
MAT 25:2 Ogho d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa bha̠ rema̠, ya̠a̠ ogho bha̠ iloghodi̠ar.
MAT 25:3 Obhel bho̠ rema̠ bho̠ ibhin rato̠di̠ d̠awa bho̠, ibhin ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ amu̠nu̠ oliv e̠b̠aram.
MAT 25:4 Ya̠a̠, iloghodi̠ar bho̠ ibhin amu̠nu̠ oliv d̠a̠ rakana e̠b̠aram na̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ato̠di̠ d̠awa bho̠.
MAT 25:5 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ ma̠ oru bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa iduka̠ sa̠ adi̠la ibhinom awa.
MAT 25:6 “I̠se̠, d̠a̠ egum a̠d̠io, sa̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n izul ma̠a̠: ‘O̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠misi! Imite ma̠ eru ra̠ e̠bi̠ghan i̠na!’
MAT 25:7 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kar anwi̠i̠nyan bho̠ i̠su̠ma, sa̠ i̠pi̠ki̠ ma̠ rato̠di̠ d̠awa ibu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
MAT 25:8 Sa̠ rema̠ bho̠ ifugh inigha̠ ma̠ iloghodi̠ar bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Inigha̠ i̠yar idi amu̠nu̠ oliv d̠inyin; ato̠di̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ ed̠im.’
MAT 25:9 “Ya̠a̠, iloghodi̠ar bho̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠ ‘E̠nyi̠, ita̠ i̠yar eka̠ ko olei d̠o̠ i̠yar. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ewol bho̠ ka̠ egho ma̠ iya̠ inyin.’
MAT 25:10 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a ka̠ ogho bho̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ a̠ru. Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ ikokod̠ia̠n bho̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na id̠igh d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ erogh bho̠, sa̠ u̠du̠ ma̠ otu bho̠.
MAT 25:11 “A̠tepa̠, sa̠ re̠kar anwi̠i̠nyan iyed̠i iru nyen, sa̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, Wa̠nwuna̠, gurone ma̠ a̠d̠ighom i̠yar!’
MAT 25:12 “Ya̠a̠, i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ya̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ inyin.’
MAT 25:13 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, igone, ezin bho̠ inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ obhel bho̠.
MAT 25:14 “Irileghom ote̠nai̠ny od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ ob̠etina̠ e̠gi̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠kokod̠i ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ aru̠gi̠ awa ma̠ i̠di̠ar d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ okponom.
MAT 25:15 Sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi ogho e̠kpa ikpoki,sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi i̠wal, sa̠ odi onin, o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ e̠mi̠ bho̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ epa̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠.
MAT 25:16 O̠ni̠ wa̠ ada ma̠ ogho e̠kpa ikpoki obhel obha̠, sa̠ a̠bhin a̠b̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠b̠ua̠, sa̠ ate̠i̠ asu̠o̠ ogho ab̠aram.
MAT 25:17 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, wa̠ i̠wal bho̠ eka̠, ate̠i̠ asu̠o̠ i̠wal ab̠aram.
MAT 25:18 Ya̠a̠, wa̠ unigha̠ ma̠ onin bho̠, agi̠ ka̠ a̠gbo d̠a̠ a̠de awo̠gi̠ ma̠ okpoki ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 25:19 “Owewegh obhel a̠ten, sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠ru ma̠ oselegi o̠wal ogir d̠awa.
MAT 25:20 Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ unigha̠ ma̠ ogho e̠kpa ikpoki ab̠ar na̠ ipa̠n ogho e̠kpa a̠ru, sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, anwa inigha̠ ami̠ ogho e̠kpa ikpoki, bi̠ghe̠, ami̠ i̠te̠i̠ asu̠o̠ ipa̠n ogho e̠kpa.’
MAT 25:21 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa a̠gir, anwa a̠ga̠i ob̠a̠ra̠motu! Anwa ibhin onyen ologi a̠gir d̠a̠ i̠ki̠kara i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ inigha̠ nyam bho̠, ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠se̠n ami̠ na̠ aso̠n anwa ma̠ orileghom i̠di̠ar ya̠ ib̠uiy ipu ma̠ i̠nye̠n. Ke̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠no̠gho̠man ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ nyam.’
MAT 25:22 “Sa̠ wa̠ unigha̠ i̠wal e̠kpa ikpoki eka̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, anwa inigha̠ ami̠ i̠wal e̠kpa ikpoki, bi̠ghe̠, ami̠ i̠te̠i̠ asu̠o̠ ipa̠n i̠wal e̠kpa.’
MAT 25:23 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa amar a̠gir, anwa a̠ga̠i ob̠a̠ra̠motu! Anwa ibhin onyen ologi a̠gir d̠a̠ i̠ki̠kara i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ inigha̠ nyam bho̠, ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠se̠n ami̠ na̠ aso̠n anwa ma̠ orileghom i̠di̠ar ya̠ ib̠uiy ipu ma̠ i̠nye̠n. Ke̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠no̠gho̠man ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ nyam.’
MAT 25:24 “Sa̠ wa̠ unigha̠ ma̠ onin e̠kpa ikpoki bho̠ eka̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ amar a̠loghom anwa, anwa na̠ okpon d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ igbirigbir, anwa na̠ a̠b̠u ma̠ esi ola̠ anwa ogbebh d̠o̠, sa̠ anwa na̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa okpo d̠o̠ asar.
MAT 25:25 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ ami̠ ighil a̠rugugu, sa̠ ami̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠wo̠gi̠ ma̠ ikpoki d̠oyom d̠a̠ a̠de. Kpone, i̠do̠ ma̠ ikpoki d̠oyom.’
MAT 25:26 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa o̠gbo̠ro̠gbo̠r obhobho i̠kpo̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu. Anwa a̠loghom ma̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠u ma̠ esi ola̠ ami̠ ogbebh d̠o̠, sa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ okpo d̠o̠ asar.
MAT 25:27 Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ akpe̠ nyam o̠lo̠gh okpoki d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ otu-ikpoki bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ igiel ami̠ iru, ami̠ ate̠i̠ ikpoki d̠ami̠ na̠ asu̠o̠ ya̠ ka̠ i̠mar bho̠.
MAT 25:28 “ ‘Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ibhine ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ enigha̠ i̠na wa̠ ate̠i̠ d̠iobh ami̠na bho̠.
MAT 25:29 Ezin bho̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ ate̠i̠ ya̠ ib̠uiy bho̠, ta̠ onigha̠ ma̠ o̠gbam; ya̠a̠, i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, bebina̠ o̠nyi̠ki̠kara ya̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ bho̠ eka̠, ta̠ o̠wo̠r obhin.
MAT 25:30 Sa̠ a̠ruom ma̠ oze ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ omutiom d̠o̠ ma̠ asu̠o̠ bho̠, od̠ighom d̠a̠ obom azi̠m; i̠se̠ bha̠ esi ed̠i na̠ o̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠ od̠i.’
MAT 25:31 “Sa̠ obhel bho̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠ru na̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, eb̠la̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ta̠ ed̠igh na̠ i̠na eru, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ i̠kasi̠ a̠dila̠de irileghom isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 25:32 Sa̠ a̠nwunom eb̠la̠ ra̠dede bho̠ ta̠ ekokod̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ abagi̠o̠n awa ma̠ ebu ebu, agu̠o̠ okponom ro̠nana na̠ abagi̠o̠n ro̠nana bho̠ na̠ iwel bho̠.
MAT 25:33 Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin ro̠nana bho̠ amar a̠guri d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ iwel bho̠ d̠a̠ ekiel.
MAT 25:34 “D̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ O̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ ta̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ebu wa̠ d̠a̠ agba od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Itue ma̠ i̠se̠n, inyin ogbo ya̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ ane̠ghe̠ ma̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ ya̠ ukokod̠i uguri isisa̠n inyin ka̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠.
MAT 25:35 Ezin bho̠, o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi ami̠ sa̠ inyin unigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, e̠d̠o̠gh amu̠m a̠d̠ighi ami̠, sa̠ inyin unigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ amu̠m o̠d̠a, ami̠ iru ma̠ isuloma̠ sa̠ inyin ud̠ighom ami̠,
MAT 25:36 Ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ e̠dab̠a sa̠ inyin umuneni ami̠ ma̠ ukpe, ami̠ i̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r sa̠ inyin ukoko ami̠, u̠lo̠gh ami̠ ma̠ ikoli sa̠ inyin uru ra̠ ukpon ami̠.’
MAT 25:37 “D̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, a̠kere obhel wa̠ i̠yar u̠bi̠gh ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam sa̠ i̠yar unigha̠ nyam ed̠ia̠n bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ e̠d̠o̠gh amu̠m a̠d̠ighi nyam sa̠ unigha̠ nyam amu̠m o̠d̠a bho̠?
MAT 25:38 A̠kere obhel wa̠ i̠yar u̠bi̠gh anwa ma̠ isuloma̠ sa̠ ud̠ighom anwa bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ e̠dab̠a sa̠ umuneni nyam ukpe bho̠?
MAT 25:39 A̠kere obhel wa̠ i̠yar u̠bi̠gh ka̠ anwa na̠ anwe̠r, bo̠d̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ikoli sa̠ i̠yar u̠gi̠ ka̠ ukpon anwa bho̠?’
MAT 25:40 “Sa̠ O̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ ta̠ awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, agu̠o̠ inyin ugir unigha̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠ami̠ wa̠ ikulom ipu bho̠, bha̠ inyin ugir unigha̠ ami̠.’
MAT 25:41 “D̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ i̠na ta̠ agba a̠nigha̠ nyen ogbo ya̠ d̠a̠ ekiel bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Itene ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠ami̠, inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ osugi ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya wa̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ bho̠, wa̠ ugbonogi usisa̠n Eru Bho̠ na̠ itileduom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
MAT 25:42 Ezin bho̠ o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi ami̠, ya̠ inyin unigha̠ d̠o̠ ami̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, e̠d̠o̠gh amu̠m a̠d̠ighi ami̠ ya̠ inyin unigha̠ d̠o̠ ami̠ ma̠ amu̠m ya̠ o̠d̠a,
MAT 25:43 Ami̠ iru ma̠ isuloma̠ ya̠ inyin ud̠ighom d̠o̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ otu, ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ e̠dab̠a ya̠ inyin umuneni d̠o̠ ami̠ ma̠ ukpe, ami̠ i̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r aro̠ nyen d̠a̠ ikoli, ya̠a̠ inyin uru d̠o̠ ra̠ okpon ami̠.’
MAT 25:44 “O̠ku̠a sa̠ a̠wa ta̠ e̠wo̠ran nyen ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, a̠kere obhel wa̠ i̠yar u̠bi̠gh ka̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, bo̠d̠o̠ e̠d̠o̠gh amu̠m a̠d̠ighi nyam, bo̠d̠o̠ anwa iru ma̠ isuloma̠, bo̠d̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ e̠dab̠a, bo̠d̠o̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ asu̠nwe̠r, bo̠d̠o̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ikoli, sa̠ i̠yar u̠we̠le̠man oru ra̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ onigha̠ oyom?’
MAT 25:45 Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, agu̠o̠ inyin ogir d̠o̠ onigha̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ awa wa̠ ikulom ipu d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠ami̠ bho̠, bha̠ inyin ugir d̠o̠ onigha̠ ami̠ nyen.’
MAT 25:46 Sa̠ i̠nye̠n ta̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ alu̠kpe̠ egbika̠ wa̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ esi a̠ghud̠um ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠.”
MAT 26:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠munieni ma̠ ratu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠,
MAT 26:2 “Inyin ologhom ma̠a̠, ka̠ i̠wal a̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, bha̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠ na̠ a̠lei; sa̠ ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠du̠ ogigh.”
MAT 26:3 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei a̠nwunom bho̠ ikokod̠ia̠n d̠a̠ otu irileghom ta̠ we̠mu̠ okur bho̠ wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠keyafas bho̠,
MAT 26:4 sa̠ awa imimia̠n imutioghom re̠kal ya̠ obhin ikoiny ob̠ol A̠zizo̠s ogigh.
MAT 26:5 Ya̠a̠ imimia̠n ma̠a̠, “Ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ e̠yal bho̠ b̠o̠ka̠ elobhiri ogbo e̠ma na̠ osor.”
MAT 26:6 I̠se̠n bha̠, A̠zizo̠s od̠i d̠a̠ Abe̠tani̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh bho̠.
MAT 26:7 Sa̠ odi ani̠ a̠bhin ololo amu̠nu̠ ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠ ola̠ ibom a̠b̠ua̠, a̠ru ra̠ a̠zuom d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na od̠i d̠a̠ akpata od̠e bho̠.
MAT 26:8 Ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ i̠bi̠gh bho̠, sa̠ iguromeni ma̠ rologi ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “A̠din ere na̠ a̠robh amu̠nu̠ ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠ i̠nye̠n o̠ku̠a?”
MAT 26:9 Nab̠o̠, amu̠nu̠ i̠nye̠n elei iya̠ ka̠ uwol ibom a̠b̠ua̠ obhin onigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠.
MAT 26:10 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s a̠loghom abar wa̠ awa na̠ e̠ru̠ru̠an bho̠, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin udin ere na̠ o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i ya̠ ani̠ onon a̠gir a̠nigha̠ ami̠ bho̠?
MAT 26:11 Ronyigoiny bho̠ sa̠ od̠i na̠ inyin eb̠la̠ obhel, ya̠a̠ Ami̠ ka̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ na̠ inyin eb̠la̠ obhel.
MAT 26:12 Ezin bho̠, a̠zuom ami̠ ma̠ amu̠nu̠ ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠ nyen, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man ozu d̠ami̠ ogboloma̠ a̠ma̠d̠i d̠ami̠.
MAT 26:13 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, kesikesi ola̠ ta̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, ta̠ o̠gba nyen abar onon wa̠ i̠na a̠gir bho̠ obhin o̠ru̠ru̠an i̠na.”
MAT 26:14 Sa̠ odi d̠a̠ a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠, wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠zuda̠s Iskari̠o̠t bho̠, agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠,
MAT 26:15 ka̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ onigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ ere ka̠ ami̠ ib̠eton i̠na inigha̠ inyin?” Sa̠ awa i̠wal a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh ikpoki a̠silva̠ inigha̠ i̠na.
MAT 26:16 Ob̠eton d̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zuda̠s ake̠ ma̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ ta̠ a̠sora̠n i̠na ma̠ owol A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 26:17 D̠a̠ o̠pu̠r a̠d̠a̠ma̠ E̠yal Abe̠re̠di̠ wa̠ Owubh d̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ A̠zizo̠s iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “A̠kere esi wa̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan i̠yar o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man osisa̠n oyom, ma̠ od̠e ed̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠?”
MAT 26:18 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠: Obhel d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n, ami̠ na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠ami̠ ta̠ od̠e ma̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠ d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ igir agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom awa bho̠, sa̠ awa ikokod̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠.
MAT 26:20 Agu̠o̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule bho̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ akpata od̠e,
MAT 26:21 na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, odi o̠ni̠ inyin ta̠ a̠wol ami̠.”
MAT 26:22 Sa̠ awa ib̠ogina̠ ma̠ ibom, sa̠ o̠ni̠ o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ake̠ ma̠ opura̠n o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAT 26:23 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ wa̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ na̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ onin e̠kpa ed̠ia̠n bho̠, bha̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol ami̠ bho̠.
MAT 26:24 O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ agi̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ I̠na bho̠, ya̠a̠ itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ o̠wo̠l ob̠ol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ bho̠! O̠we̠le̠man o̠mar o̠yo̠ ka̠ ibhon a̠pu.”
MAT 26:25 Sa̠ A̠zuda̠s wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, anwa na̠ agba ma̠ ami̠, ka̠din?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ agba.”
