MAT 26:26 Obhel bho̠ awa na̠ ed̠e bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin abe̠re̠di̠, sa̠ a̠tutumeni, sa̠ a̠puron a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Ibhine ma̠ ed̠e; onon ozu d̠ami̠.”
MAT 26:27 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin okpa̠ko bho̠, sa̠ ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ awa agba ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ inyin ibhine ma̠ e̠d̠a.
MAT 26:28 Ezin bho̠ i̠nye̠n asi̠ d̠ami̠, wa̠ aghu̠ame̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠zo̠ bho̠, asi̠ wa̠ uzu unigha̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ obhin o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh.
MAT 26:29 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, obhin i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, ami̠ ko o̠d̠a mu̠ ma̠ a̠min itu a̠grep tu̠tu̠n d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ inyin ad̠a ma̠ imom a̠min d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠.”
MAT 26:30 Sa̠ awa i̠mo̠r aso̠r, sa̠ i̠d̠u̠a i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ igu Roliv.
MAT 26:31 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ inyin ta̠ eghil e̠we̠le̠man ami̠ e̠d̠u̠a ma̠ a̠d̠ugula̠n onon ebula̠ ami̠, ezin bho̠ na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠gigh okponom ro̠nana bho̠, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh ro̠nana bho̠ ta̠ e̠sasaragi̠an.’
MAT 26:32 Ya̠a̠, igiel ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ a̠b̠a̠ra̠ inyin d̠a̠ Agalili.”
MAT 26:33 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ighilighu i̠d̠u̠a eka̠, ami̠ ko oghil ani̠ d̠o̠ ad̠u̠a.”
MAT 26:34 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, a̠d̠ugula̠n onon, kisa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r bho̠ ta̠ alal, anwa ta̠ aku̠a ma̠ i̠sar igiel ma̠a̠ anwa na̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ami̠.”
MAT 26:35 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ Anwa a̠mugh eka̠, ami̠ ka̠ o̠ku̠a d̠o̠ nyam.” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ifugh ani̠ ma̠ onin agu̠o̠.
MAT 26:36 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan do̠yo̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ esi ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Age̠tsemani, sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠a̠, “I̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠dila̠de, ya̠ ami̠ ta̠ agi̠ ma̠ ebha̠ ka̠ a̠siseiny.”
MAT 26:37 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin A̠pita̠ na̠ i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ Aze̠bidi ab̠aragi̠ma̠ i̠na, sa̠ i̠na asu̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an a̠d̠igh i̠ku̠nu̠.
MAT 26:38 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Eloghoma̠n ozu d̠ami̠ na̠ aku̠nu̠ ma̠ ibom, aro̠ ka̠ omugh a̠sugho. I̠ro̠ omom na̠ ami̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n.”
MAT 26:39 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠kara d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ka̠ a̠b̠obhia̠n a̠siseiny a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ur nab̠o̠, d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ okpa̠ko onon a̠ten ad̠u̠a d̠ami̠. D̠a̠ o̠ku̠a eka̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ku̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠ami̠, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠oyom.”
MAT 26:40 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ sa̠ abi̠gh ma̠a̠ awa na̠ ekod̠u, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n A̠pita̠ ma̠a̠, “Inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ od̠igh na̠ ami̠ o̠ro̠ omom bebina̠ ekud̠i obhel ke̠re̠?
MAT 26:41 I̠ro̠ ma̠ omom esiseiny b̠o̠ka̠ inyin umel d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ ad̠agi̠an. E̠mu̠gh bho̠ na̠ e̠ral ya̠a̠ ozu bho̠ na̠ a̠dugh.”
MAT 26:42 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ agi̠ ma̠ oleghemeni i̠wal igiel ka̠ a̠siseiny a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠, ku̠gba ma̠ okpa̠ko egbika̠ onon ka̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a, a̠ten ka̠ Ami̠ i̠d̠a, bha̠ i̠to̠ d̠oyom emite.”
MAT 26:43 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ agi̠ ka̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa na̠ ekod̠u, ezin bho̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa na̠ e̠mu̠mo̠r ibom.
MAT 26:44 Sa̠ i̠na awe̠le̠man awa a̠puta̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠siseiny oleghemeni i̠sar igiel, a̠fugh onin abar bho̠.
MAT 26:45 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ i̠sar ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ka̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin od̠idia̠ na̠ ekod̠u na̠ esira̠ ma̠ epobh? Ikpone, iloghome ma̠ obhel wa̠ u̠to̠ ugiri bho̠ na̠ a̠lei, sa̠ ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ idighi ma̠ i̠karabh.
MAT 26:46 Ib̠egina̠! na̠ a̠lei o̠gi̠! Wa̠ a̠wol ami̠ bho̠ aro̠ ka̠ na̠ a̠misi ma̠ i̠se̠n!”
MAT 26:47 I̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠fugh, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ isibhi ma̠ rab̠e̠ge̠re̠ na̠ re̠b̠am ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ re̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zuda̠s, odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ awa a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠, a̠ru.
MAT 26:48 I̠se̠n, wa̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠ a̠tu̠o̠m elegh a̠leriom awa ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ api̠pi̠o̠bh bho̠ bha̠ O̠ni̠ bho̠, ib̠ole i̠na.”
MAT 26:49 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠ sa̠ i̠na agi̠ epa̠ d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s ka̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “We̠mu̠ Atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ a̠bheleguma̠ nyam o!” Sa̠ api̠pi̠o̠bh i̠na.
MAT 26:50 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠tologha̠n, gire ma̠ abar wa̠ anwa idin iru bho̠.” Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ iru ra̠ isibh A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ ib̠ol i̠na.
MAT 26:51 I̠se̠, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ aro̠ na̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mutiom ab̠e̠ge̠re̠ do̠yo̠ sa̠ a̠sobh a̠to ta̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠b̠uton.
MAT 26:52 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s aghaghana i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Lo̠ghe̠ ma̠ ab̠e̠ge̠re̠ d̠oyom ma̠ esi wa̠ akpe̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ bho̠, ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ esibh ab̠e̠ge̠re̠, na̠ emugh d̠a̠ ab̠e̠ge̠re̠.
MAT 26:53 Bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ anwa na̠ aru̠ru̠an ma̠a̠, ami̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ o̠fi̠ri̠ma ami̠ ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ro̠lo̠ghitileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n i̠se̠n, ke̠re̠?
MAT 26:54 O̠ku̠a ka̠ ta̠ od̠ighi eka̠ omuzoghod̠iom ya̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, ya̠ i̠kpe̠ ma̠ omite bho̠?”
MAT 26:55 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n o̠go̠ ebhugh ke̠re̠, ma̠ ola̠ inyin ubhin rab̠e̠ge̠re̠ na̠ re̠b̠am na̠ oru ra̠ ob̠ol ami̠. Ami̠ i̠ro̠ghan a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠a̠ inyin ub̠ol d̠o̠ ami̠.
MAT 26:56 Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n imite ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ i̠ge̠ iguri d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠we̠le̠ i̠na i̠ghil i̠d̠u̠a.
MAT 26:57 Ogbo ya̠ ib̠ol A̠zizo̠s bho̠, ibhin i̠na e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠keyafas, we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, esi wa̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ na̠ ekokod̠ia̠n bho̠.
MAT 26:58 Ya̠a̠, A̠pita̠ aro̠ ma̠ egbeiny atu̠o̠no̠m i̠na ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ ogigo ta̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de na̠ rokponomotu bho̠, ma̠ o̠bi̠gh agu̠o̠ ta̠ a̠bhin a̠kunugiom.
MAT 26:59 Sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo osobh ase̠ bho̠ i̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ agba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠ a̠b̠ologiom A̠zizo̠s, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ ebhin esobh ase̠ bho̠ ebhumeni i̠na egigh.
MAT 26:60 A̠d̠izo ronyob̠a̠ igunugha̠ emite, ya̠a̠ abar ola̠ a̠sibh i̠na na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠. D̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠wal ronyob̠a̠ imite,
MAT 26:61 i̠gba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ onon agba ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ogion otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ Ami̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠lo amado̠n d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ amara a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa̠ ka̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Onon ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien abar ola̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ ob̠ologiom anwa?”
MAT 26:63 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s aro̠ b̠u̠b̠o̠m. Sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠, na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠: Sibhigha̠ ku̠gba ma̠ anwa Akrai̠st O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAT 26:64 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ agba a̠mutiom. O̠ku̠a eka̠, Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, obhin i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ a̠limon ka̠ na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠.”
MAT 26:65 Sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ ago̠go̠i̠ny ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ a̠fugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̱ A̠zib̠a̠! Ta̠ odin ere o̠bho̠ro̠ghan opa̠n onyob̠a̠? I̠bi̠ghe̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠fugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̱ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAT 26:66 Inyin u̠bi̠gh eka̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ api̠o̠gho̠m, akpe̠ ma̠ omugh.”
MAT 26:67 Sa̠ awa i̠si̠ro̠gho̠m i̠na ma̠ i̠gho̠r d̠a̠ a̠misigh, sa̠ igorogh i̠na, sa̠ ipa̠n a̠nwunom i̠b̠abhagh i̠na,
MAT 26:68 ifugh ma̠a̠, “Akrai̠st! Wa̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠gor anwa bho̠.”
MAT 26:69 I̠se̠n A̠pita̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ etire d̠a̠ ologi ogigo bho̠, sa̠ odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu o̠nyani̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa odi o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠ro̠ ani̠ na̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Agalili bho̠.”
MAT 26:70 Ya̠a̠, i̠na aku̠a d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ta̠ eb̠la̠ awa, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ anwa na̠ agba bho̠.”
MAT 26:71 Sa̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ogigo bho̠, sa̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ abi̠gh i̠na, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Onon odi o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠rilogha̠n A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t bho̠.”
MAT 26:72 Sa̠ i̠na a̠puta̠ aku̠a, a̠sibhigha̠ ma̠a̠: “Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠!”
MAT 26:73 O̠nyi̠ obhel a̠ten, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠pita̠, sa̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, anwa odi o̠ni̠ awa nyen, ezin bho̠ a̠nem d̠oyom na̠ agba nyam na̠ a̠mutiom.”
MAT 26:74 O̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ ogurugia̠n, o̠ghad̠i̠an ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠!” Ogbo na̠ onin sa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r alal.
MAT 26:75 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ aru̠ru̠an iwowa̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ a̠wa̠ ma̠a̠, “Kisa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r ta̠ alal, anwa ta̠ aku̠a ami̠ i̠sar igiel, ma̠a̠ anwa na̠ a̠loghom d̠o̠ ami̠.” Sa̠ i̠na a̠rile a̠mite d̠a̠ ogigo bho̠ ka̠ a̠leghe agba ma̠ igbir.
MAT 27:1 Ame̠ghe̠le̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠, ikokod̠ia̠n imimia̠n iya̠ ogir ogboloma̠ A̠zizo̠s, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ osobh ase̠ obhumeni o̠yo̠ ogigh.
MAT 27:2 Sa̠ awa i̠bhad̠i̠ i̠na ibhin i̠gi̠o̠m Apai̠let we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠.
MAT 27:3 Igiel bho̠ A̠zuda̠s wa̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠ abi̠gh ma̠ na̠ osobh ase̠ obhumeni ma̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ a̠loghoma̠n ma̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir api̠e̠. Sa̠ a̠mulumeni ma̠ a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh ikpoki a̠silva̠ bho̠ agi̠o̠m we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠,
MAT 27:4 agba ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠karabh, a̠wol o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠pi̠o̠gho̠m d̠o̠, a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ uzu ma̠ asi̠ d̠o̠yo̠.” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ere a̠gboloma̠ i̠yar? Anwa ku kpone ma̠ a̠d̠ighom.”
MAT 27:5 Sa̠ i̠na a̠zu ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a ka̠ akpo̠ a̠sina̠ a̠mugh.
MAT 27:6 Ya̠a̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ ikpokpo ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, “Na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ obhin ka̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ esi wa̠ na̠ okoko ma̠ ikpoki bho̠, agu̠o̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ ikpoki ogigha̠n o̠ni̠ bho̠.”
MAT 27:7 O̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan obhin ikpoki bho̠ ka̠ ogho a̠de ta̠ ob̠olob̠ol ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ obhin otenemeni o̠karabh esi ola̠ od̠i risuloma̠.
MAT 27:8 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, obhin obhel obha̠ ra̠ o̠te̠i̠ a̠didon, na̠ obhelegi ma̠ a̠de obha̠, ma̠a̠, “A̠de Asi̠.”
MAT 27:9 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ umuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ wa̠ owil A̠zerimaya a̠wa̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Sa̠ awa ibhin a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh ikpoki a̠silva̠ bho̠, ikpoki e̠mu̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ anwi̠i̠ny Izre̠l ima̠ra̠ ma̠ awa ta̠ o̠kpe̠ bho̠.
MAT 27:10 Sa̠ awa ibhin ikpoki bho̠ igho ma̠ a̠de ta̠ ob̠olob̠ol ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠, agu̠o̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠ruom ami̠ bho̠.”
MAT 27:11 I̠se̠ sa̠ ibhin A̠zizo̠s ka̠ i̠marame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Anwa o̠li̠le̠ma ogbo A̠zu bho̠ ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ agba aman.”
MAT 27:12 Sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ ikpon abarabar ib̠ologiom i̠na, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠ ma̠ abar.
MAT 27:13 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ Apai̠let a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ya̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ ob̠ologiom anwa bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAT 27:14 Ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠, bebina̠ abar, sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n ibom ma̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠.
MAT 27:15 I̠se̠n d̠a̠ e̠yal bho̠, bha̠ obhel wa̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ na̠ a̠mutiomgha̠n o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ikoli ola̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ipuru.
MAT 27:16 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, bha̠ odi obom od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s Abarabas aro̠ d̠a̠ ikoli.
MAT 27:17 D̠a̠ obhel bho̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ekokod̠ia̠n bho̠, sa̠ Apai̠let a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan ami̠ ma̠ imutiom oken d̠a̠ i̠wal awa onigha̠ inyin: A̠zizo̠s Abarabas, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠?”
MAT 27:18 Ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠loghom ma̠a̠ awa ibhin d̠a̠ egbugbo ologi eb̠eton A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st enigha̠ i̠na.
MAT 27:19 Agu̠o̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ i̠kasi̠ osobh ase̠ bho̠, sa̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ruom a̠duom agi̠o̠m i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ko ogir abar a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ o̠pi̠o̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ abar bho̠. Ezin bho̠, ami̠ i̠bigh ibom ali̠gam a̠ruzu d̠a̠ amala ma̠ a̠didon d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠.”
MAT 27:20 Ya̠a̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ itumugiom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ epuru ku ma̠ Abarabas, ya̠a̠ ogigh A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st.
MAT 27:21 Sa̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ i̠wal awa ka̠ ami̠ imutiom oken inigha̠ inyin?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Abarabas.”
MAT 27:22 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ ogir ere ogboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠?” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Du̠e̠ ma̠ a̠gigh!”
MAT 27:23 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere, a̠gir a̠kere a̠d̠ien i̠karabh?” Sa̠ imula̠ i̠lo̠gh e̠mi̠ imulughu ma̠a̠, “Du̠e̠ ma̠ a̠gigh!”
MAT 27:24 Ya̠ Apai̠let a̠loghoma̠n ma̠ abar ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue a̠gir alo̠gh bo̠ bho̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ e̠ko̠ro̠, sa̠ a̠bhin amu̠m a̠tita̠la̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ abhe̠bhi̠la d̠a̠ a̠misigh eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ id̠igh ani̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠kpe̠ ogigha̠n o̠ni̠ onon. Inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ ka̠ ekpon ed̠ighom!”
MAT 27:25 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Asi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ ranwi̠i̠ny d̠a̠ i̠yar!”
MAT 27:26 O̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠na a̠mutiom Abarabas a̠nigha̠ awa, ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh na̠ o̠du̠ o̠yo̠ ogigh.
MAT 27:27 Sa̠ ogbo e̠gham ta̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ ibhin A̠zizo̠s i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ sa̠ ikokod̠i ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo e̠gham bho̠.
MAT 27:28 Sa̠ i̠ko̠gi̠o̠n ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ i̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na ma̠ obom akapa ododo,
MAT 27:29 sa̠ ilo ma̠ eghoi ib̠ub̠ulom izuom e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠lo̠gh okpeti i̠ki̠ani̠ d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ ikpuluma̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠ iduom i̠na ma̠a̠, “E O̠li̠le̠ma A̠zu, i̠yar na̠ okpud̠ia̠n o!”
MAT 27:30 Sa̠ i̠si̠ro̠gho̠m i̠na ma̠ i̠gho̠r, sa̠ ibhin okpeti i̠ki̠ani̠ bho̠ ib̠orogh e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 27:31 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ awa na̠ eduom i̠na e̠we̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠ko̠gi̠o̠n ibura̠ ododo ya̠ awa i̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ inwe i̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na ma̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ibhin i̠na i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ka̠ o̠du̠ o̠yo̠ ogigh.
MAT 27:32 Agu̠o̠ awa na̠ emite bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠manana ma̠ o̠ni̠ A̠sirin ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Asai̠mo̠n, sa̠ iponoma̠ i̠na ma̠ orol e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 27:33 Sa̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ imisi ma̠ esi ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠a̠ Ago̠lgo̠ta, (a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “Esi okpokpo e̠mu̠.”)
MAT 27:34 Sa̠ awa inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠min ya̠ u̠gu̠a na̠ a̠non; ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na ad̠e̠d̠i̠ma bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠gin o̠d̠a.
MAT 27:35 Sa̠ awa i̠du̠ i̠na, sa̠ irobh okob̠a̠ ibhin i̠ru̠gi̠an ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 27:36 Sa̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de igon i̠na.
MAT 27:37 Sa̠ awa i̠ge̠ ma̠ iku wa̠ i̠gba igboloma̠ i̠na bho̠, i̠ke̠ri̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠: ONON A̠ZIZO̠S, O̠LI̠LE̠MA A̠ZU BHO̠.
MAT 27:38 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠du̠ i̠na bho̠, i̠du̠ na̠ i̠wal aru̠gba, odi d̠a̠ od̠iom agba d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠a̠ uwed̠i d̠a̠ okiel.
MAT 27:39 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eten bho̠ i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na inyegi ma̠ aru̠mu̠ d̠awa
MAT 27:40 ifugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa wa̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠b̠ogion otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠lo amado̠n d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, tenemeni ma̠ ozu d̠oyom, agu̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, bha̠ sore ma̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠!”
MAT 27:41 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠, na̠ ikei bho̠ iduom i̠na nyen efugh ma̠a̠,
MAT 27:42 “I̠na na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo, ya̠a̠ na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ otenemeni ozu d̠o̠yo̠! O̠li̠le̠ma Izre̠l! I̠se̠n sore d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ ma̠ a̠ru, sa̠ i̠yar ta̠ oma̠ra̠ nyam.
MAT 27:43 I̠na a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ a̠lei A̠zib̠a̠ a̠tenemeni i̠na ma̠ i̠se̠n, ku̠gba ma̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ma̠ra̠! Ezin bho̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.’ ”
MAT 27:44 Sa̠ aru̠gba ya̠ u̠du̠gi̠ d̠a̠ aka ta̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ bho̠ eka̠ erogi i̠na.
MAT 27:45 Obeton d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ o̠wal ma̠ obhel bho̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal d̠a̠ e̠sala̠d̠io ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ i̠sar d̠a̠ etita̠n, sa̠ azi̠m a̠kpegiom eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom.
MAT 27:46 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ o̠wal ma̠ obhel bho̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ i̠sar d̠a̠ etita̠n, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mulughu na̠ obom okoroko ma̠a̠, “E̠lai̠, E̠lai̠,lama sabaktani̠?” (onon a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠zib̠a̠ d̠ami̠, A̠zib̠a̠ d̠ami̠, ere wa̠ Anwa na̠ awe̠le̠man ami̠ bho̠?”)
MAT 27:47 Sa̠ idi awa ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Na̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ I̠lai̠za.”
MAT 27:48 D̠a̠ ogbo na̠ onin, sa̠ odi awa a̠kpo ma̠ eghil ka̠ a̠bhin asapu̠ ato̠ri̠ d̠a̠ igheghed̠um a̠min, sa̠ akpu̠o̠m d̠a̠ okpeti a̠b̠eton a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠d̠a.
MAT 27:49 Ya̠a̠ ipa̠n ogbo ifugh ma̠a̠, “I̠we̠le̠, ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ka̠ I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠tenemeni i̠na.”
MAT 27:50 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠nwe a̠mulughu na̠ obom okoroko, sa̠ ekpo epobh bho̠ a̠sobha̠n.
MAT 27:51 Sa̠ ukpe wa̠ ubhin usobhom a̠lukpesi e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠b̠eton d̠a̠ eb̠o bho̠ agu̠an a̠sor aru̠gi̠an i̠wal a̠bin, sa̠ a̠de bho̠ a̠nyegia̠n, sa̠ ra̠de o̠gbi̠o̠ma bho̠ ib̠ob̠omia̠n i̠saragi̠an.
MAT 27:52 Sa̠ ranyu̠ od̠i bho̠ ikpegina̠ sa̠ a̠d̠izo imumugh ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ib̠egina̠.
MAT 27:53 Sa̠ awa imiteghu d̠a̠ a̠rugugua̠ a̠ma̠d̠i bho̠, i̠gi̠ ka̠ imutuma̠ ma̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom d̠a̠ E̠ma E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.
MAT 27:54 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ we̠mu̠ ogbo e̠gham bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i na̠ i̠na na̠ egon A̠zizo̠s bho̠, i̠bi̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠de bho̠ a̠nyegia̠n a̠b̠obomia̠n a̠d̠igh bho̠, na̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠, sa̠ ibom a̠rugugu isibh awa, sa̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, onon O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!”
MAT 27:55 A̠d̠izo anwani̠ ya̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠mghan A̠zizo̠s igir ogir inigha̠ i̠na bho̠, ob̠eton d̠a̠ Agalili, i̠ro̠ ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAT 27:56 Idi awa bha̠, A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠, A̠meri oweni ta̠ A̠zemsi na̠ A̠zose̠fu̠, na̠ oweni anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ Aze̠bidi.
MAT 27:57 Agu̠o̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule bho̠, sa̠ o̠li̠la ola̠ Ari̠mati̠a ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠, ola̠ ra̠ a̠ten ani̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan ta̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ru.
MAT 27:58 I̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ Apai̠let ka̠ a̠puru ma̠ ozu ta̠ A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ Apai̠let a̠ruom ma̠ enigha̠.
MAT 27:59 Sa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ a̠bhin omom ukpe asi̠ni̠ni̠n ola̠ amar ab̠ab̠ala a̠bhurugi ma̠ egua̠de bho̠,
MAT 27:60 sa̠ a̠d̠i d̠a̠ omom od̠i ola̠ o̠yo̠, ola̠ i̠na a̠b̠u a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠de o̠gbi̠o̠ma ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠kiligi ma̠ obom o̠pad̠i̠ o̠gbi̠o̠ma a̠kpegiom o̠nu̠ od̠i bho̠ sa̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a.
MAT 27:61 Sa̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠ na̠ A̠meri uwed̠i bho̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de isumogha̠n od̠i bho̠.
MAT 27:62 I̠b̠ala bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Apai̠let,
MAT 27:63 ka̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “We̠mu̠, ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ o̠ni̠ igelemeni bho̠ agba ma̠ igiel wa̠ i̠na od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Ka̠ i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, ami̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh.’
MAT 27:64 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ruome ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ e̠mar ekponom od̠i bho̠ tu̠tu̠n d̠a̠ oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ o̠gi̠ d̠o̠ ka̠ eb̠igh e̠si̠ghe̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, sa̠ igelemeni wa̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ ta̠ a̠gurom a̠pu ma̠ o̠pu̠r bho̠.”
MAT 27:65 Sa̠ Apai̠let agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ibhine ma̠ ogbo e̠gham ma̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ ekponom, i̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ ekponom agu̠o̠ inyin uloghom obhin okponom bho̠.”
MAT 27:66 Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠mar i̠lo̠ ma̠ od̠i bho̠ igir, sa̠ i̠lo̠gh elegh a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh, sa̠ iguri ma̠ ogbo e̠gham ma̠ o̠ro̠ okponom.
MAT 28:1 A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠ a̠ten, agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠nyiroghom o̠b̠al d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r a̠d̠a̠ma̠ esi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠ na̠ A̠meri uwed̠i i̠gi̠ ka̠ okpon anyu̠ od̠i bho̠.
MAT 28:2 D̠a̠ awai̠, sa̠ a̠de bho̠ a̠nyegia̠n ibom, ezin bho̠ otileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠sor a̠ru ra̠ a̠kiligi ma̠ o̠pad̠i̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠ a̠guri d̠a̠ aka, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠.
MAT 28:3 I̠na a̠mite awar agu̠o̠ i̠me̠me̠gi̠na agbararan, sa̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ab̠al agu̠o̠ ab̠ala.
MAT 28:4 Ebula̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekponom esi bho̠, ighil a̠rugugu ka̠ e̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠, awa ibhin igiri imugh onyinye.
MAT 28:5 Ya̠a̠, otileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ anwani̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu, ami̠ a̠loghom ma̠ inyin uru ra̠ okpon A̠zizo̠s wa̠ o̠du̠ ugigh bho̠.
MAT 28:6 I̠na bo̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n, i̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ agba bho̠. Itue ra̠ e̠bi̠gh esi wa̠ uselegi i̠na bho̠,
MAT 28:7 ma̠ e̠nu̠r e̠gi̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠: ‘I̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili ka̠ ob̠a̠ra̠ inyin. Obha̠ esi wa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠.’ I̠nagha, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin!”
MAT 28:8 Sa̠ awa inugia̠n i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠ na̠ a̠rugugu na̠ ibom a̠libhon ologi, sa̠ ikpo ma̠ eghil ka̠ o̠gba onigha̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠.
MAT 28:9 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mutuma̠ awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ a̠bheleguma̠ o!” Sa̠ awa iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na ighinigia̠n a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠ ibuom i̠na.
MAT 28:10 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu. I̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ a̠rumor d̠ami̠ ma̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili, awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh ami̠ ma̠ ebha̠.”
MAT 28:11 Igiel bho̠ anwani̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ idi ogbo ikponom bho̠ id̠igh d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ka̠ i̠gba ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠ inigha̠ ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠.
MAT 28:12 Sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ imimia̠n na̠ ikei bho̠, sa̠ inigha̠ ma̠ ogbo e̠gham bho̠ ma̠ ikpoki ya̠ i̠mo̠mo̠nya,
MAT 28:13 sa̠ i̠gba inigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ ogba ma̠a̠, ‘Ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iru ma̠ a̠d̠ugula̠n ra̠ eb̠igh i̠na e̠si̠ghe̠, ma̠ obhel ola̠ i̠yar na̠ okod̠u.’
MAT 28:14 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠, asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n ed̠igh d̠a̠ a̠to ta̠ we̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠, i̠yar ta̠ ob̠okumeni ma̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ b̠o̠ka̠ inyin ud̠igh d̠a̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu.”
MAT 28:15 Sa̠ awa ibhin ikpoki bho̠ igir agu̠o̠ uruom awa bho̠. A̠nwunom A̠zu od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n na̠ e̠sasaragi̠ tu̠tu̠n ka̠ a̠didon.
MAT 28:16 Sa̠ d̠iobh na̠ onin ogbo ogir bho̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ igu d̠a̠ Agalili, d̠a̠ esi wa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom awa ma̠ o̠gi̠ bho̠.
MAT 28:17 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠, sa̠ ibuom i̠na, ya̠a̠ idi awa ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠na A̠zizo̠s.
MAT 28:18 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠ighoma̠ awa agba ma̠a̠, “Na̠ onigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠limon d̠a̠ a̠de na̠ iya̠ d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny.
MAT 28:19 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ egir agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ eten ogbo atu̠ghan d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠dede, ma̠ ewur awa ma̠ amu̠m d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠, na̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠, na̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.
MAT 28:20 I̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ osibh ogir eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ iruom inyin ogir bho̠. Iloghome ma̠a̠, ami̠ od̠i na̠ inyin kigiel kigiel tu̠tu̠n d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠.”
MAR 1:1 Onon agu̠o̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin ake̠ bho̠.
MAR 1:2 D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire ta̠ owil Ai̠zaya bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Nagha o! Ami̠ ta̠ a̠bhin a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ d̠ami̠ a̠ruom o̠ni̠ a̠duom, ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man eten bho̠ ob̠a̠ra̠ oyom.”
MAR 1:3 “Okoroko na̠ a̠si na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ e̠sala a̠de i̠si̠sar bho̠, ma̠a̠, ‘I̠tu̠ghu̠mane̠ ma̠ eten bho̠ ma̠ esisia̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, ma̠ eselegi ma̠ reten bho̠.’”
MAR 1:4 Sa̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ e̠sala a̠de i̠si̠sar bho̠, sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, a̠nwunom etiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠awa ewura̠ ma̠ amu̠m, sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠awa.
MAR 1:5 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh A̠zudia̠ sekina̠ a̠nwunom A̠zeruse̠le̠m id̠u i̠gi̠ do̠yo̠. Sa̠ awa i̠gba ma̠ i̠karabh d̠awa imutiom, sa̠ i̠na a̠wur awa ma̠ amu̠m d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan.
MAR 1:6 Azo̠n a̠bura̠ ma̠ ibura̠ ya̠ ubhin ipur e̠nam-a̠dol u̠le̠m, sa̠ i̠na akpo̠aghan o̠kara ozu e̠nam d̠a̠ eka̠ka̠gh d̠o̠yo̠. Ed̠ia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bha̠ i̠ganw na̠ ame̠ ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ aparapa.
MAR 1:7 Sa̠ Azo̠n agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ aman d̠ami̠ bho̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ami̠, ya̠a̠ ami̠ ilei d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ozuma̠n o̠ko̠gi̠o̠n id̠id̠igh ragbaka do̠yo̠.
MAR 1:8 Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin amu̠m na̠ a̠wur inyin, ya̠a̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠wur inyin.”
MAR 1:9 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, a̠zuzua̠n ola̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ Anazare̠t d̠a̠ ebhugh Agalili ka̠ ate̠i̠ Azo̠n. Sa̠ Azo̠n a̠wur i̠na ma̠ amu̠m d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan.
MAR 1:10 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠bhun bho̠ sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh ka̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ a̠gurona̠, sa̠ E̠mu̠gh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠sor ra̠ akpasan i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ okur osege.
MAR 1:11 Sa̠ okoroko a̠si a̠mite d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ma̠a̠: “Anwa o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, wa̠ ami̠ itula̠n ibom bho̠, wa̠ ologi d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠bhon na̠ a̠ni̠gha̠ bho̠.”
MAR 1:12 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠ sa̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠rileghom i̠na ka̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ e̠sala a̠de i̠si̠sar.
MAR 1:13 I̠na aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ d̠a̠ e̠sala a̠de i̠si̠sar bho̠ ma̠ eruba̠l ra̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ Eru Bho̠ ad̠agi̠an i̠na. A̠zizo̠s aro̠ na̠ i̠nam ed̠um, sa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ iru ra̠ i̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ inigha̠ i̠na.
MAR 1:14 Igiel bho̠ na̠ ob̠ol Azo̠n o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ikoli bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili ka̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
MAR 1:15 sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “Na̠ ate̠i̠ obhel wa̠ omuzoghod̠iom bho̠, i̠rileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n. Itiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh, ma̠ ed̠umom ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠!”
MAR 1:16 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile agbal Abadi̠ Agalili, sa̠ abi̠gh i̠wal a̠rumor, Asai̠mo̠n na̠ Anduru umor d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ awa na̠ erobh o̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ abadi̠ bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa i̠ku̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠.
MAR 1:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠tu̠o̠no̠me̠ Ami̠, sa̠ Ami̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni inyin i̠ku̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠ a̠nwunom.”
MAR 1:18 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠ sa̠ awa i̠we̠le̠man i̠gbo̠ d̠awa i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAR 1:19 O̠d̠u̠a i̠se̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh A̠zemsi o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Aze̠bidi na̠ Azo̠n umor d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ologi oghugh na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠man i̠gbo̠ d̠awa.
MAR 1:20 Ogbo na̠ onin sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi awa, sa̠ awa i̠we̠le̠ epa̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠awa Aze̠bidi d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠ na̠ ipa̠n ogbo ogir ya̠ awa i̠ko̠ bho̠ sa̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAR 1:21 Awa i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Akapanu̠m, sa̠ ate̠i̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
MAR 1:22 Ed̠igh ilologia̠n a̠nwunom o̠mu̠gho̠n atu̠ghu̠me̠ni d̠o̠yo̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠bhin a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ agba ma̠ asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠, i̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ita̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ roloko bho̠.
MAR 1:23 Odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh na̠ a̠nyegi, aro̠ d̠a̠ ologi otu u̠gala bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin obom okoroko a̠mulughu. Sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠,
MAR 1:24 “Anwa na̠ i̠yar ka̠ unwuna̠ ma̠ ere, A̠zizo̠s Anazare̠t? Anwa na̠ a̠ru ra̠ o̠pi̠e̠gi̠ i̠yar o̠man ke̠re̠? I̠yar ologhom ma̠a̠ anwa We̠b̠ab̠ala wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin a̠ru bho̠!”
MAR 1:25 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s aghaghana i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m! Mite d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠!”
MAR 1:26 Sa̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠teb̠eli i̠na, sa̠ i̠na asalaghu̠ a̠mulughu na̠ obom o̠kparakpar okoroko ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 1:27 Sa̠ abar bho̠ a̠d̠igh eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ ilologia̠n, sa̠ awa imogha̠, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠pura̠n odi ma̠a̠, “Woo, onon ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠! I̠na na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ na̠ aghaghana ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh, sa̠ awa na̠ e̠nagha i̠na.”
MAR 1:28 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ o̠du̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s asi̠saragi̠an ka̠ ate̠i̠ kesi kesi d̠a̠ ebhugh Agalili.
MAR 1:29 Awa i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ otu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin A̠zemsi̠ na̠ Azo̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Asai̠mo̠n na̠ Anduru.
MAR 1:30 D̠a̠ obhel bho̠ awa i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Asai̠mo̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh o̠yo̠go̠-onweni ta̠ Asai̠mo̠n d̠a̠ e̠mana na̠ asu̠nwe̠r amu̠m o̠bhi̠i̠y na̠ a̠sibh i̠na, sa̠ awa i̠nu̠r i̠gba i̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 1:31 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ ka̠ a̠sibh ani̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ a̠b̠eton, sa̠ amu̠m-o̠bhi̠i̠y bho̠ ad̠u̠a, sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ed̠ia̠n aki̠o̠m awa.
MAR 1:32 Ate̠i̠ a̠dule d̠a̠ obhel ogogo bho̠ na̠ a̠d̠ugh, sa̠ awa ibhinogh eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠ na̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ enyegi iru d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 1:33 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ e̠ma bho̠ ikokod̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh otu bho̠.
MAR 1:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠koko ma̠ a̠d̠izo ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere asu̠nwe̠r bho̠ a̠d̠umeni, sa̠ i̠na a̠zegi ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ asi̠ghe̠gi̠, ya̠ i̠na na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ ma̠ ofugh abar, ezin bho̠ awa e̠mar eloghom ma̠ i̠na.
MAR 1:35 D̠a̠ ob̠om ame̠ghe̠le̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ esi ola̠ od̠i kukunum a̠siseiny a̠siseiny.
MAR 1:36 Sa̠ Asai̠mo̠n na̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ i̠na bho̠ id̠igh o̠bho̠ro̠gh o̠yo̠.
MAR 1:37 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh anwa.”
MAR 1:38 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Id̠ighi ta̠ oten o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ipa̠n a̠risisi, d̠a̠ re̠ma iyed̠i ya̠ itua̠n bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ ami̠ agba ani̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ a̠nigha̠ awa. Ezin bho̠ ami̠ i̠tu̠n o̠ku̠a a̠ru.”
MAR 1:39 Sa̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a ma̠ e̠ma a̠ten e̠ma d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh Agalili, agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠rutu u̠gala d̠awa, sa̠ a̠zegi ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh asi̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ a̠ruzu a̠nwunom.
MAR 1:40 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh a̠ru ra̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Wa̠nwuna̠! Ku̠gba ma̠ anwa ta̠ a̠ma̠ra̠, bha̠ koko ami̠ ma̠ ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠.”
MAR 1:41 Sa̠ igbirigbir o̠ni̠ bho̠ id̠ighi ma̠ A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ i̠na a̠selegheni ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠kula̠n i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ a̠ma̠ra̠. B̠ab̠ala!”
MAR 1:42 Sa̠ asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh bho̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ab̠ab̠ala.
MAR 1:43 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠ a̠ten a̠yel, sa̠ aghaghana i̠na ma̠a̠:
MAR 1:44 “Bi̠ghe̠! Ko o̠gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ gi̠e̠ ka̠ a̠leriom ozu d̠oyom ma̠ okur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ akpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ozu wa̠ A̠mozizi ato̠ bho̠, ma̠ oleriom ma̠ anwa na̠ a̠d̠um.”
MAR 1:45 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, i̠na a̠ten agi̠ ka̠ agba ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠ kesi kesi, ma̠ ola̠ o̠du̠ ogir ilologia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ asi̠saragi̠an agi̠ ma̠ egbeiny. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, A̠zizo̠s na̠ opita̠ d̠o̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ebhugh bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na aro̠ghan d̠a̠ etire a̠risisi ya̠ od̠i kukunum. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, a̠nwunom i̠d̠u̠a kesi kesi eru d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 2:1 Ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mula̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ Akapanu̠m. Sa̠ a̠nwunom i̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠a̠, i̠na od̠i d̠a̠ otu d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.
MAR 2:2 Sa̠ ro̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ikokod̠ia̠n d̠a̠ otu bho̠ imuzo ma̠ ola̠ e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ otu bho̠ na̠ o̠mara d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ otu bho̠, na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠. Sa̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.
MAR 2:3 Sa̠ inya̠ a̠nwunom irol o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠b̠ogina̠ ma̠ obhin ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ o̠yo̠.
MAR 2:4 Igiel bho̠ awa orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh e̠ti̠ti̠gha od̠igh bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠. Sa̠ awa i̠si̠n ibhun d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ i̠kpakpagi̠o̠n imutiom oyol d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu bho̠. Sa̠ i̠wo̠lo̠me̠ni̠ isoroni i̠na d̠a̠ a̠kporokporo bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 2:5 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠awa bho̠, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ bho̠, na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠oyom.”
MAR 2:6 Sa̠ idi ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠, id̠igh i̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ epura̠n d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa ma̠a̠,
MAR 2:7 “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ o̠ni̠ onon na̠ a̠fugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠! A̠nyen ta̠ a̠rue awe̠le̠man i̠karabh ta̠ o̠ni̠, a̠ten A̠zib̠a̠?”
MAR 2:8 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s a̠loghoma̠n d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an rologi d̠awa, sa̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ inyin na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ rologi d̠inyin?
MAR 2:9 Oken wa̠ a̠b̠ur a̠pu ma̠ ofugh onigha̠ o̠ni̠ onon wa̠ na̠ a̠b̠ogina̠ bho̠, ‘Na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠oyom,’ bo̠d̠o̠ ofugh ma̠a̠, ‘B̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠bhin a̠kporokporo d̠oyom ma̠ a̠rile’?
MAR 2:10 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan ma̠a̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠de onon.” Sa̠ i̠na akparame̠ni̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ukula̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠,
MAR 2:11 “Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, b̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠bhin a̠kporokporo d̠oyom ma̠ a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom.”
MAR 2:12 Sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ a̠bhin a̠kporokporo d̠o̠yo̠ a̠rile d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ eb̠la̠ awa ad̠u̠a, ma̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ awa ima̠gha̠, sa̠ awa itutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “I̠yar ta̠ od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh abar ola̠ o̠ko̠no̠n!”
MAR 2:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠mula̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ aka o̠bhi̠i̠y bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ iru d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa.
MAR 2:14 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh erile bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh A̠livai̠, o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Ali̠fi̠o̠s ka̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ e̠fe̠m ogun otua̠-ebhugh, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Tu̠o̠no̠me̠ ami̠,” Sa̠ A̠livai̠ a̠b̠etina̠ atu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAR 2:15 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ o̠gho̠ na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠livai̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠izo igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh iru ra̠ id̠igh na̠ i̠na na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ id̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠. Sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom iten ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 2:16 Igiel bho̠ idi ogbo a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠bi̠gh ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠ed̠ia̠n id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh na̠ igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ awa ipura̠n ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere, ka̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠inyin na̠ a̠d̠ed̠ia̠n na̠ igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠ka̠rabh bho̠?”
MAR 2:17 A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠n a̠pura̠n onon, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ogbo ya̠ o̠nwe̠r d̠o̠ i̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ owil, ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r bho̠. Ami̠ iru ma̠ ra̠ olebh id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh, ya̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom d̠o̠.”
MAR 2:18 Aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Azo̠n na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠. Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Azo̠n na̠ ita̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, ya̠a̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom ine ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠?”
MAR 2:19 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ogbo erogh bho̠ ta̠ e̠tu̠n ere ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ od̠i na̠ awa bho̠? Yii, awa ko orue d̠o̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, ezin bho̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ od̠i na̠ awa.
MAR 2:20 Ya̠a̠, obhel na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ erogh bho̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa, sa̠ awa ta̠ ene ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠.
MAR 2:21 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin o̠go̠go̠ra omom ukpe na̠ ab̠ad̠i̠ ma̠ opupu akapa bo̠. Ezin bho̠, esi wa̠ u̠b̠ad̠i̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠puruna̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ akapa bho̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ agu̠an a̠peleni ma̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ bho̠.
MAR 2:22 Obha̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ko o̠lo̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ imom a̠min d̠a̠ opupu akana ozu-e̠nam, bo̠d̠o̠ bha̠ akana ozu-e̠nam bho̠ ta̠ a̠pol, sa̠ a̠min bho̠ ta̠ ezugia̠n ebhe, sa̠ akana bho̠ ta̠ api̠an. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, na̠ o̠lo̠gh imom a̠min d̠a̠ imom rakana ozu-e̠nam.”
MAR 2:23 A̠mite ma̠ ola̠ d̠a̠ odi A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osirepobh bho̠, A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ eten d̠a̠ ari̠si̠ i̠bu̠kpa, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ib̠oghi ma̠ itu i̠bu̠kpa bho̠.
MAR 2:24 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Nagha! Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ awa na̠ egir abar ola̠ oloko bho̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh bho̠?”
MAR 2:25 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ abar wa̠ A̠devidi a̠gir igiel bho̠ o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠na sekina̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ i̠na bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAR 2:26 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu akpu̠ru̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m wa̠ Abi̠ata aro̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ okur bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ abe̠re̠di̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ ya̠ i̠ro̠ inigha̠ ma̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ku̠ku̠m ma̠ od̠e. Sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ nyen a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ i̠na bho̠.”
MAR 2:27 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Umutiom A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠-epobh bho̠ onigha̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ u̠le̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ o̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ epobh bho̠.
MAR 2:28 Ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ bha̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠ epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠.”
MAR 3:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mina̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠. Odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ na̠ akpari̠an aro̠ ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAR 3:2 Idi ogbo d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠ghan e̠kal abar ola̠ odin ob̠ologiom A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ awa ikimeni na̠ egon o̠bi̠gh ku̠gba ma̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠koko ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠.
MAR 3:3 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ akpari̠an bho̠ ma̠a̠, “B̠etina̠ ma̠ amara d̠a̠ a̠misigh eb̠la̠ ogbo.”
MAR 3:4 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ere ma̠ abar wa̠ oloko bho̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ ogir d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠: ogir ib̠eb̠i bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ ogir i̠karabh, otenemeni o̠ni̠ onigha̠ a̠ghud̠um bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ ogigh o̠ni̠?” Ya̠a̠, awa inima̠ i̠ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m.
MAR 3:5 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kpon eb̠la̠ awa a̠kitineni̠ na̠ ibom i̠gam, ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ e̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠awa bho̠, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Selegheni ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom.” Sa̠ i̠na a̠selegheni ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ a̠selegha̠n a̠bhon.
MAR 3:6 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a ka̠ imimia̠n na̠ ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m ta̠ E̠ro̠d igboloma̠ i̠na, ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa ta̠ ebhin egigh i̠na.
MAR 3:7 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ aka o̠bhi̠i̠y eko. Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ Agalili na̠ A̠zudia̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
MAR 3:8 Ipa̠n ro̠lo̠gh ya̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, na̠ Idumia̠ na̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan, na̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma Ataya na̠ Asi̠do̠n. Eb̠la̠ awa iru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n e̠mi̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir bho̠.
MAR 3:9 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ awa eguri ma̠ oghugh esisa̠n i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠igh, bo̠ka̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ i̠ni̠ro̠m i̠na.
MAR 3:10 Ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠koko ma̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu asu̠nwe̠r, ma̠ ola̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ ad̠ien kere kere asu̠nwe̠r na̠ ekukurugha̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ka̠ okula̠n o̠yo̠.
MAR 3:11 Ka̠ obhel ka̠ obhel ola̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ e̠b̠am i̠bi̠gh i̠na, sa̠ awa ta̠ emeleghu d̠a̠ a̠de emulughu d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ efugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAR 3:12 Sa̠ i̠na alo̠gh e̠mi̠ ab̠ab̠agi̠na awa ma̠a̠, od̠ighi̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ eloghom i̠na.
MAR 3:13 A̠zizo̠s asi̠n d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu sa̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan oru d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠. Sa̠ awa iru.
MAR 3:14 Sa̠ i̠na aso̠n d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal, a̠ghol awa ma̠ ogbo-ogir d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ ed̠igh na̠ i̠na e̠ro̠, na̠ oruom awa o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ o̠sasaragi̠,
MAR 3:15 na̠ onigha̠ awa ma̠ a̠limon obhin ozegi i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh o̠si̠ghe̠gi̠.
MAR 3:16 I̠nye̠n d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo ya̠ i̠na aso̠n bho̠: Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ i̠na a̠ghol A̠pita̠ bho̠.
MAR 3:17 A̠zemsi̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Aze̠bidi, na̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠ Azo̠n (ya̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ghol ma̠ A̠boanazis, wa̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “anwi̠i̠ny agbararan bho̠”),
MAR 3:18 na̠ Anduru, na̠ A̠filip, na̠ Abatolomio, na̠ Amatiu, na̠ Ato̠mo̠si̠, na̠ A̠zemsi o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Ali̠fi̠o̠s, na̠ Atadi̠o̠s, na̠ Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ ughol a̠d̠ien ma̠ A̠zilo̠t bho̠,
MAR 3:19 na̠ A̠zuda̠s I̠skari̠o̠t, wa̠ ra̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠.
MAR 3:20 Odi obhel A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu wa̠ i̠na na̠ aro̠ghan bho̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ikokod̠ia̠n, ma̠ ola̠ i̠na sekina̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ irue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ od̠e ed̠ia̠n nyen.
MAR 3:21 D̠a̠ obhel bho̠ ogbo a̠ghisia̠n ta̠ A̠zizo̠s i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ emite bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ obhin o̠yo̠ o̠d̠u̠a, ezin bho̠ na̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, “I̠na bo̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.”
MAR 3:22 Sa̠ ogbo a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m iru ra̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ onon na̠ a̠bhum A̠belzibul, sa̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠limon ta̠ A̠belzibul, we̠mu̠ a̠ruru bho̠ na̠ a̠ze ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ a̠zegi.”
MAR 3:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhelegi awa a̠kokod̠i. Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Eru bho̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠ze ma̠ eru asi̠ghe̠?
MAR 3:24 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ a̠de e̠ma na̠ aru̠gi̠an na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠, a̠de e̠ma obha̠ ko orue d̠o̠ amara.
MAR 3:25 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ eghun otu na̠ aru̠gi̠an na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠, eghun otu obha̠ ko orue d̠o̠ amara.
MAR 3:26 Sa̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ Eru bho̠ na̠ aru̠gi̠an na̠ a̠wia̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ko orue d̠o̠ amara; o̠ku̠a bha̠ ita̠ o̠yo̠ na̠ ekunugiom.
MAR 3:27 Ya̠a̠ opa̠n agu̠o̠ o̠gba. A̠nyen o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu omomona̠n ka̠ a̠ghumi ma̠ i̠di̠ar d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, a̠sigimeni ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ abhad̠i̠ ma̠ omomona̠n bho̠? I̠se̠ kisa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue afo̠i̠ny otu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 3:28 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, i̠karabh ka̠ i̠karabh ya̠ o̠ni̠ a̠gir, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ ya̠ o̠ni̠ a̠fugh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man.
MAR 3:29 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, ko o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠. Ezin bho̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠sor oloko ogir i̠karabh ola̠ ta̠ aro̠ kid̠ud̠ul.”
MAR 3:30 A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠nigha̠ awa, ezin bho̠ awa na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ a̠bhin a̠limon i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ a̠gir ogir d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 3:31 Sa̠ onweni na̠ a̠rumor ta̠ A̠zizo̠s iru ra̠ i̠mara d̠a̠ etire. Sa̠ awa iruom a̠duom odi o̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠gba onigha̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠ i̠na a̠ru ra̠ abi̠ghan awa.
MAR 3:32 Ya̠a̠, o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom na̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de eko i̠na, sa̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, onweni d̠oyom na̠ a̠rumor d̠oyom od̠i d̠a̠ etire na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠bi̠ghan oyom.
MAR 3:33 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Onweni d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠rumor d̠ami̠ ka̠ wa̠ a̠nyen?”
MAR 3:34 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kpon awa ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de bho̠ a̠kitineni, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ikpone, i̠nye̠n onweni d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠rumor d̠ami̠.
MAR 3:35 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ato̠ bho̠, bha̠ umor d̠ami̠, na̠ u̠marani̠ d̠ami̠, na̠ onweni d̠ami̠.”
MAR 4:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠puta̠ ake̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ aka o̠bhi̠i̠y eko. Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom isor esi bho̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y eko bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ egbolom.
MAR 4:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin ra̠sidogh atu̠ghu̠me̠ni awa ma̠ a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar agba ma̠a̠:
MAR 4:3 “I̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠nagha o! Ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ ogbebh ed̠ia̠n.
MAR 4:4 Sa̠ a̠mite ma̠ ola̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠kpo ma̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠ asar bho̠, sa̠ idi ikpo imel d̠a̠ eten, sa̠ i̠nu̠r iru ra̠ ikpokpoiny id̠e i̠mado̠n.
MAR 4:5 Ya̠a̠, idi ikpo sa̠ imel d̠a̠ a̠de o̠gbe̠o̠ma, esi ola̠ o̠do̠gho̠l bho̠ okud̠um d̠o̠. Sa̠ awa i̠rabh epa̠ ma̠ o̠su̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠do̠gho̠l bho̠ okud̠um d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAR 4:6 Ya̠a̠ igiel ogogo a̠mite bho̠, sa̠ i̠nyu̠n i̠ghaghara d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ osi d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠ka bho̠.
MAR 4:7 Sa̠ idi ikpo imel d̠a̠ e̠ko̠ko̠ ib̠ub̠ulom, sa̠ ib̠ub̠ulom bho̠ i̠su̠ ikpegiom ed̠ia̠n bho̠ i̠bhu̠ghu̠d̠i̠, ma̠ ola̠ awa o̠su̠ d̠o̠ emum itu.
MAR 4:8 “Ya̠a̠, idi ikpo bho̠ imel d̠a̠ ob̠eb̠i a̠de, sa̠ i̠su̠ imite, imum a̠d̠izo itu. Idi imum a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh (30) a̠bin ya̠ ubhin ugbebh bho̠, idi e̠rabharabh (60) a̠bin, idi i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100) a̠bin.”
MAR 4:9 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to, anagha o!”
MAR 4:10 D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ A̠zizo̠s ku̠ku̠m odi ma̠ esi, sa̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo ogir bho̠, na̠ ipa̠n ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠, ipura̠n i̠na ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ra̠sidogh bho̠.
MAR 4:11 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ inyin bha̠, na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ologhom i̠di̠ar e̠wo̠gi̠na irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Ya̠a̠, ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ ani̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠inyin bho̠, kabar kabar bha̠ awa ta̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n d̠a̠ a̠sidogh.
MAR 4:12 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, “ ‘awa ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ okpon okpon, ya̠a̠ awa ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠, ta̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠a̠ awa ko o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠. B̠o̠ka̠ awa itiba̠ra̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠awa!’”
MAR 4:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin u̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ ezin a̠sidogh onon ke̠re̠? O̠ku̠a ka̠ inyin ta̠ od̠ighi eka̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan eb̠la̠ ra̠sidogh?
MAR 4:14 Ogbebhma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠ a̠gbebh ikpo a̠fugh bho̠.
MAR 4:15 Ikpo ya̠ imel d̠a̠ eten bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠, agu̠o̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n ikpo a̠fugh bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ Eru bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ asi̠ghe̠gi̠ ma̠ ikpo a̠fugh bho̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa.
MAR 4:16 Ya̠a̠, ikpo ya̠ imel d̠a̠ a̠de o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n ikpo a̠fugh bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ ibhin d̠a̠ a̠libhon ologi i̠da ibhin.
MAR 4:17 Ya̠a̠, isi d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠ka, sa̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ ekud̠i obhel. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ali̠gam a̠ruzu na̠ ad̠agi̠an ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ awa ku̠ku̠m, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ikpo a̠fugh bho̠, sa̠ imel i̠d̠u̠a.
MAR 4:18 Ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ imel d̠a̠ ed̠um ib̠ub̠ulom bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n ikpo a̠fugh bho̠,
MAR 4:19 ya̠a̠ a̠tepa̠ sa̠ i̠nyo̠gho̠nyo̠gh e̠mara̠nwunom, e̠li̠la na̠ e̠me̠me̠m e̠mara̠nwunom i̠su̠ i̠mi̠no̠m ma̠ ikpo a̠fugh bho̠ ma̠ ola̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ omum itu.
MAR 4:20 Ya̠a̠, ikpo ed̠ia̠n ya̠ imel d̠a̠ ob̠eb̠i a̠de bho̠, bha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n ikpo a̠fugh bho̠ sa̠ i̠da ibhin, sa̠ imum itu: idi a̠d̠usubh na̠ d̠iobh (30), idi e̠rabharabh (60), idi i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100), d̠a̠ ikpo ya̠ ubhin ugbebh bho̠.”
MAR 4:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ asu̠o̠m ato̠di̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠bhin abafu̠ a̠kpegiom bo̠d̠o̠ ta̠ oguri d̠a̠ ekpukpu akpata od̠i ke̠re̠? I̠na ko o̠gbam d̠o̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ esi ola̠ a̠sora̠n ke̠re̠?
MAR 4:22 Abar ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ola̠ ko omutiom d̠o̠ bo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ abar ola̠ u̠wo̠gi̠ ola̠ ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ obhin omutiom oyol bo̠.
MAR 4:23 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to, amar amu̠gho̠n o!”
MAR 4:24 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mina̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ibhine ma̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠ ma̠ e̠tu̠o̠m abar. A̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ inyin ibhin u̠tu̠o̠m abar bho̠ bha̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ inyin ta̠ obhin o̠mu̠gho̠nyan, sa̠ ta̠ o̠lo̠gho̠m o̠gbam.
MAR 4:25 O̠ni̠ ola̠ ate̠i̠ ya̠ ib̠ui ta̠ o̠lo̠gho̠m o̠gbam. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ ate̠i̠ i̠ki̠kara, iya̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ bho̠ eka̠, ta̠ o̠wo̠r obhin.”
MAR 4:26 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bha̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n ola̠ a̠kpo ma̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n sa̠ asar d̠a̠ o̠si̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 4:27 A̠d̠igh a̠d̠uga̠la̠n, bo̠d̠o̠ etita̠n, ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠ na̠ a̠kod̠u na̠ asu̠ma, ya̠a̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠ na̠ e̠mu̠r na̠ e̠su̠ na̠ emite. Ya̠a̠, i̠na na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠ na̠ ebhin na̠ e̠su̠.
MAR 4:28 A̠de bho̠ na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ ekpo ed̠ia̠n na̠ asu̠ na̠ a̠mum otu; ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠pol a̠mutiom i̠mu̠nu̠mu̠n, sa̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom egum, ka̠ a̠tepa̠ sa̠ ta̠ a̠mum otu ola̠ ta̠ amar akpo̠.
MAR 4:29 Otu o̠bu̠kpa bho̠ ma̠ o̠kpo̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ ogbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ogh, ezin bho̠ obhel ib̠ua̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠lei.”
MAR 4:30 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ ta̠ obhin o̠tu̠o̠m ere? Bo̠d̠o̠, ka̠ i̠yar ta̠ obhin a̠kere a̠sidogh o̠tu̠o̠m?
MAR 4:31 Agu̠b̠an ekpo amu̠stadola̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin a̠gbebh d̠a̠ a̠lei, ya̠a̠ ekpo bho̠ aki̠r a̠pu ma̠ eb̠la̠ ipa̠n ikpo ed̠ia̠n,
MAR 4:32 sa̠ asu̠ a̠mite a̠ten obom oriren wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ i̠gha, sa̠ i̠nu̠r iru ra̠ ilo ma̠ a̠rutu d̠a̠ i̠gha bho̠.”
MAR 4:33 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh a̠d̠izo a̠sidogh ya̠ o̠ku̠a, a̠bhin atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ awa ta̠ erue e̠mu̠gho̠nyan.
MAR 4:34 I̠na na̠ o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ abar a̠nigha̠ awa, ma̠ ola̠ i̠na obhin d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠sidogh agba. Ya̠a̠, igiel i̠na sekina̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ku̠ku̠m od̠i, sa̠ i̠na na̠ amar na̠ agba kabar kabar na̠ asi̠si̠ghe̠ni̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.
MAR 4:35 A̠dule a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Id̠ighi ta̠ o̠b̠e̠i̠y d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y eko bho̠.”
MAR 4:36 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠we̠le̠man o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ka̠ id̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh wa̠ A̠zizo̠s od̠i bho̠, sa̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠b̠e̠i̠y. Sa̠, idi ipa̠n a̠rughugh i̠gbo̠gbu̠an awa i̠gi̠.
MAR 4:37 Sa̠ obom ebiri a̠sor d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y-eko bho̠, sa̠ abadi̠ bho̠ agam ma̠ ola̠ amu̠m ipoka̠n id̠igh na̠ emuzo d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠ ma̠ owiyom.
MAR 4:38 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s amanaghan d̠a̠ agba eti oghugh bho̠ agbam e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ob̠enegioma̠ e̠mu̠, sa̠ ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ a̠kod̠u. Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠su̠me̠ni̠ i̠na ifugh ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, a̠d̠ugh wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin i̠yar bho̠, na̠ ogboloma̠ d̠o̠ nyam ke̠re̠?”
MAR 4:39 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠etina̠ ab̠ab̠agi̠na ma̠ ebiri bho̠ ma̠a̠ “Kima̠!” Sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ abadi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “B̠okume!” Sa̠ ebiri bho̠ a̠kima̠, sa̠ abadi̠ bho̠ a̠b̠okum, sa̠ ekima̠ a̠mite.
MAR 4:40 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh awa ma̠a̠, “Ere ka̠ inyin na̠ oghil a̠rugugu? Ere wa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠?”
MAR 4:41 Sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa ma̠ ibom, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠pura̠n odi ma̠a̠, “Onon ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠, ma̠ ola̠ ebiri na̠ abadi̠ eka̠ na̠ e̠nagha i̠na?”
MAR 5:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠b̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y eko Agalili d̠a̠ agba ebhugh Age̠rasa.
MAR 5:2 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠sor d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh na̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ozu bho̠ a̠bia̠, ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠karabh esi bho̠ ra̠ ami̠nana i̠na.
MAR 5:3 O̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ o̠karabh esi, ya̠a̠ bebina̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠rue ma̠ o̠bhad̠i̠ o̠yo̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, ubhin eka̠ ma̠ i̠go̠ro̠go̠ro̠ o̠bhad̠i̠ i̠na isibhom d̠o̠ eguri ma̠ onin esi nyen.
MAR 5:4 A̠d̠izo igiel, ubhin gha̠n i̠go̠ro̠go̠ro̠ na̠ ikoli o̠du̠o̠m i̠na d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ na̠ a̠sike oguri ma̠ esi, ya̠a̠ i̠na a̠gbugbo gha̠n i̠go̠ro̠go̠ro̠ na̠ ikoli ya̠ ubhin u̠du̠o̠m i̠na bho̠, sa̠ a̠nwinigi gha̠n ikpo a̠rukurogh ya̠ ubhin u̠du̠o̠m a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ nyen. Sa̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ igba̠ ya̠ obhin osibh o̠yo̠ oguri onin esi na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
MAR 5:5 A̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n a̠d̠io i̠na na̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ o̠karabh esi na̠ d̠a̠ ranyu̠ od̠i na̠ d̠a̠ a̠rugugum, na̠ a̠mulughu na̠ a̠bhin i̠pad̠i̠ i̠gbaki̠ghe̠ na̠ a̠guyogh ozu d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 5:6 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh A̠zizo̠s ma̠ esi egbeiny bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ghil ka̠ a̠mel a̠kpud̠ia̠n a̠nigha̠ i̠na.
MAR 5:7 Sa̠ a̠bhin obom okoroko a̠mulughu a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ ami̠ ka̠ odi a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ere a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ odi? A̠zizo̠s, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Wagi̠manyu̠ A̠pu bho̠. Ami̠ na̠ a̠siseiny anwa d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ko ogbikimeni ami̠!”
MAR 5:8 Ezin bho̠ bha̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠karabh e̠mu̠gh mite ma̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠ onon.”
MAR 5:9 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠d̠ien d̠oyom ka̠ ubhelegi eka̠?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “A̠d̠izo,” ezin bho̠ i̠yar a̠b̠utu.
MAR 5:10 Sa̠ i̠na akparame̠ni̠ ale̠gh A̠zizo̠s ma̠ i̠na oze d̠o̠ awa asi̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh obha̠.
MAR 5:11 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, obom o̠lo̠gh roporopo i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ eb̠ub̠um a̠de d̠a̠ aka esi bho̠, na̠ eb̠u na̠ ed̠e.
MAR 5:12 Sa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ruome i̠yar o̠gi̠ ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ruzu roporopo bho̠.”
MAR 5:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ma̠ra̠ a̠nigha̠ awa. Sa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh bho̠ imite ka̠ id̠igh d̠a̠ roporopo bho̠. Roporopo bho̠ ta̠ elei agu̠o̠ o̠gho̠ o̠ni̠r (2,000), sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ eb̠ub̠um a̠de bho̠ ighil isor d̠a̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y-eko bho̠, i̠bhu̠ghu̠d̠i̠an imugughu.
MAR 5:14 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekponom roporopo bho̠ ighil ka̠ i̠gba d̠a̠ ibom na̠ i̠gbara re̠ma bho̠, ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠. Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ imite iru ra̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠.
MAR 5:15 Igiel bho̠ awa iru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu bho̠ ka̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de, na̠ a̠loghoma̠n ozu, a̠bura̠ ma̠ ibura̠, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa.
MAR 5:16 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠, i̠gba ma̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ozu bho̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠um, sekina̠ iya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ roporopo bho̠.
MAR 5:17 Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠le̠gh A̠zizo̠s ma̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ebhugh d̠awa.
MAR 5:18 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ozu bho̠ a̠puru ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Ma̠ra̠ ami̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m anwa.”
MAR 5:19 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Mula̠ ma̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom, ma̠ ka̠ agba ma̠ a̠mutiom ibom i̠di̠ar ya̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠gir a̠nigha̠ nyam bho̠, na̠ okpon igbirigbir ya̠ i̠na a̠leriom anwa bho̠.”
MAR 5:20 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠ten agi̠ ka̠ agba asasaragi̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh A̠d̠iobh Re̠ma bho̠, ma̠ ibom i̠di̠ar ya̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠gir a̠nigha̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠.
MAR 5:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠puta̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh ab̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ikokod̠ia̠n iru d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ aka o̠bhi̠i̠y eko bho̠.
MAR 5:22 Sa̠ odi we̠mu̠ okponom ma̠ otu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Azari̠o̠s a̠ru ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠. Igiel bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠,
MAR 5:23 ale̠gh i̠na akparame̠ni̠ agba ma̠a̠, “O̠gbara o̠nyani̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ ra̠ omugh. Siseiny, tue ra̠ agbam agu̠o̠ d̠oyom d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠koko i̠na ma̠ a̠d̠umeni.”
MAR 5:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh na̠ i̠na agi̠, sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zizo̠s iko i̠na ikiton.
MAR 5:25 Odi ani̠ ola̠ asi̠ na̠ e̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ ozu bho̠ ma̠ a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) ala aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAR 5:26 I̠na na̠ a̠gbika̠ ma̠ ibom d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ a̠d̠izo a̠riwil, a̠robh eb̠la̠ ikpoki d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ okokua̠n, ya̠a̠ esi bho̠ aro̠ ku ma̠ opu opu.
MAR 5:27 Igiel bho̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n iya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠kukurugha̠n d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠, awo̠l d̠a̠ aman ta̠ A̠zizo̠s ka̠ a̠kula̠n ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 5:28 Ezin bho̠, i̠na a̠ma̠ra̠ d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠kula̠n ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ku̠ku̠m eka̠, bha̠ ami̠ od̠um.”
MAR 5:29 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ asi̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠gbo̠ bho̠ isobha̠n, sa̠ i̠na a̠loghoma̠n ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠um d̠a̠ asu̠nwe̠r bho̠.
MAR 5:30 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠loghoma̠n ma̠a̠ a̠limon na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ adama ma̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “A̠nyen a̠kula̠n ibura̠ d̠ami̠?”
MAR 5:31 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ abi̠gh agu̠o̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom na̠ e̠ni̠ran eko nyam ekiton, sa̠ anwa na̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, ‘A̠nyen a̠kula̠n ami̠?’”
MAR 5:32 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s a̠kpon d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ a̠kitineni ma̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠kula̠n i̠na bho̠.
MAR 5:33 Igiel bho̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠loghoma̠n abar wa̠ na̠ a̠mutuma̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠rugugu, a̠bhin igiri a̠ru ra̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠bhin ya̠gia̠ga̠i agba ma̠ eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ abar bho̠ a̠mite a̠nigha̠ i̠na.
MAR 5:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠nyani̠ bho̠, ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠koko nyam. Gi̠e̠ na̠ ekima̠ ma̠ a̠miza̠n d̠a̠ egbika̠ d̠oyom.”
MAR 5:35 A̠zizo̠s od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ agba ma̠ i̠nye̠n, sa̠ idi a̠nwunom i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Azari̠o̠s ra̠ i̠gba i̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ekpo epobh o̠nyani̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠sobha̠n! Ko onyegi mu ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠.”
MAR 5:36 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhogia̠n asu̠gbagba d̠awa, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ u̠gala A̠zu bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ko oghil a̠rugugu, ma̠ra̠ ka̠ a̠ma̠ra̠.”
MAR 5:37 I̠na na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m o̠yo̠, a̠ten A̠puta̠, na̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n umor ta̠ A̠zemsi.
MAR 5:38 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ we̠mu̠ otu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh ka̠ a̠nwunom od̠i d̠a̠ asu̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an, sa̠ na̠ emulughu na̠ eleghe na̠ e̠gba ma̠ igbir.
MAR 5:39 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi otu bho̠, sa̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ odin ere na̠ o̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an, na̠ oleghe ma̠ o̠ku̠a? O̠nyani̠ bho̠ ta̠ omugh d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ na̠ a̠kod̠u ma̠ adala.”
MAR 5:40 Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠mo̠lo̠gh i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na. Ya̠a̠, i̠na a̠ze awa a̠mutiom, sa̠ a̠bhin onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na bho̠, a̠d̠igh agi̠ d̠a̠ esi wa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ aro̠ bho̠.
MAR 5:41 Sa̠ i̠na a̠sibh o̠nyani̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠a̠, “Talita, Kumi!” wa̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠gbara o̠nyani̠, b̠etina̠!”
MAR 5:42 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠ ake̠ ma̠ orile (i̠na d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ala). Sa̠ abar bho̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ ibom.
MAR 5:43 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s a̠bukiom awa ma̠a̠ awa o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ a̠mite bho̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ o̠ni̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ abar ta̠ a̠d̠e.”
MAR 6:1 A̠zizo̠s na̠ Ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠ten e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma wa̠ i̠na a̠mite bho̠.
MAR 6:2 Ate̠i̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ otu u̠gala bho̠. Sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n a̠d̠izo ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠na bho̠. Sa̠ awa ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “I̠na ate̠i̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n d̠a̠ a̠ken? I̠nye̠n ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien eloghom abar ya̠ unigha̠ i̠na bho̠? Ma̠ ola̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir ibom ilologia̠n ya̠ o̠ko̠no̠n?
MAR 6:3 Onon o̠du̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠meri bho̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Umor ta̠ A̠zemsi̠ na̠ A̠zosisi na̠ A̠zud na̠ Asai̠mo̠n d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Aru̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠ na̠ i̠yar i̠se̠n ke̠re̠?” Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ awa ighel i̠na.
MAR 6:4 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Esi ola̠ owil olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar bo̠, a̠ten d̠a̠ e̠ma wa̠ i̠na a̠mite bho̠, sekina̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ogbo a̠ghisia̠n, na̠ d̠a̠ eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAR 6:5 I̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir bebina̠ onin ilologia̠n i̠se̠, a̠ten o̠gbamagi̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ a̠ruzu i̠ki̠kara a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠, okoko awa od̠umeni.
MAR 6:6 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh i̠na ma̠ ilologia̠n ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠ten agi̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ eghighira̠ bho̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom.
MAR 6:7 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠, sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠ ob̠etina̠ erile, i̠wal o̠ni̠ ma̠ ebu, a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ a̠limon ya̠ obhin oze i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh,
MAR 6:8 sa̠ akparame̠ni̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko obhin bebina̠ abar ma̠ eb̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, a̠ten okpeti. Ed̠ia̠n o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, e̠kpa o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, okpoki o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ro̠kara ikpoki d̠inyin nyen.
MAR 6:9 I̠lo̠gi̠ane̠ ma̠ ragbaka, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ko obhin akapa onwegina̠.”
MAR 6:10 Igiel inyin ud̠igh d̠a̠ otu-esul, i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ tu̠tu̠n inyin ta̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.
MAR 6:11 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ inyin u̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma ola̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ o̠da d̠o̠ inyin ebhin, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ inyin, bha̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ ma̠ ekpukpu ma̠ ibhugh bho̠ ma̠ e̠si̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ re̠b̠ab̠a a̠sike d̠inyin. Obha̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ elegh ebhum ase̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.
MAR 6:12 Sa̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠gba imutiom ma̠ a̠nwunom etiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
MAR 6:13 Awa ize ma̠ a̠d̠izo i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh sa̠ izugioghom a̠d̠izo ogbo asu̠nwe̠r ma̠ amu̠nu̠, ikoko awa id̠umeni.
MAR 6:14 Sa̠ o̠du̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s asi̠saragi̠an ate̠i̠ kesikesi, ma̠ ola̠ O̠li̠le̠ma E̠ro̠d amu̠gho̠n a̠gboloma̠ i̠na. Idi ogbo i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠a̠, i̠na Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um, bha̠ ezin bho̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ a̠limon ya̠ obhin ogir ilologia̠n bho̠.
MAR 6:15 Ipa̠n ogbo sa̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “I̠na I̠lai̠za.” Ipa̠n sa̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠, “I̠na odi owil wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ igied̠i bho̠.”
MAR 6:16 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ E̠ro̠d amu̠gho̠n a̠gboloma̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “Azo̠n wa̠ ami̠ isobh e̠mu̠ igigh bho̠ na̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um.”
MAR 6:17 E̠ro̠d na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠bhin i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ruom a̠nwunom ob̠ol Azo̠n, o̠bhad̠i̠ o̠yo̠ od̠ighom ikoli, ma̠ ebula̠ E̠ro̠di̠as ani̠ ta̠ A̠filip umor d̠o̠yo̠, wa̠ i̠na E̠ro̠d akpakpa a̠bhin bho̠.
MAR 6:18 Azo̠n aro̠ ma̠ o̠gba o̠gba onigha̠ E̠ro̠d ma̠a̠, “Na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ nyam o̠kpakpa ani̠ umor d̠oyom obhi̠n.”
MAR 6:19 E̠ro̠di̠as a̠din o̠ku̠a a̠gurumeni ma̠ ologi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Azo̠n sa̠ abho̠ro̠gh ogigh o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠.
MAR 6:20 E̠ro̠d a̠ghila̠n Azo̠n sa̠ a̠kponom i̠na, ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠loghom ma̠a̠ Azo̠n o̠ni̠ igielake̠ sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. A̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar ya̠ Azo̠n agba bho̠ e̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠ ma̠ ologi ta̠ E̠ro̠d, ku̠ku̠m eka̠, i̠na a̠ba̠ra̠ ma̠ o̠nagha asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 6:21 Ekunuguma̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠sora̠n a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ E̠ro̠d a̠soroni ma̠ o̠d̠e̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ irileghom ebhugh bho̠, na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ e̠gham, na̠ ogbo ya̠ ilei abar d̠a̠ Agalili, ma̠ o̠ghe̠re̠ghu̠o̠m a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ u̠mar i̠na bho̠.
MAR 6:22 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ ta̠ E̠ro̠di̠as a̠d̠igh a̠ru ra̠ aghe̠r i̠gba d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠gba bho̠ id̠igh ologi ma̠ E̠ro̠d na̠ ogbo ya̠ isor d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ E̠ro̠d agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠gbara o̠nyani̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Puru ami̠ ma̠ abar na̠ abar ola̠ na̠ ebhir anwa ma̠ o̠te̠i̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam.”
MAR 6:23 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠ia̠n i̠zo̠ a̠gua̠n a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠ “Kabar kabar ola̠ anwa ipuru, ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam, aro̠ ku̠ ma̠ atu̠gi̠an irileghom d̠ami̠ eka̠.”
MAR 6:24 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ ad̠u̠a agi̠ ka̠ a̠pura̠n onweni d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ipuru ma̠ ere?” Sa̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “E̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠,”
MAR 6:25 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ a̠nugia̠n ka̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ O̠li̠le̠ma bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh anwa ma̠ onigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n epa̠ ma̠ e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠kpa imobh”
MAR 6:26 Sa̠ E̠ro̠d a̠kpon igbirigbir ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ibom, ku̠ku̠m eka̠ i̠na na̠ one d̠o̠ ma̠ ogineni o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ ri̠zo̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠d̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ isor d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠.
MAR 6:27 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom epa̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠kponom i̠na bho̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu ikoli bho̠ ka̠ osobh e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠sobh e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n,
MAR 6:28 sa̠ i̠na alo̠gh e̠mu̠ ta̠ Azo̠n d̠a̠ e̠kpa imobh bho̠ a̠bhin a̠ruom o̠nyani̠ bho̠, sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ a̠bhin agi̠o̠m onweni d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 6:29 Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ Azo̠n i̠mu̠gho̠n abar bho̠, sa̠ awa iru ra̠ ibhin eputa̠ ozu bho̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ id̠i.
MAR 6:30 Sa̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ imula̠ iru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s ra̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ awa igir bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ awa ubhin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAR 6:31 Sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom idi na̠ eru, idi na̠ e̠gi̠, ma̠ ola̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ bebina̠ e̠ti̠ti̠gha obhel ola̠ od̠e abar. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Itue oten o̠gi̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ i̠yar ku̠ku̠m ta̠ o̠ro̠, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin osira̠ ma̠ epobh ekud̠i obhel.”
MAR 6:32 Sa̠ awa id̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh iten i̠gi̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ awa ku̠ku̠m ta̠ e̠ro̠.
MAR 6:33 Ya̠a̠, a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom e̠bi̠gh igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠d̠u̠a bho̠ sa̠ i̠wal iloghom esi bho̠ awa na̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠. Sa̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠ma bho̠, ikpo ma̠ eghil i̠wo̠l ya̠ a̠wel ka̠ id̠ia̠ imisi ma̠ esi bho̠.
MAR 6:34 Igiel bho̠ awa isul bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pel a̠bhun, abi̠gh obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom, sa̠ igbirigbir a̠nwunom bho̠ id̠ighi i̠na, ezin bho̠ awa i̠gu̠b̠an ro̠nana ya̠ o̠ni̠ okponom o̠to̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin obhel atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar.
MAR 6:35 Igiel bho̠ a̠d̠io na̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Onon esi ola̠ od̠i kukunum, ya̠a̠ obhel bho̠ na̠ a̠ten.
MAR 6:36 Ruome ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ eten e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠sala ari̠si̠ na̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma ya̠ itua̠n bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ awa e̠bho̠ro̠gh abar egho ed̠e.”
MAR 6:37 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ inigha̠ awa ma̠ abar ed̠e.” Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a bha̠ i̠yar obhin ikpoki ya̠ ta̠ elei agu̠o̠ ogho e̠wala (200) a̠dinari̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ ogho ma̠ abe̠re̠di̠ onigha̠ awa ma̠ od̠e ke̠re̠?”
MAR 6:38 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin unwuna̠ ma̠ i̠ni̠ ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠? I̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ ekpon.” Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ ikpon sa̠ iru ra̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠yar unwuna̠ ogho ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠ na̠ i̠wal ikpo ina̠.”
MAR 6:39 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ e̠gba enigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ bho̠ ma̠ ebu ebu.
MAR 6:40 Sa̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ rebu i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100) na̠ eruba̠l na̠ d̠iobh (50) o̠ni̠.
MAR 6:41 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin ogho ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠ bho̠ na̠ i̠wal ikpo ina̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠tutumeni ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠puinyogh ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠ bho̠ na̠ ina̠ bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠ru̠gi̠ onigha̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠.
MAR 6:42 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa id̠e ilegha̠n,
MAR 6:43 sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ikokod̠i ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r abe̠re̠di̠ na̠ ina̠ ya̠ isugho bho̠, sa̠ imuzo ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal (12) a̠rukpuom.
MAR 6:44 O̠nu̠ ilobhiri a̠nwunom ya̠ id̠e ani̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠, ilei d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala (5,000).
MAR 6:45 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠nugi ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh od̠ia̠ ob̠etina̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠tsai̠da d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ o̠bhi̠i̠y eko bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na ta̠ aro̠ a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ oyeleghu.
MAR 6:46 Igiel bho̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ eyeleghu bho̠, sa̠ i̠na asi̠n igu ka̠ a̠d̠igh a̠siseiny.
MAR 6:47 D̠a̠ a̠dule a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, ma̠ igiel ola̠ oghugh bho̠ na̠ a̠misi d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io o̠bhi̠i̠y eko bho̠, bha̠ A̠zizo̠s ku̠ku̠m od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ egbolom.
MAR 6:48 Sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh ka̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠gbaghala ma̠ i̠d̠o̠m, ezin bho̠ awa i̠zo̠ghu̠ na̠ e̠dama ma̠ okukugh bho̠. D̠a̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa, sa̠ a̠ru ra̠ orile oten.
MAR 6:49 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ awa i̠bi̠gh ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rile d̠a̠ anyu̠ amu̠m bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠a̠ awa na̠ e̠bi̠gh egua̠de, sa̠ awa ikpogion izul imulughu.
MAR 6:50 A̠rugugu isibh ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s anu̠r agba a̠nigha awa ma̠a̠, “I̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin! Ami̠-o! O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu!”
MAR 6:51 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pel a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh wa̠ awa od̠i bho̠, sa̠ okukugh bho̠ a̠kugh a̠kunugiom. Sa̠ id̠igh ilologia̠n ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ma̠ ibom,
MAR 6:52 ezin bho̠ awa ta̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ obhin ogir ilologia̠n wa̠ ina̠ a̠b̠uyumeni ma̠ abe̠re̠di̠ bho̠, o̠mu̠gho̠nyan e̠mi̠ a̠limon ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
MAR 6:53 I̠nye̠n iten, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠b̠e̠i̠ ka̠ isul d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠, d̠a̠ Age̠ne̠sare̠t.
MAR 6:54 Igiel bho̠ awa ipel ibhun d̠a̠ egbolom bho̠, sa̠ a̠nwunom ilelegi epa̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 6:55 Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ighil igir eb̠la̠ ebhugh bho̠ ka̠ i̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo. Sa̠ a̠nwunom irod̠i d̠a̠ ra̠kporokporo ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠ghu̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na kesikesi ola̠ i̠na a̠misi.
MAR 6:56 Kesikesi ola̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠misi, a̠d̠igh o̠gbara e̠ma, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ obom e̠ma, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ re̠sala ari̠si̠, a̠nwunom ibhin ogbo asu̠nwe̠r e̠gi̠ ka̠ e̠te̠i̠ i̠na d̠a̠ regbolom a̠b̠ua̠, ma̠ i̠na ma̠ okoko. Sa̠ awa i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠ oma̠ra̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogbo asu̠nwe̠r bho̠ ta̠ ekula̠n bebina̠ akapa anyu̠ d̠o̠yo̠, d̠a̠ esi bho̠ u̠labh bho̠. Sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ ikula̠n i̠na bho̠ id̠um.
MAR 7:1 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ idi i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m iru ra̠ ikokod̠ia̠n sa̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na.
MAR 7:2 Sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh ma̠, idi ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ibhin aru̠gu̠o̠ ya̠ o̠b̠ab̠ala d̠o̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, o̠ku̠a bha̠ awa ititila̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ kisa̠ na̠ ed̠e.
MAR 7:3 Ya̠a̠, Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo A̠zu bho̠ id̠egha̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n ku̠gba ma̠ awa i̠mar d̠o̠ etitila̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa. Awa na̠ esibhom i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ d̠awa.
MAR 7:4 Ka̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ esi a̠b̠ua̠ iru, ka̠ awa otitila̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ egirghan bho̠, awa id̠e d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n. Sa̠ isibhom ipa̠n a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar iya̠ awa i̠tu̠ghan d̠a̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ bho̠, iya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠: otitol rokpa̠ko amu̠m, oloko amu̠m, ra̠sugh e̠ko̠lo̠gho̠l amu̠m.
MAR 7:5 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ezin kere ma̠ ola̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom o̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ bho̠, sa̠ na̠ ebhin aru̠gu̠o̠ ya̠ o̠b̠ab̠ala d̠o̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n?”
MAR 7:6 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Azaya a̠wa̠ ga̠i a̠gboloma̠ inyin, ma̠ inyin ribhelebhel, ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ uguri bho̠ ma̠a̠, “ ‘A̠nwunom i̠nye̠n na̠ ebhin aru̠nu̠ d̠awa na̠ edoni ami̠, ya̠a̠ rologi d̠awa esigima̠ ami̠.
MAR 7:7 Awa na̠ e̠ko̠l ami̠ ma̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠, sa̠ na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ iya̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠.’
MAR 7:8 Inyin ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ oloko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ o̠tu̠o̠m abar, sa̠ inyin na̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m ku ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ta̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠.”
MAR 7:9 Sa̠ i̠na ab̠aram agba ma̠a̠, “Inyin o̠mar ologhom agu̠o̠ oguri roloko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ aka, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin omutiom ita̠ inyin.
MAR 7:10 A̠mozizi agba ma̠a̠, izuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin, sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ onweni bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bha̠ ogigh.
MAR 7:11 Ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ ogba ma̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ oweni bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Kere kere e̠ne̠ghe̠ ola̠ inyin ka̠ u̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠,’
MAR 7:12 inyin uma̠ra̠ mu ma̠ awa egir abar enigha̠ ma̠ onweni bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠awa.
MAR 7:13 Inyin na̠ orughom ikpo a̠fugh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wokuma̠ a̠limon bo̠, ma̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ obhin i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠inyin na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny o̠gu̠man bho̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ ogir a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar iya̠ i̠gu̠b̠an o̠ku̠a.”
MAR 7:14 Sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠nagha ami̠, kere kere o̠ni̠, ma̠a̠ e̠mu̠gho̠nyan.
MAR 7:15 Abar ola̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ etire na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ d̠o̠ na̠ api̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ iya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ emite bho̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.
MAR 7:16 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to, amar amu̠gho̠n o!”
MAR 7:17 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ipura̠n i̠na igboloma̠ ma̠ a̠sidogh bho̠.
MAR 7:18 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin u̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ nyen ke̠re̠? I̠mu̠gho̠nyane̠ ma̠a̠, kabar kabar ola̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ etire na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠ d̠o̠, ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue api̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠?
MAR 7:19 Ezin bho̠ na̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ekpo ologi bho̠, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ okurogh, sa̠ na̠ a̠ten ati̠n na̠ a̠mite na̠ ad̠u̠a.” (O̠ku̠a bha̠, A̠zizo̠s agba a̠soroni ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ ed̠ia̠n e̠b̠ab̠ala.)
MAR 7:20 Sa̠ agba alo̠gho̠m ma̠a̠: “Abar wa̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠mite bho̠, bha̠ wa̠ na̠ api̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAR 7:21 Ezin bho̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi bho̠, d̠a̠ ekpo ologi o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ emite: i̠karabh i̠ru̠ru̠an, ari̠gi̠, a̠b̠igh, ogigh o̠ni̠,
MAR 7:22 od̠e e̠ma d̠a̠ ilom, o̠ku̠ku̠, igurumia̠n ologi, igelemeni, ipesi, a̠gbokia̠n, o̠gba o̠ni̠ o̠pi̠e̠, i̠re̠ma (obhuneni, o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ozu), ema̠ (esusula̠).
MAR 7:23 Eb̠la̠ i̠karabh i̠nye̠n na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi na̠ emite sa̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.”
MAR 7:24 A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Ataya sa̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠loghom, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠wo̠gi̠na.
MAR 7:25 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, ani̠ ola̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh a̠nyegi ma̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ amu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠mel agu̠ran d̠a̠ a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 7:26 Ani̠ bho̠ ola̠ A̠zu d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ ola̠ A̠fonisia̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh A̠siria̠, sa̠ ale̠gh A̠zizo̠s ma̠ oze o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyani̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 7:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ ed̠ia̠ ed̠e elegha̠n, na̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ obhin ed̠ia̠n anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ orobhod̠i onigha̠ a̠sib̠ogho.”
MAR 7:28 Sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, a̠sib̠ogho ya̠ na̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ekpukpu akpata od̠e bho̠ eka̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ na̠ emeleghu bho̠.”
MAR 7:29 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ani̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ ebula̠ awo̠ran d̠oyom, gi̠e̠, o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyani̠ d̠oyom.”
MAR 7:30 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ abi̠gh ka̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ na̠ amanaghan d̠a̠ e̠mana, sa̠ abi̠gh nyen ma̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyani̠ bho̠.
MAR 7:31 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mula̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ eghighira̠ Ataya agi̠ d̠a̠ agba A̠sido̠n d̠a̠ abadi̠ Agalili wa̠ a̠tua̠n Ebhugh A̠d̠iobh Re̠ma bho̠.
MAR 7:32 Sa̠ idi a̠nwunom ibhin o̠b̠aghab̠agh o̠ni̠ ola̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mar ofugh a̠fugh iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na, i̠le̠gh agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ agbam agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 7:33 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin i̠na d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ aka, sa̠ azo̠l asu̠nu̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ra̠to o̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ asi̠r i̠gho̠r d̠a̠ ad̠u̠nu̠ agu̠o̠ a̠bhin a̠kula̠n a̠nem o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAR 7:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny afi̠o̠ghu̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “E̠fata!” (a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “Guruna̠!” )
MAR 7:35 Sa̠ ra̠to o̠ni̠ bho̠ iguruna̠ epa̠, sa̠ abar wa̠ na̠ a̠sibhom a̠nem d̠o̠yo̠ ako̠ti̠na, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh abar geregere.
MAR 7:36 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s aghaghana ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠a̠, awa o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ imite bho̠ e̠sasaragi̠, ya̠a̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠bhin aghaghana awa bho̠, bha̠ agu̠o̠ awa ibhin i̠gba i̠sasaragi̠.
MAR 7:37 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n a̠nwunom. Sa̠ awa i̠gba ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ amar a̠gir eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar. Remua̠ bho̠ na̠ efugh a̠fugh, sa̠ i̠b̠aghab̠agh bho̠ na̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n abar.”
MAR 8:1 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom emula̠ ekokod̠ia̠n na̠ i̠na, ma̠ ola̠ abar ola̠ awa ta̠ ed̠e na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠,
MAR 8:2 “Igbirigbir a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ed̠ighi ami̠, ezin bho̠ awa na̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ ami̠ i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ unwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ awa ta̠ ed̠e.
MAR 8:3 Ku̠gba ma̠ ami̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠ oyel o̠ko̠i̠, bha̠ idi ta̠ e̠fu̠mu̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠. Idi awa i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ esi egbeiny eru.”
MAR 8:4 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar ta̠ orue o̠te̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n d̠a̠ a̠ken, d̠a̠ esi ola̠ kukunum o̠ko̠no̠n, ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ elei awa ma̠ od̠e?”
MAR 8:5 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin unwuna̠ ma̠ i̠ni̠ ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Od̠ua̠l.”
MAR 8:6 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ a̠de, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin od̠ua̠l ikpogh abre̠di̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ali̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠pupugion a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ma̠ o̠ru̠gi̠, sa̠ awa i̠ru̠gi̠ inigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠.
MAR 8:7 O̠nyi̠ki̠kara i̠gbara ina̠ e̠ro̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠tutumeni a̠ruom awa nyen o̠ru̠gi̠.
MAR 8:8 Sa̠ awa id̠e, sa̠ id̠e ilegha̠n. Ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ikpokpo ma̠ i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r isughia̠n bho̠, bha̠ ilei od̠ua̠l a̠rukpuom.
MAR 8:9 A̠nwunom bho̠ ilei agu̠o̠ d̠iobh o̠ni̠r (4,000) o̠ni̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom awa ma̠ oten oyel.
MAR 8:10 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Adalmanuta.
MAR 8:11 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ iru sa̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠anan o̠yo̠. D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠d̠a o̠yo̠ okpon, sa̠ awa ipuru ma̠ i̠na a̠leriom elegh ola̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru.
MAR 8:12 Sa̠ i̠na afi̠o̠ghu̠ ma̠ ibom d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ma̠ ola̠ amu̠m onon na̠ epuru ma̠ elegh bho̠? Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ elegh ola̠ ta̠ onigha̠ ma̠ amu̠m onon bo̠.”
MAR 8:13 Sa̠ i̠na awe̠le̠man awa ad̠u̠a ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ oghugh ab̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ agba uwed̠i.
MAR 8:14 Awa iweleta̠n obhin ed̠ia̠n, a̠sigimeni ma̠ onin ekpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠ ola̠ awa inwuna̠ d̠a̠ oghugh bho̠.
MAR 8:15 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kikiom awa agba ma̠a̠, “Ilelegi, ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ a̠yist ta̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ a̠yist ta̠ E̠ro̠d.”
MAR 8:16 Sa̠ awa id̠igh i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ i̠yar onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.”
MAR 8:17 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠nyan, sa̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ma̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ o̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ogboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠? I̠se̠n eka̠ bha̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan ke̠re̠? Rologi d̠inyin ta̠ okperina̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠?
MAR 8:18 Ikpo a̠rid̠ien od̠i inyin, ya̠a̠ inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh abar ke̠re̠? Ra̠to od̠i inyin, ya̠a̠ inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n abar ke̠re̠? Inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an ke̠re̠?
MAR 8:19 Obhel bho̠ ami̠ ipuinyogh ogho ikpokpogh abe̠re̠di̠ inigha̠ ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala (5,000) o̠nu̠ a̠nwunom bho̠, ka̠ i̠ni̠ a̠rukpuom i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r isughia̠n ya̠ inyin ukpokpo?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠, “D̠iobh na̠ i̠wal.”
MAR 8:20 “Obhel bho̠ ami̠ ibhin od̠ua̠l ikoko ma̠ d̠iobh o̠ni̠r bho̠, ka̠ inyin ukpokpo ma̠ i̠ni̠ a̠rukpuom i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r isughia̠n?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Od̠ua̠l.”
MAR 8:21 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ nyen, ke̠re̠?”
MAR 8:22 Sa̠ awa iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠tsai̠da. Sa̠ idi a̠nwunom ibhin o̠ni̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien iru ra̠ i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠ okula̠n o̠ni̠ bho̠.
MAR 8:23 Sa̠ i̠na a̠sibh o̠ni̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ a̠rileghom ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, asi̠r i̠gho̠r d̠a̠ a̠rid̠ien o̠ni̠ bho̠, a̠bhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠puom a̠rid̠ien o̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ abi̠gh abar ke̠re̠?”
MAR 8:24 Sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon d̠a̠ anyu̠, sa̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ abi̠gh a̠nwunom agu̠o̠ iriren iya̠ na̠ erile.”
MAR 8:25 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠puta̠ a̠bhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠puom a̠rid̠ien o̠ni̠ bho̠. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠kimigi a̠kpon, sa̠ a̠rid̠ien bho̠ imula̠ ibhon, sa̠ amar abi̠gh eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar geregere.
MAR 8:26 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom i̠na ma̠a̠, i̠na a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ aghaghana i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ko od̠igh mu d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.”
MAR 8:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠d̠u̠a i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma A̠sizeria̠ A̠filipai̠ bho̠. Agu̠o̠ awa na̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠nwunom na̠ e̠gba ma̠ ami̠ ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠?”
MAR 8:28 Sa̠ awa i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Azo̠n owurmamu̠m bho̠; ipa̠n ma̠a̠, I̠lai̠za; ya̠a̠ idi na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, odi owil bho̠.”
MAR 8:29 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ o̠gba ma̠ ami̠ ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠?” Sa̠ A̠puta̠ agba a̠mutiom ma̠a̠, “Anwa Akrai̠st.”
MAR 8:30 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s aghaghana awa ma̠a̠, awa obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ igboloma̠ i̠na e̠gba enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.
MAR 8:31 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ akpe̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ma̠ ogbika̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar, sa̠ ikei bho̠ na̠ aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ ta̠ eghel i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ egigh i̠na, sa̠ ka̠ i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ na̠ eten, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠.
MAR 8:32 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ agba ma̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ asi̠si̠ghe̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ A̠puta̠ a̠bhin i̠na ma̠ o̠nu̠ ma̠a̠, i̠na ofugh d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
MAR 8:33 Sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ a̠kpon ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ awo̠ran A̠puta̠ ab̠ab̠agi̠na ma̠a̠, “Eru bho̠, tene d̠a̠ aman d̠ami̠! Ezin bho̠ anwa na̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠o̠m abar, ya̠a̠ iya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠.”
MAR 8:34 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kokod̠i ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ ebhir o̠tu̠o̠no̠m ami̠ ta̠ aku̠a ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ aman, sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren d̠o̠yo̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠.
MAR 8:35 O̠ni̠ wa̠ ato̠ma ma̠ okighom a̠ghud̠um e̠mara̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ orobh a̠ghud̠um e̠mara̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ ami̠ na̠ ebula̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠, ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul.
MAR 8:36 Asu̠o̠ bho̠ ka̠ ere, ka̠ o̠ni̠ ate̠i̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon, sa̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠?
MAR 8:37 Ere ta̠ a̠lei o̠ni̠ ma̠ obhin onwegia̠n a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠?
MAR 8:38 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠din ami̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠ami̠ a̠d̠igh ari̠ghe̠l d̠a̠ amu̠m onon wa̠ od̠umom d̠a̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, na̠ erugh i̠karabh ado̠l bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ eka̠ ta̠ a̠din i̠na a̠d̠igh ari̠ghe̠l ma̠ obhel itileduom e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ta̠ ed̠igh na̠ i̠na eru d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠.”
MAR 9:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ idi inyin ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠ ko omugh d̠o̠ tu̠tu̠n awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh ka̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ná̠ a̠ru na̠ a̠limon.”
MAR 9:2 Odin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin A̠pita̠, na̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n asi̠n igu ola̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠, d̠a̠ esi ola̠ awa ku̠ku̠m i̠ro̠. I̠se̠ sa̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nwegia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠awa.
MAR 9:3 Sa̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ i̠b̠al, i̠mu̠, isosorogia̠n ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ bebina̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠de onon ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a bo̠.
MAR 9:4 Sa̠ I̠lai̠za na̠ A̠mozizi imite ma̠ i̠se̠ ra̠ id̠igh na̠ A̠zizo̠s i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an.
MAR 9:5 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, agu̠o̠ a̠bhon i̠yar o̠ro̠ i̠se̠n! D̠ighi i̠yar ogim i̠sar a̠rutu akpu̠ru̠: odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ oyom, odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ A̠mozizi, sa̠ odi ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ I̠lai̠za.”
MAR 9:6 (Ezin bho̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa ka̠ e̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ A̠pita̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ ofugh).
MAR 9:7 Sa̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh a̠kpegiom awa. Sa̠ okoroko a̠si d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Onon O̠nyi̠ etula̠n d̠ami̠. I̠nagha i̠na!”
MAR 9:8 D̠a̠ awai̠, sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh ka̠ A̠zizo̠s ku̠ku̠m od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAR 9:9 Agu̠o̠ awa na̠ esor d̠a̠ anyu̠ igu bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s aghaghana awa ma̠a̠, awa o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ awa i̠bi̠gh bho̠ enigha̠ bebina̠ o̠ni̠, a̠ten ka̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh.
MAR 9:10 Sa̠ awa ikighom abar bho̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa, sa̠ awa iguri i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an igboloma̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ “Ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh” a̠ma̠ra̠ bho̠.
MAR 9:11 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ere wa̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠ru bho̠?”
MAR 9:12 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠ru, ra̠ a̠selegi ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar. Ere wa̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠a̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠gbika̠ ma̠ ibom sa̠ ta̠ oghel bho̠?
MAR 9:13 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠; I̠lai̠za a̠ru, sa̠ awa ikpon abar abar igir igboloma̠ i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba ma̠ ta̠ emutuma̠ i̠na bho̠.”
MAR 9:14 Sa̠ awa iru d̠a̠ ogbo atu̠ghan iyed̠i, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ eko awa ikiton, ya̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ e̠ku̠anan awa.
MAR 9:15 I̠se̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na sa̠ id̠igh awa ma̠ ilologia̠n ma̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠yo̠, sa̠ ikpo ma̠ eghil ka̠ ibheleguma̠ i̠na.
MAR 9:16 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n o̠lo̠gh bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠ku̠anan awa ma̠ ere?”
