MAR 9:17 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ ibhin o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ ola̠ e̠mu̠gh emua̠ na̠ anyo̠gho̠gh a̠ru d̠oyom.
MAR 9:18 Ka̠ e̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠puom i̠na, sa̠ na̠ agu̠ro̠m i̠na, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠fuko d̠a̠ o̠nu̠, na̠ aghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ ozu bho̠ na̠ a̠kpari̠an. Sa̠ ami̠ iruom ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom ma̠ oze o̠si̠ghe̠, ya̠a̠ irue d̠o̠.”
MAR 9:19 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Sei! Amu̠m ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠to̠! Ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ na̠ inyin a̠bia̠ eka̠, kisa̠ inyin ta̠ oma̠ra̠? Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ne ma̠ ado̠l ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠to̠ d̠inyin a̠bia̠ eka̠? Ibhine ma̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠ eru.”
MAR 9:20 Sa̠ awa ibhin i̠na i̠gi̠. Agu̠o̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ abi̠gh A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ agu̠ro̠m epa̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠de sa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ asasalaghu̠, a̠kikila̠, a̠fuko ma̠ i̠gho̠r.
MAR 9:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n o̠we̠de̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Abar onon ka̠ ake̠ ma̠ a̠kere obhel od̠ighi o̠yo̠?” Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ake̠ d̠a̠ i̠gbara d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 9:22 Na̠ a̠robh gha̠n i̠na na̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ anya na̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogigh o̠yo̠. O̠ku̠a eka̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa ta̠ a̠rue a̠gir abar a̠gboloma̠, bha̠ kpone i̠yar igbirigbir ma̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar.”
MAR 9:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa i̠tu̠n ere na̠ a̠pura̠n ka̠ ‘anwa ta̠ a̠rue’? Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠, kabar kabar ta̠ a̠rue a̠mite.”
MAR 9:24 Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ a̠d̠umom; ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠ami̠ olei d̠a̠ eka̠, bhe̠le̠ ami̠!”
MAR 9:25 A̠zizo̠s ra̠ abi̠gh ma̠a̠, o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom na̠ eghil na̠ eru bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ab̠ab̠agi̠na ma̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa e̠mu̠gh emua̠ na̠ ab̠agh, ami̠ na̠ a̠mulughuom anwa, d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ozu o̠nyi̠ bho̠, ka̠ onyegi mu i̠na.”
MAR 9:26 Sa̠ e̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠mulughu, sa̠ alo̠gh e̠mi̠ a̠nuoghom i̠na ma̠ o̠si̠si̠laghu̠, sa̠ a̠mite ad̠u̠a. Sa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ aro̠ woma̠ na̠ a̠mugh, ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ i̠na na̠ a̠mugh.
MAR 9:27 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s a̠sibh i̠na d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ a̠b̠eton, sa̠ amara.
MAR 9:28 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ipura̠n i̠na d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ma̠a̠, “Ere wa̠ i̠yar orue d̠o̠ ma̠ oze o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh bho̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ bho̠?”
MAR 9:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ola̠ o̠ko̠no̠n ka̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠o̠, a̠ten a̠siseiny.”
MAR 9:30 A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ agi̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ i̠na o̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠loghom. I̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ Agalili,
MAR 9:31 ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ abar. Sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ogbo i̠to̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ egigh, sa̠ ta̠ egigh i̠na. Sa̠ d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠.”
MAR 9:32 Awa i̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ iwowa̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ ighil opura̠n o̠yo̠.
MAR 9:33 Awa ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ Akapani̠o̠m, sa̠ id̠igh d̠a̠ otu. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin u̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ere d̠a̠ eten bho̠?”
MAR 9:34 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠ro̠ b̠u̠b̠o̠m, ezin bho̠ awa i̠ku̠anan igboloma̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa bho̠.
MAR 9:35 Sa̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, sa̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh o̠ro̠ o̠pu̠r, bha̠ i̠na a̠d̠ia̠ aro̠ ma̠ wa̠ o̠gu̠man na̠ agu̠o̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom.”
MAR 9:36 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ amarame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa, sa̠ a̠sibh agu̠o̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠ni̠gha̠ awa ma̠a̠,
MAR 9:37 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ atu̠n a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ ada ma̠ odi d̠a̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny i̠nye̠n a̠bhin, bha̠ ada ami̠ a̠bhin. O̠ni̠ ola̠ ada ami̠ a̠bhin, bha̠ na̠ o̠da d̠o̠ ka̠ ami̠ a̠bhin, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ruom ami̠ bho̠.”
MAR 9:38 Azo̠n agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠yar u̠bi̠gh ka̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien d̠oyom na̠ a̠ze ma̠ a̠ruru, sa̠ i̠yar ukigima̠ i̠na, ezin bho̠ i̠na bo̠ ani̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠i̠yar.”
MAR 9:39 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko okigima̠ i̠na, ezin bho̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ a̠gir ilologia̠n ko o̠nu̠r d̠o̠ epa̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ami̠.
MAR 9:40 O̠ni̠ ola̠ owia̠n d̠o̠ i̠yar bha̠ od̠i na̠ i̠yar.
MAR 9:41 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ atu̠n a̠d̠ien ta̠ Akrai̠st a̠nigha̠ inyin okpa̠ko amu̠m ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠.”
MAR 9:42 O̠gho̠ro̠gi̠o̠m o̠gbe̠o̠ma d̠a̠ orum o̠ni̠ orobh o̠ni̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ abadi̠, ta̠ a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ ta̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ odi o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ ola̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ami̠, ma̠ omel od̠igh d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
MAR 9:43 Ku̠gba ma̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam omel o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sobhe ma̠ asi̠ghe̠. Anwa ma̠ obhin e̠gha ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ obhin i̠wal aru̠gu̠o̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ e̠banya, wa̠ ka̠ od̠im d̠o̠ bho̠.
MAR 9:45 Ku̠gba ma̠ a̠wel d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam omel o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sobhe ma̠ asi̠ghe̠. Anwa ma̠ o̠ro̠ ukula̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ onwuna̠ i̠wal a̠sike, sa̠ ta̠ orobh anwa o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠banya.
MAR 9:47 Ku̠gba ma̠ ekpo a̠d̠ien d̠oyom na̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam omel o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠, poko ma̠ asi̠ghe̠. Anwa ma̠ obhin onin ekpo a̠d̠ien od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ owuna̠ i̠wal a̠rid̠ien, sa̠ ta̠ orobh anwa o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠banya,
MAR 9:48 “Esi wa̠ igbukuma̠ ya̠ na̠ ed̠e ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠ ko omugh d̠o̠, sa̠ anya bho̠ od̠im d̠o̠ bho̠.”
MAR 9:49 Ta̠ obhin anya o̠sa ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ o̠me̠me̠ni̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ obhin ub̠on na̠ o̠me̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.
MAR 9:50 “Ub̠on ob̠eb̠i abar, ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ub̠on bho̠ na̠ a̠robh a̠lisibh d̠o̠yo̠, ka̠ ub̠on bho̠ ta̠ ed̠ighi eka̠ emula̠ esibh? Inwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lisibh ta̠ ub̠on d̠a̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin, ya̠ ekima̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin.”
MAR 10:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh A̠zudia̠, sa̠ ab̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ aku̠b̠o̠ Azo̠dan. Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ipita̠ iko i̠na ikiton, sa̠ a̠puta̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir gha̠n bho̠.
MAR 10:2 Sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ iru ma̠ o̠da o̠yo̠ okpon, sa̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Owolom ta̠ a̠rue a̠soroni ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAR 10:3 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “A̠mozizi agba eka̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ogbogina̠ ilom?”
MAR 10:4 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “A̠mozizi a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ onigha̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ire ogbogina̠ ilom, obhin osoroni ani̠.”
MAR 10:5 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “A̠mozizi a̠din ab̠agh e̠mu̠ d̠inyin age̠ ma̠ oloko obha̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin.
MAR 10:6 Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ale̠m awa ma̠ ‘o̠ya na̠ olobhiri.’
MAR 10:7 ‘Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, olobhiri o̠ni̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠ ma̠ oweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ ab̠araguma ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠,
MAR 10:8 sa̠ i̠wal awa ta̠ eten onin ozu.’ O̠ku̠a bha̠ awa bo̠mu̠ i̠wal, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ awa na̠ eten onin ozu.
MAR 10:9 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, abar wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ atu̠lo̠m bho̠, o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n d̠o̠.”
MAR 10:10 Igiel bha̠ awa imula̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu bho̠, sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na igboloma̠ ma̠ abar onon.
MAR 10:11 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠soroni ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ a̠bhin opa̠n, bha̠ a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ani̠ bho̠.
MAR 10:12 Ani̠ ola̠ a̠gbogina̠ ma̠ owolom d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ awal opa̠n, a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma.”
MAR 10:13 A̠nwunom ibhin i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny d̠awa eru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠kula̠n awa, ya̠a̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠b̠ab̠agi̠na ikigima̠ awa.
MAR 10:14 A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ agam a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ima̠ra̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ eru d̠ami̠, ya̠a̠ ka̠ okigima̠ awa, ezin bho̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny.
MAR 10:15 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠da d̠o̠ ma̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin agu̠o̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ologi.”
MAR 10:16 Sa̠ a̠b̠ola̠n o̠gbara o̠nyi̠, o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ i̠se̠, agbam agu̠o̠ a̠tutumeni.
MAR 10:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ erile, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠kpo ma̠ eghil ka̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n i̠na a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ere ma̠ abar wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠?”
MAR 10:18 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ atu̠n ere na̠ a̠bhelegi ami̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠? O̠ni̠ ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i bo̠, a̠ten A̠zib̠a̠.
MAR 10:19 Anwa a̠loghom roloko bho̠: ‘Ko ogigh o̠ni̠, ko od̠e ma̠ e̠ma, ko ob̠igh a̠b̠igh, ko o̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠, ko oniniom o̠ni̠, zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom.’”
MAR 10:20 Sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ Atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠koko ma̠ roloko i̠nye̠n keka̠ d̠a̠ i̠gbara d̠ami̠.”
MAR 10:21 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin obhel a̠kpon i̠na, sa̠ a̠ba̠ra̠ i̠na, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Onin abar a̠sugho, gi̠e̠ ka̠ a̠wol eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa inwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ ate̠i̠ e̠li̠la d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, ma̠ a̠ru ra̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠.”
MAR 10:22 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠zum d̠a̠ ebula̠ awo̠ran bho̠, sa̠ a̠ten ad̠u̠a, ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠gbo ma̠ ibom e̠li̠la.
MAR 10:23 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kpon ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ a̠gir sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ akpar aru̠lala ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!”
MAR 10:24 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠. Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mula̠ alo̠gho̠m ma̠a̠, “Anwi̠i̠ny d̠ami̠, amar akpar od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!
MAR 10:25 A̠b̠ur e̠nam a̠dol o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ oyol anu̠ga oten a̠pu ma̠ o̠li̠la ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAR 10:26 Sa̠ awa imula̠ ib̠ogina̠ ma̠ o̠gbam, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠pura̠n odi ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ a̠nyen ta̠ a̠rue a̠ten?”
MAR 10:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin obhel a̠kpon awa awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ bha̠ na̠ orue d̠o̠ a̠mite, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠o̠, d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ kabar kabar ta̠ a̠rue a̠mite.”
MAR 10:28 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Kpone! I̠yar na̠ o̠we̠le̠man kabar kabar na̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m anwa!”
MAR 10:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ awe̠le̠man eghun otu, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠rumor, bo̠d̠o̠ aru̠marani̠, bo̠d̠o̠ onweni, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠, bo̠d̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny, bo̠d̠o̠ od̠ighi, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ami̠ na̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠,
MAR 10:30 ola̠ ko o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh igiel ma̠ i̠se̠n d̠a̠ obhel onon bo̠: a̠d̠igh eghun otu, a̠rumor, aru̠marani̠, onweni, anwi̠i̠ny, a̠de od̠ighi na̠ a̠nwunom oponoma̠ ogbikimeni o̠yo̠ nyen, na̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul d̠a̠ amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.
MAR 10:31 Ya̠a̠, a̠d̠izo ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ta̠ eten d̠a̠ aman, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ aman bho̠ ta̠ eten d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠.”
MAR 10:32 D̠a̠ obhel bho̠ awa na̠ eten na̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠, A̠zizo̠s aro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠a̠ awa. Sa̠ ekpoyogh ologi na̠ a̠rugugu isibh ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠puta̠ a̠bhin d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ aka, sa̠ ake̠ ma̠ o̠gba i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ eru ra̠ omutuma̠ o̠yo̠ bho̠ onigha̠ awa,
MAR 10:33 ma̠a̠, “I̠nagha o! I̠yar na̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, sa̠ ta̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ esobh ase̠ omugh ebhumeni i̠na. Ta̠ eb̠eton i̠na o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ibhebhia̠n bho̠,
MAR 10:34 sa̠ ta̠ e̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ emurughom i̠na ma̠ i̠gho̠r, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gu̠ro̠gh i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ egigh i̠na, a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠ sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh!”
MAR 10:35 Sa̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n, anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ Aze̠bidi iru d̠a̠ o̠yo̠ ra̠ ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ a̠gir a̠nigha̠ i̠yar kabar kabar ola̠ i̠yar upuru nyam.”
MAR 10:36 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ere ma̠ abar wa̠ inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh ami̠ ma̠ ogir onigha̠ inyin bho̠?”
MAR 10:37 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “D̠ighi odi i̠yar aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom d̠oyom, sa̠ uwed̠i ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ okiel d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n d̠oyom.”
MAR 10:38 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠, “Inyin u̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ inyin na̠ opuru bho̠. Inyin ta̠ orue o̠d̠a d̠a̠ okpa̠ko wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ ad̠a bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠d̠ien owura̠ amu̠m wa̠ ta̠ owur ami̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAR 10:39 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠yar ta̠ orue.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ o̠d̠a d̠a̠ okpa̠ko wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ ad̠a bho̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ owura̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien amu̠m wa̠ ta̠ owur ami̠ bho̠,
MAR 10:40 ya̠a̠, o̠ro̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom d̠ami̠ bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ okiel d̠ami̠, bha̠ ami̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ ato̠ bho̠ d̠o̠. A̠dila̠de i̠nye̠n i̠ro̠ inigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ oguri osisa̠n bho̠.”
MAR 10:41 Igiel wa̠ d̠iobh ogbo ogir iyed̠i i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ rologi d̠awa igurom inigha̠ ma̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n.
MAR 10:42 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhelegi awa agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ologhom ma̠a̠, ogbo aru̠mu̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon i̠to̠ egboloma̠ awa, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠bu̠gh e̠mi̠ bho̠ na̠ eponoma̠ awa.
MAR 10:43 Ya̠a̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh o̠bu̠gh e̠mi̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin bho̠, aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠inyin,
MAR 10:44 sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh o̠ro̠ o̠pu̠r, a̠d̠ia̠ aro̠ ma̠ e̠bana ta̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwu̠nom.
MAR 10:45 Ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ oru d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠ro̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na a̠ru ma̠ o̠ro̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu onigha̠ a̠nwunom, na̠ onigha̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ obhin o̠ta a̠d̠izo ogbo.”
MAR 10:46 Sa̠ awa iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Aze̠riko. Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ Aze̠riko bho̠, bha̠ Abatimi̠o̠s o̠ni̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠timi̠o̠s aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ aka eten, na̠ a̠puru ma̠ ipupuru.
MAR 10:47 Igiel bho̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n ma̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t na̠ a̠ten bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ izul, a̠mulughu ma̠a̠, “A̠zizo̠s, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir!”
MAR 10:48 Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠b̠ab̠agi̠na i̠na ma̠a̠ i̠na a̠nima̠, ya̠a̠, i̠na alo̠gh e̠mi̠ omulughu ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir!”
MAR 10:49 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s amara kpom, sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠ obhelegi o̠ni̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠ oruom o̠yo̠, sa̠ awa ibhelegi i̠na i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Kpo̠luzu! B̠etina̠! I̠na na̠ a̠bhelegi nyam.”
MAR 10:50 Sa̠ i̠na ake̠gi̠na ma̠ akapa anyu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠robh, sa̠ a̠pel amara a̠rile agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 10:51 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ami̠ ma̠ ogir ere onigha̠ oyom?” Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “We̠mu̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh omula̠ o̠bi̠gh abar.”
MAR 10:52 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠, “Yele, ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠koko nyam.” Ogbo na̠ onin, sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ abi̠gh abar, sa̠ i̠na atu̠o̠no̠m A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠.
MAR 11:1 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ eten na̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, sa̠ iru ra̠ itua̠n Abe̠ti̠fagi̠ na̠ Abe̠tani d̠a̠ aka Igu Oliv bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ od̠ia̠ o̠gi̠ na̠ awa,
MAR 11:2 sa̠ agba a̠nigha awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma wa̠ a̠sumogha̠n inyin bho̠. Sa̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ od̠igh bho̠, inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ a̠rile. I̠ko̠to̠ne̠ ma̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠ ma̠ ebhin eru.
MAR 11:3 Sa̠, ka̠ o̠ni̠ a̠pura̠n inyin ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin na̠ udin ere na̠ ogir abar onon?’ Ma̠ e̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh orughom, sa̠ ta̠ anu̠r a̠mulumeni a̠ru ma̠ i̠se̠n i̠se̠n.’ ”
MAR 11:4 Sa̠ awa iten i̠gi̠, sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠ ola̠ na̠ o̠kpo̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ogigo d̠a̠ aka eten bho̠. Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠ko̠to̠n bho̠,
MAR 11:5 sa̠ idi a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ odin ere na̠ o̠ko̠to̠n o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠?”
MAR 11:6 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom awa bho̠, sa̠ ima̠ra̠ awa ma̠ obhin.
MAR 11:7 Sa̠ awa ibhin o̠nyi̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠ iruom A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ i̠gbamagi̠ ma̠ rakapa anyu̠ d̠awa d̠a̠ anyu̠ e̠nam bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s asi̠n d̠a̠ anyu̠ e̠nam bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de.
MAR 11:8 A̠d̠izo a̠nwunom i̠de̠ ma̠ rakapa anyu̠ d̠awa d̠a̠ eten bho̠, sa̠ ipa̠n ogbo igbodo ma̠ ra̠to iriren d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠ ibhin i̠de̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠.
MAR 11:9 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ bho̠ na̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ aman bho̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ omulughu o̠gba okue ma̠a̠, “Ozana! Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠! A̠zib̠a̠ a̠tutumeni i̠na wa̠ na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠!
MAR 11:10 E̠no̠gho̠man e̠te̠i̠ irileghom ta̠ obom o̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar A̠devidi wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠. Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ a̠pu bho̠!”
MAR 11:11 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ogigo Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠kpon a̠kitineni abi̠gh agu̠o̠ i̠di̠ar od̠i. Ya̠a̠ agu̠o̠ obhel bho̠ na̠ a̠ten a̠pu d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠tani̠.
MAR 11:12 I̠b̠ala bho̠, ma̠ igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ Abe̠tani na̠ emula̠ na̠ eru bho̠, sa̠ o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠na.
MAR 11:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ egbeiny abi̠gh oriren a̠fig ola̠ ra̠to a̠to imuzo, sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠ighoma̠ ka̠ i̠na ta̠ abi̠gh itu. Igiel bho̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ bho̠, i̠na na̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ bebina̠ otu oriren a̠ten ra̠to, ezin bho̠ ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel ra̠fig.
MAR 11:14 Sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠fig bho̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ o̠bi̠gh mu̠ ma̠ otu d̠oyom a̠d̠e tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul!” Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ e̠mu̠gho̠n i̠na.
MAR 11:15 Igiel bho̠ awa imisi d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ ozegi eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eghoyogh i̠di̠ar na̠ eb̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠b̠ua̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠. I̠na a̠kpululeni ma̠ rakpata a̠b̠ua̠ ta̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ enwegi ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ na̠ ri̠kasi̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ewod̠i ma̠ rukurosege bho̠.
MAR 11:16 Sa̠ na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin abar a̠b̠ua̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ rogigo Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
MAR 11:17 Sa̠ i̠na atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “U̠ge̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Ta̠ obhelegi ma̠ otu d̠ami̠ ma̠ otu a̠siseiny eb̠la̠ ra̠dede’? Ya̠a̠, inyin na̠ otenemeni ma̠ e̠fe̠m ib̠igh ma̠ a̠b̠igh!”
MAR 11:18 Igiel bho̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan agu̠o̠ obhin ogigh A̠zizo̠s. Awa ighil i̠na, ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ema̠gha̠ ma̠ ebula̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 11:19 Ate̠i̠ a̠dule, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.
MAR 11:20 I̠b̠ala bho̠ ma̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠, ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa na̠ erile d̠a̠ eten bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh oriren a̠fig bho̠ ka̠ na̠ aghi̠ghara d̠a̠ eb̠o a̠sor d̠a̠ i̠ki̠ka bho̠.
MAR 11:21 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ aru̠ru̠an abar wa̠ a̠mite bho̠ sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, kpone! Oriren a̠fig wa̠ anwa irogi bho̠ na̠ aghi̠ghara.”
MAR 11:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Inwuna̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
MAR 11:23 “Ya̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ igu onon ma̠, ‘B̠uruna̠ ka̠ a̠mel d̠a̠ abadi̠,’ sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ i̠wal rologi, ya̠a̠ i̠na a̠ma̠ra̠, bha̠ omite epa̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
MAR 11:24 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, kabar kabar ola̠ inyin na̠ esiseiny na̠ opuru, bha̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ inyin na̠ o̠te̠i̠ abar bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ o̠ku̠a a̠nigha̠ inyin.
MAR 11:25 Igiel inyin ub̠etina̠ u̠mara ma̠ osiseiny a̠siseiny, bha̠ i̠we̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ i̠karabh ya̠ inyin unwuna̠ ugboloma̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, b̠o̠ka̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ eka̠ awe̠le̠man i̠karabh od̠ighi̠ i̠di̠ar d̠oyom. [
MAR 11:26 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa na̠ o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh opa̠n o̠ni̠, bha̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ eka̠ ko o̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh od̠ighi̠ i̠di̠ar d̠oyom.”]
MAR 11:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo ogir d̠o̠yo̠ imula̠ iru d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m. Agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rile na̠ a̠gir d̠a̠ ologi Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, na̠ ikei bho̠, iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na,
MAR 11:28 sa̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ a̠bhin a̠kere a̠d̠ien a̠limon na̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n? A̠nyen a̠nigha̠ nyam a̠limon obhin ogir ogir i̠nye̠n?”
MAR 11:29 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ onin ipura̠n ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠pura̠n inyin. Ka̠ inyin u̠wo̠ran, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ agba ma̠ esi bho̠ ami̠ i̠te̠i̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠.
MAR 11:30 Owura̠ amu̠m ta̠ Azo̠n ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠? I̠wo̠rane̠ Ami̠!”
MAR 11:31 Sa̠ awa ibhin i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ i̠yar u̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru,’ sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠pura̠n i̠yar ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin udin ere o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ oma̠ra̠ asu̠gbagba ta̠ Azo̠n?’
MAR 11:32 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ i̠yar u̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ a̠ru’ ...” (Awa ighil a̠nwunom bho̠, ezin bho̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ Azo̠n owil ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.)
MAR 11:33 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “I̠yar uloghom d̠o̠.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ eka̠ ami̠ ko o̠gba d̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠dila̠de a̠limon wa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin na̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠.”
MAR 12:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s ake̠ ma̠ orogh a̠sidogh onigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Odi o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠gbebh ra̠grep d̠a̠ a̠lei d̠o̠yo̠. Sa̠ a̠ko ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ a̠kiton, sa̠ a̠gbo ma̠ ogugua̠ ola̠ omumogh a̠min a̠grep bho̠ omutiom. I̠na a̠lo ma̠ otu ipoiny nyen, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠ko̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ agi̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n ebhugh.
MAR 12:2 Igiel bho̠ a̠lei obhel o̠ku̠ a̠grep bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠limon odi e̠bana d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ obhin a̠bin imuma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ oru.
MAR 12:3 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ipuom i̠na, sa̠ id̠ul, sa̠ imulumeni i̠na ma̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠.
MAR 12:4 Opa̠n igiel, sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠limon opa̠n e̠bana d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ obhin a̠bin imuma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ oru. Sa̠ awa id̠ul i̠na, ib̠om e̠mu̠, i̠lo̠gh i̠na ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l.
MAR 12:5 Sa̠ a̠puta̠ a̠ruom opa̠n e̠bana ma̠ o̠gi̠, sa̠ awa igigh obha̠. Obha̠ agu̠o̠ awa id̠ulogh ipa̠n iya̠ uruom, ya̠a̠ i̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ idi.
MAR 12:6 “Opa̠n o̠ni̠ ola̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ oruom bo̠, a̠ten ogini o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ wa̠ i̠na a̠tula̠n ibom bho̠. Ekunuguma̠ bho̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠limon o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ awa, ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ awa ta̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠.’
MAR 12:7 “Ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠, odi a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi ma̠a̠, ‘Onon o̠nyi̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠. Itue ta̠ ogigh i̠na, sa̠ i̠di̠ar ad̠i̠a d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ a̠ten iya̠ i̠yar.’
MAR 12:8 Sa̠ awa ipuom o̠nyi̠ bho̠, sa̠ igigh i̠na, sa̠ id̠ud̠ur ozu bho̠ irobh d̠a̠ etire.”
MAR 12:9 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ere? I̠na ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ aze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom i̠ye̠ ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton a̠lei bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo.
MAR 12:10 Inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠, ma̠ esi bho̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ekpokpogh ikputu wa̠ iloma̠rutu bho̠ ighel bho̠ na̠ ra̠ a̠ten e̠ko̠ wa̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu bho̠;
MAR 12:11 onon abar ola̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠gir, sa̠ amar a̠bhon d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠i̠yar o̠bi̠gh’?”
MAR 12:12 Ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ eloghom ma̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh a̠sidogh bho̠ a̠gboloma̠ awa, sa̠ awa i̠ru̠ru̠an ob̠ol o̠yo̠. Ya̠a̠ awa ighil o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ awa i̠we̠le̠man i̠na iten i̠d̠u̠a.
MAR 12:13 Sa̠ awa ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ bho̠ iruom idi Afarisi na̠ idi ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m ta̠ E̠ro̠d ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠kpati̠ o̠yo̠ ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠fugh abar api̠o̠m.
MAR 12:14 Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠yar ologhom ma̠ anwa na̠ amar na̠ a̠gir d̠a̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠oyom, sa̠ anwa na̠ okpon d̠o̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠gurumeni abhe̠l opa̠n, sa̠ anwa na̠ a̠bhin ya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zib̠a̠. Gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, A̠sora̠n i̠yar otua̠ otua̠-ebhugh onigha̠ A̠siza̠ ke̠re̠? I̠yar otua̠ bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ i̠yar otua̠ d̠o̠?”
MAR 12:15 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠loghom ikoiny d̠awa sa̠ awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin udin ere na̠ o̠kpati̠ ami̠? Ibhine ma̠ a̠dinari̠ ma̠ eru ami̠ ta̠ abi̠gh.”
MAR 12:16 Sa̠ awa ibhin a̠dinari̠ bho̠ iruom i̠na, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Onon ka̠ a̠misigh ta̠ a̠nyen, sa̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ a̠nyen d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ita̠ A̠siza̠.”
MAR 12:17 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a bha̠, inigha̠ ma̠ A̠siza̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ta̠ A̠siza̠, ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ita̠ A̠zib̠a̠.” Sa̠ awa ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠ d̠a̠ ebul awo̠ran d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 12:18 Ogbo Asadusi ya̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh od̠i bho̠, i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠zizo̠s epura̠n ma̠a̠,
MAR 12:19 “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, A̠mozizi age̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar ma̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ umor o̠ni̠ a̠mugh awe̠le̠man ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ad̠u̠a, ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠, ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ani̠ umor bho̠ b̠o̠ka̠ amar anwi̠i̠ny a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 12:20 I̠se̠n bha̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor e̠ro̠; sa̠ okei bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ sa̠ a̠mugh awe̠le̠man ani̠ bho̠ ad̠u̠a.
MAR 12:21 Sa̠ oleghemeni i̠wal umor bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ bho̠, i̠na eka̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ sa̠ a̠mugh. Obha̠ onin agu̠o̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ wa̠leghemeni i̠sar umor bho̠.
MAR 12:22 A̠mite ma̠ o̠ku̠a oku̠a tu̠tu̠n sa̠ eb̠la̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor ya̠ ibhin ani̠ bho̠ imugughu, i̠mar d̠o̠ bebina̠ ekpo o̠nyi̠. Ekunuguma̠ bho̠ sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠mugh nyen.
MAR 12:23 Igiel ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ ka̠, ani̠ bho̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ani̠ ta̠ a̠nyen, d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ ani̠ bho̠ na̠ awal eb̠la̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor bho̠?”
MAR 12:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Inyin ta̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠ o̠pi̠e, ebula̠ agu̠o̠ inyin u̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ ratu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠limon ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠?
MAR 12:25 Igiel imumugh bho̠ ta̠ eb̠egina̠, awa ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny. Awa ko obhinogh d̠o̠ ma̠ anwani̠, sa̠ ko onigha̠nom d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠nyan anwi̠i̠ny nyen.
MAR 12:26 Iya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ta̠ eb̠egina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, inyin ta̠ osen d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire ta̠ A̠mozizi ma̠ asu̠gbagba ed̠um bho̠ ma̠ iya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na bho̠ ke̠re̠? Ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Ebraham, na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Azi̠ki̠, na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠.’
MAR 12:27 I̠na A̠zib̠a̠ imumugh d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na ola̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um. Inyin o̠mar o̠ru̠ru̠an o̠pi̠e̠!”
MAR 12:28 Odi o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ amu̠gho̠n i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an d̠awa, sa̠ abi̠gh ma̠ I̠na amar awo̠ran awa, sa̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ roloko bho̠ ka̠ oken a̠lei abar a̠pu?”
MAR 12:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Onon wa̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu bho̠: ‘I̠nagha, E Izre̠l! Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠i̠yar, i̠na ku̠ku̠m Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
MAR 12:30 Bhine ma̠ eb̠la̠ ekpo ologi d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ eloghoma̠n ozu d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an ologi d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mi̠ d̠oyom, ma̠ a̠tula̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom.’
MAR 12:31 Oleghemeni i̠wal bho̠, bha̠ onon: ‘Tula̠ne ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ aka d̠oyom bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa itula̠n ozu d̠oyom bho̠.’ Oloko ola̠ a̠pu ma̠ i̠nye̠n bo̠.”
MAR 12:32 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa amar agba ma̠ iya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠. Onin A̠zib̠a̠ ku̠ku̠m od̠i, opa̠n bo̠, a̠ten i̠na.
MAR 12:33 Sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠bhin eb̠la̠ ekpo ologi d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an ologi d̠oyom, na̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mi̠ d̠oyom a̠tula̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom. Sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠tula̠n o̠ni̠ etua̠n d̠oyom ma̠ agu̠o̠ ozu d̠oyom, a̠lei abar a̠pu ma̠ obhin i̠nam o̠kpe̠ alu̠kpe̠ na̠ ipa̠n ralu̠kpe̠.”
MAR 12:34 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh ma̠a̠ i̠na amar awo̠ran bho̠, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ osigima̠ mu nyam.” Sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠ne ma̠ opita̠ opura̠n abar na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
MAR 12:35 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ edin ere na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠ Witenemeni bho̠ ma̠a̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi?
MAR 12:36 E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ta̠ A̠devidi na̠ agu̠o̠ agba ma̠a̠, “ ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠a̠: “Ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ tu̠tu̠n ami̠ ta̠ a̠guri ma̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom d̠a̠ ekpukpu a̠sike d̠oyom.” ’
MAR 12:37 A̠devidi na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠bhelegi i̠na ma̠ ‘Wa̠nwuna̠.’ O̠ku̠a ka̠ I̠na aro̠ eka̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠?” Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ibhin a̠libhon ologi i̠nagha ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 12:38 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠. Awa iba̠ra̠ ma̠ opa̠n obura̠ ibom isosora̠n rakapa, sa̠ iba̠ra̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom obhin d̠a̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi obheleguma̠ awa d̠a̠ regbolom a̠b̠ua̠,
MAR 12:39 sekina̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠dila̠de edim d̠a̠ a̠rutu u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ a̠risisi edim d̠a̠ ro̠d̠e̠.
MAR 12:40 Awa na̠ eponoma̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠ na̠ e̠wo̠ro̠gh i̠di̠ar, sa̠ awa na̠ esiseiny iwewegh ra̠siseiny b̠o̠ka̠ olelegi awa. Awa ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ ibom ebhum ase̠.”
MAR 12:41 A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de a̠sumogha̠n igba̠ alu̠kpe̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠kpon agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom na̠ ebhin na̠ e̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ ikpoki ali̠se̠bh d̠awa bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh ka̠ a̠d̠izo aru̠lala na̠ e̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠b̠utu ikpoki d̠a̠ ologi.
MAR 12:42 Sa̠ odi onyigoiny ekpukele ani̠, agi̠ ka̠ alo̠gh i̠wal i̠gbara ikpoki ako̠pa, ya̠ ilei ape̠ni̠.
MAR 12:43 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ igba̠ bho̠, onyigoiny ekpukele ani̠ onon alo̠gh a̠pu.
MAR 12:44 Ezin bho̠, eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n na̠ ibom e̠li̠la d̠awa, wa̠ a̠ru, ape̠to̠n o̠nyi̠ esi d̠a̠ e̠li̠la d̠o̠yo̠ alo̠gh. Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ologi igoiny d̠o̠yo̠, i̠na a̠kpukpu ma̠ eb̠la̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠ alo̠gh.”
MAR 13:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Kpone! A̠libhon ikputu bho̠ na̠ a̠rutu bho̠!”
MAR 13:2 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh ibom a̠rutu i̠nye̠n? Bebina̠ ikputu ola̠ ta̠ a̠sughonom i̠se̠n ola̠ odi ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ ta̠ odi bo̠, ola̠ ko ob̠ogion d̠o̠ bo̠.”
MAR 13:3 A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ anyu̠ Igu Oliv d̠a̠ esumogha̠n Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ A̠puta̠, na̠ A̠zemsi, na̠ Azo̠n, na̠ Anduru, iru ra̠ ipura̠n i̠na d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ma̠a̠,
MAR 13:4 “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ka̠ ta̠ emite ma̠ a̠kere obhel? Sa̠ i̠yar ta̠ obhin a̠kere a̠d̠ien elegh ologhom ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ etua̠n omite?”
MAR 13:5 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ko ogelemeni d̠o̠ inyin.
MAR 13:6 A̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhin a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ eru ra̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ i̠na!’ sa̠ awa ta̠ egelemeni ma̠ a̠d̠izo ogbo.
MAR 13:7 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ko okperenuma̠ ma̠ igiel inyin u̠mu̠gho̠n oghur re̠gham na̠ i̠mu̠mu̠gho̠n re̠gham. O̠kpo̠ ya̠ o̠ku̠a ta̠ emite, ya̠a̠ o̠ku̠a na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ na̠ ate̠i̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠.
MAR 13:8 Ebhugh ta̠ a̠wia̠n ebhugh, sa̠ a̠de e̠ma ta̠ a̠wia̠n a̠de e̠ma. Ra̠de ta̠ eb̠ob̠omia̠n kesi kesi, sa̠ o̠ko̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n ta̠ a̠sor. Ya̠a̠, i̠nye̠n ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠pu̠r o̠ke̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ma̠ agu̠o̠ iguna̠ i̠mara.
MAR 13:9 “Be̠le̠ni̠, i̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠. Ta̠ ob̠ologh inyin obhin o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ a̠rutu osobh ase̠ d̠a̠ re̠ma bho̠ na̠ d̠a̠ a̠rutu u̠gala A̠zu, sa̠ ta̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh inyin. Sa̠ ta̠ o̠marame̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ a̠misigh ogbo aru̠mu̠ ebhugh na̠ aru̠lala e̠ma d̠a̠ ebula̠ ami̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠gba ami̠ onigha̠ awa.
MAR 13:10 Ta̠ od̠ia̠ o̠gba nyen ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ omutiom onigha̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠dede.
MAR 13:11 Sa̠ igiel ubhin inyin u̠gi̠o̠m awa, o̠ni̠ ko od̠ia̠ ma̠ e̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ obhin o̠gba o̠nu̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, i̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar iya̠ unigha̠ inyin d̠a̠ ogbo obhel bha̠. Ezin bho̠, inyin d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ta̠ e̠gba bho̠, ya̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.
MAR 13:12 “Umor ta̠ a̠wol umor ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogigh, sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ ta̠ a̠wol o̠nyi̠, sa̠ anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ ewia̠n ronweni na̠ ro̠we̠de̠ ma̠ o̠ze̠gi̠ awa.
MAR 13:13 Sa̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ta̠ asu̠a inyin d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ne tu̠tu̠n ka̠ a̠kunugiom bho̠, bha̠ oten.
MAR 13:14 “Igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ‘ka̠ ibom i̠pi̠o̠gho̠m wa̠ na̠ api̠e̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠’ na̠ amara ma̠ esi bho̠ osora̠n d̠o̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠ro̠ bho̠, (bha̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠sen bho̠ amu̠gho̠nyan), o̠ni̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠ a̠kpo ma̠ eghil ad̠u̠a agi̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh rigu bho̠.
MAR 13:15 O̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu osor d̠o̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠bhin abar d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mite.
MAR 13:16 O̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ o̠si̠ omula̠ d̠o̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin akapa anyu̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 13:17 Ekulom anwani̠ a̠rughun na̠ iya̠ anwi̠i̠ny od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ e̠mam d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠ye̠.
MAR 13:18 Ya̠a̠, isiseinye ma̠ o̠kpo̠ i̠nye̠n omite d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel a̠d̠igho.
MAR 13:19 Ezin bho̠, a̠d̠ien egbika̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠ye̠ ta̠ omite d̠o̠ ka̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton o̠le̠me̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ale̠m bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ra̠ ate̠i̠ i̠se̠n, sa̠ ka̠ omula̠ mu emite.
MAR 13:20 “Sa̠ ku̠gba ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ okperemeni d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel bho̠, bha̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠miza̠n bo̠. O̠ku̠a eka̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n a̠bhin bho̠, bha̠ i̠na na̠ a̠kperemeni ma̠ obhel bho̠.
MAR 13:21 Sa̠ d̠a̠ obhel obha̠, ka̠ o̠ni̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Ikpone! Akrai̠st od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n!’ bo̠d̠o̠, ‘Ikpone! I̠na od̠i ma̠ ebha̠,’ o̠ni̠ ko oma̠ra̠.
MAR 13:22 Rakrai̠st igunugha̠ na̠ a̠riwil igunugha̠ ta̠ emite eru ra̠ egir ilologia̠n, sa̠ ta̠ emutioghom relegh ya̠ obhin ogelemeni a̠nwunom, ku̠gba ma̠ a̠b̠ur, bha̠ ogbo iya̠ na̠ o̠so̠n bho̠ nyen.
MAR 13:23 Ikpona̠ o! Ami̠ nà̠ agba kabar kabar a̠nigha̠ inyin i̠se̠n kisa̠ obhel bho̠ ta̠ a̠lei.
MAR 13:24 “D̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠ye̠, ma̠ igiel ali̠gam a̠ruzu bho̠ na̠ eten, “ ‘sa̠ ogogo bho̠ ta̠ azu̠, sa̠ uwetire bho̠ ko o̠mu̠ mu̠;
MAR 13:25 sa̠ i̠ni̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny emeleghu, sa̠ ra̠limon e̠nai̠ny ta̠ enyegia̠n.’
MAR 13:26 “Sa̠ d̠a̠ obhel obha̠, a̠nwunom ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ka̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ na̠ a̠ru na̠ ibom a̠limon na̠ isosorogia̠n.
MAR 13:27 Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ruom itileduom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ okokod̠i ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n bho̠, d̠a̠ inya̠ re̠ku̠l e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, ob̠eton d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠gbaki̠ a̠de ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ obhubhulom.
MAR 13:28 “I̠se̠n, ibhine ma̠ a̠sidogh oriren a̠figbho̠ ma̠ e̠tu̠ghan abar. Igiel i̠gha d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ edugh sa̠ i̠mu̠nu̠mu̠n bho̠ na̠ e̠mu̠r na̠ emite, bha̠ inyin na̠ ologhom ma̠ a̠kozogh na̠ a̠tua̠n.
MAR 13:29 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ka̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ emite, bha̠ iloghome ma̠a̠, na̠ a̠tua̠n, na̠ a̠misi d̠a̠ o̠nu̠otu.
MAR 13:30 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, amu̠m onon ko oten d̠o̠ kisa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite.
MAR 13:31 A̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny ta̠ eten e̠d̠u̠a, ya̠a̠ ikpo a̠fugh d̠ami̠ ko oten d̠o̠ na̠ oten e̠d̠u̠a.
MAR 13:32 “I̠se̠n, iya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bo̠d̠o̠ obhel bho̠, bebina̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠loghom bo̠, a̠d̠igh itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, O̠nyi̠ bho̠ eka̠, a̠sigimeni ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠.
MAR 13:33 Ikpona̠! Igone! Ezin bho̠ inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel bho̠ ekunuguma̠ obhel bho̠ ta̠ aro̠.
MAR 13:34 Agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠, sa̠ awe̠le̠man eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ igoni d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ okponom, o̠ni̠no̠ o̠ni̠no̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ ta̠ a̠gir, sa̠ a̠ruom okponomotubho̠ ma̠a̠, aro̠ ma̠ omom a̠gon.
MAR 13:35 “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, igone, ezin bho̠ inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel bho̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru. Ta̠ a̠rue aro̠ ma̠ a̠dule, bo̠d̠o̠ egum a̠d̠io, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ obhel olobhiri e̠nu̠r na̠ alal, bo̠d̠o̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠.
MAR 13:36 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ka̠ a̠ru ma̠ awai̠, i̠na o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ anwa na̠ a̠kod̠u.
MAR 13:37 Sa̠ abar wa̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin bho̠, bha̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠. ‘Igone!’ ”
MAR 14:1 I̠se̠n bha̠ i̠wal a̠d̠a̠ma̠ isugho ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠ sekina̠ E̠yal Abe̠re̠di̠ ya̠ Owubh d̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ imimia̠n agu̠o̠ awa ta̠ ebhin ikoiny eb̠ol A̠zizo̠s egigh.
MAR 14:2 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠gba ma̠a̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ e̠yal bho̠, bo̠d̠o̠ bha̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ esoroni ma̠ elobhiri.
MAR 14:3 I̠se̠n, bha̠ A̠zizo̠s od̠i d̠a̠ Abe̠tani̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh bho̠. Sa̠ odi ani̠ a̠bhin ololo alabasta ola̠ u̠lo̠gh a̠ga̠i amu̠nu̠ Aspai̠knad obom a̠b̠ua̠ a̠ru. Sa̠ a̠b̠om o̠nu̠no̠nu̠ ololo bho̠ a̠zugioghom amu̠nu̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 14:4 Sa̠ idi ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ i̠ki̠kai̠ngha, sa̠ odi a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi ma̠a̠, “I̠na a̠din ere na̠ a̠robh amu̠nu̠ ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠ bho̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a?
MAR 14:5 Onon sa̠ ka̠ urue owol opeleni ma̠ od̠ua̠l e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh a̠dinari̠ (300) obhin o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠.” Sa̠ awa i̠li̠o̠m ani̠ bho̠ ma̠ ibom.
MAR 14:6 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠we̠le̠ ma̠ ani̠ bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠. Inyin udin ere na̠ onigha̠ i̠na ma̠ ali̠gam a̠luzu? I̠na na̠ a̠gir ob̠eb̠i abar a̠nigha̠ ami̠.
MAR 14:7 Ronyigoiny bho̠ sa̠ od̠i na̠ inyin eb̠la̠ obhel, inyin ta̠ orue o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ onigha̠ awa kere kere obhel ola̠ a̠d̠igh inyin ologi. Ya̠a̠ ami̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ na̠ inyin eb̠la̠ obhel.
MAR 14:8 I̠na a̠gir abar wa̠ i̠na a̠rue ma̠ ogir bho̠, ma̠ od̠ia̠ ozuom ami̠ amu̠nu̠ iya̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man ozu d̠ami̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠ma̠d̠i.
MAR 14:9 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, kesi kesi ola̠ ta̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠ebi̠ asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, ta̠ o̠gba nyen, ogir onon wa̠ ani̠ onon a̠gir bho̠, ma̠ obhin o̠ru̠ru̠an o̠yo̠.”
MAR 14:10 Sa̠ A̠zuda̠s I̠skari̠o̠t, odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠, a̠ten agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠wol A̠zizo̠s a̠nigha̠ awa.
MAR 14:11 Sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ ibhon ologi ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠ i̠na agba bho̠, sa̠ igua̠n onigha̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠ ikpoki. Ob̠eton d̠a̠ obhel obha̠ sa̠ A̠zuda̠s abho̠ro̠gh e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ ta̠ a̠sora̠n owol A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 14:12 D̠a̠ o̠pu̠r a̠d̠a̠ma̠ E̠yal Abe̠re̠di̠ wa̠ Owubh d̠o̠ bho̠, a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ na̠ ogigh o̠nyi̠ o̠nana E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠, sa̠ ogbo ogir ta̠ A̠zizo̠s iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na, ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “A̠kere esi wa̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan i̠yar o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man osisa̠n oyom ma̠ od̠e ed̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠?”
MAR 14:13 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom i̠wal ogbo ogir d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh od̠i o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rol izoko amu̠m, i̠tu̠o̠no̠me̠ i̠na.
MAR 14:14 Sa̠ i̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠igh bho̠ ma̠a̠: ‘O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠: oken e̠kpe̠ isuloma̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ogbo ogir d̠ami̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠?’
MAR 14:15 Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ atu̠o̠m a̠leriom inyin obom e̠kpe̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu a̠b̠ekei bho̠, ola̠ na̠ o̠mar oburi oguri, ma̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠man i̠se̠ ma̠ esisa̠n i̠yar.”
MAR 14:16 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠tu̠ghu̠man ed̠ia̠n Opel Oten bho̠.
MAR 14:17 Ate̠i̠ a̠dule, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠ iten i̠gi̠.
MAR 14:18 Agu̠o̠ awa od̠i d̠a̠ akpata od̠e na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, odi o̠ni̠ inyin wa̠ na̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠e bho̠, ta̠ a̠wol ami̠.”
MAR 14:19 Sa̠ awa id̠igh i̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ ibom, sa̠ o̠ni̠ o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ake̠ ma̠ opura̠n o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAR 14:20 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Odi o̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠tiom d̠a̠ onin e̠kpa ed̠ia̠n na̠ ami̠ bho̠.
MAR 14:21 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠mugh agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ ogboloma̠ ina̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ bho̠. Ka̠ ibhon a̠pu ma̠ u̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ obha̠!”
MAR 14:22 D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ ed̠e bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin abe̠re̠di̠ a̠tutumeni, sa̠ a̠puiny a̠nigha̠ awa sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ibhine, onon ozu d̠ami̠ wa̠ na̠ onigha̠ inyin bho̠.”
MAR 14:23 Sa̠ a̠bhin okpa̠ko a̠min, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ali̠se̠bh, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ awa, sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa ibhin i̠d̠a.
MAR 14:24 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Onon asi̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ d̠a̠ omom i̠zo̠ bho̠, wa̠ uzu, ma̠ o̠ta eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom o̠si̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
MAR 14:25 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ob̠eton i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ami̠ ko o̠d̠a mu̠ ma̠ a̠min itu a̠grep tu̠tu̠n a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ ad̠a ma̠ omom bho̠ d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.”
MAR 14:26 Sa̠ awa i̠mo̠r aso̠r, sa̠ i̠d̠u̠a i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Igu Roliv.
MAR 14:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ inyin ta̠ oghel A̠zib̠a̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ami̠ ta̠ agu̠r okponom ro̠nana bho̠ a̠teb̠eli, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh ro̠nana bho̠ ta̠ e̠sasaragi̠an.’
MAR 14:28 Ya̠a̠, igiel ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠ten agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili ka̠ a̠b̠a̠ra̠ inyin.”
MAR 14:29 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom i̠we̠le̠man anwa iten i̠d̠u̠a eka̠, ami̠ ko oghil ani̠ d̠o̠ ad̠u̠a.”
MAR 14:30 Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, a̠d̠ugula̠n onon, kisa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r ta̠ alal i̠wal igiel, anwa ta̠ aku̠a ami̠ ma̠ i̠sar igiel, ma̠a̠ anwa na̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ami̠.”
MAR 14:31 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ akparame̠ni̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ anwa a̠mugh eka̠, ami̠ ko o̠ku̠a d̠o̠ nyam.” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom iyed̠i ifugh ani̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
MAR 14:32 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan do̠yo̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ esi ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Age̠tse̠mane̠, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de ma̠ i̠se̠n, ya̠ ami̠ ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠siseiny.”
MAR 14:33 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin A̠puta̠ na̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Azo̠n ab̠aragu̠ma i̠na, sa̠ ibom asu̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an na̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ ra̠ id̠igh i̠na.
MAR 14:34 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Eloghoma̠n ozu d̠ami̠ na̠ ku̠nu̠ ma̠ ibom, aro̠ ka̠ omugh a̠sugho. I̠ro̠ ma̠ omom ma̠ i̠se̠n.”
MAR 14:35 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠kara ka̠ a̠mel a̠b̠obhia̠n d̠a̠ a̠de, sa̠ a̠siseiny ma̠a̠, ta̠ a̠b̠ur nab̠o̠, obhel onon ka̠ iten ad̠u̠a d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 14:36 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Ada, O̠we̠de̠, anwa ta̠ a̠rue a̠gir kabar kabar, si̠ghe̠ ma̠ okpa̠ko onon d̠a̠ ozu d̠ami̠. Ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ku d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠ami̠, aro̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠oyom.”
MAR 14:37 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa, sa̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa na̠ ekod̠u, sa̠ a̠pura̠n A̠puta̠ ma̠a̠, “Asai̠mo̠n, anwa na̠ a̠kod̠u ke̠re̠? Kpo̠ruzu ma̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ omom bebina̠ o̠nyi̠ obhel.
MAR 14:38 I̠ro̠ ma̠ omom ma̠ esiseiny b̠o̠ka̠ inyin umel d̠o̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ ad̠agi̠an. Na̠ ebhir e̠mu̠gh bho̠, ya̠a̠ ozu bho̠ na̠ a̠dugh.”
MAR 14:39 Sa̠ i̠na a̠puta̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠siseiny onin agu̠o̠ bho̠.
MAR 14:40 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠ru ra̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa na̠ ekod̠u eten, ezin bho̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa na̠ e̠mu̠mo̠r ibom ma̠ ola̠ awa iloghom mu ma̠ abar ola̠ o̠wo̠ran o̠yo̠.
MAR 14:41 A̠zizo̠s a̠ru ma̠ oleghemeni i̠sar igiel bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Inyin od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ okod̠u na̠ osira̠ ma̠ epobh ke̠re̠? Na̠ a̠bhon! Obhel wa̠ u̠to̠ uguri bho̠ na̠ a̠lei. Ikpone, na̠ owol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.
MAR 14:42 Ib̠egina̠! Id̠ighi ta̠ oten o̠gi̠. O̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠wol ami̠ bho̠ od̠i d̠a̠ aka.”
MAR 14:43 A̠zizo̠s od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠fugh, sa̠ A̠zuda̠s odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal bho̠ a̠ru na̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠kpanaki̠an ralapa ogidi na̠ re̠b̠am, iya̠ aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ iruom.
MAR 14:44 I̠se̠n, o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠ na̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ api̠pi̠o̠bh bho̠ bha̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠, ib̠ole i̠na ma̠ esibhom e̠kparame̠ni̠.”
MAR 14:45 Sa̠ A̠zuda̠s a̠ru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ Atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠,” sa̠ api̠pi̠o̠bh i̠na.
MAR 14:46 Sa̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ iru ra̠ ipuom A̠zizo̠s d̠a̠ agu̠o̠, sa̠ ib̠ol i̠na, isibhom i̠kparame̠ni̠.
MAR 14:47 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ etua̠n, abho̠ro̠n alapa ogidi d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ a̠sobh a̠to ta̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠b̠uton.
MAR 14:48 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n o̠go̠ ebhugh ke̠re̠, ma̠ ola̠ inyin ubhin alapa a̠rigidi na̠ re̠b̠am uru ra̠ ob̠ol ami̠?
MAR 14:49 Ka̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ inyin d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ inyin ub̠ol d̠o̠ ami̠. Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ emite ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠di̠ar ya̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.”
MAR 14:50 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠we̠le̠ i̠na ighil i̠d̠u̠a.
MAR 14:51 Odi o̠nyi̠ oyel ola̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ani̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠, i̠na alagha ma̠ ososora̠n akapa asi̠ni̠ni̠n ku̠ku̠m. A̠nwunom bho̠ i̠b̠ar na̠ i̠na esibh,
MAR 14:52 sa̠ i̠na a̠gbugbugha̠ awe̠le̠ ma̠ ososora̠n akapa asi̠ni̠ni̠n bho̠ a̠ghil ad̠u̠a ma̠ e̠dab̠a.
MAR 14:53 Sa̠ awa ibhin A̠zizo̠s i̠gi̠o̠m we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ aru̠mu̠ okur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ ikokod̠ia̠n.
MAR 14:54 Sa̠ A̠puta̠ aro̠ ma̠ egbeny atu̠o̠no̠m i̠na tu̠tu̠n ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ogigo i̠gada ase̠ ta̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠. Sa̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de a̠sumogha̠n e̠banya bho̠ na̠ amu̠ga.
MAR 14:55 I̠se̠ sa̠ ibom rokur bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ Ogbo Osobh Ase̠ A̠zu bho̠ i̠bho̠ro̠ghan a̠nwunom ya̠ ta̠ e̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠ eb̠ologiom A̠zizo̠s, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ ebhin esobh ase̠ ebhumeni i̠na egigh, ya̠a̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠.
MAR 14:56 A̠d̠izo ronyob̠a̠ igunugha̠ emite ra̠ e̠gba ma̠ o̠nu̠ eb̠ologiom i̠na, ya̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠awa id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ onin.
MAR 14:57 Sa̠ idi ronyob̠a̠ imite, sa̠ i̠gba ma̠ igunugha̠ ib̠ologiom i̠na ma̠a̠:
MAR 14:58 “I̠yar u̠mo̠gho̠n ka̠ o̠ni̠ onon a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ogion Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ a̠lo bho̠, sa̠ d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠lo ma̠ opa̠n ola̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ olo.’ ”
MAR 14:59 Eb̠la̠ i̠se̠ eka̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ awa i̠gba ib̠ologiom A̠zizo̠s bho̠ id̠igh d̠o̠ onin.
MAR 14:60 Sa̠ We̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠rile a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa a̠pura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Onon ka̠ a̠kere a̠d̠ien abar ola̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ ob̠ologiom anwa?”
MAR 14:61 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s aro̠ b̠u̠b̠o̠m, na̠ o̠wo̠ran d̠o̠ ma̠ abar. Sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ a̠puta̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa Akrai̠st O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ akpe̠ ma̠ otutumeni bho̠ ke̠re̠?”
MAR 14:62 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ i̠na. Inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ka̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ na̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ agba od̠iom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ A̠limon A̠pu bho̠. Sekina̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ru na̠ ro̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny.”
MAR 14:63 Sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ ago̠ ma̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ta̠ odin ere o̠bho̠ro̠ghan ipa̠n ronyob̠a̠?”
MAR 14:64 “I̠bi̠ghe̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠fugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠ na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Inyin u̠bi̠gh eka̠?” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ api̠o̠gho̠m, akpe̠ ma̠ omugh.”
MAR 14:65 Sa̠ idi awa i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠si̠ro̠gho̠m o̠yo̠ ma̠ i̠gho̠r, sa̠ ibinom a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ib̠orogh i̠na, sa̠ ifugh inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠ “Wa̠.” Sa̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ ibhin i̠na ib̠orogh.
MAR 14:66 Sa̠ agu̠o̠ A̠puta̠ od̠i ma̠ agba wa̠ ade̠bh d̠a̠ ologi ogigo bho̠, sa̠ odi o̠nyani̠, ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠,
MAR 14:67 abi̠gh ka̠ A̠puta̠ na̠ amu̠ga ma̠ anya, sa̠ a̠gbiom a̠kpon i̠na, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa odi o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠ro̠ ani̠ na̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t bho̠.”
MAR 14:68 Sa̠, A̠puta̠ aku̠a a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ anwa na̠ agba bho̠, ami̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ nyam nyen.” Sa̠ A̠puta̠ a̠mite agi̠ ka̠ amara d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ogigo bho̠, sa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r alal.
MAR 14:69 Sa̠ o̠nyani̠ bho̠ abi̠gh i̠na sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ odi d̠a̠ aka bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Onon odi o̠ni̠ awa!”
MAR 14:70 Sa̠ a̠mula̠ aku̠a. O̠nyi̠ obhel oten, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ aka bho̠ ifugh inigha̠ ma̠ A̠puta̠ ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i anwa odi o̠ni̠ awa, ezin bho̠ anwa ola̠ Agalili.”
MAR 14:71 O̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ osibhigha̠, ogurugia̠n ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon wa̠ inyin na̠ ofugh ogboloma̠ bho̠!”
MAR 14:72 I̠se̠ sa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r alal wa̠ a̠leghemeni i̠wal igiel. Sa̠ A̠puta̠ aru̠ru̠an agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Kisa̠ e̠nu̠r ta̠ alal i̠wal igiel, anwa ta̠ aku̠a ami̠ ma̠ i̠sar igiel” Sa̠ A̠puta̠ aku̠ru̠ru̠ a̠sorogi ma̠ izin.
MAR 15:1 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠, d̠a̠ obom ame̠ghe̠le̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ okur bho̠ na̠ ikei bho̠, na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko, na̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo i̠gada ase̠ bho̠ imimia̠n iya̠ ogir ogboloma̠ A̠zizo̠s. Sa̠ i̠bhad̠i̠ i̠na, irileghom i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Apai̠let.
MAR 15:2 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠: “Anwa o̠li̠le̠ma A̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠ ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ agba.”
MAR 15:3 Sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ okur bho̠ i̠gba ma̠ a̠d̠izo o̠kpo̠ ib̠ologiom i̠na.
MAR 15:4 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠mula̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Abar ola̠ anwa inwuna̠ ma̠ o̠wo̠ran bo̠ ke̠re̠? Mu̠gho̠ne̠ ma̠ a̠d̠izo riku ya̠ uler anwa bho̠!”
MAR 15:5 Ya̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s na̠ omula̠ d̠o̠ awo̠ran abar, ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠igh Apai̠let ilologia̠n.
MAR 15:6 Kigiel kigiel ola̠ E̠yal Opel Oten a̠sor, bha̠ na̠ omutiom gha̠n d̠a̠ ikoli ma̠ onin o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ipuru.
MAR 15:7 D̠a̠ igiel obha̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Abarabas, ola̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ipa̠n ogbo a̠wia̠n a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ igigh o̠ni̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ e̠ma bho̠ na̠ a̠bhighibhighi bho̠, aro̠ d̠a̠ ikoli.
MAR 15:8 Sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ opuru agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ ogir agu̠o̠ na̠ ogir gha̠n bho̠.
MAR 15:9 Sa̠ Apai̠let awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh ma̠ ami̠ imutiom o̠li̠le̠ma A̠zu bho̠ inigha̠ inyin ke̠re̠?”
MAR 15:10 Ezin bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ okur bho̠ ibhin d̠a̠ egbugbo ologi eb̠ol i̠na.
MAR 15:11 Ya̠a̠, ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ itumugiom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ opuru agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ omutiom Abarabas onigha̠ awa.
MAR 15:12 Sa̠, Apai̠let a̠puta̠ a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh ma̠ ami̠ igir ere igboloma̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ inyin na̠ obhelegi ma̠ o̠li̠le̠ma A̠zu bho̠?”
MAR 15:13 Sa̠ awa ipita̠ i̠ko̠ro̠ ma̠a̠, “I̠du̠e̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠gigh!”
MAR 15:14 Ya̠a̠, Apai̠let a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere? I̠na a̠gir ere api̠e̠?” Sa̠ awa imula̠ i̠lo̠gh e̠mi̠ imulughu ma̠a̠, “Du̠e̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠gigh!”
MAR 15:15 Od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ ologi a̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ ab̠al, sa̠ Apai̠let a̠mutiom Abarabas a̠nigha̠ awa. Sa̠ a̠ruom ma̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ a̠b̠eton a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ o̠du̠ ogigh.
MAR 15:16 Sa̠ ogbo e̠gham bho̠ ibhin A̠zizo̠s i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ta̠ we̠mu̠ ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ ikokod̠i ma̠ eb̠la̠ odi ebu ogbo e̠gham bho̠.
MAR 15:17 Sa̠ iburi i̠na ma̠ ososora̠n akapa ozu a̠dolo, sa̠ ilo ma̠ eghoi ib̠ub̠ulom izuom i̠na.
MAR 15:18 Sa̠ awa i̠ke̠ ma̠ obhelegima̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “E O̠li̠le̠ma A̠zu! I̠yar na̠ obheleguma̠ nyam o!”
MAR 15:19 Sa̠ ibhin okpeti ib̠orogh e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠si̠ro̠gho̠m i̠na ma̠ i̠gho̠r, sa̠ ikpud̠ia̠n i̠na izuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi.
MAR 15:20 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na e̠we̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠ko̠gi̠o̠n ibura̠ ozu a̠dolo bho̠, sa̠ inwe i̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na ma̠ ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ irileghom i̠na i̠d̠u̠a ma̠ ka̠ o̠du̠ o̠yo̠ ogigh.
MAR 15:21 Sa̠ awa i̠mi̠nana ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ A̠sirin ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Asai̠mo̠n, o̠we̠de̠ ta̠ Ale̠gzanda na̠ A̠rufo̠si̠, d̠a̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠sala na̠ a̠ru, sa̠ iponoma̠ i̠na ma̠ orol e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 15:22 Sa̠ inuoghom A̠zizo̠s i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Ago̠lgo̠ta (a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “Esi okpokpo e̠mu̠.”)
MAR 15:23 Sa̠ i̠gu̠a ma̠ amaya d̠a̠ a̠min inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠d̠a, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ko ologhoma̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ali̠gam, ya̠ i̠na na̠ o̠d̠a d̠o̠.
MAR 15:24 Sa̠ ogbo e̠gham bho̠ i̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠. Sa̠ awa irobh okob̠a̠ ibhin i̠ru̠gi̠an ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
MAR 15:25 I̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ esugho o̠wal-obhel ma̠ asi̠ro̠.
MAR 15:26 Sa̠ i̠ge̠ ma̠ iku ase̠ d̠o̠yo̠ i̠du̠o̠m d̠a̠ anyu̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ ma̠a̠: “O̠LI̠LE̠MA A̠NWUNOM A̠ZU BHO̠.”
MAR 15:27 Sa̠ i̠du̠ nyen i̠wal i̠bho̠ru̠bho̠ru̠ aru̠gba, odi d̠a̠ agba od̠iom d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠a̠ uwed̠i d̠a̠ okiel. [
MAR 15:28 I̠nye̠n imuzoghod̠iom agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠; “U̠wal ani̠ i̠na o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ogbo id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.”]
MAR 15:29 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eten bho̠ i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na izizigha̠ ma̠ aru̠mu̠ d̠awa inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ e̠ka ifugh ma̠a̠, “A̠soroma̠ nyam! Anwa wa̠ i̠gba ma̠ anwa ta̠ a̠rue a̠b̠ogion Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠lo amado̠n d̠a̠ a̠bin i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.
MAR 15:30 Tenemeni ma̠ ozu d̠oyom, ma̠ a̠sor d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ ma̠ a̠ru!”
MAR 15:31 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ id̠igh na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠fugh na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi ma̠a̠: “I̠na na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo, ya̠a̠ na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ otenemeni ozu d̠o̠yo̠!
MAR 15:32 Akrai̠st O̠li̠le̠ma Izre̠l bho̠! I̠se̠n, sore d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ ma̠ a̠ru, sa̠ i̠yar ta̠ od̠umom anwa!” Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ u̠du̠ na̠ i̠na bho̠ i̠ki̠ri̠ ani̠ i̠na.
MAR 15:33 O̠te̠i̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal o̠wal-obhel d̠a̠ azai̠ny, sa̠ azi̠m a̠kpegiom eb̠la̠ ebhugh bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ i̠sar o̠wal-obhel ma̠ etita̠n.
MAR 15:34 D̠a̠ i̠sar o̠wal-obhel bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mulughu na̠ obom okoroko ma̠a̠, “E̠lo̠i̠, E̠lo̠i̠, lama sabaktani̠?” (onon a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠zib̠a̠ d̠ami̠, A̠zib̠a̠ d̠ami̠, anwa idin ere na̠ a̠gin ami̠?”)
MAR 15:35 Sa̠ idi awa ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, “Na̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ I̠lai̠za.”
MAR 15:36 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ awa a̠ghil ka̠ ato̠ri̠ ma̠ asapu̠ d̠a̠ igheghed̠um a̠min, sa̠ akpu̠o̠m d̠a̠ o̠lo̠ a̠b̠eton a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠d̠a, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “I̠we̠le̠, ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ka̠ I̠lai̠za ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠soroni i̠na.”
MAR 15:37 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin obom okoroko a̠mulughu, sa̠ ekpo epobh bho̠ a̠sobha̠n.
MAR 15:38 Sa̠ ukpe wa̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, ake̠ d̠a̠ eb̠o bho̠ agu̠an a̠sor i̠wal a̠bin.
MAR 15:39 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ we̠mu̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham wa̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ aka a̠sumogha̠n A̠zizo̠s, abi̠gh agu̠o̠ bho̠ i̠na a̠bhin a̠mugh bho̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, onon O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!”
MAR 15:40 Idi anwani̠ e̠ro̠ nyen ma̠ ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ egbeny ekpon. Anwani̠ i̠ye̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠, na̠ A̠meri onweni ta̠ A̠zemsi o̠gbara bho̠ na̠ A̠zosisi o̠gbara bho̠, na̠ Asalomi.
MAR 15:41 Awa i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na e̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ enigha̠ i̠na ma̠ obhel bho̠ i̠na aro̠ d̠a̠ Agalili bho̠. A̠d̠izo ipa̠n anwani̠ ya̠ id̠igh na̠ i̠na i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠ e̠ro̠ ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
MAR 15:42 Igiel bho̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule A̠d̠a̠ma̠ A̠kokod̠ia̠n bho̠, wa̠ i̠b̠ala bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠,
MAR 15:43 sa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ wa̠ Ari̠mati̠a bho̠, odi o̠ni̠ i̠gada ase̠ bho̠, ola̠ ubhin i̠tu̠o̠m abar ibom, ola̠ na̠ a̠gon irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, akpo̠ ma̠ ologi agi̠ d̠a̠ Apai̠let ka̠ a̠puru ma̠ ozu ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 15:44 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n Apai̠let ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠mugh ka̠ a̠mugha̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ we̠mu̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham bho̠ a̠pura̠n ku̠gba ma̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠mugh ga̠i.
MAR 15:45 Sa̠ igiel bho̠ Apai̠let na̠ amu̠gho̠n d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ we̠mu̠ e̠gham bho̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu bho̠ ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠.
MAR 15:46 Sa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ a̠gho ma̠ ukpe asi̠ni̠ni̠n, sa̠ a̠soroni ma̠ egua̠de bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhin ukpe bho̠ a̠bhurugi. Sa̠ a̠d̠i i̠na d̠a̠ od̠i ola̠ i̠na a̠b̠u a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠gbo o̠gbi̠o̠ma, sa̠ a̠kikiligi ma̠ o̠gbi̠o̠ma a̠kpegiom od̠i bho̠.
MAR 15:47 Sa̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠ na̠ A̠meri onweni ta̠ A̠zosisi i̠bi̠gh esi wa̠ ud̠i i̠na bho̠.
MAR 16:1 A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠ a̠ten, sa̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠ na̠ A̠meri onweni ta̠ A̠zemsi na̠ Asalomi, igho ma̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ eduduom ozu ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
MAR 16:2 Obom ogbo asi̠ro̠ i̠b̠ala A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠, sa̠ awa iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogogo bho̠ a̠pu na̠ a̠mite bho̠.
MAR 16:3 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠pura̠n odi ma̠a̠, “A̠nyen ta̠ a̠kikiligi ma̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠ asi̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ od̠i bho̠?”
MAR 16:4 Sa̠ awa ikpon d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ bha̠ na̠ okikiligi ma̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠ o̠si̠ghe̠. Ezin bho̠ o̠gbe̠o̠ma bho̠ abu̠gh ibom.
MAR 16:5 Sa̠ awa id̠igh d̠a̠ ologi od̠i bho̠ i̠bi̠gh o̠nyi̠ oyel ola̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agba bho̠, ibura̠ bho̠ na̠ esosorogia̠n, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa.
MAR 16:6 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko o̠ku̠nu̠! Inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t bho̠, wa̠ u̠du̠ ugigh d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠. I̠na na̠ b̠etina̠. I̠na bo̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n! I̠bi̠ghe̠ ma̠ esi bho̠ u̠mu̠ni̠e̠ni̠ i̠na bho̠.
MAR 16:7 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠gi̠e̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ i̠na A̠puta̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, na̠ a̠ten na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalili ka̠ ob̠a̠ra̠ inyin. Obha̠ esi inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠na, ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ inyin bho̠.’ ”
MAR 16:8 Sa̠ awa ighil i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠ d̠a̠ ekpoyogha̠n ologi na̠ a̠rugugu. Ya̠a̠, awa i̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ abar enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, ma̠ ebula̠ a̠rugugu. [
MAR 16:9 Obhel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, ma̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r a̠d̠a̠ma̠ d̠a̠ esi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, bha̠ i̠na a̠d̠ia̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠, ani̠ wa̠ i̠na a̠ze ma̠ od̠ua̠l i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh asi̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ ozu bho̠.
MAR 16:10 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ten agi̠ ka̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠, ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ na̠ ed̠i bho̠.
MAR 16:11 Sa̠ obhel bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠, ya̠ ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ abi̠gh bho̠, ku̠ku̠m eka̠ awa id̠umom d̠o̠.
MAR 16:12 Onon a̠ten, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ i̠wal ogbo i̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ opa̠n a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ awa na̠ erile na̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ odi o̠gbara e̠ma.
MAR 16:13 Sa̠ awa imula̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ iyed̠i, ku̠ku̠m eka̠, id̠umom d̠o̠ awa.
MAR 16:14 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ onin bho̠ ma̠ obhel ola̠ awa na̠ ed̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, sa̠ ali̠o̠m awa ma̠ ebula̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa od̠umom d̠o̠ bho̠. Ezin bho̠ awa ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo iya̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠.
MAR 16:15 Sa̠ a̠ruom awa ma̠a̠: “I̠gi̠e̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠.
MAR 16:16 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ sa̠ uwur amu̠m bha̠ oten, ya̠a̠ ola̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ bha̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ebhum ase̠.
MAR 16:17 Sa̠ relegh i̠nye̠n ta̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m ogbo ya̠ id̠umom bho̠; d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠, awa ta̠ eze ma̠ i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh, sa̠ ta̠ efugh irorua̠ aru̠nu̠ e̠ma,
MAR 16:18 sa̠ awa ta̠ ebhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa esibhi ma̠ i̠karabh i̠di̠ar, ya̠a̠ abar ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ awa, sa̠ ka̠ awa i̠d̠a ma̠ abar ola̠ na̠ a̠gigh o̠ni̠ eka̠, abar ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ awa, ta̠ e̠gbam aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r, sa̠ awa ta̠ ed̠um.”
MAR 16:19 Igiel bho̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠nigha̠ awa awe̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ ubhin i̠na ubhuneni d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny, sa̠ i̠na ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
MAR 16:20 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ iten imite ka̠ i̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ kesi kesi, sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ awa a̠gir, sa̠ a̠muzoghod̠iom o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ bho̠ na̠ ogir ilologia̠n.]
LUK 1:1 E! Wa̠ a̠lei abar A̠tiofilo̠s, a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom na̠ e̠ge̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ omuzoghod̠iom d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠a̠ i̠yar,
LUK 1:2 ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠pu̠r ronyob̠a̠ bho̠ i̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ inigha̠ i̠yar bho̠.
LUK 1:3 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, agu̠o̠ bho̠ ami̠ na̠ amar a̠bhin obhel a̠lelegi ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ka̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, akpe̠ ami̠ ma̠ o̠ge̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n oselegi onigha̠ onyom,
LUK 1:4 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ amar a̠loghom iya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠, ma̠ d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ anwa bho̠.
LUK 1:5 D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ E̠ro̠d aro̠ ma̠ O̠li̠la ebhugh A̠zudia̠, okur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Azakaraya d̠a̠ ebu rokur ta̠ Abi̠za aro̠. E̠li̠zabe̠t ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ eka̠ ola̠ eghun ta̠ Ero̠n.
LUK 1:6 I̠wal awa irugh a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ikoko ma̠ eb̠la̠ roloko na̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠; e̠kal ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m awa na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 1:7 Ya̠a̠ awa o̠nyi̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, ezin bho̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t aro̠ ma̠ e̠marani̠. Awa na̠ e̠mar eten ikei-a̠nwunom.
LUK 1:8 Igiel bho̠ a̠gir ate̠i̠ ebu rokur ta̠ Azakaraya ma̠ ogir ogir-okur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ Otuta̠zib̠a̠ bho̠,
LUK 1:9 sa̠ awa irobh okob̠a̠ ibhin i̠so̠n Azakaraya ma̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar rokur bho̠, ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ o̠su̠o̠m i̠tani̠ ed̠u-e̠nu̠nu̠.
LUK 1:10 Igiel bho̠ a̠lei o̠su̠o̠m i̠tani̠ ed̠u-e̠nu̠nu̠ bho̠, eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n bho̠, i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ etire na̠ esiseiny.
LUK 1:11 Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠mutuma̠ i̠na d̠a̠ agba od̠iom enwen i̠ko̠l i̠tani̠ ed̠u-e̠nu̠nu̠ bho̠.
LUK 1:12 Igiel bho̠ Azakaraya abi̠gh orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ Azakaraya a̠kpa̠ra̠noma̠, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh i̠na.
LUK 1:13 Ya̠a̠, orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠: “Azakaraya, ko oghil a̠rugugu; na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n a̠siseiny d̠oyom. Ani̠ d̠oyom E̠li̠zabe̠t ta̠ amar olobhiri o̠nyi̠ a̠nigha̠ nya̠m, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠ghol i̠na ma̠ Azo̠n.
LUK 1:14 I̠na ta̠ a̠bhin a̠libhon ologi na̠ ibo a̠ruom anwa, sa̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhon ologi d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠mara d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 1:15 I̠na ta̠ abu̠gh d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠. I̠na ko o̠d̠a d̠o̠ na̠ o̠d̠a ma̠ a̠min ya̠ na̠ epuru ma̠ o̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ ta̠ obhin E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠, omuzoghod̠i d̠a̠ okurogh, kisa̠ ta̠ o̠mar i̠na.
LUK 1:16 I̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom Izre̠l ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ eru d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠awa.
LUK 1:17 I̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠ru na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien e̠mu̠gh na̠ a̠limon ya̠ I̠lai̠za a̠rughom bho̠, a̠tulugi ma̠ rologi ta̠ ronweni na̠ ro̠we̠de̠, na̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠awa; sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ bho̠ ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ erugh a̠ghud̠um igielake̠, na̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man a̠nwunom ya̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ eb̠a̠ra̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.”
LUK 1:18 Sa̠ Azakaraya a̠pura̠n orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ abar onon, i̠se̠n wa̠ ani̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ ami̠ na̠ o̠kpo̠ bho̠?”
LUK 1:19 Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ A̠gebre̠l. Ami̠ na̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ I̠na a̠ruom ami̠ ma̠ o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n onigha̠ oyom.
LUK 1:20 Nagha, anwa ko orue mu a̠fugh abar tu̠tu̠n ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite bho̠; ezin bho̠, anwa na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ asu̠gbagba d̠ami̠ ya̠ ta̠ emite d̠a̠ obhel bho̠ na̠ o̠to̠ oguri bho̠.”
LUK 1:21 Igiel bho̠ a̠nwunom na̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ eb̠a̠ra̠ ma̠ Azakaraya bho̠, sa̠ a̠d̠igh awa ma̠ ilologia̠n o̠bi̠gh ma̠ i̠na na̠ aro̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 1:22 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠mite a̠ru bho̠, i̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ ofugh abar, sa̠ awa iloghom ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ abi̠gh aghi̠m d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ i̠tu̠o̠gho̠m i̠tu̠o̠gho̠m ya̠ na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ ofugh abar omutiom.
LUK 1:23 Obhel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir a̠muzoghod̠iom d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ya̠ u̠to̠ unigha̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ten a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 1:24 Na̠ obia̠ d̠o̠, sa̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠mumor, sa̠ a̠bhin ogho uwetire aro̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ o̠yo̠.
LUK 1:25 Sa̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “I̠se̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠kpon ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom.”
LUK 1:26 Igiel bho̠ eghun ta̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠lei odin uwetire bho̠, sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠ruom orileduom d̠o̠yo̠ A̠gebre̠l, ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Anazare̠t e̠ma ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ Agalili,
LUK 1:27 ka̠ o̠bi̠ghan e̠kar o̠nyani̠, ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠meri, ola̠ odi o̠nyi̠ eghun ta̠ A̠devidi, ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠, na̠ a̠sibh obhin ani̠.
LUK 1:28 Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ A̠meri a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ a̠bheleguma̠ ma̠ anwa o, anwa wa̠ e̠no̠gho̠man na̠ e̠te̠i̠ bho̠! Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ od̠i na̠ anwa.”
LUK 1:29 Sa̠ ikpo a̠fugh d̠o̠yo̠ i̠lo̠gh e̠mi̠ i̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠ ma̠ A̠meri, sa̠ i̠na aru̠ru̠an a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ezin ipelegima̠ bho̠.
LUK 1:30 Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠meri, ko oghil a̠rugugu, e̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ anwa.
LUK 1:31 Anwa ta̠ a̠mumor amar olobhiri o̠nyi̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠ghol a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 1:32 I̠na ta̠ abu̠gh e̠mi̠ sa̠ ta̠ obhelegi i̠na ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ Wagi̠manyu̠ A̠pu bho̠. Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ i̠kasi̠ o̠li̠le̠ma e̠ma o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ A̠devidi,
LUK 1:33 sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rileghom otu ta̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠, ad̠u̠a ma̠ amu̠m a̠ten amu̠m; ekunuguma̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠.”
LUK 1:34 Sa̠ A̠meri a̠pura̠n orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Abar onon ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠mite, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ ta̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ olobhiri-o̠ni̠ bho̠?”
LUK 1:35 Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠sor a̠ru ra̠ a̠mutuma̠ nyam, sa̠ a̠limon ta̠ Wagi̠manyu̠ A̠pu bho̠ ta̠ a̠ghughuom anwa; ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠nyi̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ wa̠ ta̠ o̠mar bho̠, ta̠ obhelegi ma̠a̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 1:36 Kpone, E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠ghisia̠n d̠oyom eka̠ na̠ a̠mumor olobhiri-o̠nyi̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n i̠na na̠ akpo̠ bho̠. Ughol gha̠n i̠na ma̠ a̠d̠ien ma̠ i̠na e̠marani̠, ya̠a̠ onon odin uwetire i̠na od̠i na̠ eghun.
LUK 1:37 Ezin bho̠, abar ola̠ akpar a̠pu ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ogir bo̠.”
LUK 1:38 Sa̠ A̠meri awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠. Omuzughod̠iom onigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa i̠gba bho̠.” Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ awe̠le̠man i̠na a̠ten ad̠u̠a.
LUK 1:39 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ A̠meri a̠nugia̠n a̠kokod̠ia̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ebhugh a̠rugugum d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠,
LUK 1:40 sa̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ otu ta̠ Azakaraya sa̠ a̠bheleguma̠ ma̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t.
LUK 1:41 Igiel bho̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t amu̠gho̠n ibheleguma̠ ta̠ A̠meri bho̠, sa̠ o̠nyi̠ wa̠ ta̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ bho̠, wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu-imara d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ a̠nyegia̠n, sa̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ozu ta̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠muzo.
LUK 1:42 Sa̠ a̠bhin okoroko ola̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ anwa a̠pu d̠a̠ e̠ma ra̠ anwani̠, na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ o̠nyi̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ otu-imara d̠oyom bho̠!
LUK 1:43 Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ e̠no̠gho̠man iya̠ o̠ko̠no̠n na̠ eru ra̠ e̠te̠i̠ ami̠, ma̠ ola̠ onweni ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠zua̠n ami̠?
LUK 1:44 Agu̠o̠ okoroko ibheleguma̠ d̠oyom a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ a̠to d̠ami̠ bho̠, sa̠ o̠nyi̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ okurogh d̠ami̠ bho̠ a̠bhin a̠libhon ologi a̠nyegia̠n.
LUK 1:45 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ i̠na wa̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠muzoghod̠iom i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠gua̠n a̠nigha̠ i̠na bho̠.”
LUK 1:46 Sa̠ A̠meri a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Eloghoma̠n ozu d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠.
LUK 1:47 E̠mu̠gh d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠bhon ologi na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠ami̠,
LUK 1:48 ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠loghom ado̠l o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠. A̠b̠eton i̠se̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, ad̠u̠a ma̠ amu̠m a̠ten amu̠m ta̠ obhelegi ami̠ ma̠a̠, wa̠ na̠ otutumeni bho̠,
LUK 1:49 ezin bho̠, i̠na Wa̠ A̠limon i̠bu̠gh ipu bho̠ na̠ a̠gir ibom i̠di̠ar a̠nigha̠ ami̠. E̠tu̠tu̠ bha̠ a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 1:50 Igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eghila̠n i̠na bho̠, ad̠u̠a ma̠ amu̠m a̠ten amu̠m.
LUK 1:51 I̠na na̠ a̠bhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠gir ibom i̠di̠ar; i̠na na̠ asasaragi̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠a̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an d̠awa.
LUK 1:52 I̠na na̠ a̠sorogi ma̠ ogbo i̠rileghom bho̠ d̠a̠ ra̠dila̠de d̠awa, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ a̠b̠egion ogbo ya̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar bho̠.
LUK 1:53 I̠na na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠di̠ar ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ bho̠ ma̠ od̠e olegha̠n, sa̠ a̠ze ma̠ aru̠li̠la bho̠ ma̠ oyel obhobho i̠kpo̠.
LUK 1:54 I̠na aru̠ru̠an okpon igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠ abhe̠l ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ Izre̠l,
LUK 1:55 na̠ Ebraham na̠ anwi̠i̠ny igha̠la̠ d̠o̠yo̠ kid̠ud̠ul, ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠gua̠n a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ro̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar bho̠.”
LUK 1:56 A̠meri a̠bhin agu̠o̠ i̠sar uwetire aro̠ na̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t ka̠ a̠mula̠ a̠yel d̠a̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 1:57 Obhel bho̠ eghun ta̠ E̠li̠zabe̠t a̠legha̠n bho̠, sa̠ amar olobhiri o̠nyi̠.
LUK 1:58 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh na̠ etua̠n i̠na bho̠, na̠ ogbo a̠ghisia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ id̠igh na̠ i̠na ibhon ologi ma̠ d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠kpon i̠na ma̠ ibom igbirigbir bho̠.
LUK 1:59 D̠a̠ obhel wa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠lei o̠bhabhanya a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa iru ra̠ oti ipo d̠o̠yo̠. Sa̠ awa iru ra̠ ogholom o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ Azakaraya,
LUK 1:60 ya̠a̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “E̠nyi̠! Ta̠ oghol i̠na ma̠ Azo̠n.”
LUK 1:61 Sa̠ awa i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ a̠ghisia̠n d̠inyin, o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ a̠d̠ien obha̠ bo̠.”
LUK 1:62 Sa̠ awa ibhin i̠tu̠o̠gho̠m ipura̠n o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ghol o̠nyi̠ bho̠.
LUK 1:63 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin i̠tu̠o̠gho̠m a̠puru ma̠ ad̠u̠b̠o̠ ola̠ obhin o̠ge̠ abar, sa̠ age̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ Azo̠n.” Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠.
LUK 1:64 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠ sa̠ o̠nu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ akpati̠na, sa̠ a̠nem d̠o̠yo̠ ako̠gi̠na, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ ofugh abar, sa̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 1:65 Sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh d̠a̠ eghighira̠ d̠awa bho̠. Sa̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠ i̠te̠i̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh a̠rugugum A̠zudia̠, sa̠ a̠nwunom na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n.
LUK 1:66 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba bho̠ ibhin i̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa, sa̠ odi na̠ a̠pura̠n odi ma̠a̠, “O̠gbara-o̠nyi̠ onon ta̠ a̠mite aro̠ eka̠?” Agu̠o̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ od̠i na̠ i̠na.
LUK 1:67 Sa̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ozu o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ Azakaraya a̠muzo, sa̠ i̠na a̠wa̠ ma̠ iwowa̠ ma̠a̠,
LUK 1:68 “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠, A̠zib̠a̠ Izre̠l, ezin bho̠, I̠na na̠ a̠zua̠n a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠, ata awa a̠bhin.
LUK 1:69 I̠na na̠ a̠b̠eton o̠bhal itenemeni a̠nigha̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ eghun otu ta̠ A̠devidi ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠,
LUK 1:70 agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠rughom a̠riwil e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠gua̠n d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ bho̠,
LUK 1:71 ma̠ omiza̠n d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠i̠yar, na̠ d̠a̠ a̠limon ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠su̠a i̠yar bho̠.
LUK 1:72 I̠na aru̠ru̠an i̠zo̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ okpon igbirigbir a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul d̠i̠yar,
LUK 1:73 i̠zo̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠d̠ed̠ia̠n na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar Ebraham bho̠:
LUK 1:74 ma̠ otenemeni i̠yar d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠i̠yar, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠yar ubhin a̠rugugu o̠ko̠l i̠na,
LUK 1:75 ya̠a̠ obhin d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala na̠ ado̠l igielake̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠i̠yar.
LUK 1:76 Sa̠ anwa, o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, ta̠ obhelegi nyam ma̠ owil ta̠ Wagi̠manyu̠ A̠pu bho̠; ezin bho̠ anwa ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, ma̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠man eten bho̠ onigha̠ o̠yo̠,
LUK 1:77 na̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ eloghom abar oten, wa̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ okpon i̠karabh o̠si̠ghe̠ a̠d̠ien a̠ru bho̠,
LUK 1:78 d̠a̠ ebula̠ okpon igbirigbir ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠i̠yar, ogogo wa̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ ad̠i̠ro̠ bho̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny amu̠o̠m i̠yar
LUK 1:79 ma̠ onigha̠ e̠b̠alab̠al ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ azi̠m, na̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ omugh bho̠, na̠ orileghom re̠b̠ab̠a a̠sike d̠i̠yar ka̠ od̠ighom d̠a̠ eten ekima̠.”
LUK 1:80 Sa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ a̠bhobh sa̠ aghu̠a d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh. A̠rugh d̠a̠ e̠ghana tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ obhel wa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ Izre̠l bho̠.
LUK 2:1 D̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠, sa̠ A̠siza̠ O̠go̠sto̠s alo̠gh oloko ma̠a̠, o̠wal eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ekpukpu ebhugh A̠rom.
LUK 2:2 (Onon o̠pu̠r o̠wal a̠nwunom wa̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ amu̠m igiel wa̠ Akwi̠ri̠ni̠o̠s na̠ a̠rileghom ebhugh A̠siria̠.)
LUK 2:3 Sa̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ a̠ten agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ka̠ o̠ge̠ a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 2:4 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ eka̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma Anazare̠t d̠a̠ Agalili a̠ten agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na ola̠ eghun otu ta̠ A̠devidi.
LUK 2:5 I̠na ab̠ar na̠ A̠meri, wa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠sibh obhin ani̠ bho̠ a̠bhin agi̠ d̠a̠ o̠wal a̠nwunom bho̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ eghun bho̠ na̠ a̠legha̠n.
LUK 2:6 D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ awa od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ sa̠ eghun ta̠ A̠meri ake̠ ma̠ ogun.
LUK 2:7 Sa̠ i̠na amar o̠kpana o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠, olobhiri. Sa̠ a̠bhin a̠rukpe a̠bhurugi i̠na, sa̠ amu̠ni̠e̠ni̠ i̠na d̠a̠ igba̠ ola̠ na̠ obhin na̠ o̠lo̠gh ed̠ia̠n na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ i̠nam, ezin bho̠ e̠kpe̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ otu esul bho̠.
LUK 2:8 Ikponom ro̠nana e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ e̠sala i̠gho̠gho̠ ola̠ a̠tua̠n, na̠ ekponom i̠nam d̠awa ma̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n obha̠.
LUK 2:9 Odi orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠mutuma̠ awa, sa̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ amu̠o̠m awa ma̠ ola̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa.
LUK 2:10 Ya̠a̠, orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu. Ami̠ ibhin ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ibom a̠libhon ologi ya̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom a̠ruom inyin.
LUK 2:11 Na̠ o̠mar Witenemeni bho̠ onigha̠ inyin d̠a̠ e̠ma ta̠ A̠devidi ma̠ a̠didon. I̠na Akrai̠st Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
LUK 2:12 Onon ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ elegh a̠nigha̠ inyin: Inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠nyi̠ ola̠ ubhin a̠rukpe ubhurugi, sa̠ u̠mu̠ni̠e̠ni̠ d̠a̠ igba̠ ola̠ na̠ obhin na̠ o̠lo̠gh ed̠ia̠n na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ i̠nam.”
LUK 2:13 D̠a̠ awai̠, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny iru ra̠ i̠b̠aragu̠ma ma̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, sa̠ itutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ efugh ma̠a̠,
LUK 2:14 “Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny wa̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ a̠pu bho̠, ya̠a̠ ekima̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ a̠de onon a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ bho̠.”
LUK 2:15 D̠a̠ obhel wa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ i̠we̠le̠ awa ibhun d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠, sa̠ ikponom ro̠nana bho̠ odi a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi ma̠a̠, “Id̠ighi o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠ti̠li̠he̠m ka̠ o̠bi̠gh abar onon wa̠ na̠ a̠mite bho̠, wa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ na̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠yar bho̠.”
LUK 2:16 Sa̠ awa inugia̠n i̠gi̠ sa̠ i̠bi̠gh A̠meri na̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ na̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠, wa̠ awa i̠mu̠ni̠e̠ni̠ d̠a̠ igba̠ ola̠ na̠ obhin na̠ o̠lo̠gh ed̠ia̠n na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ i̠nam bho̠.
LUK 2:17 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠bi̠gh o̠nyi̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gba i̠sasaragi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠, na̠ iya̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ onon a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠.
LUK 2:18 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh ilologia̠n eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba ya̠ ikponom ro̠nana bho̠ i̠gba inigha̠ awa bho̠.
LUK 2:19 Ya̠a̠ A̠meri a̠bhin eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n alo̠gh d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ a̠guri, sa̠ aru̠ru̠an ghan a̠gboloma̠.
LUK 2:20 Ikponom ro̠nana bho̠ imula̠ iyel, sa̠ itutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠na d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh bho̠, d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ u̠gba unigha̠ awa bho̠.
LUK 2:21 Oleghemeni o̠bhabhanya a̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠mara bho̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠lei oti ipo o̠nyi̠ bho̠, sa̠ ughol i̠na ma̠ A̠zizo̠s, a̠d̠ien wa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠ghol kisa̠ umumor i̠na bho̠.
LUK 2:22 Obhel wa̠ ate̠i̠ i̠ko̠l o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ozu bho̠, d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi bho̠, sa̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ na̠ A̠meri ibhin i̠na i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m ma̠ ob̠eton o̠yo̠ onigha̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠,
LUK 2:23 (ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ oloko ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Kerekere o̠kpana olobhiri o̠nyi̠ ma̠ ta̠ ob̠eton onigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠.”)
LUK 2:24 Sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠ko̠l i̠ko̠l o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ozu, ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠to̠ d̠a̠ oloko ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠. I̠di̠ar i̠ko̠l bho̠ bha̠ i̠wal ikpo rokur osege, bo̠d̠o̠ i̠wal ikubh rukpugh.
LUK 2:25 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠simio̠n aro̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, ma̠ ola̠ a̠rugh ado̠l igielake̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. I̠na aro̠ na̠ a̠gon Witenemeni bho̠ ma̠ oru ra̠ otenemeni Izre̠l. E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 2:26 E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba a̠nigha i̠na ma̠ i̠na ko omugh d̠o̠, a̠ten ka̠ i̠na na̠ abi̠gh Witenemeni wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gua̠n bho̠.
LUK 2:27 E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠rileghom i̠na ka̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ ologi Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Obha̠ onin obhel wa̠ A̠meri na̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ ibhin o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ A̠zizo̠s id̠igh bho̠, ma̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠to̠to̠gi̠ oloko bho̠.
LUK 2:28 Sa̠ A̠simio̠n a̠bube i̠na sa̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠:
LUK 2:29 “Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠limon bho̠, d̠ighi ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠oyom agi̠ d̠a̠ ekima̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa igua̠n bho̠.
LUK 2:30 A̠rid̠ien d̠ami̠ na̠ e̠bi̠gh itenemeni d̠oyom,
LUK 2:31 wa̠ anwa i̠to̠ iguri ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom eb̠la̠ ra̠dede ta̠ e̠bi̠gh bho̠:
LUK 2:32 ma̠ o̠ro̠ e̠b̠alab̠al onigha̠ ogbo o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ awa eloghom itenemeni ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ obhin edim onigha̠ a̠nwunom d̠oyom Izre̠l.”
LUK 2:33 Ed̠igh ilologia̠n onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ ta̠ A̠zizo̠s o̠mu̠gho̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ u̠gba̠ ugboloma̠ i̠na bho̠.
LUK 2:34 Sa̠ A̠simio̠n a̠du ma̠ o̠gho̠r a̠tutumeni awa sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠meri, onweni o̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ aso̠n o̠nyi̠ onon obhin emel na̠ ob̠etina̠ oruom a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom d̠a̠ Izre̠l, na̠ o̠ro̠ elegh ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ eghel.
LUK 2:35 Sa̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an e̠wo̠gi̠na ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ologi a̠d̠izo ogbo bho̠ ta̠ eb̠ugh emite. Sa̠ anwa ta̠ aku̠nu̠ ma̠ e̠mi̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ ya̠ ta̠ e̠gu̠b̠an ka̠ alapa ogidi a̠gim ologi d̠oyom awo̠lo̠me̠ni̠.”
LUK 2:36 Owil ani̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Ana, o̠nyani̠ ta̠ Afanu̠e̠l d̠a̠ eghun ta̠ Asa eka̠ aro̠. I̠na a̠d̠um, akpo̠ zighizighi. I̠na awal ilom, sa̠ irugha̠n od̠ua̠l ala ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ owolom d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mugh.
LUK 2:37 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ten ekpukele ani̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠d̠um i̠wal e̠wala na̠ inya̠ ala ma̠ igiel bho̠. I̠na na̠ o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ghan d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ ogir ogir, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ ako̠l ghan A̠zib̠a, a̠ne ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠, a̠siseiny a̠siseiny, a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n.
LUK 2:38 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa, sa̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Sa̠ agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ egon itenemeni A̠zeruse̠le̠m.
LUK 2:39 D̠a̠ obhel wa̠ A̠meri na̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ na̠ egir eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ Oloko ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ato̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa imula̠ iyel d̠a̠ e̠ma d̠awa Anazare̠t, d̠a̠ ebhugh Agalili.
LUK 2:40 Sa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ a̠bhobh na̠ alu̠kpo̠ a̠luzu, sa̠ eloghom abar imuzo d̠a̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ i̠na.
LUK 2:41 Kerekere ala o̠we̠de̠ na̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠ i̠gi̠ghan d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m ka̠ od̠e E̠yal Opel Oten.
LUK 2:42 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠lei d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ala bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠yal bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ od̠i d̠a̠ od̠ud̠ul bho̠.
LUK 2:43 E̠yal bho̠ a̠ten, sa̠ awa na̠ emula̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠sobha̠n aro̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, ya̠a̠ awa iloghoma̠n d̠o̠.
LUK 2:44 Awa na̠ erile ma̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ kisa̠ awa iloghoma̠n ma̠ i̠na bo̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa, ezin bho̠, awa i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ i̠na od̠i ani̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa. Sa̠ awa i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ rebu a̠ghisia̠n na̠ ra̠tologha̠n d̠awa.
LUK 2:45 Agu̠o̠ awa o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ awa imula̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m ka̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠yo̠.
LUK 2:46 I̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ iten, kisa̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de, d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠. I̠na aro̠ na̠ anagha awa, na̠ a̠pura̠n ipupura̠n.
LUK 2:47 Ilologia̠n ed̠igh eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠na bho̠, d̠a̠ e̠mi̠ amu̠gho̠nyan na̠ awo̠yo̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 2:48 Obhel awa i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠, sa̠ awa ib̠a̠gha̠gha̠. Sa̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, a̠mite eka̠ ka̠ anwa na̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠yar o̠ko̠no̠n? O̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom na̠ ami̠ na̠ obhin ekpoyogh ologi na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan anwa kesikesi.”
LUK 2:49 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Inyin u̠tu̠n ere na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan ami̠? Inyin uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ otu O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠, d̠u̠ko̠?”
LUK 2:50 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ i̠na na̠ agba bho̠.
LUK 2:51 Sa̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh na̠ awa a̠sor agi̠ d̠a̠ Anazare̠t, sa̠ anagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠awa. Ya̠a̠, oweni d̠o̠yo̠ a̠koko ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠guri ma̠ iya̠ eko d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 2:52 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhobh d̠a̠ eloghom abar na̠ d̠a̠ ozu, sa̠ ate̠i̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠.
LUK 3:1 Oleghemeni a̠d̠iobh na̠ ogho ala wa̠ A̠siza̠ A̠tiberi̠o̠s, o̠li̠le̠ma A̠rom, na̠ a̠rileghom ebhugh bho̠, Apo̠nti̠o̠s Apai̠let aro̠ ma̠ o̠li̠la ebhugh A̠zudia̠, sa̠ E̠ro̠d na̠ a̠rileghom Agalili, odi a̠bin ebhugh bho̠, ya̠a̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠ A̠filip sa̠ na̠ a̠rileghom Ituria̠ na̠ Atrakonitis, odi a̠bin ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ Ali̠sani̠as na̠ a̠rileghom A̠bilene, odi a̠bin ebhugh bho̠.
LUK 3:2 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, Anas na̠ Akai̠afas i̠ro̠ ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, sa̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ate̠i̠ Azo̠n o̠nyi̠ ta̠ Azakaraya d̠a̠ e̠ghana.
LUK 3:3 I̠na a̠rile ma̠ eb̠la̠ eghighira̠ O̠bhi̠i̠y Azo̠dan agba ma̠ asu̠gbagba otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh, na̠ owura̠ amu̠m oleriom ma̠ awa na̠ etiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠awa e̠te̠i̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
LUK 3:4 ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire ta̠ Ai̠zaya owil bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Okoroko o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠si na̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ e̠ghana bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠tu̠ghu̠mane̠ ma̠ eten ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠ eguri, ma̠ eselegi ma̠ reten bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ i̠na.
LUK 3:5 Kerekere ogugua̠ ta̠ ob̠a̠la̠me̠ni̠, kerekere igu na̠ egugum ta̠ ogbo o̠de̠bhe̠me̠ni̠. Sa̠ reten ya̠ ib̠eb̠elegia̠n bho̠ ta̠ oselegi, sa̠ ta̠ otulugi ma̠ rigbogolo reten bho̠.
LUK 3:6 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom d̠a̠ ra̠dede bho̠ ta̠ ebi̠gh itenemeni ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.’ ”
