Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ obhin aghan-od̠od̠ua̠ na̠ u̠ki̠a na̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere i̠gho̠gho̠ a̠mubobh, na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ odi a̠bin d̠a̠ a̠d̠iobh, sa̠ inyin ugin a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ na̠ etula̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. I̠nye̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ inyin ogir, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ko o̠we̠le̠ ma̠ onigha̠ a̠bin a̠d̠iobh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 11:43 “Ekulom inyin Rafarisi bho̠! Ezin bho̠ inyin uba̠ra̠ ma̠ ra̠dila̠de idoni d̠a̠ ru̠gala A̠zu, na̠ ipelegima̠ d̠a̠ regbolom a̠b̠ua̠ bho̠.
LUK 11:44 “Ekulom inyin Rafarisi bho̠! Ezin bho̠, inyin od̠i ka̠ ranyu̠od̠i ya̠ elegh o̠to̠, ya̠ a̠nwunom ologhom d̠o̠ sa̠ na̠ erile d̠a̠ anyu̠ na̠ eten.”
LUK 11:45 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ awa ola̠ na̠ aku̠ro̠m d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, anwa i̠b̠aram na̠ i̠yar a̠rogi d̠a̠ a̠fugh i̠nye̠n.”
LUK 11:46 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ekulom inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ku̠ro̠m d̠a̠ roloko bho̠! Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ obhin a̠dol ya̠ i̠mu̠mo̠r na̠ o̠gbam d̠a̠ aru̠mu̠ a̠nwonom orol; ya̠a̠, inyin ub̠eton d̠o̠ ma̠ ad̠u̠nu̠ agu̠o̠ okula̠n a̠dol bho̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠.
LUK 11:47 “Ekulom inyin! Ezin bho̠, inyin na̠ ob̠olob̠ol na̠ oburi ma̠ ranyu̠od̠i a̠riwil ya̠ ro̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin igigh bho̠.
LUK 11:48 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ inyin na̠ oleriom ma̠a̠, inyin oma̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ro̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin igir bho̠. Awa i̠ze̠ ma̠ a̠riwil bho̠, sa̠ inyin na̠ ob̠olob̠ol ranyu̠od̠i d̠awa.
LUK 11:49 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, d̠a̠ ibom eloghom abar ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ afi̠ri̠ma ma̠ a̠riwil sekina̠ ogbo ogir agi̠o̠m a̠wa̠. Idi sa̠ a̠wa̠ ta̠ egigh, ipa̠n sa̠ a̠wa̠ ta̠ egbikimeni.’
LUK 11:50 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ta̠ osibh a̠nwunom a̠mu̠m onon odinom ebula̠ asi̠ ta̠ eb̠la̠ a̠riwil ya̠ u̠ze̠gi̠ bho̠, d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ i̠se̠n;
LUK 11:51 ob̠eton d̠a̠ asi̠ ta̠ Ebe̠l ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ asi̠ ta̠ Azakaraya wa̠ ugigh d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io enwen i̠ko̠l bho̠ na̠ a̠lukpesi e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ta̠ opuru ma̠ amu̠m onon ma̠ asi̠ i̠nye̠n.
LUK 11:52 “Ekulom inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ku̠ro̠m d̠a̠ roloko A̠zu bho̠! Ezi̠n bho̠, inyin na̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ i̠sabi̠ eloghom abar bho̠. Inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ ud̠igh d̠o̠ ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ okigima̠ ma̠ ipa̠n a̠nwunom od̠i̠gh.”
LUK 11:53 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ad̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ Rafarisi bho̠ na̠ ogbo a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ owia̠n o̠yo̠, opupura̠n o̠yo̠ a̠d̠i̠zo i̠di̠ar,
LUK 11:54 opoiny o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠ ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠fugh abar ola̠ awa ta̠ edin esibh i̠na.
LUK 12:1 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ ro̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ ipel a̠d̠usubh o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala, id̠u iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ odi na̠ aze̠r odi. Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠ia̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ a̠yist Rafarisi bho̠, ya̠ awa na̠ e̠gba ma̠ ipa̠n na̠ egir ipa̠n bho̠.
LUK 12:2 Abar ola̠ ukpegiom ola̠ ko omite d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠ma bo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ola̠ odi d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ola̠ ko ologhom d̠o̠ bo̠.
LUK 12:3 Abar ola̠ inyin ufugh d̠a̠ a̠d̠io azi̠m, ola̠ a̠nwunom ka̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ etita̠n a̠d̠io bo̠, abar ola̠ inyin ubhobhula̠ d̠a̠ re̠bhai̠, ta̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ a̠rutu o̠gba o̠sasaragi̠.
LUK 12:4 “Ra̠tologha̠n d̠ami̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ko oghil ogbo ya̠ na̠ egigh ozu bho̠ sa̠ ko orue mu egir opa̠n abar e̠lo̠gho̠m.
LUK 12:5 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin o̠kparakpar okoroko na̠ a̠kikiom inyin o̠ni̠ wa̠ akpe̠ inyin oghil bho̠: ighile i̠na wa̠, ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gigh ozu bho̠ awe̠le̠, sa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon orobh inyin o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠banya bho̠. Yii, ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, i̠na wa̠ oghil bho̠.
LUK 12:6 Uwol d̠o̠ ma̠ ogho ikpo ro̠gi̠e̠ ta̠ egule ma̠ i̠wal ape̠ni̠ ke̠re̠? Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, bebina̠ onin awa ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠weleta̠n bo̠.
LUK 12:7 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, eb̠la̠ ikpo asi̠ghal aru̠mu̠ d̠inyin eka̠ na̠ o̠wal. O̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu; inyin ulei abar opu ma̠ o̠lo̠gh ro̠gi̠e̠ ta̠ egule.
LUK 12:8 “Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ agba ami̠ a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠nwunom, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ agba ani̠ i̠na a̠mutiom d̠a̠ a̠misigh itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 12:9 Ya̠a̠, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ aku̠a ami̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠nwunom, ta̠ o̠ku̠a ani̠ i̠na d̠a̠ a̠misigh itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 12:10 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠, ta̠ okpon o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien; ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, ko okpon d̠o̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien.
LUK 12:11 “Igiel uler inyin iku d̠a̠ u̠gala A̠zu, sa̠ u̠marame̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ a̠misigh ogbo ya̠ na̠ erileghom ebhugh bho̠ na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ bho̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠wo̠yo̠ghan awa, bo̠d̠o̠ agu̠o̠ obhin o̠gba o̠nu̠.
LUK 12:12 Ezin bho̠, E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ta̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ o̠ku̠a, ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ isora̠n o̠gba omutiom bho̠.”
LUK 12:13 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, fughe ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na na̠ ami̠ ta̠ o̠ru̠gi̠an ad̠i̠a o̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar.”
LUK 12:14 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ bho̠, a̠nyen aso̠n ami̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ osobh ma̠ ase̠, bo̠d̠o̠ wi̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠inyin?”
LUK 12:15 Sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠! I̠we̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere ado̠l o̠ku̠ku̠; a̠ga̠i a̠ghud̠um o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ bo̠ d̠a̠ e̠mi̠ e̠li̠la ya̠ i̠na a̠gbo bho̠.”
LUK 12:16 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “O̠si̠ odi o̠li̠la o̠ni̠ a̠mite ma̠ opa̠n.
LUK 12:17 Sa̠ i̠na aru̠ru̠an d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠se̠n ka̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠? Ami̠ inwuna̠ mu ma̠ esi okpol ed̠ia̠n d̠ami̠ oguri ya̠ eko.’
LUK 12:18 “Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ogion re̠kpe̠ okoko ed̠ia̠n d̠ami̠ a̠lo ma̠ ipa̠n ya̠ i̠bu̠gh ipu ma̠ i̠nye̠n. Sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighoghom eb̠la̠ ed̠ia̠n ib̠ua̠ d̠ami̠ a̠kpol d̠a̠ ologi.
LUK 12:19 Sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠ami̠ ma̠a̠, “Anwa na̠ a̠kpol ed̠ia̠n a̠guri ma̠ iya̠ eko ya̠ ta̠ elei od̠e a̠d̠izo rala d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ri̠la ti̠to̠i̠ny ma̠ a̠d̠e, ma̠ ad̠a, ma̠ ad̠e̠ ma̠ o̠d̠e̠.” ’
LUK 12:20 “Ya̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Sa̠ ema̠! A̠d̠uga̠la̠n onon, ta̠ opuru nyam a̠ghud̠um d̠oyom. Sa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa ikokod̠i iguri bho̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ a̠nyen?’
LUK 12:21 “Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠kpol i̠di̠ar a̠guri a̠sisa̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ awe̠le̠man ogbo e̠li̠la d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
LUK 12:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠: “O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan ologi ma̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠inyin, a̠d̠igh abar ola̠ inyin ta̠ od̠e; bo̠d̠o̠ abar ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠lagha.
LUK 12:23 Ezin bho̠, a̠ghud̠um a̠lei abar a̠pu ma̠ ed̠ia̠n, sa̠ ozu o̠ni̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu ma̠ ibura̠.
LUK 12:24 Ikpone ma̠ ed̠ighom a̠ghud̠um i̠nu̠r ya̠ od̠i ka̠ e̠gbar bho̠: Awa igbebh d̠o̠, awa ib̠u d̠o̠, inwuna̠ d̠o̠ nyen e̠bhai̠, bo̠d̠o̠ e̠kpe̠ ola̠ okpol ed̠ia̠n. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠koko awa. Ya̠a̠, inyin ulei abar opu ma̠ i̠nu̠r ya̠ na̠ e̠bhe̠bh d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠!
LUK 12:25 O̠ni̠ inyin ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan ologi alo̠gho̠m ekud̠i obhel d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ od̠i ke̠re̠?
LUK 12:26 Ku̠gba ma̠ inyin ko orue d̠o̠ ogir o̠gbara abar ola̠ o̠ku̠a, ka̠ inyin ta̠ odin ere o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan ologi ogboloma̠ ma̠ ipa̠n i̠di̠ar?
LUK 12:27 “Ikpone ma̠ ed̠ighom d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um ra̠lele bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ ebhin na̠ e̠su̠ bho̠. Awa igir d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠kparakpar ogir, awa ilo d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ma̠lo nyen. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠ a̠ga̠i Aso̠lo̠mo̠n eka̠, d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ obura̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ibura̠ ya̠ ibhon ile̠i ita̠ odi a̠lele i̠se̠.
LUK 12:28 Ku̠gba ma̠ obha̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠buri ma̠ i̠gho̠gho̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠, ya̠ a̠didon od̠i sa̠ elegien ta̠ orobh o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ anya bho̠, o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠buri inyin a̠peleni ma̠ o̠ku̠a-inyin ogbo ya̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ o̠ghu̠a d̠o̠ bho̠!
LUK 12:29 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, o̠ni̠ ko onigha̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin ma̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ma̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ od̠e, bo̠d̠o̠ ya̠ o̠d̠a; o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan egboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠ku̠a.
LUK 12:30 Ezin bho̠, a̠nwunom e̠mara̠nwunom onon, na̠ ewia̠n o̠te̠i̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠, ya̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin a̠loghom ma̠ a̠bhon inyin o̠te̠i̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠.
LUK 12:31 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, i̠bho̠ro̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ta̠ o̠b̠ar na̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n onigha̠ inyin.
LUK 12:32 “Inyin o̠gbara o̠lo̠gh, o̠ni̠ ko oghil a̠rugugu. Ezin bho̠, a̠d̠igh ologi ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin onigha̠ inyin irileghom bho̠.
LUK 12:33 Iwole ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ inyin unwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠ ebhin e̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠. Iguri ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ eko d̠inyin d̠a̠ e̠kpa ola̠ ko o̠ghu̠r d̠o̠, i̠di̠ar ya̠ ilei abar d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ya̠ ko omunia̠n d̠o̠; d̠a̠ esi ola̠ aru̠gba ko otua̠n d̠o̠, sa̠ afi̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠d̠e api̠e̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 12:34 Esi wa̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ilei abar d̠inyin od̠i bho̠, i̠se̠ esi rologi d̠inyin ta̠ e̠ro̠ nyen.
LUK 12:35 “I̠kpaki̠ane̠ ma̠ e̠kpo̠a ma̠ ro̠kara, ma̠ e̠su̠o̠m rato̠di̠ d̠inyin e̠ro̠ ma̠ omumor omumor,
LUK 12:36 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ib̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ na̠ egon wa̠nwuna̠ d̠awa ma̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ erogh omula̠ oru, b̠o̠ka̠ obhel i̠na ra̠ a̠kpukpu awa e̠nu̠r eguron enigha̠.
LUK 12:37 Ta̠ ebhon enigha̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠awa ta̠ ra̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa i̠ro̠ na̠ egon i̠na, ma̠ igiel i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ a̠bura̠ ma̠ ibura̠ ogir iyo̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠fugh awa ma̠ o̠ro̠ a̠dila̠de, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ aru̠gi̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n a̠nigha̠ awa.
LUK 12:38 Ta̠ ebhon enigha̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠awa ta̠ ra̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa i̠ro̠ na̠ egon i̠na; i̠na a̠ru ka̠ ma̠ egum a̠d̠io, bo̠d̠o̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠ eka̠.
LUK 12:39 Ya̠a̠, i̠mare̠ ma̠ e̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar onon: Ku̠gba ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ amar a̠loghom obhel wa̠ o̠gba bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru bho̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠b̠om otu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠d̠igh.
LUK 12:40 Inyin eka̠ ikokod̠ia̠ne ma̠ eb̠a̠ra̠, ezin bho̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ inyin o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠ na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an.”
LUK 12:41 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, anwa na̠ a̠rogh a̠sidogh onon na̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar ku̠ku̠m ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo?”
LUK 12:42 Sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ a̠nyen ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ wa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ aso̠n o̠ro̠ we̠mu̠ okponom rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠, onigha̠ gha̠n awa ra̠bin ed̠ia̠n d̠awa ma̠ obhel wa̠ akpe̠ bho̠?
LUK 12:43 Ta̠ ebhon enigha̠ ma̠ ogoni bho̠, ka̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru sa̠ ta̠ abi̠gh ma̠a̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ u̠to̠ bho̠.
LUK 12:44 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ a̠b̠eton eb̠la̠ i̠d̠i̠ar d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ okponom.
LUK 12:45 Ya̠a̠ ta̠ aro̠ eka̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠fugh d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ ma̠ oru,’ sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ od̠ulogh rob̠a̠ra̠motu iyed̠i, anwani̠ na̠ ilobhiri, sa̠ a̠d̠e ad̠a ka̠ ate̠i̠ esi ola̠ a̠min bho̠ na̠ epuru i̠na?
LUK 12:46 Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu obha̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ i̠na o̠ru̠ru̠an d̠o̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ i̠na ologhom d̠o̠ nyen. Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠gbikimeni i̠na ma̠ egbika̠ ya̠ igurom ipu bho̠, a̠d̠ighom i̠na ma̠ esi wa̠ ogbo ya̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ bho̠.
LUK 12:47 Ob̠a̠ra̠motu wa̠ a̠loghom abar wa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ i̠na na̠ a̠puru i̠na ma̠ ogir bho̠, sa̠ awe̠le̠man okokod̠ia̠n ob̠a̠ra̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ogir agu̠o̠ bho̠ akpe̠ i̠na ma̠ ogir bho̠, ta̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh ibom.
LUK 12:48 Ya̠a̠, i̠na wa̠ ologhom d̠o̠, sa̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ ma̠ o̠gu̠r o̠yo̠ bho̠, ta̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh o̠nyi̠ki̠kara ku̠ku̠m. O̠ni̠ ola̠ unigha̠ ma̠ ya̠ ib̠uiy, ta̠ opuru i̠na ma̠ iya̠ ib̠uiy. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ unigha̠ ma̠ ya̠ ib̠uiy ibom, ta̠ opuru i̠na ma̠ iya̠ ib̠uiy ibom.
LUK 12:49 “Ami̠ iru ma̠ ra̠ o̠lo̠gh anya d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon. Ya̠ i̠se̠n anya bho̠ na̠ e̠ke̠ na̠ emumor na̠ ab̠o̠, ka̠ id̠igh ami̠ ma̠ ologi!
LUK 12:50 Ami̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ owura̠ amu̠m ali̠gam a̠luzu d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ola̠ agu̠o̠ omiza̠n o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, sa̠ na̠ ane̠mu̠o̠m ami̠ a̠guri tu̠tu̠n ta̠ a̠ten!
LUK 12:51 Inyin u̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ ami̠ iru ra̠ omutiom ekima̠ d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon d̠u̠ko̠? E̠nyi̠, ami̠ iru ra̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n a̠nwunom.
LUK 12:52 Ob̠eton i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, eghun otu ogho o̠ni̠ ta̠ abagi̠na; i̠sar ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ agba, sa̠ i̠wal ta̠ ewia̠n awa, bo̠d̠o̠, i̠wal ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ agba, sa̠ i̠sar ta̠ ewia̠n awa.
LUK 12:53 Awa ta̠ e̠bagi̠na, o̠we̠de̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠nyi̠, sa̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠we̠de̠; onweni ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠nyani̠, sa̠ o̠nyani̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n onweni; o̠yo̠go̠-onweni ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠yo̠go̠-o̠nyani̠, sa̠ o̠yo̠go̠-o̠nyani̠ ta̠ a̠wia̠n o̠yo̠go̠-onweni.”
LUK 12:54 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ka̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ na̠ a̠lo na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ agba wa̠ ogogo bho̠ na̠ a̠sor bho̠, onin obhel bho̠ sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘A̠d̠io ta̠ alo̠bh,’ sa̠ na̠ a̠mite ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
LUK 12:55 Ya̠a̠, igiel o̠fe̠gu̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ esoroma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ a̠ru, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘A̠d̠io ta̠ asi̠so̠,’ sa̠ na̠ a̠mite ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
LUK 12:56 Sa̠ ribhelebhel! Inyin na̠ orue na̠ okpon a̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan agu̠o̠ a̠d̠io na̠ a̠bhin na̠ a̠lologia̠n; ya̠a̠, ezin ka̠ ere ma̠ wa̠ inyin orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ emite d̠a̠ obhel onon bho̠?
LUK 12:57 “Ya̠a̠, ezin ka̠ ere wa̠ inyin orue ani̠ d̠o̠, ma̠ o̠wal ologho̠m abar wa̠ a̠bhon bho̠?
LUK 12:58 Igiel anwa na̠ agi̠ ka̠ o̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an o̠kpe̠ na̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠ler anwa ma̠ iku bho̠, wia̠ne ma̠ a̠tulugia̠n na̠ i̠na d̠a̠ eten, kisa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ esi osobh ase̠ bho̠. Bo̠d̠o̠ bha̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin anwa agi̠o̠m osobh ma̠ ase̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠nu nyam agi̠o̠m o̠ni̠-oloko bho̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠-oloko bho̠ ta̠ a̠sibh anwa alo̠gh d̠a̠ ikoli.
LUK 12:59 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, anwa ko orue d̠o̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ ikoli bho̠ a̠ten ka̠ anwa na̠ akpe̠ kabar kabar amado̠n, ma̠ ola̠ bebina̠ ape̠ni̠ eka̠ ko osugho d̠o̠.”
LUK 13:1 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ idi a̠nwunom iru ra̠ i̠gba inigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, Apai̠let aze̠ ma̠ idi a̠nwunom Agalili d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ awa na̠ e̠ko̠l i̠ko̠l, ma̠ ola̠ asi̠ d̠awa i̠gu̠a na̠ asi̠ i̠nam i̠ko̠l bho̠.
LUK 13:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠a̠, ezin wa̠ a̠nwunom Agalili i̠nye̠n ya̠ i̠mu̠gh o̠ko̠no̠n bho̠, ma̠a̠ awa igir i̠karabh epu ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom Agalili iyed̠i ke̠re̠?
LUK 13:3 E̠e̠nyi̠! Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠ten ka̠ inyin utiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin, eb̠la̠ inyin eka̠ ta̠ omugh obhe.
LUK 13:4 Bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠, d̠iobh na̠ o̠bhabhanya o̠ni̠ ya̠ owewegh otu-ipoiny d̠a̠ Asi̠lo̠m a̠mel a̠bhum bho̠, ka̠ awa igir i̠karabh epu ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ erugh d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠ ke̠re̠?
LUK 13:5 E̠e̠nyi̠! Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ ka̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠ten ka̠ inyin utiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin, eb̠la̠ inyin eka̠ ta̠ omugh obhe.”
LUK 13:6 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh a̠sidogh onon: “Odi o̠ni̠ a̠gbebh a̠fig d̠a̠ a̠lei d̠o̠yo̠; sa̠ agi̠gha̠n ka̠ a̠kpon ka̠ i̠na ta̠ abi̠gh itu aku̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ bebina̠ onin otu.
LUK 13:7 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠kponom a̠lei bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Onon sa̠ i̠sar ala ami̠ na̠ a̠guri gha̠n na̠ a̠ru ma̠ i̠se̠n ra̠ okpon ka̠ ami̠ ta̠ abi̠gh otu d̠a̠ a̠fig onon, ya̠a̠ ami̠ ta̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ bebina̠ onin otu. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, gue ma̠ oriren bho̠ ma̠ a̠teb̠eli! Ta̠ atu̠n ere aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ a̠robh a̠b̠uruko a̠de bho̠?’
LUK 13:8 “Sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠kponom a̠lei bho̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, we̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ a̠guri ma̠ opa̠n ala, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠gbo ma̠ a̠de bho̠ a̠gir esin oriren bho̠ a̠bhin a̠b̠uruko a̠b̠ologhom.
LUK 13:9 Ku̠gba ma̠ a̠fig bho̠ a̠mum otu ma̠ ala wa̠ na̠ a̠ru, bha̠ ob̠eb̠i; bo̠d̠o̠ bha̠ gue ma̠ a̠teb̠eli.’ ”
LUK 13:10 Odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh, A̠zizo̠s na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ odi otu u̠gala A̠zu,
LUK 13:11 ya̠a̠ odi ani̠ ola̠ o̠karabh e̠mu̠gh alo̠gh e̠gha-aman d̠iobh na̠ o̠bhabhanya ala aro̠. Ani̠ bho̠ akpu̠lan ola̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mara oselegha̠n.
LUK 13:12 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh ani̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhelegi a̠mutiom a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ani̠ bho̠, na̠ okoko ma̠ anwa od̠umeni d̠a̠ asu̠nwe̠r d̠oyom.”
LUK 13:13 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agbam aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ozu ani̠ bho̠. D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠nwe amara a̠selegha̠n sa̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 13:14 Ya̠a̠ ologi ta̠ we̠mu̠ u̠gala A̠zu bho̠, a̠gurom ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠koko ma̠ a̠likoko d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Odin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esi-a̠d̠a̠ma̠ d̠i̠yar ma̠ obhin ogir ogir. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, itue d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠ ma̠ ra̠ ekokua̠n; o̠ni̠ ko oru ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠.”
LUK 13:15 Ya̠a̠, Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Inyin ibhelebhel! O̠ni̠ inyin ola̠ o̠ko̠to̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ anam d̠o̠yo̠, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠su̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mutiom d̠a̠ otu i̠nam bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ amu̠m, ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠, od̠i ke̠re̠?
LUK 13:16 O̠ku̠a ka̠, na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyani̠ ta̠ Ebraham onon wa̠ Eru bho̠ abhad̠i̠ a̠guri ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ o̠bhabhanya ala bho̠, ma̠ omiza̠n d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh a̠nwunom A̠zu bho̠, ke̠re̠?”
LUK 13:17 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠fugh o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ ari̠ghe̠l isibh eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠dama i̠na bho̠; ya̠a̠, o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ebhon ologi d̠a̠ ebula̠ rogir ilologia̠n ya̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠gir bho̠.
LUK 13:18 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ od̠i eka̠? Ami̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ere atu̠o̠m?
LUK 13:19 Od̠i ka̠ ekpo amu̠stad ola̠ o̠ni̠ a̠bhin a̠gbebh d̠a̠ a̠lei d̠o̠yo̠; sa̠ asu̠ a̠mite a̠ten oriren, sa̠ i̠nu̠r iru ra̠ ilo ma̠ a̠rutu d̠a̠ i̠gha bho̠.”
LUK 13:20 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ere atu̠o̠m irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠?
LUK 13:21 Od̠i ka̠ o̠nyi̠ki̠kara a̠yist ya̠ ani̠ebhom a̠bhin alo̠gh d̠a̠ o̠to̠ma̠ i̠sar-abafu̠ ed̠ia̠n ibhugh sa̠ iwubhmeni ma̠ eb̠la̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.”
LUK 13:22 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠l d̠a̠ ibom na̠ i̠gbara re̠ma a̠ten, na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom kesikesi d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ten na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠.
LUK 13:23 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, o̠nyi̠ki̠kara a̠nwunom ku̠ku̠m ta̠ eten ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠,
LUK 13:24 “Iwia̠ne ma̠ ibom ma̠ o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ o̠nu̠-otu wa̠ a̠kporia̠n bho̠; ezin bho̠, a̠d̠izo ogbo ta̠ e̠bho̠ro̠ghan o̠wo̠l i̠se̠ od̠igh, ya̠a̠ ko orue d̠o̠.
LUK 13:25 Ku̠gba ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ adu̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠-otu bho̠, sa̠ inyin uru ra̠ u̠mara d̠a̠ etire u̠kpukpu ma̠ egugh bho̠ i̠le̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, gurone ma̠ otu bho̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar.’ “I̠na ta̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ inyin, esi inyin na̠ o̠d̠u̠a na̠ oru eka̠ ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠.’
LUK 13:26 “Sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠go̠ya ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar od̠igh na̠ anwa od̠e, o̠d̠a; sa̠ anwa i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠a̠ reten d̠i̠yar nyen.’
LUK 13:27 “Yaa̠, i̠na ta̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ inyin, na̠ esi inyin na̠ o̠d̠u̠a na̠ oru. Itene ma̠ e̠d̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠n, eb̠la̠ inyin rod̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.’
LUK 13:28 “A̠nwunom ta̠ e̠gba ma̠ igbir, e̠ghi̠r ib̠ub̠ura̠, ma̠ igiel inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh Ebraham, na̠ Azi̠ki̠, na̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠, na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠riwil d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ya̠a̠ inyin sa̠ ta̠ orobh omutiom d̠a̠ etire.
LUK 13:29 A̠nwunom ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ agba wa̠ ogogo na̠ a̠pu na̠ a̠mite bho̠, na̠ agba wa̠ ogogo na̠ a̠sor bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ eb̠o na̠ d̠a̠ esoroma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom eru ra̠ ebhin ra̠dila̠de d̠awa, d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠sor d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
LUK 13:30 Ya̠ga̠i, ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ ola̠ idi ogbo ya̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ ta̠ eten i̠pu̠r, sa̠ idi i̠pu̠r bho̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ u̠man.”
LUK 13:31 D̠a̠ obhel wa̠ i̠na na̠ agba ma̠ o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ idi ogbo Afarisi iru ra̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “D̠u̠a ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠ten agi̠ ma̠ opa̠n esi. E̠ro̠d na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ogigh oyom.”
LUK 13:32 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ ka̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ududu obha̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ozegi ozegi i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh na̠ okoko okoko a̠nwunom od̠umeni, ma̠ a̠didon na̠ elegien a̠ru; oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠muzoghod̠iom ogir d̠ami̠.’
LUK 13:33 O̠ku̠a eka̠, ami̠ ta̠ agi̠o̠m d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ma̠ erile d̠ami̠ ma̠ a̠didon, na̠ elegien a̠ru, na̠ a̠melegien. Ezin bho̠, ugigh gha̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ owil opa̠n esi, a̠ten d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m!
LUK 13:34 “A̠zeruse̠le̠m, E A̠zeruse̠le̠m, e̠ma wa̠ na̠ a̠guri gha̠n na̠ a̠robhod̠i na̠ aze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠riwil na̠ ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin a̠dila̠de-i̠to̠ a̠ruom oru d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠! Ya̠a̠ i̠ni̠ igiel ma̠ iya̠, na̠ ebhir ami̠ ma̠ okokod̠i eb̠la̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠oyom oguri onin esi, ma̠ agu̠o̠ e̠nu̠r-e̠ma na̠ a̠bhin rapu̠ba d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠ghughuom anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ anwa na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 13:35 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, nagha ma̠ abar wa̠ ta̠ a̠mite bho̠! Ta̠ ogin otu d̠inyin oguri ma̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠. Sa̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, inyin ko o̠bi̠gh mu ami̠ tu̠tu̠n ta̠ ate̠i̠ igiel inyin ta̠ ofugh ma̠a̠, ‘Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ i̠na wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.’ ”
LUK 14:1 Odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ A̠zizo̠s agi̠ d̠a̠ otu odi we̠mu̠ ogbo Afarisi, ka̠ od̠igh na̠ awa od̠e ed̠ia̠n, sa̠ a̠nwunom i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ epoiny
LUK 14:2 na̠ e̠nagha i̠na! I̠se̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠ bha̠ odi o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ na̠ anwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r wa̠nopelbho̠.
LUK 14:3 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ku̠ro̠m d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ ogbo Afarisi bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Oloko bho̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ okoko o̠ni̠ od̠umeni ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠?”
LUK 14:4 Ya̠a̠ awa inima̠ i̠ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠sibh o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠b̠eton, sa̠ a̠koko i̠na a̠d̠umeni, sa̠ a̠ruom i̠na ma̠ oten oyel.
LUK 14:5 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ inyin a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠, bo̠d̠o̠ anam ola̠ a̠mel a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ogugua̠-amu̠m ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ osira̠-epobh, i̠na ko o̠nu̠r d̠o̠ agi̠ ka̠ ato̠ro̠n ke̠re̠?”
LUK 14:6 Ya̠a̠ awa irue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠wo̠ran a̠pura̠n onon.
LUK 14:7 Igiel bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ iru d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠so̠n ra̠dila̠de edim na̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ akpata-od̠e bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh onon a̠nigha̠ awa:
LUK 14:8 “Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠lebh anwa ma̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ erogh, ko o̠so̠n a̠dila̠de edim aro̠; ka̠din olebh ani̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ abu̠gh e̠mi̠ a̠pu nyam.
LUK 14:9 Ku̠gba ma̠ oku̠a, sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lebh inyin bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ anwa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘B̠etina̠ d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de d̠oyom ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon.’ Obhel o̠ku̠a, sa̠ ari̠ghe̠l ta̠ esibh anwa, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠kpon bo̠ agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ aki̠r edim.
LUK 14:10 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠lebh anwa, gi̠e̠ ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ esi wa̠ aki̠r edim a̠pu bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ igiel o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lebh anwa bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru, i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, ‘A̠tologha̠n, b̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠bhun ka̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de ola̠ a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ onon.’ Sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠d̠igh edim d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom iyed̠i ya̠ ulebh bho̠.
LUK 14:11 Ezin bho̠, ogbo ya̠ i̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠, ta̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠; ya̠a̠, ogbo ya̠ i̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠, ta̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.”
LUK 14:12 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠, wa̠ a̠lebh i̠na bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Igiel anwa na̠ a̠soroni ma̠ o̠d̠e̠, a̠d̠igh etita̠n bo̠d̠o̠ a̠dule, ko olebh ra̠tologha̠n d̠oyom, na̠ a̠rumor d̠oyom, bo̠d̠o̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠oyom, na̠ ogbo a̠ghisia̠n, bo̠d̠o̠ aru̠li̠la eghighira̠ d̠oyom. Ka̠ anwa igir o̠ku̠a, awa ta̠ emula̠ elebh ani̠ nyam e̠kpe̠, sa̠ obha̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ amu̠kpe̠ d̠oyom.
LUK 14:13 Yaa̠, igiel anwa na̠ a̠soroni ma̠ o̠d̠e̠, lebhe ma̠ ronyigoiny bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ a̠risisi ozu na̠ e̠kpari̠an bho̠, na̠ a̠rukula̠ bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ a̠rid̠ien na̠ eb̠omia̠n bho̠,
LUK 14:14 sa̠ anwa ta̠ ate̠i̠ itutumeni. Awa ko orue d̠o̠ e̠kpe̠ nyam emulumeni; ya̠a̠, ta̠ o̠kpe̠ nyam d̠a̠ igiel ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh i̠b̠ab̠alab̠ab̠ala bho̠.”
LUK 14:15 Igiel bho̠ odi o̠ni̠ ola̠ aro̠ ani̠ d̠a̠ akpata-od̠e bho̠ amu̠gho̠n abar onon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Itutumeni od̠i na̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ ad̠e̠ ma̠ o̠d̠e̠ d̠a̠ esi irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.”
LUK 14:16 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Odi o̠ni̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n osoroni obom o̠d̠e̠ sa̠ a̠lebh a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom.
LUK 14:17 Ate̠i̠ obhel o̠d̠e̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gba onigha̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na a̠lebh bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Itue, ezin bho̠ na̠ okokod̠i̠an kabarkabar ola̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠ oguri.’
LUK 14:18 “Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ awa sa̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ omutioghom reb̠ologuma̠ ya̠ awa ko orue d̠o̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ o̠d̠e̠ bho̠. O̠pu̠r bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠se̠n kisa̠ ami̠ igho ma̠ egbolom, sa̠ a̠bhon ami̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠bi̠gh esi bho̠. Ko o̠gam, ami̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠ru.’
LUK 14:19 “Wa̠leghemeni i̠wal bho̠ sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠se̠n kisa̠ ami̠ igho ma̠ o̠gho̠ etire anam-ogir, ami̠ ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ ad̠a awa a̠kpon. Ko o̠gam, ami̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠ru.’
LUK 14:20 “Wa̠leghemeni i̠sar bho̠ sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘I̠se̠n kisa̠ ami̠ ibhin ani̠, ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠ru.’
LUK 14:21 “Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mula̠ agi̠ ka̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ wa̠nwuna̠ i̠na bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠wo̠ran bho̠. Sa̠ ologi ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ a̠gurom, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ i̠gam bho̠ a̠ruom ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Nu̠re̠ ma̠ a̠ten agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ reten bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ reten-a̠kposi bho̠, ma̠ a̠gun ronyigoiny bho̠, ogbo ya̠ a̠risisi ozu na̠ e̠kpari̠an bho̠, a̠nwunom ya̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien bho̠, na̠ a̠rukula̠ bho̠ ma̠ a̠ru.’
LUK 14:22 “Sa̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ anwa iruom ami̠ bho̠, ya̠a̠ esi bho̠ ta̠ omuzo d̠o̠.’
LUK 14:23 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Tene ma̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ibom reten bho̠, na̠ reten d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ eghighira̠ bho̠, ma̠ a̠wia̠n a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ ed̠igh eru, b̠o̠ka̠ otu d̠ami̠ a̠muzo.
LUK 14:24 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, bebina̠ o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ ulebh bho̠ ko od̠igh d̠o̠ ad̠e̠d̠i̠ma ma̠ o̠d̠e̠ d̠ami̠.’ ”
LUK 14:25 I̠se̠n obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom id̠igh na̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ e̠gi̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ a̠kpon awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠,
LUK 14:26 “Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠ru d̠ami̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ otula̠n d̠o̠ ami̠ a̠pu ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ onweni d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠, a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ku̠a ko orue d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠ami̠.
LUK 14:27 O̠ni̠ ola̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠rol e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren d̠o̠yo̠ atu̠o̠no̠m ami̠, ko orue d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠ami̠.
LUK 14:28 “Obhin o̠tu̠o̠m ma̠ na̠ ebhir odi o̠ni̠ inyin ma̠ olo owewegh otu-ipoiny, o̠ni̠ bho̠ ko od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de awal a̠b̠ua̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ a̠kpon, ma̠ ologhom ka̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ ikpoki ya̠ ta̠ elei obhin omunieni ogir bho̠ ke̠re̠?
LUK 14:29 Ezin bho̠, ka̠ anwa i̠ke̠ ma̠ ozu o̠de̠-otu bho̠, sa̠ anwa orue d̠o̠ ma̠ omunieni, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ abi̠gh o̠ku̠a ta̠ aki̠ri̠ nyam,
LUK 14:30 a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ onon ake̠ ma̠ olo otu, ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ omunieni.’
LUK 14:31 “Bo̠d̠o̠, obhin o̠tu̠o̠m o̠li̠la ebhugh ola̠ na̠ agi̠ ka̠ owe e̠gham ma̠ o̠li̠la opa̠n ebhugh. I̠na ko od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de awal a̠kpon ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin o̠lo̠gh e̠gham a̠d̠usubh na̠ ogho o̠ni̠r (10,000) o̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠, adama ma̠ i̠na wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin o̠lo̠gh e̠gham eruba̠l na̠ d̠iobh o̠ni̠r (20,000) o̠ni̠, na̠ a̠ru ra̠ owe o̠yo̠ bho̠ ke̠re̠?
LUK 14:32 Ku̠gba ma̠ i̠na ko orue d̠o̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ ato̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ o̠li̠la ebhugh uwed̠i ma̠ obhel ola̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham d̠o̠yo̠ od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ esi egbeiny. Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠puru ma̠ o̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an omutiom ekima̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa.
LUK 14:33 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, o̠ni̠ ko orue d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghan d̠ami̠, a̠ten ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue awe̠le̠man eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
LUK 14:34 “Ub̠on ob̠eb̠i abar, ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ ub̠on bho̠ na̠ a̠robh a̠lisibh d̠o̠yo̠, ka̠ ub̠on bho̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠mula̠ ate̠i̠ a̠lisibh d̠o̠yo̠?
LUK 14:35 Ub̠on ya̠ o̠ku̠a ibhon d̠o̠ ma̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠de, bo̠d̠o̠ oguri d̠a̠ esi ola̠ na̠ okpol a̠b̠uruko nyen; ya̠a̠ ta̠ ozu orobh. “Wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠to ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n, i̠na amu̠gho̠n.”
LUK 15:1 Odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠, igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh a̠nwunom na̠ ekokod̠ia̠n na̠ ekin A̠zizo̠s ma̠ o̠nagha atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 15:2 Ya̠a̠ a̠nwunom Afarisi bho̠ na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi bho̠, i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ eghunuma̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ onon na̠ ada ma̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh na̠ a̠bhin, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ awa na̠ a̠d̠ed̠ia̠n.”
LUK 15:3 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh a̠sidogh onon a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠:
LUK 15:4 “Obhin o̠tu̠o̠m ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ inyin a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠gh ro̠nana ya̠ ilei i̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh (100), sa̠ odi o̠nana bho̠ a̠bhe, i̠na ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ d̠iobh na̠ esugho (99) ro̠nana iyed̠i d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠, agi̠ ka̠ abho̠ro̠ghan o̠nana wa̠ a̠bhe bho̠ ke̠re̠?
LUK 15:5 Igiel i̠na abi̠gh o̠nana bho̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin a̠libhon ologi a̠b̠eton o̠nana bho̠ ale̠ti̠an d̠a̠ o̠kpalu̠ma d̠o̠yo̠ a̠rol a̠bhin a̠yel.
LUK 15:6 Igiel i̠na na̠ a̠misi d̠a̠ otu, i̠na ta̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ ra̠tologha̠n d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh na̠ etua̠n i̠na bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Id̠ighe na̠ ami̠ ma̠ ebhon ologi, ezin bho̠, ami̠ na̠ abi̠gh o̠nana d̠ami̠ wa̠ a̠bhe bho̠.’
LUK 15:7 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ibo d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny d̠a̠ ebula̠ onin od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠tiba̠ra̠, ta̠ epu ma̠ ibo d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠wal e̠wala na̠ d̠iobh na̠ esugho (99) a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala bho̠.
LUK 15:8 “Bo̠d̠o̠, ani̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ d̠iobh adrakma sa̠ odi a̠bhe. I̠na ko o̠su̠o̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ ato̠di̠, a̠gber otu bho̠, a̠bhin obhel abho̠ro̠ghan tu̠tu̠n i̠na ta̠ abi̠gh ke̠re̠?
LUK 15:9 Igiel i̠na abi̠gh okpoki bho̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ ra̠tologha̠n d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh na̠ etua̠n i̠na bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, ‘Id̠ighe na̠ ami̠ ma̠ ebhon ologi, ezin bho̠ ami̠ na̠ abi̠gh okpoki d̠ami̠ wa̠ a̠bhe bho̠.’
LUK 15:10 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ibo od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ka̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh o̠ni̠ a̠tiba̠ra̠.”
LUK 15:11 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh opa̠n a̠sidogh amar agba a̠mutiom ma̠a̠, “Odi o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ i̠wal anwi̠i̠ny.
LUK 15:12 Sa̠ o̠gbara bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠awa ma̠a̠, ‘O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠, ru̠gi̠ ma̠ ad̠i̠a d̠oyom ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ a̠bin d̠ami̠.’ Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ bho̠ aru̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ i̠wal awa.
LUK 15:13 “Na̠ obia̠ d̠o̠, sa̠ o̠gbara bho̠ a̠kokod̠i ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠bhin a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n ebhugh ola̠ a̠gbeiny, sa̠ a̠rugh ado̠l i̠te̠i̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ eb̠la̠ e̠li̠la d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ iyobh.
LUK 15:14 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ eb̠la̠ ikpoki d̠o̠yo̠ amado̠n bho̠, sa̠ o̠ko̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n a̠sor d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ebhugh bho̠, sa̠ e̠kparama ado̠l ate̠i̠ i̠na.
LUK 15:15 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ odi o̠nyi̠ eghun ebhugh bho̠, ma̠ onigha̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠ ogir. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠ruom i̠na ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ okponom roporopo d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 15:16 Sa̠, o̠ko̠i̠ a̠d̠ighi i̠na ate̠i̠ esi ola̠, i̠na ra̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ e̠d̠o̠gh od̠e ani̠ ed̠ia̠n ya̠ roporopo bho̠ na̠ ed̠e bho̠, ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠na bebina̠ abar od̠e na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 15:17 “Igiel bho̠ i̠na ra̠ a̠loghoma̠n ozu bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘I̠ni̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ ako̠ ma̠ ogir ogir onigha̠ o̠yo̠, ya̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n ed̠e esughieni bho̠? Ya̠a̠ ami̠ od̠i ma̠ enen na̠ a̠mugh o̠ko̠i̠!
LUK 15:18 Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ten a̠yel ka̠ ate̠i̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠: O̠we̠de̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ anwa na̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
LUK 15:19 Ami̠ i̠kpe̠ mu̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠oyom. Bhine ami̠ ma̠ a̠guri ma̠ agu̠o̠ odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu ola̠ anwa i̠ko̠.’
LUK 15:20 Sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠. “I̠na od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ esi egbeiny sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ abi̠gh ka̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ru, sa̠ igbirigbir na̠ etula̠n o̠nyi̠ bho̠ isibh i̠na, sa̠ i̠na a̠ghil agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ sa̠ a̠b̠ola̠n i̠na.
LUK 15:21 “Sa̠ o̠nyi̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘O̠we̠de̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ anwa na̠ ote̠nai̠ny. Ami̠ i̠kpe̠ mu̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠oyom.’
LUK 15:22 “Sa̠, o̠we̠de̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠nu̠re̠! Ibhine ma̠ akapa wa̠ a̠bhon a̠pu bho̠ ma̠ eburi i̠na, ma̠ e̠lo̠gh a̠gulu d̠a̠ ad̠u̠nu̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ e̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na ma̠ ragbaka.
LUK 15:23 Ibhine ma̠ e̠nam e̠nu̠m bho̠ ma̠ eru ra̠ egigh, sa̠ ta̠ od̠e ma̠ e̠yal obhon ologi.
LUK 15:24 Ezin bho̠, o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ onon a̠mugh a̠mugha̠ sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um i̠se̠n; i̠na a̠bhe a̠bha̠ sa̠ na̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠na ma̠ i̠se̠n.’ Sa̠ awa i̠ke̠ ma̠ od̠e e̠yal bho̠.
LUK 15:25 “D̠a̠ onin obhel wa̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ emite bho̠, okei o̠nyi̠ bho̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠um na̠ a̠gir ogir. Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠mula̠ na̠ a̠yel na̠ a̠tua̠n otu d̠awa bho̠, sa̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n okoroko a̠ma̠ti na̠ aso̠r na̠ i̠gba.
LUK 15:26 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠pura̠n abar wa̠ na̠ a̠mite bho̠.
LUK 15:27 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Umor d̠oyom na̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru, sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom a̠gigh e̠nam e̠nu̠m bho̠ sa̠ na̠ o̠ghe̠re̠ghu̠o̠m. Ezin bho̠, i̠na na̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um na̠ alu̠kpo̠ a̠luzu.’
LUK 15:28 “Sa̠ ologi ta̠ okei umor bho̠ a̠gurom sa̠ i̠na a̠gin od̠igh d̠a̠ ologi otu. Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mite agi̠ ka̠ ale̠gh i̠na.
LUK 15:29 Sa̠, i̠na awo̠ran o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Kpone! Eb̠la̠ rala i̠nye̠n ya̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠gir a̠nigha̠ ma̠ anwa ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogoni bho̠, a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ ami̠ i̠pi̠o̠m i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠oyom na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠. O̠ku̠a eka̠, a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ anwa inigha̠ ami̠ bebina̠ o̠nyi̠ ewel ola̠ obhin od̠igh na̠ ra̠tologha̠n d̠ami̠ od̠e e̠yal na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 15:30 Ya̠a̠, o̠nyi̠ d̠oyom onon wa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠li̠la d̠oyom iyobh na̠ id̠eme̠ma a̠mula̠ a̠ru bho̠, sa̠ anwa igigh e̠nam e̠nu̠m bho̠ inigha̠ i̠na!’
LUK 15:31 “Sa̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, anwa od̠i na̠ ami̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ igiel. Kabarkabar ola̠ ami̠ inwuna̠, oloyom.
LUK 15:32 Akpe̠ i̠yar od̠e e̠yal obhon ologi. Ezin bho̠, umor d̠oyom onon a̠mugh a̠mugha̠ sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um, i̠na a̠bhe a̠bha̠ sa̠ na̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠na.’ ”
LUK 16:1 A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Odi o̠li̠la aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠guri ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ we̠mu̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠. Sa̠ u̠gba unigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠ we̠mu̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠rughom i̠di̠ar d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ya̠ i̠te̠i̠.
LUK 16:2 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhelegi i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘I̠gho̠r i̠nye̠n ya̠ ami̠ na̠ amu̠gho̠n na̠ a̠gboloma̠ nyam bho̠, ka̠ imite eka̠? Gba ma̠ a̠mutiom ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ a̠bhin na̠ a̠rileghom ogir d̠ami̠, ezin bho̠, anwa ko orileghom mu ma̠ ogir bho̠.’
LUK 16:3 “Sa̠ we̠mu̠ ogir bho̠ aru̠ru̠an d̠a̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n wa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ ogir bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠? Ami̠ i̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠limon ogbo a̠de, sa̠ ari̠ghe̠l na̠ esibh ami̠ ma̠ opuru ipupuru.
LUK 16:4 Ami̠ na̠ a̠loghom abar ami̠ ta̠ a̠gir, b̠o̠ka̠ igiel uze ami̠ d̠a̠ ogir bho̠, a̠nwunom e̠da ami̠ ed̠ighom d̠a̠ a̠rutu d̠awa.’
LUK 16:5 “Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠na a̠lebh eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ id̠ikighu i̠mu̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ma̠ oru. Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n o̠pu̠r bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠mu̠gh ya̠ anwa id̠igh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠ ka̠ i̠ni̠?’
LUK 16:6 “Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘I̠wal e̠wala na̠ a̠d̠usubh a̠tini amu̠nu̠ oliv.’ “Sa̠ we̠mu̠ ogir bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Bhine ma̠ a̠d̠ire o̠mu̠gh d̠oyom, ma̠ anu̠r aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de, ma̠ a̠nwe ma̠ age̠ ma̠ eruba̠l na̠ d̠iobh.’
LUK 16:7 “Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n oleghemeni i̠wal o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa ka̠ o̠mu̠gh d̠oyom ka̠ i̠ni̠?’ “Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘I̠wal o̠ni̠r na̠ ogho e̠wala re̠kpa i̠bu̠kpa.’ “Sa̠ we̠mu̠ ogir bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Bhine ma̠ a̠d̠ire o̠mu̠gh d̠oyom, ma̠ a̠nwe ma̠ age̠ ma̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠r.’
LUK 16:8 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ogir bho̠ ase̠bh oniniom ma̠ a̠niniom we̠mu̠ ogir bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠bhin a̠koiny ikoiny bho̠. Ezin bho̠, a̠nwunom e̠mara̠nwunom onon na̠ ekoiny na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom amu̠m d̠awa na̠ epu ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny e̠b̠alab̠al na̠ erughom e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠awa bho̠.
LUK 16:9 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ibhine ma̠ e̠li̠la e̠mara̠nwunom e̠te̠i̠ ra̠tologha̠n iya̠ inyin, b̠o̠ka̠ igiel e̠li̠la d̠inyin na̠ ekun, od̠ighom inyin d̠a̠ a̠rutu esul ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠.
LUK 16:10 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rugh ya̠ igielake̠ d̠a̠ i̠gbara i̠di̠ar, ta̠ a̠rugh ya̠ igielake̠ d̠a̠ ibom i̠di̠ar. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ a̠niniom d̠a̠ i̠gbara i̠di̠ar, ta̠ a̠niniom d̠a̠ ibom i̠di̠ar nyen.
LUK 16:11 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni, ku̠gba ma̠ inyin ta̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ obhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ orileghom e̠li̠la e̠mara̠nwunom, ka̠ a̠nyen ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠ga̠i e̠li̠la ma̠ okponom?
LUK 16:12 Sa̠, ku̠gba ma̠ inyin urue d̠o̠ ma̠ obhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ okponom i̠di̠ar opa̠n o̠ni̠, ka̠ a̠nyen ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin i̠di̠ar iya̠ inyin?
LUK 16:13 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu a̠nigha̠ ma̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom ya̠ inwuna̠ i̠na bo̠. O̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ku̠a ta̠ alo̠gh a̠d̠ien odi sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠tula̠n uwed̠i, bo̠d̠o̠ ta̠ a̠bhin eb̠la̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ a̠gir a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi, sa̠ ta̠ a̠kpon uwed̠i ado̠ti̠me̠ni̠. O̠ni̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ okpoki.”
LUK 16:14 Igiel bho̠ Rafarisi ya̠ iba̠ra̠ ma̠ okpoki i̠mu̠gho̠n eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠ki̠ri̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 16:15 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ oleriom a̠ruzu d̠inyin ma̠ inyin ib̠eb̠i d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠nwunom, ya̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠loghom rologi d̠inyin. I̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠nwunom na̠ ebhin na̠ e̠tu̠o̠m abar ibom bho̠, i̠nye̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 16:16 “Oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi na̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ i̠ge̠ bho̠ e̠ro̠ erileghom i̠to̠to̠gi̠ bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ igiel bho̠ Azo̠n a̠ru bho̠. Ob̠eton obhel obha̠, na̠ o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom, sa̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ na̠ alo̠gh e̠mi̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n od̠igh d̠a̠ ologi ma̠ onyen.
LUK 16:17 A̠b̠ur a̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny o̠mai̠ny o̠d̠u̠a a̠pu, ma̠ ekpo abar ola̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ ma̠ o̠pe̠ti̠na omel obhe.
LUK 16:18 “O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gbogina̠ ma̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin opa̠n ani̠ a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma, sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin ani̠ wa̠ owolom a̠gbogina̠ bho̠ eka̠, a̠sor oloko od̠e e̠ma.”
LUK 16:19 “Odi o̠li̠la o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠bhin ib̠eb̠i a̠rukpe ododo na̠ asi̠ni̠ni̠n a̠bura̠ gha̠n ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠duduga̠na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠li̠la ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠.
LUK 16:20 Odi onyigoiny o̠ni̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Alazaro̠s eka̠ aro̠, ola̠ re̠b̠e̠ imuzo d̠a̠ ozu bho̠, ola̠ ubhin gha̠n uru d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ogigo o̠li̠la bho̠.
LUK 16:21 Sa̠ ibhir i̠na ma̠ okpokpo i̠pe̠re̠pe̠r ed̠ia̠n ya̠ na̠ emeleghu d̠a̠ akpata-od̠e o̠li̠la bho̠ od̠e. A̠sib̠ogho eka̠ e̠gi̠ ghan ka̠ e̠lai̠ re̠b̠e̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 16:22 “Ekunuguma̠ bho̠, sa̠ onyigoiny bho̠ a̠mugh, sa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ irileghom i̠na ka̠ id̠ighom d̠a̠ agba ta̠ Ebraham. O̠li̠la bho̠ eka̠ sa̠ a̠mugh, sa̠ ud̠i i̠na,
LUK 16:23 sa̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠o̠yo̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma imumugh. D̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ibom ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠kpon d̠a̠ anyu̠ abi̠gh Ebraham esi egbeiny na̠ Alazaro̠s d̠a̠ aka d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 16:24 Sa̠ o̠li̠la bho̠ a̠kele ma̠ Ebraham ma̠a̠, ‘E O̠we̠de̠ Ebraham, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir, ma̠ a̠ruom Alazaro̠s ato̠ri̠ ma̠ ad̠u̠nu̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m ra̠ a̠b̠okumeni ma̠ a̠nem d̠ami̠. Ezin bho̠, ami̠ od̠i d̠a̠ obom ali̠gam a̠luzu d̠a̠ ologi e̠banya onon.’
LUK 16:25 “Ya̠a̠ Ebraham awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘O̠nyi̠ ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠oyom d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom, anwa i̠te̠i̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠di̠ar, ya̠a̠ Alazaro̠s ate̠i̠ i̠karabh sa̠ a̠gbika̠ ma̠ egbika̠. Ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n, i̠na od̠i d̠a̠ e̠no̠gho̠man enen, ya̠a̠ anwa od̠i d̠a̠ ali̠gam a̠luzu na̠ a̠gbika̠.
LUK 16:26 O̠ku̠a ku̠ku̠m d̠o̠, obom okud̠umkud̠um oghololo od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin na̠ d̠i̠yar, b̠o̠ka̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ebhir o̠d̠u̠a d̠inyin o̠b̠e̠i̠y oru d̠i̠yar irue; o̠ni̠ ko orue d̠o̠ ad̠u̠a ma̠ ebha̠ d̠inyin ab̠e̠i̠ a̠ru ma̠ enen d̠i̠yar.’
LUK 16:27 “Sa̠ o̠li̠la bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Siseiny O̠we̠de̠ Ebraham, ruome ma̠ Alazaro̠s agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ eghun-otu o̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠,
LUK 16:28 ezin bho̠ ami̠ inwuna̠ ogho a̠rumor. I̠na agi̠ ka̠ anyagh ra̠to d̠awa, b̠o̠ka̠ awa eka̠ iru d̠a̠ esi onon wa̠ ibom ali̠gam a̠ruzu od̠i bho̠.’
LUK 16:29 “Sa̠ Ebraham awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘A̠mozizi na̠ a̠riwil bho̠ od̠i na̠ awa. Awa e̠nagha ma̠ a̠kikiom d̠awa.’
LUK 16:30 “Sa̠ o̠li̠la bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘E̠nyi̠, E o̠we̠de̠ Ebraham! Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ ad̠u̠a ma̠ enen d̠a̠ e̠ma imumugh agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa, awa ta̠ ed̠umom etiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh.’
LUK 16:31 “Sa̠ Ebraham awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Ku̠gba ma̠ awa i̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠mozizi na̠ a̠riwil bho̠, o̠ni̠ a̠b̠etina̠ eka̠ d̠a̠ omugh agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ awa, awa ko od̠umom d̠o̠.’ ”
LUK 17:1 A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Ad̠agi̠an ya̠ ta̠ ed̠ighi ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ omel od̠igh d̠a̠ i̠karabh ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ omite; ya̠a̠, itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ ad̠agi̠an i̠nye̠ ta̠ e̠wo̠l emite bho̠.
LUK 17:2 O̠gho̠ro̠gi̠o̠m obom o̠gbe̠o̠ma d̠a̠ orum o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ku̠a orobh o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ abadi̠, ta̠ a̠bhon a̠pu ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠ od̠ighi ola̠ odi o̠gbara o̠nyi̠ i̠se̠ ta̠ a̠mel a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
LUK 17:3 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin. “Ku̠gba ma̠ umor d̠oyom, bo̠d̠o̠ u̠marani̠ d̠oyom a̠d̠ighi nyam ma̠ i̠karabh, kikiome̠ i̠na; ka̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠o̠yo̠, kpone i̠na ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien.
LUK 17:4 Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ obha̠ a̠d̠ighi nyam i̠karabh ma̠ od̠ua̠l igiel d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ eka̠, sa̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠siseiny anwa ma̠ od̠ua̠l igiel sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ na̠ a̠tiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠ami̠,’ kpone i̠na ma̠ asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien.”
LUK 17:5 Sa̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ ifugh inigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠i̠yar!”
LUK 17:6 Sa̠ I̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ inyin u̠te̠i̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ ola̠ aki̠r ka̠ ekpo amu̠stad, inyin ta̠ orue ofugh onigha̠ ma̠ obom oriren onon ma̠a̠, ‘B̠uruna̠ ma̠ ka̠ a̠gbebha̠n d̠a̠ abadi̠,’ sa̠ oriren bho̠ ta̠ anagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠inyin.
LUK 17:7 “A̠nyen o̠ni̠ inyin ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ola̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ari̠si̠, bo̠d̠o̠ na̠ a̠kponom ro̠nana, sa̠ ka̠ i̠na a̠mutiom a̠ru, wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Dighe ma̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ abar ke̠re̠’?
LUK 17:8 E̠nyi̠, i̠na ko ofugh d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a. I̠na ta̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘D̠ighi ma̠ ed̠ia̠n a̠dule d̠ami̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠; ma̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n aro̠ ma̠ a̠b̠a̠ra̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠e ad̠a. Igiel ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠e awe̠le̠ ka̠ ma̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ad̠a ma̠ itoyom’?
LUK 17:9 Ta̠ a̠sora̠n wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ ma̠ o̠se̠bh o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ rogir ya̠ uruom i̠na ma̠ ogir bho̠ ke̠re̠?
LUK 17:10 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, igiel inyin ugir eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ uruom inyin ogir bho̠, inyin ta̠ ofugh ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar ibhobho i̠kpo̠ ib̠a̠ra̠motu; i̠yar ugir i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ i̠yar ogir bho̠ ku̠ku̠m.’ ”
LUK 17:11 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠ten na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠, i̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ o̠gbaki̠ Asameria̠ na̠ Agalili.
LUK 17:12 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tua̠n od̠igh d̠a̠ odi o̠gbara e̠ma bho̠, sa̠ d̠iobh a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠nwe̠r asu̠nwe̠r ekid̠igh i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na. Awa i̠mara ma̠ esi ola̠ a̠sigima̠ i̠na,
LUK 17:13 sa̠ awa ibhin obom okoroko ikele i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠zizo̠s, Wa̠nwuna̠, kpone i̠yar igbirigbir!”
LUK 17:14 Igiel bho̠ i̠na abi̠gh awa bho̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠, ka̠ eleriom a̠ruzu d̠inyin rokur bho̠.” Sa̠ igiel bho̠ awa iten na̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa id̠um i̠b̠ab̠ala.
LUK 17:15 Igiel bho̠ odi o̠ni̠ awa abi̠gh ma̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠um bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s, na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ obom okoroko.
LUK 17:16 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mel a̠b̠obhia̠n d̠a̠ a̠sike ta̠ A̠zizo̠s ase̠bh i̠na. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ onon ola̠ Asameria̠.
LUK 17:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Ukoko d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠iobh a̠nwunom o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ke̠re̠? Ya̠a̠, iken esugho a̠nwunom iyed̠i?
LUK 17:18 Ka̠ na̠ a̠ten isuloma̠ onon, o̠ni̠ awa ola̠ na̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru ma̠ ra̠ onigha̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ itutumeni bo̠ ke̠re̠?”
LUK 17:19 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “B̠etina̠ ma̠ a̠yel, ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠koko nyam a̠d̠umeni.”
LUK 17:20 Odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ Rafarisi bho̠ ipura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠ ologhom igiel irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠ru, sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Eruoma̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bo̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ obhin elegh olelegi,
LUK 17:21 bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n,’ bo̠d̠o̠, ‘Od̠i ma̠ ebha̠,’ ezin bho̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io inyin.”
LUK 17:22 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, “Obhel na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ ebhir inyin o̠bi̠gh odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ inyin ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠.
LUK 17:23 A̠nwunom ta̠ e̠gba enigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ‘Ikpone, i̠na od̠i ma̠ ebha̠,’ bo̠d̠o̠, ‘Ikpone, i̠na od̠i ma̠ enen,’ ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ko o̠tu̠o̠no̠m awa.
LUK 17:24 A̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ i̠me̠me̠gi̠na agbararan na̠ ame̠me̠gi̠na na̠ a̠mutiom e̠b̠alab̠al d̠a̠ odi e̠ku̠l o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠, sa̠ na̠ ame̠me̠gi̠na na̠ ab̠e̠i̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n e̠ku̠l bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru bho̠.
LUK 17:25 Ya̠a̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ amar abi̠gh a̠d̠izo ali̠gam a̠ruzu, sa̠ a̠nwunom amu̠m onon ta̠ eghel i̠na.
LUK 17:26 “A̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ A̠nua̠ bho̠, onin agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠.
LUK 17:27 A̠nwunom i̠ro̠ na̠ ed̠e na̠ e̠d̠a, na̠ ebhinogh anwani̠, na̠ enigha̠nom anwi̠nyan d̠awa tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ A̠nua̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ obom oghugh bho̠. Sa̠ obom amu̠m a̠d̠igho a̠ru ra̠ a̠kunugi ma̠ eb̠la̠ awa.
LUK 17:28 “Obha̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ Alo̠t nyen. A̠nwunom i̠ro̠ na̠ ed̠e na̠ e̠d̠a, na̠ egho na̠ ewod̠i ma̠ i̠di̠ar, na̠ egbebhegh ed̠ia̠n, na̠ eloyogh a̠rutu,
LUK 17:29 tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ Alo̠t ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ Aso̠do̠m bho̠. Sa̠ anya na̠ aso̠lfo̠, i̠lo̠bh d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny isor ra̠ ikunugi ma̠ eb̠la̠ awa.
LUK 17:30 “Obha̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ wa̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru bho̠.
LUK 17:31 D̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠ otu, osor d̠o̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin abar d̠a̠ ologi otu. Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠sala bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ omula̠ d̠o̠ a̠yel d̠a̠ otu.
LUK 17:32 I̠ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ ani̠ ta̠ Alo̠t bho̠!
LUK 17:33 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠wia̠n otenemeni a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠, ta̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠; ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠robh a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 17:34 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠d̠uga̠la̠n obha̠, i̠wal a̠nwunom ta̠ ekod̠u d̠a̠ onin akpata; odi ta̠ obhin, uwed̠i sa̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠se̠.
LUK 17:35 I̠wal anwani̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ onin esi e̠gbe̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar; odi ta̠ obhin, uwed̠i sa̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠se̠.”
LUK 17:36 [I̠wal a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ o̠si̠ egir ogir, odi ta̠ obhin, uwed̠i sa̠ ta̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠se̠.]
LUK 17:37 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite d̠a̠ken?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Esi ola̠ omumugh ozu od̠i, bha̠ esi ola̠ ro̠de̠le̠ ta̠ ekokod̠ia̠n.”
LUK 18:1 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rogh a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ a̠kikiom ma̠a̠, awa e̠ro̠ ma̠ osiseiny osiseiny A̠zib̠a̠ ya̠ o̠tabh d̠o̠ awa.
LUK 18:2 I̠na agba ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ odi e̠ma, odi osobh ma̠ ase̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ oghila̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ atu̠o̠m abar nyen.
LUK 18:3 Sa̠ odi ekpukele ani̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ o̠yo̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ali̠gam a̠luzu ola̠ ate̠i̠ i̠na, sa̠ ale̠gh i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Sobhe ma̠ ase̠ igielake̠ ma̠ a̠tenemeni ami̠, d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠.’
LUK 18:4 “I̠na na̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir abar ogboloma̠ ani̠ bho̠ ma̠ owewegh obhel; ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ a̠loghom ma̠ ami̠ ighila̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ami̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ atu̠o̠m abar nyen.
LUK 18:5 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ebula̠ agu̠o̠ ekpukele ani̠ onon na̠ a̠guri na̠ a̠nyegi ami̠ bho̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠sobh ase̠ bho̠ ma̠ ya̠ igielake̠, b̠o̠ka̠ awe̠le̠man ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠!’ ”
LUK 18:6 Sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “I̠nagha ma̠ abar wa̠ o̠karabh osobh ma̠ ase̠ onon a̠fugh bho̠.
LUK 18:7 A̠zib̠a̠ ko osobh d̠o̠ ma̠ ase̠ igielake̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n bho̠, ya̠ na̠ eleghe na̠ enigha̠ i̠na ma̠ etita̠n na̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n bho̠ ke̠re̠? I̠na ta̠ a̠bhogia̠n awa a̠guri ma̠ esi egbeiny ke̠re̠?
LUK 18:8 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin onyen a̠sobh ase̠ bho̠ ma̠ ya̠ igielake̠ a̠nigha̠ awa. Aro̠ eka̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a, igiel O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru, i̠na ta̠ abi̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n a̠de onon ke̠re̠?”
LUK 18:9 A̠zizo̠s ab̠ar na̠ a̠sidogh onon a̠rogh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ id̠umom d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa ma̠ awa na̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala bho̠, sa̠ na̠ ekpon ipa̠n a̠nwunom na̠ e̠do̠ti̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠:
LUK 18:10 “I̠wal a̠nwunom iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ osiseiny a̠siseiny. Odi, Afarisi; ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ uwed̠i, ogun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh.
LUK 18:11 Afarisi bho̠ a̠b̠etina̠ amara sa̠ a̠siseiny o̠ko̠no̠n: ‘A̠zib̠a̠, anwa a̠d̠ighi ami̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ipa̠n a̠nwunom. Ami̠ bo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠bi̠gh ma̠ a̠b̠igh, na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh, na̠ id̠e ma̠ e̠ma, bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh onon nyen.
LUK 18:12 Ami̠ na̠ a̠ne ma̠ o̠ko̠i̠ i̠wal igiel d̠a̠ ologi od̠ua̠l ra̠d̠a̠ma̠, sa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ gha̠n A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ odi a̠bin atu̠gi̠-a̠d̠iobh bho̠, d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ inwuna̠ bho̠.’
LUK 18:13 “Ya̠a̠, ogun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh bho̠ amara ma̠ esi egbeiny. I̠na na̠ one d̠o̠ ma̠ ob̠eka̠ okpon d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny nyen; Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ i̠na a̠bhuma̠ ma̠ ekpa̠kpa̠gh d̠o̠yo̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘E A̠zib̠a̠! Kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir, ezin bho̠ ami̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.’
LUK 18:14 “Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ada ma̠ a̠siseiny od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh onon a̠bhin, sa̠ i̠na a̠yel agu̠o̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ Afarisi bho̠ d̠o̠. Ezin bho̠, eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠ ta̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠; sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠ sa̠ ta̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.”
LUK 18:15 A̠nwunom i̠b̠aram na̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny ebhin eru d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s, ma̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠gbam agu̠o̠ otutumeni. Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠bi̠gh oku̠a bho̠, sa̠ ikigima̠ awa.
LUK 18:16 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhelegi ma̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ima̠ra̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny bho̠ eru d̠ami̠. O̠ni̠ ko okigima̠ awa, ezin bho̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny i̠nye̠n.
LUK 18:17 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠da d̠o̠ ma̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠, ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ologi.”
LUK 18:18 Odi o̠li̠la ebhugh A̠zu a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠-atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠?”
LUK 18:19 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ere a̠d̠ighi ka̠ anwa na̠ a̠bhelegi ami̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠? Ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ bo̠, usigimeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ku̠ku̠m.
LUK 18:20 Anwa a̠loghom oloko wa̠ agba ma̠a̠: ‘Anwa ko od̠e d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠ma. Anwa ko ogigh d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠. Anwa ko ob̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠b̠igh. Anwa ko o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ onyob̠a̠ igunugha̠. Zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ d̠oyom.’ ”
LUK 18:21 Sa̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ roloko i̠nye̠n ami̠ na̠ a̠koko ka̠ d̠a̠ i̠gbara d̠ami̠.”
LUK 18:22 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s amu̠gho̠n o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Odi abar od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ anwa ma̠ ogir. Wole ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa inwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ikpoki bho̠ ma̠ inyigoiny bho̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ ate̠i̠ e̠li̠la d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny. Igiel anwa na̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a awe̠le̠, ma̠ a̠mula̠ ma̠ a̠ru ra̠ ato̠no̠m ami̠.”
LUK 18:23 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n e̠kal onon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na aku̠ru̠ru̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠gbo ma̠ e̠li̠la ma̠ ibom.
LUK 18:24 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s abi̠gh agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠bhin aku̠ru̠ru̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Amar akpar ogbo ya̠ igbo ma̠ e̠li̠la ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ ologi irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠!
LUK 18:25 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, e̠nam-a̠dol o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ oyol anu̠ga oten ta̠ a̠b̠ur a̠pu, ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gbo ma̠ e̠li̠la ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ ologi irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
LUK 18:26 A̠nwunom ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n i̠nye̠n bho̠ sa̠ ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠ a̠nyen ta̠ a̠rue a̠ten?”
LUK 18:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Abar ola̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ko orue d̠o̠ na̠ orue a̠gir, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠gir.”
LUK 18:28 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar na̠ o̠we̠le̠man eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠yar unwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m anwa.”
LUK 18:29 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ awe̠le̠man otu, bo̠d̠o̠ ani̠, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠rumor, bo̠d̠o̠ aru̠marani̠, bo̠d̠o̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠, bo̠d̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny, ma̠ ebula̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
LUK 18:30 o̠ni̠ bho̠ ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ipel o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ amu̠m onon, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ bho̠.”
LUK 18:31 A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ a̠d̠ukun, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠nagha, i̠yar ta̠ obhun o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, esi bho̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom eb̠la̠ iwowa̠ ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ i̠ge̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ bho̠.
LUK 18:32 Ta̠ ob̠eton i̠na o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠. A̠nwunom ta̠ e̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na, sa̠ awa ta̠ erogi i̠na ekpon e̠do̠ti̠me̠ni̠, sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠si̠ro̠gho̠m i̠na ma̠ i̠gho̠r.
LUK 18:33 Awa ta̠ e̠gu̠ro̠gh i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ egigh i̠na. Sa̠ oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um.”
LUK 18:34 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ bebina̠ abar d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ya̠ i̠na agba bho̠. U̠wo̠gi̠o̠m awa ma̠ ezin i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na agba bho̠, sa̠ awa ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na na̠ agba na̠ a̠gboloma̠ bho̠.
LUK 18:35 I̠se̠n a̠mite ma̠ ola̠, agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ a̠tua̠n Aze̠riko bho̠, bha̠ odi o̠ni̠ ikpom a̠rid̠ien aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ aka eten bho̠ na̠ a̠puru ma̠ ipupuru.
LUK 18:36 Igiel bho̠ i̠na amu̠gho̠n oghoroghor o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ eten bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n ologhom abar wa̠ na̠ a̠mite bho̠.
LUK 18:37 Sa̠ awa i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t bho̠ na̠ a̠ten.”
LUK 18:38 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mulughu a̠kele ma̠a̠, “A̠zizo̠s, o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir!”
LUK 18:39 Sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠, imulughuom i̠na ma̠ i̠na aro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m. Ya̠a̠, i̠na aro̠ ma̠ omulughu omulughu izul d̠o̠yo̠ o̠gi̠o̠m anyu̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi, kpone ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir!”
LUK 18:40 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s amara kpom, sa̠ a̠bhin okparakpar okoroko a̠ruom agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ obhin o̠ni̠ bho̠ oru d̠o̠yo̠. Igiel bho̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠,
LUK 18:41 “Ere ma̠ abar wa̠ anwa na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ami̠ ma̠ ogir onigha̠ oyom bho̠?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠. “Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh o̠bi̠gh abar.”
LUK 18:42 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠rid̠ien d̠oyom e̠kpagi̠na! Ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom na̠ a̠koko nyam a̠d̠umeni.”
LUK 18:43 D̠a̠ onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh abar, sa̠ atu̠o̠no̠m A̠zizo̠s, na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Igiel bho̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ i̠bi̠gh o̠ku̠a bho̠, sa̠ awa itutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 19:1 A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ Aze̠riko sa̠ awo̠l na̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.
LUK 19:2 Odi o̠li̠la o̠ni̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Azaki̠o̠s aro̠. I̠na we̠mu̠ igun ma̠ otua̠-ebhugh bho̠.
LUK 19:3 I̠na a̠wia̠n o̠bi̠gh ani̠ A̠zizo̠s, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠lukper d̠o̠yo̠ i̠na na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ okpon opeleni o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠yo̠.
LUK 19:4 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠na a̠ghil a̠ten o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, sa̠ asi̠n oriren ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ a̠sikamo̠; b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na a̠rue abi̠gh i̠na, ezin bho̠ A̠zizo̠s ta̠ awo̠l i̠se̠ a̠ten.
LUK 19:5 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s ate̠i̠ esi bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon d̠a̠ anyu̠ a̠bhelegi i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Azaki̠o̠s! Nu̠re̠ ma̠ a̠sor a̠ru; ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh aro̠ d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom a̠didon.”
LUK 19:6 Onin obhel obha̠, sa̠ i̠na anu̠r a̠sor agi̠ ka̠ ada i̠na a̠bhin na̠ a̠libhon ologi.
LUK 19:7 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠bi̠gh o̠ku̠a bho̠, i̠ke̠ ma̠ oghunuma̠ ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠suloma̠ ma̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.”
LUK 19:8 Sa̠ Azaki̠o̠s a̠b̠etina̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Kpone, E Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ ta̠ aru̠gi̠ ma̠ e̠li̠la d̠ami̠ i̠wal a̠bin a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi a̠bin ronyigoiny bho̠; ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ami̠ ininiom abar, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ akpe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ ma̠ inya̠ a̠bin abar i̠se̠.”
LUK 19:9 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠didon, itenemeni na̠ eru d̠a̠ otu onon, ezin bho̠, o̠ni̠ onon eka̠ o̠nyi̠ ola̠ Ebraham.
LUK 19:10 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ atu̠n o̠bho̠ro̠gh, na̠ otenemeni ogbo ya̠ na̠ ebhe bho̠ a̠ru.”
LUK 19:11 Agu̠o̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ e̠nagha ma̠ iya̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ agba bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh ab̠aram. Ezin bho̠, awa na̠ e̠walama ma̠a̠, agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tua̠n A̠zeruse̠le̠m bho̠ ma̠a̠, irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ omite i̠se̠ onin obhel obha̠.
LUK 19:12 Sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “Odi obom o̠ni̠ ola̠ amar agbi̠r a̠mitia̠n, a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ esi egbeiny d̠a̠ opa̠n ebhugh, ola̠ ta̠ o̠lo̠gh i̠na ma̠ O̠li̠le̠ma sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru.
LUK 19:13 Kisa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, i̠na a̠bhelegi ma̠ d̠iobh rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ i̠se̠ ami̠na, sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ibhine ma̠ ikpoki i̠nye̠n ma̠ eb̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠b̠ua̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n ami̠ na̠ agi̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠.’
LUK 19:14 “Ya̠a̠, a̠nwunom ebhugh d̠o̠yo̠ e̠su̠a i̠na, sa̠ awa i̠to̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom obha̠ra̠nom o̠yo̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠go̠ya d̠a̠ esi bho̠ i̠na na̠ agi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘I̠yar u̠bho̠ro̠ghan d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon o̠ro̠ o̠li̠le̠ma d̠i̠yar.’
LUK 19:15 “A̠mite ma̠ ola̠ u̠lo̠gh i̠na ma̠ o̠li̠la ebhugh d̠awa, sa̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠yel. Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom obhelegi rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ikpoki bho̠, ma̠ opura̠n ologhom asu̠o̠ ya̠ awa igir imutiom bho̠.
LUK 19:16 “O̠pu̠r bho̠ a̠ru sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, okpoki d̠oyom amar ipa̠n a̠d̠iobh ami̠na a̠mutiom.’
LUK 19:17 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa amar a̠gir. Anwa ob̠eb̠i ob̠a̠ra̠motu! Ebula̠ agu̠o̠ anwa ileriom ma̠a̠, ta̠ orue obhin anwa ob̠em ologi d̠a̠ o̠nyo̠gbara abar bho̠, anwa ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ola̠ orileghom a̠d̠iobh ibom re̠ma.’
LUK 19:18 “O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠ sa̠ oleghemeni i̠wal ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, okpoki d̠oyom amar ipa̠n ogho ami̠na a̠mutiom.’
LUK 19:19 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ola̠ orileghom ogho ibom re̠ma.’
LUK 19:20 “O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠ sa̠ oleghemeni i̠sar ob̠a̠ra̠motu bho̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, onon okpoki d̠oyom; ami̠ i̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ukpe a̠guri a̠sisa̠n anwa.
LUK 19:21 Ami̠ ighil anwa, ezin bho̠ anwa o̠kparakpar o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin abar o̠la o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ oloyom, sa̠ anwa na̠ a̠b̠u ma̠ esi ola̠ anwa ogbebh d̠o̠.’
LUK 19:22 “Sa̠ wa̠nwuna̠ do̠yo̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Anwa o̠karabh ob̠a̠ra̠motu onon, Ami̠ ta̠ a̠bhin okoroko d̠oyom a̠sobh ase̠ a̠bhumeni nyam. Anwa amar a̠loghom ma̠a̠, ami̠ o̠kparakpar o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin abar ola̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ olami̠, sa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠u ma̠ esi ola̠ ami̠ ogbebh d̠o̠.
LUK 19:23 O̠ku̠a ka̠ a̠mite eka̠, ma̠ ola̠ anwa oguri d̠o̠ ma̠ okpoki d̠ami̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ ta̠ amar ipa̠n a̠mutiom, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠se̠n ami̠ imula̠ iru bho̠ ami̠ ate̠i̠ okpoki d̠ami̠ na̠ asu̠o̠ bho̠?’
LUK 19:24 “Sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ adama ma̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, ‘Ibhine ma̠ okpoki wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ d̠iobh ami̠na bho̠.’
LUK 19:25 “Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠, o̠ni̠ obha̠ na̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ d̠iobh ami̠na d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠.’
LUK 19:26 “Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, ‘Yii, i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ ate̠i̠ bho̠, ta̠ o̠lo̠gho̠m ipa̠n ya̠ ib̠uiy ipu ma̠ o̠ku̠a onigha̠ i̠na; ya̠a̠, i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, bebina̠ o̠nyi̠ki̠kara ya̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ bho̠ eka̠, ta̠ o̠wo̠r obhin.
LUK 19:27 Ya̠a̠, ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ i̠nye̠n ya̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ka̠ ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ oli̠le̠ma d̠awa bho̠, ibhine awa ma̠ eru ma̠ i̠se̠n ma̠ e̠ze̠gi̠ awa d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠ami̠.’ ”
LUK 19:28 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ agba ma̠ i̠nye̠n awe̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ten d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠awa a̠rile adama ma̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m.
LUK 19:29 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tua̠n e̠ma Abe̠ti̠fagi̠ na̠ e̠ma Abe̠tani̠ bho̠, ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ igu Oliv bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom a̠duom i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠,
LUK 19:30 “Itene ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ d̠inyin bho̠, sa̠ ka̠ inyin ud̠igh a̠d̠igha̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠bi̠gh okubh ado̠ki̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ a̠d̠igh a̠rile.
LUK 19:31 Ku̠gba ma̠ o̠ni̠ a̠pura̠n inyin ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin na̠ o̠tu̠n ere na̠ o̠ko̠to̠n okubh ado̠ki̠ bho̠?’ I̠wo̠rane̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh orughom.’ ”
LUK 19:32 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan ya̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom a̠duom bho̠ iten i̠gi̠, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh ma̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠.
LUK 19:33 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠ko̠to̠n okubh ado̠ki̠ bho̠, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ bho̠ ipura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠tu̠n ere na̠ o̠ko̠to̠n okubh ado̠ki̠ bho̠?”
LUK 19:34 Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh orughom.”
LUK 19:35 Sa̠ awa ibhin ado̠ki̠ bho̠ iruom A̠zizo̠s, sa̠ awa i̠ke̠gi̠na ma̠ ibom rakapa d̠awa ibhin i̠de̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ ado̠ki̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠ri̠lo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠.
LUK 19:36 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rile na̠ agi̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠nwunom i̠ke̠gi̠na ma̠ ibom rakapa d̠awa ibhin i̠de̠ d̠a̠ eten bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠d̠ia̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 19:37 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tua̠n esi bho̠ eten bho̠ ake̠ ma̠ okubh d̠a̠ igu Oliv osor bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠, ibhin d̠a̠ a̠libhon ologi i̠ke̠ ma̠ o̠mo̠r aso̠r otutumeni A̠zib̠a̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ogir ilologia̠n ya̠ awa na̠ e̠bi̠gh bho̠, ma̠a̠:
LUK 19:38 “Itutumeni ta̠ A̠zib̠a e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ O̠li̠le̠ma wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠!” “Ekima̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny na̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠ a̠pu bho̠.”
LUK 19:39 Idi ogbo Afarisi ya̠ i̠ro̠ ani̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ sa̠ ifugh inigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ Atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, ghi̠ghana ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠oyom ma̠ ofugh i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a!”
LUK 19:40 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ka̠ awa inima̠ i̠ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m, ikpokpogh i̠gbaki̠ghe̠ bho̠ ta̠ ekpogion izul emulughu etutumeni ami̠.”
LUK 19:41 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tua̠n abi̠gh e̠ma bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠leghe ma̠ ekulom e̠ma bho̠
LUK 19:42 a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “A̠didon ma̠ inyin na̠ ologhom i̠di̠ar ya̠ ta̠ emutiom ekima̠ enigha̠ inyin bho̠ nab̠o̠! Ya̠a̠, na̠ o̠wo̠gi̠o̠m inyin amu̠gho̠nyan i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠.
LUK 19:43 Ya̠ a̠ga̠i, ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ na̠ eru d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ma̠ iya̠, ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom ta̠ elo ma̠ e̠b̠agh ekitineni ma̠ anwa, e̠du̠o̠m a̠nwunom d̠oyom eguri awa d̠a̠ ologi d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ragba bho̠.
LUK 19:44 Awa ta̠ e̠kpi̠ghi̠d̠i̠ nyam d̠a̠ a̠de, erobhom anwa na̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠oyom d̠a̠ re̠b̠agh d̠oyom e̠ze̠gi̠ inyin. Ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom ko oguri d̠o̠ bebina̠ ekpo o̠gbaki̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ ta̠ odi, ezin bho̠ anwa na̠ olelegi d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ma̠zua̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ada i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ obhel bho̠ i̠na a̠ru d̠oyom bho̠.”
LUK 19:45 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ologi Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ ozegi ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ eb̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠b̠ua̠ bho̠.
LUK 19:46 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Na̠ o̠ge̠ oguri d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘Otu d̠ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ otu-a̠siseiny,’ ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ obhin otenemeni ma̠ ‘e̠fe̠m i̠bi̠gh ma̠ a̠b̠igh.’ ”
LUK 19:47 Ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ sa̠ i̠na aro̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ghan atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠. Ya̠a̠, ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, na̠ ikei bho̠, sa̠ i̠ke̠ ma̠ omimia̠n agu̠o̠ obhin ogigh o̠yo̠.
LUK 19:48 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, awa irue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh abar ola̠ odin ogigh o̠yo̠, ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ bho̠, na̠ ebhin obhel na̠ e̠nagha ma̠ asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠da na̠ ebhin.
LUK 20:1 Odi a̠d̠a̠ma̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, na̠ ikei bho̠ iru ra̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠na.
LUK 20:2 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, anwa na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠limon ta̠ a̠nyen na̠ a̠gir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n? A̠nyen a̠nigha̠ nyam a̠limon bho̠?”
LUK 20:3 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠pura̠n ani̠ inyin odi a̠pura̠n:
LUK 20:4 Owur amu̠m ta̠ Azo̠n ka̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ a̠ru?”
LUK 20:5 Sa̠ awa ibhin i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ i̠yar o̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru,’ sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, ‘Inyin udin ere na̠ o̠we̠le̠man od̠umom o̠yo̠?’
LUK 20:6 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ i̠yar u̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ a̠ru,’ sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ta̠ erobhod̠i i̠yar egigh; ezin bho̠, a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ ema̠ra̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa ma̠ Azo̠n owil.”
LUK 20:7 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar uloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ owur amu̠m ta̠ Azo̠n a̠bhin a̠mite.”
LUK 20:8 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ eka̠, ami̠ ko o̠gba d̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ a̠limon obhin ogir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠.”
LUK 20:9 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠tiba̠ra̠ adama ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ a̠rogh a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Odi o̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei a̠grep, sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ esi bho̠ ma̠ igbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n o̠ko̠ orughom, sa̠ a̠b̠etina̠ agi̠ ma̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n ebhugh aro̠ ma̠ owewegh obhel.
LUK 20:10 Ate̠i̠ obhel o̠ku̠ imuma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ awa, obhin a̠bin imuma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ awa i̠ku̠ d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠. Ya̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ id̠ul i̠na, sa̠ imulumeni i̠na ma̠ i̠kpo̠.
LUK 20:11 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom opa̠n ob̠a̠ra̠motu. Obha̠ eka̠ sa̠ awa id̠ul, ikpon i̠do̠ti̠me̠ni̠, sa̠ imulumeni ma̠ i̠kpo̠.
LUK 20:12 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom epa̠ ma̠ oleghemeni i̠sar ob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠; onon eka̠ sa̠ awa id̠ul i̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠ne̠m, ize imutiom.
LUK 20:13 “Sa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ aru̠ru̠an opa̠n agu̠o̠ ogir, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠? Ami̠ ta̠ a̠ruom o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ ami̠ itula̠n ibom bho̠; ka̠din awa ta̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ i̠na.’
LUK 20:14 “Igiel bho̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erughom a̠lei bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na bho̠, sa̠ awa ima̠ra̠nua̠n ma̠a̠, ‘Onon ta̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ad̠i̠a a̠lei bho̠, id̠ighi ogigh i̠na b̠o̠ka̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar o̠ni̠ bho̠ eten iyiyar.’
LUK 20:15 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ awa inu i̠na imutiom d̠a̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ igigh i̠na.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a ka̠, wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠lei bho̠ ta̠ a̠gir ere a̠gboloma̠ awa?
LUK 20:16 I̠na ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ aze̠gi̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ igbebh ma̠ ed̠ia̠n ya̠ i̠ko̠ ma̠ esi bho̠ i̠ro̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠eton a̠lei bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo.” Igiel bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ awa ifugh ma̠a̠, “A̠zib̠a̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ o̠ku̠a ma̠ omite!”
LUK 20:17 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠kpon awa d̠a̠ a̠misigh sa̠ a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “Abar wa̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire-E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “ ‘Ikputu wa̠ ilo ma̠ a̠rutu bho̠ ighel bho̠ na̠ a̠ten e̠ko̠ otu bho̠,’ ka̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ ere?
LUK 20:18 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠melema̠ ma̠ ikputu bho̠ ta̠ a̠b̠ob̠omia̠n; sa̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ ikputu bho̠ a̠mel a̠bhum eka̠ ta̠ a̠tutughud̠ia̠n.”
LUK 20:19 Ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ sa̠ i̠bho̠ro̠gh e̠ti̠ti̠gha o̠wo̠l ob̠ol o̠yo̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ d̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa iloghoma̠n ma̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh bho̠ a̠gboloma̠ awa. Ya̠a̠, awa ighil a̠nwunom bho̠.
LUK 20:20 Awa i̠ro̠ igon o̠bi̠gh e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ ob̠ol A̠zizo̠s, obhin o̠gi̠o̠m ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ na̠ a̠limon d̠a̠ ebhugh bho̠. Sa̠ awa iruom ogbo ipoiny ma̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ o̠ro̠ agu̠o̠ a̠ga̠i a̠nwunom, o̠nagha abar i̠na ta̠ a̠fugh a̠rima̠.
LUK 20:21 Sa̠ ogbo ipoiny bho̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠yar ologhom ma̠ anwa na̠ amar na̠ a̠gir d̠a̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠oyom, sa̠ anwa na̠ okpon d̠o̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ a̠gurumeni, abhe̠l opa̠n, sa̠ anwa na̠ a̠bhin iya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar eten ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 20:22 A̠bhon otua̠ otua̠-ebhugh onigha̠ A̠siza̠ ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ na̠ obhon d̠o̠?”
LUK 20:23 Ya̠a̠, i̠na abi̠gho̠m ipesi d̠awa sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠,
LUK 20:24 “Ileriome ami̠ ma̠ adi̠nari̠. U̠le̠m a̠misigh ta̠ a̠nyen, sa̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ a̠nyen d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “A̠misigh ta̠ A̠siza̠.”
LUK 20:25 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a bha̠, imulumeni ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠siza̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ta̠ A̠siza̠, ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ita̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
LUK 20:26 Awa i̠kpati̠ i̠na ma̠ osor, ya̠a̠ awo̠ran d̠o̠yo̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ awa orue d̠o̠ ma̠ osibh o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom bho̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ awo̠ran d̠o̠yo̠ a̠d̠igh awa ma̠ ilologia̠n o̠mu̠gho̠n, sa̠ awa inima̠ i̠ro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m.
LUK 20:27 Idi Rasadusi, ya̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh odi bho̠, i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠te̠i̠ A̠zizo̠s epura̠n ma̠a̠,
LUK 20:28 “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, A̠mozizi age̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar ma̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠ umor o̠ni̠ a̠mugh awe̠le̠man ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ad̠u̠a, ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠, ma̠a̠, o̠ni̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠bhin ani̠ umor bho̠ b̠o̠ka̠ ate̠i̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠nigha̠ ma̠ umor d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 20:29 I̠se̠n bha̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor e̠ro̠; sa̠ o̠pu̠r bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ ya̠a̠ i̠na na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ sa̠ a̠mugh awe̠le̠man ani̠ bho̠ ad̠u̠a.
LUK 20:30 Sa̠ oleghemeni i̠wal umor bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ bho̠, i̠na eka̠ na̠ o̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ sa̠ a̠mugh.
LUK 20:31 Sa̠ oleghemeni i̠sar umor bho̠ a̠bhin ani̠ bho̠. O̠ku̠a oku̠a tu̠tu̠n eb̠la̠ a̠rumor bho̠ ibhin ani̠ bho̠ sa̠ imugughu, i̠mar d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny eguri.
LUK 20:32 Ekunuguma̠ bho̠ sa̠ ani̠ bho̠ a̠mugh nyen.
LUK 20:33 Gba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar, igiel ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ ka̠, ani̠ bho̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ ani̠ ta̠ a̠nyen, d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ ani̠ bho̠ na̠ awal eb̠la̠ od̠ua̠l a̠rumor bho̠?”
LUK 20:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “A̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ amu̠m onon bho̠ ta̠ ebhinogh anwani̠, sa̠ ta̠ onigha̠nom anwi̠nyan anwi̠i̠ny bho̠.
LUK 20:35 Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ ada a̠bhin, ma̠ awa e̠kpe̠ ma̠ ob̠egina̠ d̠a̠ omugh od̠igh d̠a̠ amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠, ilom bo̠;
LUK 20:36 awa ko omugh mu, ezin bho̠ awa ta̠ e̠ro̠ ka̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Awa anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ezin bho̠ awa anwi̠i̠ny ya̠ na̠ eb̠egina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠.
LUK 20:37 Ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, A̠mozizi eka̠ agba a̠mutiom d̠a̠ asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠, wa̠ ed̠um bho̠ a̠mumor ya̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠o̠ bho̠. A̠mozizi a̠bhelegi ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Ebraham, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Azi̠ki̠, na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ A̠zeko̠pu̠.’
LUK 20:38 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠na A̠zib̠a̠ imumugh d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ i̠na ola̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um; ezin bho̠, d̠o̠yo̠ eb̠la̠ awa od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um.”
LUK 20:39 Sa̠ idi ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠ i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, anwa amar agba ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠.”
LUK 20:40 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ne ma̠ o̠kpato̠n o̠nu̠ opura̠n abar na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 20:41 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere wa̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠, Akrai̠st wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aso̠n a̠doni bho̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠devidi bho̠?
LUK 20:42 Ezin bho̠, A̠devidi na̠ agu̠o̠ agba a̠mutiom d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire Raso̠r bho̠ ma̠a̠, “ ‘Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠a̠: “Ri̠la d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠,
LUK 20:43 tu̠tu̠n ami̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom ma̠ okpokpolom ola̠ o̠gbam a̠sike d̠oyom.” ’
LUK 20:44 A̠devidi a̠bhelegi gha̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, ‘Wa̠nwuna̠.’ O̠ku̠a ka̠ i̠na a̠ten eka̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠?”
LUK 20:45 Igiel bho̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ e̠nagha i̠na bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠a̠,
LUK 20:46 “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ ma̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠. Awa iba̠ra̠ ma̠ opa̠n obura̠ ibom rakapa isosor, sa̠ iba̠ra̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhin d̠a̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi ebheleguma̠ awa d̠a̠ regbolom a̠b̠ua̠, sekina̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠dila̠de edim d̠a̠ a̠rutu u̠gala A̠zu, na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ rakpata o̠d̠e̠ ya̠ edim.
LUK 20:47 Awa na̠ eponoma̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠ na̠ e̠wo̠ro̠gh i̠di̠ar, sa̠ awa na̠ esiseiny iwewegh a̠siseiny b̠o̠ka̠ olelegi awa. Ta̠ o̠gu̠r awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠zagba ola̠ abu̠gh ibom.”
LUK 21:1 Igiel bho̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠b̠eka̠ a̠kpon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ aru̠li̠la bho̠ na̠ ebhin na̠ e̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ ikpoki ali̠se̠bh d̠awa d̠a̠ igba̠ o̠da ikpoki bho̠.
LUK 21:2 I̠na abi̠gh nyen ka̠ odi onyigoiny ekpukele ani̠, agi̠ ka̠ alo̠gh i̠wal i̠gbara ikpoki ako̠pa d̠a̠ ologi igba̠ bho̠.
LUK 21:3 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mutiom okoroko ma̠a̠: “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ igba̠ bho̠, onyigoiny ekpukele ani̠ onon alo̠gh a̠pu.
LUK 21:4 Ezin bho̠, eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n na̠ ibom e̠li̠la d̠awa, wa̠ a̠ru, ape̠to̠n o̠nyi̠ esi d̠a̠ e̠li̠la d̠o̠yo̠ alo̠gh. Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ologi igoiny d̠o̠yo̠, i̠na a̠kpukpu ma̠ eb̠la̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠nwuna̠ bho̠ alo̠gh.”
LUK 21:5 Idi ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ a̠libhon Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, d̠a̠ e̠mi̠ agu̠o̠ ubhin ib̠eb̠i i̠gbaki̠ghe̠, na̠ i̠d̠i̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ ya̠ ub̠eton u̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ uburi ma̠ otu bho̠. Ya̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s agba ma̠a̠,
LUK 21:6 “I̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh i̠se̠n bho̠, obhel na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ bebina̠ ekpo o̠gbaki̠ghe̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ ta̠ odi; ta̠ ob̠ogion eb̠la̠yi osoroni.”
LUK 21:7 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ka̠ ta̠ emite ma̠ a̠kere igiel? Sa̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhin a̠kere a̠d̠ien elegh eloghom ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ etua̠n omite?”
LUK 21:8 Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠ b̠o̠ka̠ ugelemeni inyin; ezin bho̠ a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom ta̠ ebhin a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠ eru, sa̠ awa ta̠ ekue inyin e̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘Ami̠ Witenemeni bho̠, obhel bho̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n!’ Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ko od̠umom e̠tu̠o̠no̠m awa.
LUK 21:9 Igiel inyin umugho̠n i̠mu̠mu̠gho̠n e̠gham na̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere a̠d̠ugh e̠mu̠, o̠ni̠ ko okpa̠ra̠noma̠. Ezin bho̠, i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ ed̠ia̠ emite; ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ekunuguma̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ onin obhel bho̠.”
LUK 21:10 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ebhugh ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠wia̠n ebhugh, sa̠ a̠de e̠ma ta̠ a̠wia̠n a̠de e̠ma.
LUK 21:11 Sa̠ a̠d̠izo ibom ib̠ob̠omia̠n a̠de ta̠ emite, sa̠ o̠ko̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n na̠ i̠karabh asu̠nwe̠r ta̠ esor a̠d̠izo a̠risisi; sa̠ ra̠d̠ugh ibom a̠rugugu na̠ ibom ilologia̠n ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny emite.
LUK 21:12 “Ya̠a̠, kisa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite, ta̠ ogbikimeni inyin ibom. Ta̠ ob̠ologh inyin, sa̠ ta̠ obhin inyin ka̠ od̠ighom d̠a̠ ru̠gala A̠zu na̠ a̠rutu ikoli, sa̠ ta̠ obhin inyin ka̠ o̠marame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh aru̠li̠le̠ma na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rebhugh, d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠d̠ien d̠ami̠.
LUK 21:13 Sa̠ onon ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin e̠ti̠ti̠gha ola̠ obhin o̠gba ami̠ omutiom.
LUK 21:14 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ko o̠nyo̠gho̠ghan egboloma̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ obhin o̠gba o̠nu̠ o̠bhe̠la, d̠a̠ riku ya̠ awa ta̠ eleregi inyin bho̠.
LUK 21:15 Ezin bho̠, ami̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠ga̠i o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ na̠ eloghom abar ya̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠rid̠ien d̠inyin ko orue d̠o̠ e̠damaghan, bo̠d̠o̠ e̠gba e̠ne̠gi̠me̠ni̠ nyen.
LUK 21:16 Ogbo ya̠ i̠mar itua̠n inyin eka̠-roweni na̠ rowede d̠inyin, a̠rumor na̠ a̠ghisia̠n, na̠ ra̠tologha̠n ta̠ ewol inyin. Sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ idi inyin.
LUK 21:17 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠din ami̠ alo̠gh inyin a̠d̠ien.
LUK 21:18 Ya̠a̠, ekpo asi̠ghal e̠mu̠ d̠inyin ola̠ ta̠ akadi̠na a̠bhe ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 21:19 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠ ine ma̠ e̠ro̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ otenemeni ma̠ aru̠mu̠gh d̠inyin.
LUK 21:20 “Igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ka̠ ro̠lo̠gh ogbo-e̠gham na̠ eko ma̠ e̠ma A̠zeruse̠le̠m ekiton, bha̠ iloghome ma̠ obhel okunugi o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n.
LUK 21:21 Obhel o̠ku̠a, ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠ ekpo ma̠ eghil e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ rigu bho̠, ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io e̠ma bho̠ eten e̠d̠u̠a, ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ re̠sala aka e̠ma bho̠, ya̠ od̠i ma̠ ipa̠n a̠risisi bho̠ eka̠, omula̠ d̠o̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠.
LUK 21:22 Ezin bho̠ i̠nye̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ od̠e olo ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ma̠ omuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ya̠ u̠ge̠ uguri bho̠.
LUK 21:23 Ekulom anwani̠ a̠rughun na̠ anwani̠ amu̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠! Ezin bho̠ ibom i̠kparama ado̠l ta̠ emuzo d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠ na̠ ibom i̠gam ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ agam a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n.
LUK 21:24 Idi awa ta̠ emugughu d̠a̠ alapa ogidi, sa̠ ta̠ obhin idi awa od̠ighom ikoli d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ rebhugh e̠mara̠nwunom. Sa̠ ogbo o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠ ta̠ ebhin a̠de ma̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, tu̠tu̠n ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom obhel ta̠ ogbo o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠.
LUK 21:25 “Relegh ta̠ emite d̠a̠ ogogo bho̠, na̠ uwetire bho̠ na̠ i̠ni̠nai̠ny bho̠. D̠a̠ a̠de onon sa̠ a̠d̠ugh ta̠ a̠bhin rebhugh bho̠, sa̠ e̠mi̠ oghur rabadi̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠gi̠o̠m anyu̠ ropoka̠n amu̠m bho̠, na̠ irorua̠ amu̠m o̠bhaghan na̠ okeleghel bho̠ ta̠ ed̠igh awa ma̠ ilologia̠n.
LUK 21:26 A̠nwunom ta̠ e̠fu̠mu̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠rugugu i̠di̠ar ya̠ ta̠ emite d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠. Ezin bho̠ ra̠limon e̠nai̠ny bho̠ ta̠ enyegia̠n.
LUK 21:27 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠bi̠gh O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠, ya̠ na̠ a̠ru na̠ a̠limon na̠ ibom isosorogia̠n.
LUK 21:28 Igiel i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ e̠ke̠ na̠ emite, bha̠ ib̠etina̠ ma̠ e̠mara, ma̠ eb̠eka̠ ma̠ ekpon d̠a̠ anyu̠; ezin bho̠ oten d̠inyin na̠ a̠tua̠n.”
LUK 21:29 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rogh a̠sidogh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠: “Ikpone ma̠ oriren wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ a̠fig bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ iriren bho̠.
LUK 21:30 Igiel i̠mu̠nu̠mu̠n d̠awa na̠ e̠mu̠r na̠ emite, bha̠ inyin na̠ ologhom ma̠ a̠d̠io a̠kozogh na̠ a̠tua̠n.
LUK 21:31 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, igiel inyin u̠bi̠gh ka̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ emite, bha̠ iloghome ma̠a̠, irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n.
LUK 21:32 “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, a̠nwunom ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠a̠ amu̠m onon bho̠, ko omugughu d̠o̠ e̠man, kisa̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite e̠man.
LUK 21:33 A̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny na̠ ta̠ eten emunia̠n, ya̠a̠ o̠nu̠-o̠kpe̠ d̠ami̠ ta̠ e̠ri̠la tu̠tu̠n ka̠ id̠ud̠ul.
LUK 21:34 I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpona̠! O̠ni̠ ko oma̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠karabh i̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ i̠ku̠nu̠, na̠ e̠ye̠gha ogir o̠d̠a a̠min, na̠ i̠nyo̠gho̠nyo̠gh a̠ghud̠um ma̠ odughumeni rologi d̠inyin, ma̠ ola̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠ ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠bhin inyin awai̠
LUK 21:35 ma̠ agu̠o̠ abar ola̠ u̠kpati̠. I̠di̠ar i̠nye̠ ta̠ emutuma̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ a̠de no̠.
LUK 21:36 Igone ma̠ esiseiny kigiel kigiel, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin o̠te̠i̠ e̠mi̠ omiza̠n eb̠la̠ ra̠d̠ugh ya̠ ta̠ emite bho̠, na̠ orue o̠mara d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠.”
LUK 21:37 Ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠, A̠zizo̠s atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ghan a̠nwunom d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠gha̠n ka̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ igu wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Oliv bho̠ ma̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n.
LUK 21:38 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠on gha̠n ib̠etina̠ ma̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠ i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠nagha i̠na d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 22:1 Igiel bho̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n E̠yal Abe̠re̠di̠ Ya̠ Owubh D̠o̠ bho̠, wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠,
LUK 22:2 sa̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ku̠ro̠m d̠a̠ roloko bho̠ ima̠ra̠nua̠n ogigh A̠zizo̠s. Ya̠a̠, awa ighil a̠nwunom bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa ipuru d̠o̠ ma̠ elobhiri ma̠ osor.
LUK 22:3 Sa̠ Eru Bho̠ a̠d̠igh A̠zuda̠s wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ Iskari̠o̠t bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ologi a̠d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠.
LUK 22:4 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekponom otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan agu̠o̠ owol A̠zizo̠s onigha̠ awa.
LUK 22:5 Sa̠ a̠d̠igh awa ma̠ ologi ma̠ opa̠n, sa̠ awa ima̠ra̠nua̠n onigha̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠ ikpoki.
LUK 22:6 Sa̠ i̠na a̠ma̠ra̠nua̠n awa, sa̠ i̠na ake̠ ma̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan obhel ola̠ ta̠ a̠sora̠n i̠na ma̠ owol A̠zizo̠s onigha̠ awa, b̠o̠ka̠ awa eb̠ol i̠na ma̠ obhel ola̠ a̠nwunom o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 22:7 I̠se̠n wa̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ E̠yal Abe̠re̠di̠ Ya̠ Owubh D̠o̠ na̠ a̠lei bho̠, ta̠ ogigh o̠nyi̠ o̠nana i̠ko̠l E̠yal Opel Oten.
LUK 22:8 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ruom A̠pita̠ na̠ Azo̠n, sa̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠gi̠e̠ ma̠ ka̠ ekokod̠ia̠n ed̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ i̠yar, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠yar od̠e ma̠ onin esi.”
LUK 22:9 Sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ken ka̠ okokod̠ia̠n e̠yal bho̠?”
LUK 22:10 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Agu̠o̠ bho̠ inyin ud̠igh d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rol afa amu̠m ta̠ abi̠ghan inyin. I̠tu̠o̠no̠me̠ i̠na ma̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ otu wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠pel a̠d̠igh bho̠,
LUK 22:11 ma̠ e̠gba ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ otu bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘O̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠pura̠n anwa ma̠a̠: Oken e̠kpe̠ isuloma̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠ami̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠?’
LUK 22:12 Sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠leriom inyin obom e̠kpe̠ otu ola̠ na̠ o̠mar oburi oguri d̠a̠ otu anyu̠. I̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ ekokod̠ia̠n ed̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠.”
