LUK 22:13 Sa̠ awa iten i̠gi̠, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠: sa̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ ikokod̠ia̠n ed̠ia̠n E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠.
LUK 22:14 Igiel obhel bho̠ a̠lei bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo ogir d̠o̠yo̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de.
LUK 22:15 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Na̠ ebhir ami̠ ka̠ obom igiel od̠igh na̠ inyin od̠e E̠yal Opel Oten onon, kisa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠gbika̠.
LUK 22:16 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ami̠ ko od̠e mu ma̠ ed̠ia̠n i̠nye̠n, a̠ten ka̠ na̠ omuzoghod̠iom d̠a̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.”
LUK 22:17 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin okpa̠ko a̠min bho̠, sa̠ ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ibhine ma̠ e̠ru̠gi̠an e̠d̠a.
LUK 22:18 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ami̠ ko o̠d̠a mu ma̠ a̠min a̠grep, a̠ten ka̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ru.”
LUK 22:19 Sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin abe̠re̠di̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠puiny a̠nigha̠ awa, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Onon ozu d̠ami̠ wa̠ na̠ onigha̠ inyin bho̠. Igire ma̠ o̠ko̠no̠n ma̠ e̠ru̠ru̠an ami̠.”
LUK 22:20 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa na̠ ed̠e e̠we̠le̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Okpa̠ko onon omom i̠zo̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ola̠ na̠ ozu ma̠ asi̠ d̠ami̠, ma̠ obhin o̠ta inyin.
LUK 22:21 Ya̠a̠, ikpone! Agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol ami̠ bho̠, od̠i na̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ onin akpata od̠e bho̠.
LUK 22:22 Ta̠ ogir onigha̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ o̠to̠ oguri bho̠. Ya̠a̠, itogi e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠wol i̠na bho̠!”
LUK 22:23 Sa̠ odi ake̠ ma̠ opura̠n odi ma̠a̠, a̠nyen o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a bho̠?
LUK 22:24 Sa̠ aku̠a̠nan a̠sor d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa ma̠a̠: “A̠nyen o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ i̠na abu̠gh a̠pu bho̠?”
LUK 22:25 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Aru̠li̠le̠ma ogbo o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zu bho̠, na̠ ebhin ibom a̠limon na̠ erileghom a̠nwunom d̠awa, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ awa na̠ erileghom bho̠ na̠ ebhelegi awa ma̠ ib̠eb̠i a̠nwunom.
LUK 22:26 Ya̠a̠, o̠ri̠la d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin. Ari̠la ka̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ abu̠gh a̠pu d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin bho̠, ta̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ i̠na aki̠r a̠pu; ya̠a̠, i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠rileghom bho̠ ta̠ aro̠ ka̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu.
LUK 22:27 D̠a̠ inyin ka̠ a̠nyen abu̠gh a̠pu? I̠na wa̠ d̠a̠ akpata od̠e bho̠ ke̠re̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ i̠na wa̠ na̠ aru̠gi̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠? I̠na wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ akpata od̠e bho̠! Ya̠a̠, ami̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin ka̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ aru̠gi̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.
LUK 22:28 Inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠igh na̠ ami̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ rad̠agi̠an d̠ami̠.
LUK 22:29 Agu̠o̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de irileghom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠dila̠de irileghom bho̠,
LUK 22:30 b̠o̠ka̠ inyin od̠igh na̠ ami̠ od̠e, o̠d̠a d̠a̠ akpata od̠e d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ irileghom d̠ami̠. Sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠ri̠la d̠a̠ ibom ra̠dila̠de irileghom, orileghom d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal roghol Izre̠l bho̠.
LUK 22:31 “Asai̠mo̠n, Asai̠mo̠n, kpona̠! Eru Bho̠ na̠ a̠puru ma̠ onyegi eb̠la̠ inyin, ma̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ obhin ozeghema̠ na̠ ozeghe ma̠ i̠bu̠kpa.
LUK 22:32 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠siseiny a̠nigha̠ nyam, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom ko od̠im d̠o̠. Igiel anwa na̠ a̠tiba̠ra̠, ghu̠ame̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠rumor d̠oyom.”
LUK 22:33 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n o̠tu̠o̠no̠m oyom o̠gi̠ ikoli sekina̠ omugh.”
LUK 22:34 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran A̠pita̠ ma̠a̠, “A̠pita̠, ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, kisa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r-e̠ma ta̠ alal a̠didon, anwa ta̠ aku̠a ami̠ i̠sar igiel ma̠ anwa na̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ami̠.”
LUK 22:35 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Obhel bho̠ ami̠ iruom inyin ka̠ o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ ifugh ma̠ o̠ni̠ ko o̠b̠ar na̠ o̠kara, e̠kpa, bo̠d̠o̠ agbaka ma̠ ebhin e̠gi̠ bho̠, abar ola̠ akparama inyin aro̠ ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran ma̠a̠, “E̠e̠nyi̠, abar ola̠ akparama i̠yar na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.”
LUK 22:36 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “A̠b̠eton i̠se̠n agi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ e̠kpa ikpoki a̠bhin; onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ okuru anya. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ alapa ogidi, a̠wol obom akapa d̠o̠yo̠ wa̠ na̠ o̠lagha d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠ a̠gho ma̠ odi.
LUK 22:37 Ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha inyin ma̠a̠, ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom abar wa̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠ire iwowa̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ‘U̠wal ani̠ i̠na o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ogbo id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.’ Sa̠, eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ i̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ ami̠ bho̠ ta̠ emite ga̠i.”
LUK 22:38 Sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, kpone, i̠nye̠n i̠wal ipod̠i ralapa ogidi.” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “I̠marame̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.”
LUK 22:39 A̠zizo̠s ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ igu Oliv ma̠ agu̠o̠ bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠guri gha̠n na̠ a̠gir bho̠; sa̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na.
LUK 22:40 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠misi ma̠ esi bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠kikiom awa ma̠a̠, “Isiseinye b̠o̠ka̠ ad̠agi̠an i̠te̠i̠ inyin.”
LUK 22:41 Sa̠ i̠na a̠toka̠n ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ ogbeiny d̠o̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠kpuluma̠n a̠siseiny ma̠a̠,
LUK 22:42 “O̠we̠de̠, ku̠gba ma̠ od̠i d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠oyom, si̠ghe̠ ma̠ okpa̠ko onon d̠a̠ ozu d̠ami̠; ku̠ku̠m eka̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠ami̠, aro̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠oyom.”
LUK 22:43 [Sa̠ orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠ru ra̠ aghu̠ame̠ni̠ i̠na.
LUK 22:44 Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ta̠ emutuma̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na alo̠gh e̠mi̠ a̠siseiny ka̠ ate̠i̠ esi ola̠, onumor d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠gharaghu̠ d̠a̠ a̠de ma̠ agu̠o̠ ikpokpogh asi̠.]
LUK 22:45 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ a̠siseiny bho̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ ogbo atu̠ghan d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh ka̠ awa na̠ ekod̠u d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠ku̠nu̠.
LUK 22:46 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere ka̠ inyin na̠ okod̠u? Ib̠etina̠ ma̠ esiseiny, b̠o̠ka̠ ad̠agi̠an na̠ o̠te̠i̠ inyin.”
LUK 22:47 I̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠fugh, sa̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom iru. O̠ni̠ wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠zuda̠s bho̠, odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ d̠iobh na̠ i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠, a̠rileghom awa a̠ru. Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠bhin i̠pi̠pi̠o̠bh a̠bhelegi ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 22:48 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠pura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “A̠zuda̠s, anwa na̠ a̠bhin ibheleguma̠ i̠pi̠pi̠o̠bh na̠ a̠wol O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ke̠re̠?”
LUK 22:49 Igiel bho̠ ogbo atu̠ghan bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ eru ra̠ omite bho̠, sa̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠, i̠yar obhin ralapa ogidi bho̠ owe awa ke̠re̠?”
LUK 22:50 Sa̠ odi awa a̠sobh od̠iom a̠to ogoni ta̠ we̠mu̠ okur bho̠ a̠b̠uton.
LUK 22:51 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran ma̠a̠: “Na̠ a̠bhon. O̠ni̠ ka̠ ogir o̠ku̠a!” Sa̠ i̠na a̠kula̠n a̠to o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠koko.
LUK 22:52 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ we̠mu̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekponom otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, na̠ ikei bho̠, ya̠ iru ra̠ ob̠ol o̠yo̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n o̠ni̠ ke̠re̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ obhin ralapa ogidi na̠ re̠ba̠m na̠ oru ra̠ ob̠ol ami̠?
LUK 22:53 Ami̠ i̠ri̠la na̠ inyin ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ya̠a̠ inyin ub̠ol d̠o̠ ami̠. Ya̠a̠, onon obhel d̠inyin wa̠ a̠limon a̠d̠io azi̠m na̠ a̠rileghom bho̠.”
LUK 22:54 Sa̠ awa ib̠ol i̠na irileghom i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ we̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, ya̠a̠ A̠pita̠ aro̠ ma̠ esi egbeiny atu̠o̠no̠m awa.
LUK 22:55 Obhel bho̠ awa na̠ egbonogi ma̠ anya d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io etire bho̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de ikiton anya bho̠, sa̠ A̠pita̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ awa ari̠la ani̠ ma̠ i̠se̠.
LUK 22:56 Sa̠ odi ob̠a̠ra̠motu o̠nyani̠ a̠bhin e̠b̠alab̠al anya bho̠ a̠lelegi ma̠ A̠pita̠, sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “O̠ni̠ onon ari̠la na̠ A̠zizo̠s.”
LUK 22:57 Sa̠ i̠na aku̠a a̠fugh ma̠a̠: “Ani̠ bho̠, ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ i̠na.”
LUK 22:58 O̠nyi̠-o̠gbara obhel a̠ten, sa̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ abi̠gh i̠na sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa odi o̠ni̠ awa.” Ya̠a̠ A̠pita̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ bho̠, ami̠ ani̠ d̠o̠!”
LUK 22:59 Obhel a̠ten, sa̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ ari̠la ma̠ ofugh ofugh ma̠a̠, “Kagu̠o̠ kagu̠o̠ u̠gba, i̠na odi o̠ni̠ bho̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na ola̠ Agalili.”
LUK 22:60 Sa̠ A̠pita̠ awo̠ran ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ bho̠, ami̠ iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar anwa na̠ agba.” I̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ awi̠oghan sa̠ olobhiri e̠nu̠r-e̠ma bho̠ alal.
LUK 22:61 Sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠tiba̠ra̠ a̠kpon A̠pita̠. Sa̠ i̠na aru̠ru̠an ikpo a̠fugh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, ya̠ a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ i̠na bho̠, ma̠a̠, “Anwa ta̠ aku̠a ami̠ ma̠ i̠sar igiel kisa̠ e̠nu̠r ta̠ alal a̠didon.”
LUK 22:62 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mite d̠a̠ etire ka̠ a̠leghe agba igbir.
LUK 22:63 Ogbo e̠gham ya̠ na̠ ekponom A̠zizo̠s bho̠, i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na ed̠ul i̠na.
LUK 22:64 Sa̠ awa ibhin abar ibinom a̠rid̠ien d̠o̠yo̠. Sa̠ isorogiom i̠na ma̠ adi̠e̠l ipura̠n ma̠a̠, “Wa̠, ma̠ agba ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠b̠or anwa bho̠.”
LUK 22:65 Sa̠ awa ikpon abar abar ifugh i̠na, ikpon i̠do̠ti̠me̠ni̠.
LUK 22:66 A̠d̠io ab̠al a̠sor, sa̠ ikei irileghom bho̠, na̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur bho̠, na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, ikokod̠ia̠n id̠igh ezue, sa̠ irileghom A̠zizo̠s ka̠ i̠marame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ogbo aru̠mu̠ i̠to̠ ebhugh d̠awa.
LUK 22:67 Sa̠ ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa Akrai̠st bho̠ ke̠re̠.” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ i̠gba eka̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, inyin ko oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠,
LUK 22:68 ka̠ ami̠ ipura̠n inyin abar eka̠, inyin ko oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ o̠wo̠ran ami̠.
LUK 22:69 Ya̠a̠ ob̠eton i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon a̠pu bho̠.”
LUK 22:70 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa ipura̠n i̠na ma̠a̠, “O̠ku̠a bha̠ anwa O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, d̠u̠ko̠?” Sa̠ i̠na awo̠ran awa ma̠a̠, “Od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa i̠gba bho̠.”
LUK 22:71 Sa̠ awa i̠gba ma̠a̠, “Ezin ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠tu̠n o̠bho̠ro̠gh opa̠n onyob̠a̠ d̠a̠ e̠kal abar onon, od̠i ke̠re̠? I̠yar na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n abar bho̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠o̠yo̠.”
LUK 23:1 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ib̠egina̠ irileghom A̠zizo̠s ka̠ i̠marame̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Apai̠let
LUK 23:2 Sa̠ awa iler i̠na ma̠ riku, ib̠ologiom i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠yar u̠bi̠gh ka̠ o̠ni̠ onon na̠ abho̠ro̠gh od̠ineni ebhugh d̠i̠yar, sa̠ na̠ a̠kigima̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom otua̠ otua̠-ebhugh onigha̠ A̠siza̠, sa̠ na̠ are̠ma ma̠ i̠na Akrai̠st, O̠li̠le̠ma.”
LUK 23:3 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠pura̠n A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “Anwa O̠li̠le̠ma a̠nwunom A̠zu ke̠re̠?” Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwa i̠gba bho̠.”
LUK 23:4 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠tiba̠ra̠ adama ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, na̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠, agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ o̠ni̠ onon a̠gir api̠e̠ d̠a̠ riku wa̠ inyin uleregi i̠na bho̠.”
LUK 23:5 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠gba o̠gba o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ a̠bhin atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠tumugi ma̠ a̠nwunom osorogi akpe̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ A̠zudia̠, ob̠eton d̠a̠ Agalili esi bho̠ i̠na ake̠ bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ra̠ ate̠i̠ enen.”
LUK 23:6 Igiel bho̠ Apai̠let amu̠gho̠n e̠kal onon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n ku̠gba ma̠ A̠zizo̠s o̠nyi̠ eghun Agalili.
LUK 23:7 Igiel bho̠ i̠na ra̠ a̠loghom ma̠ A̠zizo̠s od̠i d̠a̠ ebu i̠to̠ ta̠ E̠ro̠d bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠ruom awa ma̠ obhin A̠zizo̠s o̠gi̠o̠m E̠ro̠d. A̠sora̠n ola̠ E̠ro̠d na̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m ma̠ obhel obha̠.
LUK 23:8 Obhel igiel E̠ro̠d abi̠gh A̠zizo̠s bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhon ologi ma̠ ibom, ezin bho̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gon o̠bi̠gh ani̠ A̠zizo̠s. I̠na na̠ amu̠gho̠n o̠du̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠b̠em ologi ma̠ o̠bi̠gh obhel A̠zizo̠s ta̠ a̠gir ilologia̠n d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 23:9 I̠na a̠bhin obhel a̠pura̠n A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠ien kerekere ipura̠n, ya̠a̠ ekpo abar ola̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
LUK 23:10 Ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, na̠ ogbo a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi bho̠, i̠mara ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ emulughuom i̠na, na̠ eb̠ologiom i̠na ma̠ ibom ib̠ologiom.
LUK 23:11 A̠ga̠i E̠ro̠d na̠ o̠lo̠gh e̠gham d̠o̠yo̠ eka̠, esorogiom i̠na ma̠ adi̠e̠l, e̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na. Sa̠ ibhin obom ob̠eb̠i akapa aru̠li̠la iburi i̠na, sa̠ imulumeni i̠na i̠gi̠o̠m Apai̠let.
LUK 23:12 A̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠ sa̠ E̠ro̠d na̠ Apai̠let itulugia̠n iten ra̠tologha̠n; ma̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien.
LUK 23:13 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠kokod̠i ma̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, na̠ ikei ogbo ya̠ na̠ erileghom ebhugh bho̠, na̠ a̠nwunom bho̠,
LUK 23:14 sa̠ agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin ubhin o̠ni̠ onon oruom ami̠, o̠gba ma̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tumugi ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ osorogi akpe̠. Ami̠ na̠ ad̠a i̠na a̠kpon d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠inyin, ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ami̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ ezin ola̠ odin osobh ase̠ obhumeni o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ riku ya̠ inyin uleregi i̠na bho̠.
LUK 23:15 E̠ro̠d eka̠ na̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ i̠na api̠e̠, obha̠ ezin bho̠ i̠na a̠mulumeni i̠na a̠ruom i̠yar bho̠. Inyin o̠mar o̠bi̠gh ma̠a̠, abar ola̠ o̠ni̠ onon api̠o̠m ola̠ odin ogigh o̠yo̠ o̠lo̠gh bo̠.
LUK 23:16 D̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ ta̠ a̠ruom agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠gu̠ro̠gh i̠na, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠man i̠na ma̠ oten oyel.”
LUK 23:17 [D̠a̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ E̠yal Opel Oten bho̠, akpe̠ ma̠ Apai̠let omutiom odi o̠ni̠, d̠a̠ awa ogbo ya̠ u̠lo̠gh ikoli bho̠ onigha̠ awa]
LUK 23:18 Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom bho̠ ibhin onin okoroko emulughu, e̠gba ma̠a̠, “Si̠ghe̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon ma̠ ebhin ka̠ egigh, ma̠ a̠mutiom Abarabas a̠nigha̠ i̠yar!”
LUK 23:19 (Abarabas o̠ni̠ ola̠ u̠du̠o̠m d̠a̠ ikoli, d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh na̠ ipa̠n ogbo a̠sorogi ma̠ rakpe̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, na̠ owia̠n oghum a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ obhin, sa̠ a̠gigh o̠ni̠ nyen.)
LUK 23:20 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠nwe a̠bhelegi awa a̠kikiom, ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ abho̠ro̠gh omutiom A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 23:21 Ya̠a̠, awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ omulughu omulughu izul ma̠a̠, “I̠du̠ i̠na ma̠ egigh d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠! I̠du̠ i̠na ma̠ egigh d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠!”
LUK 23:22 Sa̠ i̠na a̠nwe a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ oleghemeni i̠sar igiel ma̠a̠, “Ezin ka̠ ere, i̠na a̠gir a̠kere a̠d̠ien i̠karabh? Ami̠ i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ ezin ola̠ odin ogigh o̠yo̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ ta̠ a̠ruom o̠gu̠ro̠gh o̠yo̠, sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom i̠na.”
LUK 23:23 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ awa i̠ro̠ ma̠ izul izul i̠nyagh ma̠a̠, o̠du̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren ogigh, sa̠ Apai̠let a̠ma̠ra̠ a̠nigha̠ awa.
LUK 23:24 Sa̠ Apai̠let a̠sobh ase̠ bho̠ a̠guri ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa na̠ epuru bho̠.
LUK 23:25 Sa̠ i̠na a̠mutiom d̠a̠ ikoli bho̠ ma̠ Abarabas, o̠ni̠ wa̠ awa i̠bho̠ro̠gh omutiom onigha̠ awa bho̠, wa̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ipa̠n ogbo a̠sorogi ma̠ rakpe̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠, na̠ owia̠n oghum a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ ebhugh bho̠ obhin bho̠, sa̠ a̠gigh nyen o̠ni̠ bho̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton A̠zizo̠s alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠awa ma̠ ogir abar rologi d̠awa ibhir.
LUK 23:26 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ erileghom A̠zizo̠s na̠ e̠d̠u̠a bho̠, sa̠ awa isibh Asai̠mo̠n wa̠ A̠sirin bho̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ i̠na na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠sala bho̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠. Sa̠ awa inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ ma̠ orol o̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 23:27 Sa̠ obom o̠lo̠gh a̠nwunom i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na d̠a̠ aman. Idi a̠nwunom d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ anwani̠, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ igbir d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠.
LUK 23:28 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠tiba̠ra̠ a̠kpon awa a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “E-e anwani̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m! O̠ni̠ ko o̠tu̠n ami̠ ma̠ e̠gba ma̠ igbir, ya̠a̠ i̠gba ma̠ igbir egboloma̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin sekina̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠inyin.
LUK 23:29 Ezin bho̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ na̠ eru d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ ma̠ igiel ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, ‘E̠b̠e̠l re̠mar anwani̠, na̠ a̠rutu-i̠mara ya̠ ta̠ o̠mara̠gi̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, na̠ aru̠mu̠mam ya̠ ta̠ o̠nigha̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny amu̠mam bho̠.’
LUK 23:30 Sa̠ “ ‘Awa ta̠ e̠le̠gh rigu bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Imele ma̠ ebhum i̠yar!” Sa̠ awa ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ efugh enigha̠ ma̠ a̠rugugum bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ikpegiome i̠yar!” ’
LUK 23:31 Ku̠gba ma̠ a̠nwunom na̠ egir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n obhel ola̠ oriren bho̠ od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ omom, ka̠a̠, ere ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ obhel ola̠ oriren bho̠ na̠ aghi̠ghara?”
LUK 23:32 Awa irileghom ipa̠n i̠wal a̠nwunom, ibom id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh, e̠b̠aram na̠ A̠zizo̠s ebhin e̠gi̠ ka̠ ogigh.
LUK 23:33 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠gi̠ ka̠ imisi d̠a̠ esi wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ “Okpokoro E̠mu̠ Bho̠,” sa̠ awa i̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren. Awa i̠b̠aram na̠ ibom id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh bho̠ e̠du̠ d̠a̠ re̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an iriren, odi d̠a̠ agba od̠iom d̠o̠yo̠, uwed̠i d̠a̠ ekiel.
LUK 23:34 [Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mution okoroko ma̠a̠, “O̠we̠de̠, we̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ i̠karabh d̠awa ma̠ a̠nigha̠ awa! Ezin bho̠, awa iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ abar awa na̠ egir.”] Sa̠ awa irobh okob̠a̠ ma̠ o̠loghom agu̠o̠ awa ta̠ ebhin e̠ru̠gi̠an ibura̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 23:35 A̠nwunom i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ ekpon; ya̠a̠, ogbo aru̠mu̠ bho̠ sa̠ isorogiom i̠na ma̠ adi̠e̠l ma̠a̠, “I̠na a̠tenemeni gha̠n ipa̠n ogbo; i̠se̠n i̠na a̠tenemeni ani̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠, ku̠gba ma̠ i̠na Akrai̠st, O̠ni̠ Wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Aso̠n bho̠ ga̠i.”
LUK 23:36 Ogbo e̠gham bho̠ eka̠ e̠d̠igh ani̠ esorogiom i̠na ma̠ adi̠e̠l, sa̠ inigha̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠min a̠viniga̠.
LUK 23:37 Sa̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ iduom i̠na ifugh ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠ anwa O̠li̠la ebhugh ogbo A̠zu ga̠i, bha̠ tenemeni ma̠ ozu d̠oyom.”
LUK 23:38 Elegh ola̠ u̠du̠ d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠ d̠a̠ agba e̠mu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠a̠, “ONON O̠LI̠LE̠MA OGBO A̠ZU.”
LUK 23:39 Odi od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh wa̠ u̠b̠aram u̠du̠ u̠ke̠ri̠ bho̠ eka̠, a̠duom i̠na a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Anwa Akrai̠st bho̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠? Tenemeni ma̠ ozu d̠oyom, ma̠ ab̠ar na̠ i̠yar a̠tenemeni!”
LUK 23:40 Ya̠a̠, od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh uwed̠i agam a̠nigha̠ i̠na, a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ya̠! Ya̠! Anwa na̠ oghila̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ke̠re̠, ma̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ o̠ni̠ onon na̠ i̠yar u̠te̠i̠ onin e̠kal ebhum ase̠ bho̠?
LUK 23:41 D̠a̠ agba d̠i̠yar, sa̠ a̠sora̠n agu̠o̠ usobh ase̠ bho̠ ubhumeni i̠yar bho̠, ezin bho̠ i̠yar na̠ ob̠u ma̠ asu̠wo̠ i̠karabh ya̠ i̠yar ugir bho̠. Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ onon na̠ o̠pi̠o̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ abar.”
LUK 23:42 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠a̠, “A̠zizo̠s, siseiny ru̠ru̠ane̠ ami̠ ma̠ igiel anwa na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom d̠oyom.”
LUK 23:43 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠a̠, a̠didon anwa ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ami̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ Ob̠eb̠i A̠lei bho̠.”
LUK 23:44 A̠d̠io bho̠ aro̠ ka̠ na̠ ate̠i̠ azai̠ny, sa̠ azi̠m a̠ru ra̠ a̠kpegiom eb̠la̠ a̠de bho̠ tu̠tu̠n ate̠i̠ i̠sar aki̠lo̠ki̠ d̠a̠ etita̠n a̠d̠io.
LUK 23:45 Sa̠ e̠b̠alab̠al ogogo bho̠ a̠d̠im; sa̠ ukpe wa̠ ubhin usobhom a̠lukpesi e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, agu̠an d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io aru̠gi̠an i̠wal a̠bin.
LUK 23:46 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin obom okoroko ed̠i a̠mulughu ma̠a̠, “O̠we̠de̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠eton e̠mu̠gh d̠ami̠ na̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom.” O̠gba o̠ku̠a o̠we̠le̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ ekpo-epobh d̠o̠yo̠ a̠sobha̠n.
LUK 23:47 Igiel bho̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠rileghom o̠lo̠gh e̠gham bho̠ abi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠tutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠mutiom okoroko ma̠a̠, “Ya̠ a̠ga̠i, onon aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala.”
LUK 23:48 Igiel bho̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ isor esi bho̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠, sa̠ awa ikonya̠ imula̠ iyel na̠ i̠ku̠nu̠.
LUK 23:49 Ya̠a̠, eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ iloghom i̠na bho̠, ka̠ u̠b̠aram na̠ anwani̠ ya̠ i̠ke̠ d̠a̠ Agalili i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na bho̠, i̠mara ma̠ esi egbeiny ekpon i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n.
LUK 23:50 Odi ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠rugh ado̠l igielake̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠zose̠fu̠ aro̠, i̠na odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ Ogbo I̠to̠ A̠zu.
LUK 23:51 (Ya̠a̠, i̠na na̠ oma̠ra̠ ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠to̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ iyed̠i.) I̠na ola̠ e̠ma Ari̠mati̠a d̠a̠ ebhugh A̠zudia̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ ebhiroma̠ na̠ a̠gon eruoma̠ irileghom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
LUK 23:52 I̠na agi̠ ka̠ ate̠i̠ Apai̠let a̠puru ma̠ ozu ta̠ A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 23:53 Sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠soroni ma̠ egua̠de bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhin ob̠eb̠i ukpe asi̠ni̠ni̠n a̠bhurugi ma̠ egua̠de bho̠. I̠na asu̠ ma̠ egua̠de bho̠ awe̠le̠ sa̠ a̠bhin ka̠ a̠d̠i d̠a̠ omom od̠i, esi ola̠ ub̠u d̠a̠ o̠gbi̠o̠ma umutiom, ola̠ ta̠ od̠i d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.
LUK 23:54 Obha̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ A̠kokod̠ia̠n ob̠a̠ra̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠-epobh. Obhel bho̠ aro̠ ka̠ na̠ ate̠i̠ osira̠ epobh d̠awa.
LUK 23:55 Anwani̠ ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ Agalili id̠igh na̠ A̠zizo̠s iru bho̠, i̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zose̠fu̠ ka̠ emisi d̠a̠ ogugua̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠bi̠gh a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ ubhin u̠mu̠ni̠e̠ni̠ ma̠ egua̠de bho̠ d̠a̠ ologi.
LUK 23:56 Sa̠ awa imula̠ iyel i̠gi̠ ka̠ i̠gu̠a ma̠ i̠gagaman i̠gho̠gho̠ na̠ relo ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠. Ya̠a̠, awa esira̠ ma̠ epobh A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠-epobh bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ oloko bho̠ ato̠ bho̠.
LUK 24:1 I̠b̠ala A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠ Epobh bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠pu̠r a̠d̠a̠ma̠ d̠a̠ esi-a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ anwani̠ bho̠ ib̠on ib̠etina̠ ma̠ obom ame̠ghe̠le̠, sa̠ ibhin i̠gho̠gho̠ ed̠ue̠nu̠nu̠ ya̠ awa i̠gbe̠ bho̠ iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠.
LUK 24:2 Awa i̠bi̠gh ka̠ na̠ od̠ur okpegima̠ od̠i bho̠ otenemeni d̠a̠ a̠d̠ukun,
LUK 24:3 ya̠a̠ igiel bho̠ awa id̠igh d̠a̠ ologi bho̠, awa i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ ozu ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s.
LUK 24:4 Igiel bho̠ awa od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠ na̠ e̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ abar bho̠, sa̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom imite ma̠ awai̠ i̠mara d̠a̠ aka d̠awa, na̠ ibura̠ ya̠ na̠ esosorogia̠n ka̠ i̠me̠me̠gi̠na e̠nai̠ny.
LUK 24:5 D̠a̠ ebula̠ a̠rugugu wa̠ a̠sibh awa bho̠, sa̠ awa izuda̠ id̠i ma̠ ra̠misigh d̠awa d̠a̠ a̠de. Ya̠a̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ ipura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “A̠mite eka̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io imumugh?
LUK 24:6 I̠na bo̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n; i̠na na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh! I̠ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ inyin igiel bho̠ i̠na aro̠ na̠ inyin d̠a̠ Agalili bho̠,
LUK 24:7 ma̠a̠, ‘Ta̠ ob̠eton O̠nyi̠ ta̠ O̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh, sa̠ ta̠ o̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren ogigh. Oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um.’ ”
LUK 24:8 Sa̠ awa i̠ru̠ru̠an iloghoma̠n o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 24:9 Igiel bho̠ awa i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠ imula̠ iyel bho̠, sa̠ awa i̠gba ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n inigha̠ ma̠ d̠iobh na̠ onin ogbo ogir bho̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom iyed̠i.
LUK 24:10 A̠meri wa̠ Amagdala bho̠, na̠ A̠zoana, na̠ A̠meri onweni ta̠ A̠zemsi, na̠ ipa̠n anwani̠ ya̠ id̠igh na̠ awa irile bho̠, i̠gba ma̠ abar wa̠ a̠mite bho̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ogir bho̠.
LUK 24:11 Ya̠a̠, asu̠gbagba i̠nye̠n i̠gu̠b̠an ibhelebhel o̠nu̠ d̠a̠ ra̠to ilobhiri bho̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠ghon, ebula̠ o̠ku̠a awa id̠umom d̠o̠.
LUK 24:12 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, A̠pita̠ a̠b̠etina̠ a̠kpo ma̠ eghil agi̠ d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠. I̠na a̠zuma̠n anwi̠nagi̠an d̠a̠ ologi od̠i bho̠, sa̠ i̠na abi̠gh i̠go̠ro̠go̠r a̠rukpe asi̠ni̠ni̠n ya̠ ubhin ubhurugi ma̠ egua̠de bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠de ma̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠. Sa̠ i̠na a̠kpon bo̠ a̠mula̠ a̠yel, a̠bhin obhel aru̠ru̠an a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ a̠mite bho̠.
LUK 24:13 Onin a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠, idi i̠wal ogbo atu̠ghan ta̠ A̠zizo̠s irile na̠ e̠gi̠ d̠a̠ e̠ma E̠mayo̠s, esi erile ola̠ a̠lei agu̠o̠ od̠ua̠l amai̠l ma̠ obhin d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m ka̠ o̠te̠i̠.
LUK 24:14 Sa̠ awa od̠i na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite bho̠.
LUK 24:15 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ awa agbo̠gbu̠an a̠rile.
LUK 24:16 Ya̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠sibhom ma̠ ikpo a̠rid̠ien d̠awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ko orue d̠o̠ elelegi i̠na.
LUK 24:17 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ orile na̠ o̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an o̠ku̠a na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ ere?” Sa̠ awa i̠mara kpom ikonya̠ na̠ i̠ku̠nu̠.
LUK 24:18 Sa̠ odi o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ i̠wal awa, wa̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠kilopas bho̠, awo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa ku̠ku̠m o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠ru ma̠ isuloma̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m, ola̠ ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n ani̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imite ma̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠ d̠u̠ko̠?”
LUK 24:19 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “A̠kere a̠d̠ien i̠di̠ar imite?” Sa̠ awa i̠wo̠ran i̠na ma̠a̠, “I̠di̠ar ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ Anazare̠t bho̠. I̠na aro̠ ma̠ owil ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom ilelegi, d̠a̠ ebula̠ e̠mi̠ a̠limon o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 24:20 Ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ na̠ ipa̠n ogbo aru̠mu̠ d̠i̠yar ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠, ib̠eton i̠na e̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ ogigh, sa̠ i̠du̠ i̠na d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren igigh;
LUK 24:21 ya̠a̠, i̠yar ubhin i̠na ob̠em ologi ma̠ i̠na Witenemeni wa̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ o̠bhe̠l ebhugh Izre̠l bho̠. O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠, a̠didon oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n imite.
LUK 24:22 O̠ku̠a bha̠, idi anwani̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠i̠yar ogbo ya̠ i̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠na bho̠, iru ra̠ i̠gba ma̠ asu̠gbagba ya̠ id̠igh i̠yar ilologia̠n o̠mu̠gho̠n. Awa iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ od̠i d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ame̠ghe̠le̠ a̠didon,
LUK 24:23 ya̠a̠ awa i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ologi. Sa̠ awa imula̠ iru ra̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠yar ma̠a̠, awa i̠bi̠gh aghi̠m ola̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ imutuma̠ awa e̠gba ma̠a̠, A̠zizo̠s od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um!
LUK 24:24 Sa̠ idi ogbo ya̠ id̠igh na̠ i̠yar i̠ro̠ bho̠, iten i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ od̠i bho̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh ani̠. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, awa i̠bi̠gh od̠i bho̠ ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ anwani̠ bho̠ i̠gba bho̠, ya̠a̠ awa i̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s.”
LUK 24:25 Sa̠ i̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Rema̠ a̠nwunom! Agu̠o̠ na̠ akparama inyin od̠umom eb̠la̠ iwowa̠ ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ iwa̠ bho̠.
LUK 24:26 U̠gba d̠o̠ o̠se̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, Akrai̠st bho̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ abi̠gh ali̠gam a̠ruzu i̠nye̠n kisa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ten a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ ke̠re̠?”
LUK 24:27 Sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠bhin obhel agba ase̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ iwowa̠ ya̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ i̠na d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ od̠ud̠ul bho̠, ob̠eton d̠a̠ ra̠d̠ire ta̠ A̠mozizi ka̠ ate̠i̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠riwil bho̠ i̠ge̠ bho̠.
LUK 24:28 Igiel bho̠ awa na̠ etua̠n e̠ma wa̠ awa na̠ e̠gi̠ bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠rile a̠ten awa a̠kue a̠d̠ighi woma̠ i̠na od̠idia̠ na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠.
LUK 24:29 Yaa̠, awa ikikiom i̠na e̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠a̠, “To̠ na̠ i̠yar. I̠se̠n na̠ ate̠i̠ a̠dule, okpegi osor a̠sughonom.” Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ awa aro̠.
LUK 24:30 Igiel bho̠ i̠na aro̠ d̠a̠ akpata od̠e bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin abe̠re̠di̠, sa̠ a̠tutumeni, sa̠ i̠na a̠puiny a̠b̠eton a̠nigha̠ awa.
LUK 24:31 I̠se̠ kisa̠ a̠rid̠ien d̠awa i̠kpakpagi̠na sa̠ awa ililegi i̠na. D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, sa̠ i̠na amai̠ny ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠awa.
LUK 24:32 Sa̠ odi a̠tiba̠ra̠ a̠kpon odi a̠pura̠n ma̠a̠, “To̠ ti̠to̠i̠ny ku, i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠yar igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh na̠ i̠yar a̠rile bho̠, ikul d̠o̠ ma̠ rologi d̠i̠yar ke̠re̠?”
LUK 24:33 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠ sa̠ awa imula̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m. Sa̠ awa i̠bi̠gh d̠iobh na̠ onin ogbo ogir bho̠, na̠ ipa̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠igh gha̠n awa na̠ erile bho̠, na̠ ekokod̠ia̠n i̠se̠
LUK 24:34 na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, “Ya̠gia̠ga̠i! Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, sa̠ na̠ a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ Asai̠mo̠n nyen.”
LUK 24:35 Sa̠ i̠wal awa ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ E̠mayo̠s imula̠ iru bho̠ eka̠, i̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ imutuma̠ awa d̠a̠ eten bho̠, sekina̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ awa ibhin ilelegi i̠na, ma̠ obhel bho̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton abe̠re̠di̠ a̠puiny a̠ni̠gha awa bho̠.
LUK 24:36 Awa od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ e̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an i̠nye̠n, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠mite amara d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠awa, sa̠ a̠du ma̠ o̠gho̠r a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “Ekima̠ aro̠ na̠ inyin.”
LUK 24:37 Sa̠ eb̠la̠ o̠lo̠gh bho̠ ikpa̠ra̠numa̠, sa̠ a̠rugugu isibh awa, ezin bho̠ awa i̠ru̠ru̠an ma̠ awa i̠bi̠gh egua̠de.
LUK 24:38 Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin na̠ o̠tu̠n ere na̠ okpa̠ra̠noma̠. Ezin ka̠ ere wa̠ rologi d̠inyin na̠ e̠gba i̠wal i̠wal bho̠?
LUK 24:39 Ikpone ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ na̠ a̠sike d̠ami̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ ologhom ma̠ ami̠ na̠ agu̠o̠. Ikula̠ne ami̠ ma̠ ekpon; egua̠de na̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ipulupul ozu o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ na̠ i̠kpo̠kpo̠, ma̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ o̠bi̠gh ozu d̠ami̠ bho̠.”
LUK 24:40 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠mutiom okoroko onon bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠leriom awa ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠.
LUK 24:41 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, awa id̠umom d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ awa imuzo na̠ a̠libhon ologi na̠ ilologia̠n. Sa̠ i̠na a̠pura̠n awa ma̠a̠, “Inyin onwuna̠ abar od̠e ma̠ i̠se̠n ke̠re̠?”
LUK 24:42 Sa̠ awa ib̠eton o̠bhu̠gi̠an ena̠ i̠nigha̠ i̠na,
LUK 24:43 sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin ena̠ bho̠ a̠puron awa d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠awa.
LUK 24:44 Sa̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, “I̠nye̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ i̠kpe̠re̠me̠ni̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin igiel bho̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠ ma̠a̠, ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ u̠ge̠ ugboloma̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire oloko ta̠ A̠mozizi bho̠, na̠ a̠riwil bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire Raso̠r bho̠.”
LUK 24:45 Sa̠ i̠na a̠kpekpegion rologi d̠awa ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.
LUK 24:46 Sa̠ i̠na a̠nimeta̠n awa ma̠a̠, “U̠ge̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠a̠, Akrai̠st ta̠ abi̠gh ali̠gam a̠ruzu, sa̠ ta̠ a̠mugh, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh oleghemeni i̠sar a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.
LUK 24:47 U̠b̠aram u̠ge̠ ma̠a̠, ta̠ o̠ke̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m obhin a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠, o̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ya̠ otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh, na̠ o̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh onigha̠ o̠ni̠, o̠saragi̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom.
LUK 24:48 Inyin ronyob̠a̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n.
LUK 24:49 Ami̠ ta̠ afi̠ri̠ma inyin abar wa̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ a̠gua̠n bho̠; o̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n d̠a̠ e̠ma bho̠ tu̠tu̠n a̠limon ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny ra̠ ate̠i̠ inyin.”
LUK 24:50 Sa̠ i̠na a̠rileghom awa a̠mutiom ka̠ ate̠i̠ d̠a̠ Abe̠tani̠, sa̠ a̠b̠egion aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ agi̠o̠m anyu̠, sa̠ a̠tutumeni awa.
LUK 24:51 Od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ ologi agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tutumeni awa bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠toka̠n ad̠u̠a d̠awa, sa̠ ukpobh i̠na ubhuneni d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny.
LUK 24:52 Sa̠ awa ikpud̠ia̠n i̠ko̠l i̠na, sa̠ awa imula̠ i̠gi̠ d̠a̠ A̠zeruse̠le̠m na̠ ibom a̠libhon ologi.
LUK 24:53 Sa̠ awa ibhin eb̠la̠ obhel d̠awa, i̠ro̠ d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ itututumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l, wa̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ i̠to̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠ten o̠ni̠ogir ta̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st bho̠, na̠ age̠ na̠ a̠ruom a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ E̠fi̠so̠s, na̠ ogbo id̠umom ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s.
EPH 1:2 E̠no̠gho̠man na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin.
EPH 1:3 Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin eb̠la̠ itutumeni d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠doni i̠yar d̠a̠ Akrai̠st.
EPH 1:4 Ezin bho̠ i̠na aso̠n i̠yar d̠a̠ Akrai̠st kisa̠ i̠na ale̠m e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom e̠b̠ab̠ala, orugh a̠ma̠rugh ola̠ abar ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m i̠yar ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 1:5 D̠a̠ etula̠n d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ato̠ a̠guri ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st obhin i̠yar ma̠ agu̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠,
EPH 1:6 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ otutumeni i̠na d̠a̠ ibom e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠, wa̠ ibom e̠no̠gho̠man na̠ e̠wo̠l d̠a̠ Wetula̠n bho̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ i̠yar bho̠.
EPH 1:7 D̠a̠ ebula̠ Akrai̠st sa̠ i̠yar u̠te̠i̠ itenemeni wa̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ alu̠kpe̠ omugh d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ru bho̠, sa̠ u̠we̠le̠man i̠karabh d̠i̠yar, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ibom e̠no̠gho̠man d̠o̠yo̠,
EPH 1:8 ya̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ i̠yar a̠muzoghod̠i d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere eloghom abar na̠ amu̠gho̠nyan,
EPH 1:9 ma̠ i̠yar ologhom e̠wo̠gi̠na i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠ isora̠n na̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠walama d̠o̠yo̠, wa̠ i̠na ato̠ d̠a̠ Akrai̠st bho̠,
EPH 1:10 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ omuzoghod̠iom i̠walama d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠ obhel bho̠, ma̠ otulugi eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠a̠ Akrai̠st, d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny na̠ d̠a̠ a̠de onon.
EPH 1:11 D̠a̠ ebula̠ Akrai̠st nyen, sa̠ u̠so̠n i̠yar ma̠ id̠e ma̠ ad̠i̠a, ma̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ od̠ia̠ o̠to̠ oguri bho̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠sora̠n d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
EPH 1:12 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ya̠ u̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠pu̠r ogbo ya̠ na̠ eb̠em ologi d̠a̠ Akrai̠st bho̠ ta̠ o̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ itutumeni isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 1:13 D̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠ sa̠ inyin u̠mu̠gho̠n nyen a̠ga̠i O̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ oten d̠inyin, wa̠ inyin ud̠umom sa̠ u̠tu̠n o̠ku̠a unigha̠ inyin E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ elegh, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ugua̠n bho̠,
EPH 1:14 wa̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ ma̠ ogua̠n bho̠ ma̠a̠, i̠yar ta̠ od̠e ma̠ ad̠i̠a d̠i̠yar bho̠, tu̠tu̠n i̠na ta̠ tenemeni ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ aman, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ onigha̠ o̠yo̠ ma̠ itutumeni d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 1:15 D̠a̠ ebul abar onon, na̠ o̠gba nyen onigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ wa̠ inyin unwuna̠ ugboloma̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s, na̠ etula̠n wa̠ inyin unwuna̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 1:16 O̠ku̠a sa̠ ami̠ ko o̠we̠le̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠tu̠n ebula̠ inyin onigha̠ gha̠n ali̠se̠bh ma̠ igiel ami̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an igboloma̠ inyin d̠a̠ a̠siseiny d̠ami̠,
EPH 1:17 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, O̠we̠de̠ isosorogia̠n bho̠, ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin E̠mu̠gh eloghom abar na̠ aghi̠m ya̠ o̠mar ologhom o̠yo̠,
EPH 1:18 na̠ okperon ologi d̠inyin ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar wa̠ i̠na atu̠n a̠bhelegi inyin bho̠, na̠ a̠b̠utu e̠li̠la ya̠ i̠na na̠ a̠gua̠n anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
EPH 1:19 sekina̠ ibom a̠limon d̠o̠yo̠ wa̠ abar ola̠ obhin o̠tu̠o̠m o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, ya̠ i̠ro̠ inigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ id̠umom bho̠, d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠mi̠ a̠limon ogir agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
EPH 1:20 wa̠ i̠na a̠gir d̠a̠ ob̠eton Akrai̠st d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, sa̠ ari̠lo̠me̠ni̠ i̠na ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny,
EPH 1:21 a̠peleni ma̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠ a̠dila̠de na̠ a̠limon na̠ i̠to̠, sekina̠ kerekere a̠d̠ien ola̠ uloghom, i̠se̠n d̠a̠ amu̠m onon sekina̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠, nyen.
EPH 1:22 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠bhin kabar kabar a̠guri d̠a̠ ekpukpu ta̠ Akrai̠st, sa̠ ato̠ ma̠a̠ i̠na we̠mu̠ eb̠la̠ i̠d̠i̠ar d̠a̠ ebula̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠,
EPH 1:23 wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, wa̠ a̠muzo na̠ i̠na bho̠, wa̠ a̠muzo ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠d̠i̠ar bho̠.
EPH 2:1 D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten, inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ imumugh d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠a̠ ebula̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ na̠ i̠karabh d̠inyin.
EPH 2:2 D̠a̠ obhel obha̠, inyin u̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠karabh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar e̠mara̠nwunom onon, ya̠ izuzua̠n a̠limon ta̠ Eru bho̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠rileghom ra̠limon d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny bho̠. I̠na e̠mu̠gh wa̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠rileghom ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ na̠ enigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 2:3 I̠ye̠ a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ eb̠la̠ i̠yar na̠ od̠ia̠ orugh otenemeni nyen, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ i̠karabh ebhiroma̠ ipulupul ozu, sa̠ i̠yar u̠tu̠o̠no̠m gha̠n ebhiroma̠ ipulupul ozu na̠ iya̠ rologi d̠i̠yar ipuru bho̠. Sa̠ d̠a̠ e̠d̠o̠lo̠gho̠ma d̠a̠ i̠yar bho̠, sa̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny ya̠ i̠kpe̠ ma̠ ogbika̠ d̠a̠ i̠gam ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ipa̠n ogbo.
EPH 2:4 Ya̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠muzo na̠ okpon igbirigbir bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ibom etula̠n ya̠ i̠na a̠tula̠n i̠yar bho̠,
EPH 2:5 d̠a̠ igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ imumugh d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠a̠ ebula̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠nigha̠ i̠yar a̠ghud̠um d̠a̠ Akrai̠st. Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ kisa̠ i̠yar uten.
EPH 2:6 Sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠b̠eton i̠yar na̠ Akrai̠st ari̠lo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ a̠risisi ote̠nai̠ny na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, d̠a̠ ebula̠ od̠ighonin na̠ Akrai̠st,
EPH 2:7 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠leriom amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠ ma̠ ibom e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gba o̠ro̠d̠o̠ bho̠ na̠ ib̠eb̠i ogir d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠yar ogbo ya̠ od̠i na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s bho̠.
EPH 2:8 Ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ inyin u̠wo̠l d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ uten, inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠, onon bha̠ enigha̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 2:9 Na̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠gir agu̠o̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠bhin are̠ma.
EPH 2:10 Ezin bho̠, i̠yar ogir agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ya̠ u̠le̠m d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s ma̠ ogir ib̠eb̠i rogir ya̠ i̠na na̠ ato̠ a̠guri, ma̠ i̠yar okpon o̠ku̠a ogir.
EPH 2:11 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu d̠a̠ imitia̠n, sa̠ ogbo A̠zu ya̠ i̠gba ma̠a̠ awa na̠ otia̠ ma̠ ipo bho̠, ibhelegi inyin ma̠ ogbo ya̠ otia̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ipo, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ogir agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ipulupul bho̠.
EPH 2:12 Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ obhel bho̠, inyin usia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st, inyin u̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun Izre̠l, u̠wal ani̠ d̠o̠ inyin o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ ri̠zo̠ na̠ rogua̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, eb̠em ologi na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ inyin, inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom e̠mara̠nwunom ya̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar egboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 2:13 Ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n, d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, inyin ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ esi egbeiny bho̠, na̠ obhin otueneni, d̠a̠ o̠wo̠l oten i̠ko̠l omugh ta̠ Akrai̠st.
EPH 2:14 Ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ bha̠ ekima̠ d̠i̠yar, wa̠ a̠bhin i̠yar a̠guri onin bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhin omugh d̠o̠yo̠ a̠b̠ogion e̠b̠agh wa̠ abagi̠o̠n i̠yar a̠guri ma̠ ogbo ologi̠an a̠d̠ien bho̠.
EPH 2:15 I̠na a̠gbogion oloko i̠to̠to̠gi̠ a̠ma̠rugh bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ onwe o̠le̠m i̠wal rebhugh bho̠ otenemeni onin a̠nwunom iya̠ o̠yo̠, ya̠ ibhon ipu ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠ro̠ bho̠, omutiom ekima̠.
EPH 2:16 D̠a̠ egbika̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠, sa̠ Akrai̠st a̠tulugi ma̠ i̠wal a̠nwunom bho̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ onin d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ a̠kunugiom o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien wa̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠i̠yar bho̠.
EPH 2:17 Sa̠ Akrai̠st a̠ru ra̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ekima̠ bho̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu bho̠, ya̠ isigima̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ na̠ i̠yar a̠nwunom A̠zu, ya̠ itua̠n A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 2:18 I̠se̠n bha̠ i̠wal rekun bho̠ ta̠ e̠wo̠l d̠o̠yo̠, ebhin d̠a̠ onin E̠mu̠gh bho̠ e̠te̠i̠ O̠we̠d̠e̠ bho̠.
EPH 2:19 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, inyin bo̠ mu̠ ma̠ isuloma̠ ya̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun, ya̠a̠ inyin na̠ oten anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ onin na̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, d̠a̠ eghun otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
EPH 2:20 ya̠ ulo d̠a̠ anyu̠ o̠de̠ ogbo ogir bho̠ sekina̠ a̠riwil bho̠, wa̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s na̠ agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ o̠gbi̠o̠ma e̠ko̠ otu bho̠.
EPH 2:21 D̠a̠ o̠yo̠ sa̠ eb̠la̠ otu bho̠ a̠tulugia̠n a̠ten onin, sa̠ abu̠gh a̠ten otupp ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
EPH 2:22 D̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠, sa̠ ulo inyin utulugi nyen, utenemeni ma̠ otu ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh.
EPH 3:1 Onon abar wa̠ ami̠ Apo̠l, o̠ni̠ ikoli ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, d̠a̠ ebula̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu bho̠, na̠ atu̠n na̠ a̠siseiny na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin bho̠.
EPH 3:2 Ami̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ na̠ o̠gba onigha̠ inyin i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ aghu̠ame̠ni̠ ami̠ ma̠ ogir ogboloma̠ inyin bho̠.
EPH 3:3 Uleriom ami̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar e̠wo̠gina ya̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ age̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠kara a̠gboloma̠ bho̠,
EPH 3:4 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ orue osen o̠mu̠gho̠nyan i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ iloghom igboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar e̠wo̠gi̠na ta̠ Akrai̠st,
EPH 3:5 ya̠ uleriom d̠o̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ramu̠m, ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n na̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠mutiom a̠leriom ogbo ogir na̠ a̠riwil d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ inigha̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠awa ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 3:6 E̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠ bha̠, ta̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ A̠zu ta̠ ed̠igh na̠ Ogbo A̠zu bho̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ id̠e ma̠ ad̠i̠a, sa̠ awa ta̠ ed̠igh onin e̠ru̠gi̠an ogua̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s.
EPH 3:7 Ami̠ iru ra̠ iten o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ agba ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ bho̠, wa̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠limon ogir d̠o̠yo̠ a̠mite bho̠.
EPH 3:8 Ami̠ i̠ki̠r a̠pu d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ya̠ unigha̠ ma̠ a̠limon obhin o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba onigha̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu bho̠, d̠a̠ e̠no̠gho̠man ya̠ imuzo d̠a̠ Akrai̠st bho̠.
EPH 3:9 Sa̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠mar eloghom kabar kabar, d̠a̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ilologia̠n na̠ i̠d̠i̠ar e̠wo̠gi̠na̠ id̠ud̠ul ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ ale̠m eb̠la̠ i̠d̠i̠ar bho̠,
EPH 3:10 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠se̠n, ta̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ a̠leriom ogbo irileghom na̠ a̠limon ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny bho̠, ma̠ a̠d̠izo re̠kal eloghom abar ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 3:11 I̠na atu̠n ebula̠ i̠walama id̠ud̠ul d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ramu̠m bho̠ a̠muzughod̠iom d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar,
EPH 3:12 wa̠ i̠yar ubhin d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ u̠te̠i̠ alu̠kpo̠ ologi ola̠ o̠gi̠ ka̠ omutuma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 3:13 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ologi d̠inyin odugh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠din inyin na̠ abi̠gh bho̠, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ itum d̠inyin bho̠.
EPH 3:14 Onon ezin bho̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠kpud̠ia̠n O̠we̠de̠ bho̠,
EPH 3:15 wa̠ u̠wo̠l ughol a̠d̠ien eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom d̠a̠ re̠nai̠ny na̠ a̠de bho̠,
EPH 3:16 ma̠a̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ ibom a̠b̠utu e̠no̠gho̠man isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠, awo̠l d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin a̠limon ya̠ ta̠ e̠ghu̠ame̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin,
EPH 3:17 ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠, sa̠ Akrai̠st ta̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ rologi d̠inyin ma̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠zu̠ o̠mara, o̠ro̠ gigiribh d̠a̠ etula̠n d̠o̠yo̠,
EPH 3:18 b̠o̠ka̠ inyin od̠igh na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ o̠mar o̠mu̠gho̠nyan e̠re̠ghe̠, na̠ eweghe, na̠ e̠gi̠o̠m anyu̠, na̠ ekud̠um
EPH 3:19 etula̠n ta̠ Akrai̠st wa̠ ob̠ur d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan o̠man bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ omuzo na̠ ado̠l ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal.
EPH 3:20 I̠na wa̠ na̠ a̠rue na̠ a̠gir na̠ a̠peleni ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠yar na̠ opuru bho̠ na̠ iya̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠limon d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠gir d̠a̠ a̠ruzu d̠i̠yar bho̠,
EPH 3:21 a̠bhin itutumeni d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ i̠na bho̠ sekina̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, ad̠u̠a ma̠ amu̠m a̠ten amu̠m tu̠tu̠n ka̠ id̠ud̠ul. Aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
EPH 4:1 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ami̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ikoli d̠a̠ ebula̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, na̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin ma̠ orugh a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ isora̠n agu̠o̠ ubhin ubhelegi inyin bho̠,
EPH 4:2 d̠a̠ ibom o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu, na̠ ekima̠, na̠ a̠ma̠ne ya̠ odi ta̠ a̠ne ma̠ odi d̠a̠ ebula̠ etula̠n.
EPH 4:3 Iwia̠ne ma̠ o̠ro̠ onin d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ekima̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ abar wa̠ akpu̠o̠m inyin bho̠.
EPH 4:4 Onin ozu na̠ onin E̠mu̠gh od̠i, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ubhelegi inyin nyen ra̠ ud̠ighom d̠a̠ onin eb̠em ologi bho̠,
EPH 4:5 onin Wa̠nwuna̠, onin ologi ima̠ra̠, onin owura̠mu̠m,
EPH 4:6 onin A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ O̠we̠de̠ ta̠ eb̠la̠ i̠yar, wa̠ a̠pu kabar kabar bho̠, sa̠ na̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠gir eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠yar.
EPH 4:7 Ya̠a̠, Akrai̠st a̠nigha̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ i̠yar enigha̠ ya̠ o̠ni̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin a̠gir e̠kal ogir d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 4:8 Obha̠ ezin bho̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ogiel bho̠ i̠na a̠bhun d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠bhin i̠di̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ikoli e̠gham bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠.”
EPH 4:9 I̠se̠n ka̠ “I̠na a̠bhun,” ka̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ eka̠, a̠sigimeni ma̠ o̠ro̠ ma̠a̠, i̠na a̠sor d̠a̠ agba wa̠ ade̠bh a̠pu d̠a̠ a̠de bho̠?
EPH 4:10 I̠na wa̠ a̠sor bho̠ bha̠ uwa̠ a̠bhun bho̠ a̠pel eb̠la̠ re̠nai̠ny bho̠ nyen, ma̠ omuzo eb̠la̠ e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠.
EPH 4:11 I̠na bha̠ wa̠ aso̠n idi ma̠ ogbogir, idi a̠riwil, idi i̠gba ma̠ asu̠gbagba, idi ikponom ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠,
EPH 4:12 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ghu̠ame̠ni̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ ogir olo ozu ta̠ Akrai̠st obhuneni bho̠,
EPH 4:13 tu̠tu̠n ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ a̠dila̠de ola̠ eb̠la̠ i̠yar ta̠ oten onin d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠, o̠mar ologhom O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ o̠mar od̠igh e̠mu̠ olegha̠n ka̠ Akrai̠st.
EPH 4:14 Sa̠ i̠yar ko o̠ro̠ mu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny, iya̠ ipoka̠na̠n amu̠m na̠ eb̠oroghom, na̠ a̠bhin na̠ agi̠ ma̠ ebha̠ na̠ enen d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere oghur atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, na̠ i̠le̠ge̠ na̠ ikoiny ogbo ya̠ na̠ egon ogelemeni a̠nwunom.
EPH 4:15 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ i̠yar obhin d̠a̠ etula̠n o̠gba ma̠ iya̠ a̠ga̠i bho̠, sa̠ i̠yar ta̠ obhobh d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal o̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ Akrai̠st we̠mu̠ bho̠.
EPH 4:16 Ad̠u̠a d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ u̠tu̠lu̠gi̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠risisi ozu bho̠ na̠ id̠id̠igh uguri ma̠ onin, sa̠ esi i̠se̠ na̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ u̠to̠ unigha̠ i̠na ma̠ ogir bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ ozu bho̠ a̠bhobh, aghu̠a, a̠muzo na̠ etula̠n.
EPH 4:17 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ob̠eton i̠se̠n o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, o̠ni̠ ko orugh mu ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu na̠ erugh bho̠, ya̠ na̠ ebhin agu̠o̠ awa eb̠em ologi o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ bho̠ na̠ e̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an.
EPH 4:18 Awa irue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar, ma̠ ola̠ awa na̠ esigima̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom bho̠. Ezin bho̠, awa iloghom d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i abar, d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠kparakpar ologi d̠awa.
EPH 4:19 Awa inwuna̠ mu ma̠ igbiriri ozu, ma̠ ola̠ awa na̠ eb̠eton a̠ruzu d̠awa enigha̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere i̠karabh, na̠ a̠ma̠rugh o̠ku̠ku̠.
EPH 4:20 Ya̠a̠, i̠nye̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ inyin u̠tu̠ghan ugboloma̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠ d̠o̠,
EPH 4:21 ku̠gba ma̠a̠, inyin o̠mar o̠mu̠gho̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ igboloma̠ i̠na bho̠, sa̠ i̠na atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin a̠gia̠ga̠i ya̠ od̠i na̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠,
EPH 4:22 bha̠ i̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ ado̠l ugba̠iny o̠ni̠ wa̠ obhon d̠o̠ bho̠ ma̠ erobh, ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ i̠karabh ebhiroma̠ igelemeni iru bho̠.
EPH 4:23 E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠nwe ma̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an d̠inyin a̠tenemeni ma̠ imom,
EPH 4:24 ma̠ erugh a̠ma̠rugh emobh o̠ni̠ ola̠ ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar bho̠ i̠gu̠b̠an ita̠ A̠zib̠a̠, d̠a̠ a̠ga̠i e̠b̠ab̠ala, na̠ igielake̠.
EPH 4:25 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠we̠le̠mane̠ ma̠ o̠gba igunugha̠, ya̠a̠ odi agba ma̠ iya̠gia̠ga̠i a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi, ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ i̠yar onin d̠a̠ Akrai̠st.
EPH 4:26 Inyin ta̠ orue o̠gam i̠gam, ya̠a̠ i̠gam bho̠ od̠ighi d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ ogir i̠karabh. I̠gam bho̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ tu̠tu̠n ogogo bho̠ ta̠ a̠sor.
EPH 4:27 O̠ni̠ ko onigha̠ ma̠ Eru bho̠ ma̠ e̠ti̠ti̠gha.
EPH 4:28 O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rugh ado̠l a̠b̠igh ob̠igh mu, ya̠a̠ a̠bhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ akparame̠ni̠ a̠gir ogir ola̠ asu̠o̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ abar ola̠ onigha̠ ani̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠dila̠de bho̠ na̠ a̠puru ma̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠.
EPH 4:29 I̠karabh a̠fugh omite d̠o̠ d̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ d̠inyin. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i abar ola̠ ta̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ ed̠igh asu̠o̠ enigha̠ awa.
EPH 4:30 O̠ni̠ ko od̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh i̠ku̠nu̠, i̠na wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ elegh wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠bhin na̠ a̠lelegi ma̠a̠ inyin iya̠ o̠yo̠ bho̠, na̠ oleriom ma̠a̠ inyin ta̠ oten d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ itenemeni bho̠.
EPH 4:31 I̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ igurumia̠n ologi, na̠ ibom i̠gam, na̠ i̠karabh ebhiroma̠, izul o̠te̠i̠ abar onyen, na̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠, na̠ ado̠l o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien, sekina̠ eghir ologi d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠inyin.
EPH 4:32 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ odi alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi, odi a̠kpon odi ma̠ igbirigbir, odi a̠kpon i̠karabh ta̠ odi asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien, ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ atu̠n ebula̠ Akrai̠st a̠kpon i̠karabh d̠inyin asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien bho̠.
EPH 5:1 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠ta ma̠ ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny ed̠ighologi d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:2 Irughe ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh etula̠n agu̠o̠ Akrai̠st a̠tula̠n i̠yar bho̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ abar alu̠kpe̠, ola̠ u̠kpe̠ unigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ a̠bhur ed̠u e̠nu̠nu̠.
EPH 5:3 Agu̠o̠ inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ o̠gba ma̠a̠, odi o̠ni̠ inyin na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ e̠ma, bo̠d̠o̠ na̠ a̠pesi ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ipesi, bo̠d̠o̠ na̠ a̠kori ma̠ i̠di̠ar na̠ a̠bhin. A̠ghud̠um i̠nye̠n ibhon d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ orugh.
EPH 5:4 Bo̠d̠o̠ osenegi isenegi, ofugh a̠fugh iya̠ i̠te̠i̠, bo̠d̠o̠ okue ikue ya̠ osora̠n d̠o̠. Ado̠l i̠nye̠n ibhon d̠o̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ i̠se̠bhe̠ ma̠ ali̠se̠bh.
EPH 5:5 Iloghome ma̠a̠, od̠e ma̠ e̠ma, bo̠d̠o̠ opesipesi, bo̠d̠o̠ okorikori (wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ko̠l ma̠ eru bho̠), ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠de onwuna̠ e̠ma ta̠ Akrai̠st na̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 5:6 O̠ni̠ ko oma̠ra̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ obhin ibhelebhel o̠nu̠ oru ra̠ ogelemeni inyin. Ezin bho̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠din o̠kpo̠ ya̠ o̠ko̠no̠n agam ibom i̠gam a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:7 O̠ni̠ ko od̠igh awa ma̠ egir a̠d̠ien i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ awa na̠ egir bho̠.
EPH 5:8 Ezin bho̠, obhel aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin u̠ro̠ d̠a̠ azi̠m, ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n inyin na̠ oten a̠nwunom ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠b̠alab̠al bho̠, bha̠, irughe ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ i̠gu̠b̠an ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠b̠alab̠al.
EPH 5:9 Ezin bho̠, e̠b̠alab̠al onon wa̠ od̠i na̠ inyin bho̠, na̠ amu̠ na̠ a̠mutiom ib̠eb̠i, na̠ igielake̠, na̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i,
EPH 5:10 ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ owia̠n ogir ya̠ i̠kpe̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:11 O̠ni̠ ko od̠igh ani̠ ma̠ egir i̠d̠i̠ar obhobho i̠kpo̠ i̠ye̠ ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ azi̠m bho̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ i̠gba ma̠ emutiom agu̠o̠ igurom i̠te̠i̠.
EPH 5:12 O̠kpo̠ i̠ye̠ ya̠ awa na̠ egir d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠, iya̠ ari̠ghe̠l nyen ma̠ ofugh ogboloma̠.
EPH 5:13 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ umutiom eb̠la̠ o̠kpo̠ i̠ye̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠alab̠al, sa̠ ta̠ ologhom agu̠o̠ obhin od̠i.
EPH 5:14 Ezin bho̠ e̠b̠alab̠al na̠ a̠leriom kabar kabar, agu̠o̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “B̠etina̠ d̠a̠ adi̠la d̠oyom, b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, sa̠ Akrai̠st ta̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam amu̠gho̠nyan.”
EPH 5:15 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠ ikpona̠, o̠ni̠ ko orugh agu̠o̠ rema̠ a̠nwunom, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ iloghodi̠ar a̠nwunom.
EPH 5:16 I̠mare̠ ma̠ egir i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ inyin ogir d̠a̠ obhel bho̠, ezin bho̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠n i̠karabh.
EPH 5:17 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, o̠ni̠ ko o̠ro̠ ma̠ rema̠, ya̠a̠ iwia̠ne ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan i̠to̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 5:18 O̠ni̠ ko o̠d̠a ma̠ a̠min e̠te̠i̠ esi ola̠ ta̠ epuru inyin, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠ye̠me̠ni̠ inyin. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠ a̠muzo d̠a̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin.
EPH 5:19 Ibhine ma̠ raso̠r ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, na̠ raso̠r ya̠ a̠nwunom ima̠ra̠, na̠ raso̠r ya̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin, ma̠ e̠mo̠r d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin, ma̠ etutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠inyin.
EPH 5:20 I̠se̠bhe̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ kigiel kigiel ma̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar, d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st.
EPH 5:21 Odi a̠zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi d̠a̠ ebula̠ oghila̠n Akrai̠st.
EPH 5:22 Inyin anwani̠, izuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ a̠siwolom d̠inyin, ma̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ ogir na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:23 Ezin bho̠, owolom we̠mu̠ ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ Akrai̠st aro̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ na̠ Witenemeni aso̠si̠ bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:24 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, anwani̠ eka̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ a̠siwolom d̠awa d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar.
EPH 5:25 Inyin a̠siwolom, itula̠ne ma̠ anwani̠ d̠inyin, ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ Akrai̠st a̠tula̠n aso̠si̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ a̠dinom.
EPH 5:26 I̠na a̠gir o̠ku̠a b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na a̠bhin o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠wur amu̠m ma̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ a̠guri d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala.
EPH 5:27 Akrai̠st a̠gir o̠ko̠no̠n b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ aso̠si̠ ola̠ edim, ola̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ bebina̠ abar ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m, bo̠d̠o̠ ipa̠n i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala na̠ ola̠ ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ o̠pi̠e̠.
EPH 5:28 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ a̠siwolom e̠kpe̠ ma̠ otula̠n anwani̠ d̠awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa itula̠n a̠ruzu d̠awa bho̠. I̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠tula̠n ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, bha̠ a̠tula̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠ nyen.
EPH 5:29 Ezin bho̠, bebina̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ asu̠a ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bo̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ amar na̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n na̠ a̠kponom ozu d̠o̠yo̠, onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ Akrai̠st na̠ a̠gir na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠,
EPH 5:30 ezin bho̠ i̠yar a̠risisi ozu d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 5:31 Onin agu̠o̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Olobho̠ro̠ni̠ ta̠ awe̠le̠man onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ka̠ akpabhan ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠wal awa ta̠ eten onin ozu.”
EPH 5:32 Onon obom e̠wo̠gi̠na, ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st na̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠.
EPH 5:33 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, id̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ inyin ta̠ a̠tula̠n ani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠tula̠n ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ani̠ a̠zuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi a̠nigha̠ ma̠ owolom d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 6:1 I̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny i̠nagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, onon agu̠o̠ akpe̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠.
EPH 6:2 “Izuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠ d̠inyin.” Obha̠ o̠pu̠r oloko wa̠ u̠b̠aram na̠ ogua̠n bho̠ ma̠a̠,
EPH 6:3 “sa̠ ta̠ ebhon enigha̠ inyin, sa̠ inyin ta̠ od̠um iwewegh a̠ghud̠um d̠a̠ a̠de onon.”
EPH 6:4 Ro̠we̠de̠, o̠ni̠ ko orugh ado̠l ya̠ o̠gamame̠ni̠ rologi anwi̠i̠ny d̠inyin, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ ibhine d̠a̠ a̠kikiom na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠ ekponom awa ma̠ ed̠ighom aru̠mu̠.
EPH 6:5 Aru̠bana, izuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ inyin i̠se̠n a̠de onon bho̠, ma̠ e̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu na̠ eb̠la̠ rologi d̠inyin, ma̠ enigha̠ awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin ta̠ oghila̠n Akrai̠st bho̠.
EPH 6:6 O̠ni̠ ko ogir agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠bi̠gh inyin, ya̠a̠ igire kuma̠ agu̠o̠ aru̠bana ta̠ Akrai̠st ya̠ na̠ ebhin eb̠la̠ rologi d̠awa na̠ egir i̠to̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 6:7 Ibhine ma̠ onyen ologi ma̠ egir rogir d̠inyin, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin na̠ ogir na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ya̠a̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠.
EPH 6:8 Iloghome ma̠a̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ asu̠o̠ ib̠eb̠i ogir d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, a̠d̠igh e̠bana, a̠d̠igh o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠bana.
EPH 6:9 Inyin ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ aru̠bana, igire ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ma̠ enigha̠ awa. O̠ni̠ ko o̠pa awa. Iloghome ma̠a̠, Wa̠nwuna̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠ a̠nwuna̠ inyin sekina̠ awa, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ i̠na o̠bhe̠l d̠o̠ ma̠ odi a̠kpon odi a̠gurumeni.
EPH 6:10 D̠a̠ okunugiom bho̠, bha̠ i̠mara gigiribh d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ ibom e̠mi̠ a̠limon d̠o̠yo̠.
EPH 6:11 I̠lo̠gi̠ane̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ o̠kpo̠ erorobhi ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin orue o̠damaghan i̠karabh akpati̠an ta̠ Eru bho̠.
EPH 6:12 Ezin bho̠, i̠yar uwia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ asi̠ na̠ ipulupul, ya̠a̠ na̠ owia̠n ogbo irileghom, na̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ra̠dila̠de i̠to̠, na̠ ogbo irileghom e̠mara̠nwunom azi̠m onon, na̠ a̠limon i̠karabh aru̠mu̠gh ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ re̠nai̠ny bho̠.
EPH 6:13 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ibhine ma̠ eb̠la̠ o̠kpo̠ erorobhi ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ e̠kpaki̠an, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin orue o̠marama ma̠ o̠karabh a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠ ma̠ igiel ta̠ a̠ru. Sa̠ igiel inyin na̠ o̠ne̠gi̠me̠ni̠ kabar kabar, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠mara gigiribh.
EPH 6:14 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠mara gigiribh ma̠ ebhin ya̠gia̠ga̠i ma̠ e̠kpo̠a ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠kara d̠a̠ eka̠ka̠gh d̠inyin, ma̠ ebhin a̠ghud̠um igielake̠ ma̠ eguri ma̠ agu̠o̠ ekpeke d̠a̠ ekpa̠kpa̠gh d̠inyin,
EPH 6:15 ma̠ ebhin ebhiroma̠ o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ekima̠ bho̠ ma̠ e̠lo̠gi̠an agu̠o̠ agbaka.
EPH 6:16 Wa̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu bho̠, i̠lo̠gi̠ane̠ ma̠ ekpeke ologi ima̠ra̠, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin orue o̠damaghan eb̠la̠ i̠so̠bh ya̠ na̠ emumor anya bho̠, ya̠ o̠karabh o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠robhod̠i bho̠.
EPH 6:17 Ibhine ma̠ itenemeni e̠mu̠gh ma̠ ezuoma̠ ka̠ eghoi e̠gham, ma̠ esibh ogidi e̠gham ta̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
EPH 6:18 Isiseinye ma̠ a̠d̠ien kerekere a̠siseiny ma̠ eb̠la̠ igiel d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh bho̠, ma̠ e̠mar ekpona̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ne, ma̠ esiseiny egboloma̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
EPH 6:19 Isiseinye ma̠ enigha̠ ami̠ nyen, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠, b̠o̠ka̠ igiel ami̠ i̠kpato̠n o̠nu̠ d̠ami̠, ami̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ alu̠kpo̠ ologi agba ma̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ a̠mutiom.
EPH 6:20 U̠tu̠n ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ o̠so̠n ami̠ ma̠ obhin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Akrai̠st o̠mara, sa̠ ami̠ od̠i ma̠ ikoli ma̠ ebula̠ o̠ku̠a. Isiseinye ma̠ enigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ alu̠kpo̠ ologi agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ akpe̠ ami̠ ma̠ o̠gba bho̠.
EPH 6:21 Od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ eloghom agu̠o̠ ami̠ od̠i, na̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠gir bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ iruom Atai̠siku̠s, umor ed̠ighologi d̠a̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ onin ima̠ra̠ ologi bho̠, na̠ o̠ni̠ogir igielake̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠,
EPH 6:22 ma̠ oru ra̠ o̠gba agu̠o̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar od̠i onigha̠ inyin, na̠ o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ rologi d̠inyin.
EPH 6:23 Ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, sekina̠ etula̠n na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠, e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠a̠ ami̠ ya̠ onin ima̠ra̠ ologi bho̠.
EPH 6:24 E̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ etula̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st na̠ etula̠n wa̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ bho̠.
1TH 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l na̠ Asai̠las na̠ A̠timoti, na̠ o̠ge̠ na̠ oruom inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠gi̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠ d̠a̠ Ate̠saloni̠ka bho̠, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st ma̠a̠: “E̠no̠gho̠man na̠ ekima̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin.”
1TH 1:2 I̠yar na̠ o̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ ogboloma̠ inyin kigiel kigiel, sa̠ i̠yar na̠ osenegi inyin d̠a̠ ra̠siseiny d̠i̠yar.
1TH 1:3 I̠yar na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ ogboloma̠ inyin d̠a̠ a̠siseiny, ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ obhin ologi ima̠ra̠ na̠ ogir ogir bho̠, na̠ agu̠o̠ etula̠n d̠inyin na̠ a̠nu inyin ogir ogir bho̠, na̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ eb̠em ologi d̠inyin d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st bho̠.
1TH 1:4 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ ed̠ighologi d̠i̠yar ya̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, i̠yar ologhom ma̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠tula̠n inyin, sa̠ aso̠n inyin o̠ro̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠.
1TH 1:5 Ezin bho̠, i̠yar ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ku̠ku̠m oruom inyin, ya̠a̠ u̠b̠aram na̠ a̠limon na̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠ga̠i amu̠gho̠nyan. Inyin ologhom ado̠l d̠i̠yar igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠, na̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ d̠i̠yar d̠a̠ ebula̠ inyin.
1TH 1:6 Sa̠ inyin u̠ta ma̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar d̠i̠yar na̠ ita̠ Wa̠nwuna̠, ma̠ ola̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io ibom ali̠gam a̠ruzu eka̠, bha̠ inyin u̠da ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠ obhin na̠ a̠libhon ologi wa̠ na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.
1TH 1:7 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, inyin na̠ oten a̠nwunom ya̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ema̠ra̠ ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠ d̠a̠ Ame̠sidonia̠ na̠ Akai̠ya ta̠ e̠ta ma̠ ado̠l bho̠ erugh.
1TH 1:8 Ebula̠ inyin, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠sasaragi̠an d̠o̠ d̠a̠ Ame̠sidonia̠ na̠ Akai̠ya ku̠ku̠m, ya̠a̠ na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n o̠du̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin a̠d̠izo a̠risisi. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠yar unwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ omula̠ ofugh.
1TH 1:9 Ezin bho̠, a̠nwunom i̠ye̠ na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin u̠da i̠yar ubhin, na̠ agu̠o̠ inyin utiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ o̠ko̠l ro̠ye̠bo̠ iru na̠ o̠ko̠l a̠ga̠i A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠,
1TH 1:10 na̠ ogon O̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny oru, O̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, wa̠ a̠tenemeni i̠yar d̠a̠ ibom i̠gam ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.
1TH 2:1 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar, inyin ologhom ma̠a̠, e̠gi̠ d̠i̠yar wa̠ i̠yar uru ra̠ uzua̠n inyin bho̠ na̠ obhe d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠kpo̠.
1TH 2:2 Inyin ologhom agu̠o̠ ugbikimeni i̠yar, sa̠ u̠ki̠ri̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ A̠filipai̠ kisa̠ i̠yar uten uru d̠inyin. D̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ibom i̠damaghan bho̠ eka̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar alu̠kpo̠ ologi o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ eru bho̠ onigha̠ inyin.
1TH 2:3 Agu̠o̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠gh inyin bho̠, bo̠ ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar ubhin d̠a̠ e̠kal ola̠ amu̠gho̠nyan ibhioma̠ i̠yar, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh i̠walama, bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠a̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠ge̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠.
1TH 2:4 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠b̠eton Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠. I̠yar uwia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ obhononmeni rologi a̠nwunom, a̠ten A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ ad̠a ma̠ rologi d̠i̠yar na̠ a̠kpon bho̠.
1TH 2:5 Inyin ologhom ma̠a̠ i̠yar ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ ibhelebhel aru̠nu̠ oru d̠inyin, bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠a̠ i̠yar na̠ obhelebhel na̠ okpegiom ado̠l o̠ku̠ku̠. A̠zib̠a̠ onyob̠a̠ d̠i̠yar.
1TH 2:6 I̠yar uwia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ itutumeni d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠, ya̠ ta̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠inyin eru, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ipa̠n ogbo.
1TH 2:7 Agu̠o̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ ogbogir ta̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, akpe̠ i̠yar obhin a̠dila̠de i̠to̠ d̠i̠yar o̠te̠i̠ i̠d̠iar d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠inyin na̠ otutumeni i̠yar, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠gbara anwi̠i̠ny d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin, ma̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ onweni na̠ a̠kponom anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
1TH 2:8 obha̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ i̠yar ukponom inyin. I̠yar otula̠n inyin ibom. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, i̠yar ubhin d̠o̠ d̠a̠ onyen ologi o̠gba ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ ku̠ku̠m o̠nigha̠ inyin, ya̠a̠ i̠yar u̠b̠aram na̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠i̠yar.
1TH 2:9 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, inyin ta̠ orue o̠ru̠ru̠an agu̠o̠ i̠yar ugbosuom a̠ruzu d̠i̠yar na̠ e̠kparama ado̠l, ugir a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n, bo̠ka̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠dol d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ u̠gba ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ unigha̠ inyin bho̠.
1TH 2:10 Inyin ronyob̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ onyob̠a̠ nyen, ma̠a̠, i̠yar urugha̠n inyin ogbo ya̠ uma̠ra̠ bho̠, d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala na̠ igielake̠, sa̠ abar ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m i̠yar o̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
1TH 2:11 Inyin ologhom ma̠a̠, i̠yar urughom ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ inyin agu̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠ na̠ a̠rughom anwi̠i̠ny iyo̠yo̠ na̠ agu̠o̠.
1TH 2:12 I̠yar o̠le̠gh inyin, o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin, sa̠ ukpon inyin d̠a̠ obhel i̠ku̠nu̠, sa̠ unuom gha̠n inyin orugh a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ ta̠ etutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠bhelegi inyin a̠d̠ighom ani̠ d̠a̠ irileghom, na̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
1TH 2:13 Opa̠n abar ola̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠tu̠n na̠ otutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bha̠, inyin u̠nagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ d̠i̠yar, sa̠ inyin u̠da ubhin agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ga̠i bho̠, ma̠a̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ a̠nwunom e̠mara̠nwunom d̠o̠. Sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ bho̠ na̠ elol nyen d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠inyin ogbo ya̠ uma̠ra̠ bho̠.
1TH 2:14 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar, inyin uten a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ta ma̠ ado̠l ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st d̠a̠ raso̠si̠ A̠zudia̠ bho̠. Inyin ugbika̠ ma̠ onin a̠d̠ien regbika̠ d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ a̠nwunom d̠inyin agu̠o̠ raso̠si̠ i̠ye̠ igbika̠ d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ ogbo A̠zu bho̠,
1TH 2:15 ya̠ igigh Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, sa̠ i̠ze̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠riwil bho̠, sa̠ izegi i̠yar oten o̠d̠u̠a nyen bho̠. Od̠ighi i̠di̠ar d̠awa id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ologi, sa̠ ighir eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ologi.
1TH 2:16 Awa na̠ e̠ghaghana i̠yar o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ onigha̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun A̠zu, od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ eten. Ka̠ ukpon ud̠ighom, bha̠ awa na̠ egir i̠ye̠ kigiel kigiel ma̠ omuzoghod̠i i̠karabh d̠awa. Ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n, i̠gam ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ awa d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠.
1TH 2:17 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar, i̠yar u̠bagi̠na inyin awai̠ (d̠a̠ ipulupul, ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ ekpo ologi d̠o̠), ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ ebhebhia̠ inyin i̠mar id̠ighi i̠yar, ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar uwia̠n ibom omula̠ ra̠ o̠bi̠gh inyin a̠d̠ien.
1TH 2:18 E̠mar ebhir i̠yar omula̠ oru d̠inyin. Ami̠ Apo̠l na̠ agu̠o̠ amar a̠wia̠n oru ra̠ o̠bi̠gh inyin, ya̠a̠ Eru bho̠ a̠kigima̠ i̠yar.
1TH 2:19 Eb̠em ologi d̠i̠yar, na̠ a̠libhon ologi d̠i̠yar, na̠ asu̠o̠ ibo d̠i̠yar d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠ igiel i̠na ta̠ a̠ru ka̠ ere? Inyin d̠o̠ ke̠re̠?
1TH 2:20 Yii, inyin asu̠o̠ ibo d̠i̠yar na̠ a̠libhon ologi d̠i̠yar.
1TH 3:1 Igiel bho̠ i̠yar orue mu̠ ma̠ one bho̠, sa̠ i̠yar u̠mu̠gho̠nyan ma̠a̠, i̠yar o̠ro̠ esi ola̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ Ate̠ns ta̠ a̠bhon a̠pu.
1TH 3:2 Sa̠ i̠yar uruom A̠timoti umor d̠i̠yar wa̠ na̠ i̠yar na̠ ogir ogir ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ wa̠ na̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ta̠ Akrai̠st na̠ asasaragi̠ bho̠, ma̠ oru ra̠ o̠ghu̠ame̠ni̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ rologi d̠inyin,
1TH 3:3 b̠o̠ka̠ egbika̠ i̠nye̠n ko odughumeni ma̠ ologi odi o̠ni̠ inyin. Inyin o̠mar ologhom ma̠a̠, i̠ye̠ idi regbika̠ ya̠ ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ i̠yar bho̠.
1TH 3:4 Igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠, i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠gba o̠gba onigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠ i̠yar ta̠ ogbika̠, sa̠ na̠ emite ma̠ o̠ku̠a nyen.
1TH 3:5 Obha̠ ezin bho̠ igiel bho̠ ami̠ one mu bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ iruom A̠timoti ma̠ oru ra̠ ologhom agu̠o̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin od̠i. Ami̠ ighil ka̠ Eru bho̠ na̠ ad̠agi̠an inyin ola̠ eb̠la̠ ogir d̠i̠yar na̠ ebhe ma̠ i̠kpo̠.
1TH 3:6 Ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n A̠timoti na̠ ad̠u̠a d̠inyin a̠mula̠ a̠ru ra̠ agba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ etula̠n d̠inyin a̠nigha̠ i̠yar. I̠na agba a̠nigha̠ i̠yar ma̠a̠ inyin na̠ o̠ru̠ru̠an na̠ ogboloma̠ i̠yar kigiel kigiel, sa̠ ebhebhia̠ i̠yar na̠ ed̠ighi inyin agu̠o̠ ebhebhia̠ inyin na̠ ed̠ighi i̠yar bho̠.
1TH 3:7 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar, iloghome ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io i̠nyo̠gho̠nyo̠gh na̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ i̠yar bho̠, ma̠a̠, ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠i̠yar.
1TH 3:8 I̠se̠n agu̠o̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ aghu̠a d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, bha̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar e̠mi̠ a̠ghud̠um.
1TH 3:9 I̠yar ta̠ o̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ eka̠ ma̠ ebula̠ inyin? I̠yar na̠ o̠se̠bh i̠na ma̠ a̠libhon ologi wa̠ i̠yar unwuna̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ ebula̠ inyin bho̠.
1TH 3:10 A̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n, i̠yar na̠ obhin eb̠la̠ ologi d̠i̠yar na̠ osiseiny A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ oru ra̠ o̠bi̠gh inyin a̠d̠ien, onigha̠ inyin i̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠ghu̠ame̠ni̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin opeleni agu̠o̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠.
1TH 3:11 A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ agu̠o̠, na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar A̠zizo̠s erileghom i̠yar a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ inyin.
1TH 3:12 Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠, e̠mi̠ etula̠n wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin na̠ ipa̠n ogbo bho̠, ta̠ agi̠ ma̠ anyu̠, ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ i̠yar utula̠n inyin u̠te̠i̠ bho̠.
1TH 3:13 I̠na akparame̠ni̠ inyin ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ abar o̠li̠o̠m inyin ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, ya̠a̠ inyin ta̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar, ma̠ igiel Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ta̠ a̠ru na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom e̠b̠ab̠ala d̠o̠yo̠.
1TH 4:1 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, d̠a̠ okunugiom bha̠, iloghome ma̠a̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin agu̠o̠ orugh ado̠l ya̠ ta̠ ed̠igh A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ ologi, sa̠ inyin na̠ orugh o̠ku̠a nyen. I̠se̠n i̠yar na̠ obhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ A̠zizo̠s na̠ o̠le̠gh inyin, na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin, ogir opeleni o̠ku̠a nyen.
1TH 4:2 Ezin bho̠, inyin ologhom ra̠kikiom ya̠ i̠yar ubhin a̠limon ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ukikiom inyin bho̠.
1TH 4:3 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠ghan inyin o̠b̠ab̠ala. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ighele ma̠ ado̠l od̠e e̠ma.
1TH 4:4 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ inyin, a̠sibhom ozu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠rugh ado̠l e̠b̠ab̠ala na̠ edim,
1TH 4:5 o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ obhibhirigha̠n a̠ruzu ya̠ ipesi, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ egir bho̠.
1TH 4:6 D̠a̠ e̠kal abar onon, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ odi o̠ni̠ inyin ta̠ a̠bhin ikoiny a̠gir i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ umor, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠pesiom u̠marani̠. I̠yar na̠ od̠ia̠ o̠gba onigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠gbikimeni ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gir i̠karabh ya̠ o̠ku̠a.
1TH 4:7 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ obhelegi d̠o̠ i̠yar orugh ado̠l od̠e e̠ma, ya̠a̠ i̠yar orugh a̠ghud̠um e̠b̠ab̠ala.
1TH 4:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠gin i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ ogin d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ a̠ghel A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
1TH 4:9 Ezin ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠tu̠n o̠ge̠ oruom inyin agu̠o̠ ola̠ odi ta̠ a̠tula̠n odi bo̠, ezin bho̠ inyin na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ o̠tu̠ghan d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ odi ta̠ a̠tula̠n odi.
1TH 4:10 Sa̠ inyin na̠ ogir o̠ku̠a nyen. Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, inyin na̠ otula̠n eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ inyin uma̠ra̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ Ame̠sidonia̠ bho̠. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠gh inyin ogir opeleni o̠ku̠a nyen.
1TH 4:11 Iguri d̠a̠ i̠walama d̠inyin orugh ado̠l ekima̠, ma̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ esi ola̠ inyin, ma̠ ebhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠inyin egir ogir, ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠yar ud̠ia̠ ukikiom inyin bho̠.
1TH 4:12 Ka̠ inyin ugir o̠ku̠a sa̠ inyin ta̠ od̠igh edim d̠a̠ a̠misigh ogbo ya̠ d̠a̠ etire ya̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, sa̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ obhin o̠ni̠ ob̠em ologi.
1TH 4:13 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar, i̠yar na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠ghan inyin onwuna̠ amu̠gho̠nyan ogboloma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ emugughu bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ inyin u̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ eb̠em ologi.
1TH 4:14 Agu̠o̠ i̠yar uma̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠mugh sa̠ a̠b̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠, obha̠ onin agu̠o̠ i̠yar uma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, igiel i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠b̠egion imumugh ya̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠awa bho̠ ab̠aram a̠bhin a̠ru.
1TH 4:15 I̠yar na̠ obhin d̠a̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ onigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, igiel Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru, i̠yar ogbo ya̠ ta̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um o̠te̠i̠ igiel i̠na ta̠ a̠ru bho̠, ko od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ emugughu bho̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ i̠na.
1TH 4:16 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠sor a̠ru na̠ obom okoroko izul, na̠ izul ta̠ we̠mu̠ itileduom bho̠, na̠ okoroko od̠od̠ue ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st kisa̠ imugh bho̠ ta̠ ed̠ia̠ eb̠egina̠.
1TH 4:17 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠ sa̠ A̠zib̠a ta̠ a̠kpobh i̠yar ogbo ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠a̠ obhel obha̠ bho̠ a̠bhuneni, ka̠ a̠d̠ighom na̠ awa d̠a̠ o̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh ka̠ e̠te̠i̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ e̠nai̠ny. Ob̠eton d̠a̠ obhel obha̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ sa̠ i̠yar ta̠ od̠igh na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ o̠ro̠ tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul.
1TH 4:18 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, odi a̠bhin ro̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ i̠nye̠n akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi ta̠ odi.
1TH 5:1 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, ezin bo̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠tu̠n o̠ge̠ ogboloma̠ obhel wa̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ta̠ emite bho̠ oruom inyin.
1TH 5:2 Ezin bho̠ inyin o̠mar ologhom ma̠a̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gba ma̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n.
1TH 5:3 Igiel a̠nwunom na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠, “Kabar kabar od̠i d̠a̠ ekima̠ na̠ d̠a̠ eko,” bha̠ a̠d̠ugh ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ awa ma̠ awai̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ iguna̠ na̠ ate̠i̠ ani̠ eghun, sa̠ awa ko orue d̠o̠ emiza̠n.
1TH 5:4 Ya̠a̠ inyin a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠ami̠ bo̠ d̠a̠ azi̠m, ma̠ ola̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠b̠ol inyin u̠man ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gba.
1TH 5:5 Eb̠la̠ inyin anwi̠i̠ny e̠b̠alab̠al na̠ etita̠n a̠d̠io. I̠yar iya̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n a̠d̠io na̠ azi̠m d̠o̠.
1TH 5:6 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠yar okod̠u d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ipa̠n ogbo, ya̠a̠, i̠yar o̠ro̠ ma̠ omom okpon okimeni ma̠ a̠ruzu.
1TH 5:7 Ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekod̠u ma̠ adi̠la na̠ ekod̠u ma̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n, sa̠ i̠d̠ama̠min bho̠ na̠ e̠d̠a na̠ e̠bhu̠ghu̠d̠i̠an a̠d̠uga̠la̠n.
1TH 5:8 Ya̠a̠ agu̠o̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny etita̠n bho̠, i̠yar okimeni ma̠ a̠ruzu. I̠yar o̠lo̠gi̠an ologi ima̠ra̠ na̠ etula̠n ka̠ ekpeke-e̠gham, ozuoma̠ ma̠ eb̠em ologi itenemeni ka̠ eghoiy-e̠gham.
1TH 5:9 Ezin bho̠, A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ odin d̠o̠ i̠yar o̠bi̠gh ali̠gam a̠ruzu i̠gam d̠o̠yo̠ aso̠n i̠yar, ya̠a̠ atu̠n i̠yar o̠te̠i̠ itenemeni d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st.
1TH 5:10 I̠na a̠mugh a̠nigha̠ i̠yar agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ od̠igh na̠ i̠na orugha̠n, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ i̠yar od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ i̠yar na̠ omugughu eka̠.
1TH 5:11 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, odi akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi ta̠ odi, alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠no̠ni̠no̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ ogir i̠se̠n bho̠.
1TH 5:12 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠gh inyin olelegi ogbo ya̠ na̠ egir ibom d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin bho̠, sa̠ na̠ erileghom, na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin agu̠o̠ orugh a̠ghud̠um igielake̠ onigha̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
1TH 5:13 Ibhine awa ma̠ e̠tu̠o̠m abar ma̠ etula̠n awa d̠a̠ ebula̠ ogir d̠awa. Ekima̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin.
1TH 5:14 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ onigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, ikikiome ma̠ i̠gbu̠o̠ro̠gbu̠o̠r, ma̠ e̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠ku̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien bho̠, ma̠ e̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ edugh bho̠, ma̠ ene ma̠ egboloma̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠.
1TH 5:15 Iwia̠ne ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ odi ko od̠e d̠o̠ ma̠ odi ma̠ olo, ya̠a̠ id̠ighi odi a̠gir abar wa̠ a̠bhon ogir bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ odi na̠ eb̠la̠ ipa̠n ogbo.
1TH 5:16 I̠ro̠ d̠a̠ a̠libhon ologi kigiel kigiel.
1TH 5:17 Isiseinye ma̠ eb̠la̠ igiel.
1TH 5:18 Kabar kabar ola̠ a̠mite, i̠se̠bhe̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Ezin bho̠ onon abar wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh inyin ogir bho̠, d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ inyin u̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st bho̠.
1TH 5:19 O̠ni̠ ko odughumeni ma̠ E̠mu̠gh e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠.
1TH 5:20 O̠ni̠ ko o̠ki̠ri̠ ma̠ iwowa̠,
1TH 5:21 ya̠a̠ i̠d̠a kabar kabar ekpon, ma̠ e̠da ma̠ iya̠ ibhon bho̠ ma̠ ebhin,
1TH 5:22 ma̠ eghel ka̠d̠ien ka̠d̠ien i̠karabh.
1TH 5:23 A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ekima̠ bho̠ na̠ agu̠o̠, ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ inyin d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal a̠ghud̠um d̠inyin, d̠a̠ e̠mu̠gh, d̠a̠ eloghoma̠n ozu, na̠ d̠a̠ ipulupul ozu. A̠zib̠a̠ a̠guri inyin agu̠o̠ ola̠ ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m inyin ma̠ igiel A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru.
1TH 5:24 I̠na wa̠ a̠bhelegi inyin bho̠ na̠ a̠sibh ogua̠n, sa̠ ta̠ a̠gir agu̠o̠ agba bho̠.
1TH 5:25 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, isiseinye ma̠ enigha̠ i̠yar.
1TH 5:26 Ipura̠ne ma̠ eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ a̠libhon ologi na̠ etula̠n.
1TH 5:27 Ami̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠limon ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠ruom inyin osen a̠d̠ire a̠lebh onon onigha̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ i̠na bho̠.
1TH 5:28 E̠no̠gho̠man ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin.
2TH 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l, na̠ Asai̠las, na̠ A̠timoti, na̠ o̠ge̠ na̠ oruom inyin ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠gi̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠ d̠a̠ Ate̠salonia̠ bho̠, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st ma̠a̠:
2TH 1:2 E̠no̠gho̠man na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠, na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin.
2TH 1:3 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, akpe̠ i̠yar o̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ eb̠la̠ kigiel ebula̠ agu̠o̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ a̠bhobh bho̠, sa̠ etula̠n wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin na̠ abu̠gh e̠mi̠ bho̠.
2TH 1:4 Obha̠ bha̠ ezin wa̠ i̠yar na̠ obhin inyin na̠ obo d̠a̠ raso̠si̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠. I̠yar na̠ obo d̠a̠ a̠ma̠ne d̠inyin, na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin, na̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ osibhom a̠ruzu d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io i̠damaghan na̠ egbika̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 1:5 I̠nye̠n na̠ eleriom ma̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠sobh ase̠ igielake̠, sa̠ na̠ e̠gba na̠ emutiom ma̠a̠ inyin o̠kpe̠ ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ one ma̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 1:6 Agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ igielake̠ bho̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ enigha̠ inyin ali̠gam a̠ruzu bho̠,
2TH 1:7 sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠tenemeni inyin d̠a̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ inyin bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ ab̠aram na̠ i̠yar a̠tenemeni. I̠na ta̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a ma̠ igiel Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ta̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny a̠mite a̠ru na̠ imoma̠na̠n itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠,
2TH 1:8 na̠ e̠ba anya ola̠ na̠ a̠mumor belembelem na̠ a̠rubhula̠, ma̠ obhin o̠kpe̠ ogbo ya̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ i̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i O̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar A̠zizo̠s bho̠.
2TH 1:9 Ta̠ ogbikimeni awa ma̠ egbika̠ kid̠ud̠ul, sa̠ ta̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n awa o̠si̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠limon isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠.
2TH 1:10 Igiel i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru, eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ima̠ra̠ i̠na bho̠ ta̠ e̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ a̠d̠igh awa ma̠ ilologia̠n. Inyin od̠i ani̠ d̠a̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠awa, ezin bho̠ inyin oma̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠yar u̠gba unigha̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 1:11 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠yar na̠ osiseiny na̠ onigha̠ inyin kigiel kigiel, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin ma̠ o̠ro̠ agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ta̠ erugh ado̠l wa̠ akpe̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n bho̠ ma̠ orugh. I̠na a̠bhin a̠limon d̠o̠yo̠ a̠muzoghod̠iom eb̠la̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠walama d̠inyin, na̠ rogir ya̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠inyin na̠ enuom inyin ogir bho̠.
2TH 1:12 I̠yar na̠ osiseiny o̠ku̠a b̠o̠ka̠ otutumeni ma̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ma̠ ebula̠ inyin, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠tutumeni inyin nyen, d̠a̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st.
2TH 2:1 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠gh inyin, ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ omula̠ oru ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s, na̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n wa̠ i̠yar ta̠ ka̠ o̠te̠i̠ i̠na bho̠, ma̠a̠:
2TH 2:2 o̠ni̠ ko o̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠an d̠a̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an, o̠ni̠ ko okpa̠ra̠noma̠ nyen egboloma̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ ta̠ ekue e̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ iwowa̠ d̠i̠yar, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠fugh o̠nu̠, bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠lebh eru, sa̠ ta̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠ru.
2TH 2:3 Agu̠o̠ ka̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ e̠bhi̠bhi̠ri̠gi̠, o̠ni̠ ko oma̠ra̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ma̠ ogelemeni inyin. Ezin bho̠, kisa̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠ru, a̠nwunom ta̠ ewia̠n a̠limon ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ ta̠ e̠damaghan i̠na ma̠ o̠kparakpar agu̠o̠, sa̠ O̠karabh O̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ orobh o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ e̠ba anya od̠im o̠to̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom ozu.
2TH 2:4 O̠karabh O̠ni̠ bho̠ ta̠ adamaghan kabar kabar ola̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ ta̠ abu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ a̠peleni kabar kabar ola̠ na̠ obhelegi ma̠ a̠zib̠a̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ola̠ na̠ o̠ko̠l. I̠na ta̠ agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ Otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ nyen are̠ma ma̠a̠ i̠na A̠zib̠a̠.
2TH 2:5 Ka̠ inyin ta̠ orue o̠ru̠ru̠an, ami̠ agba gha̠n i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠nigha̠ inyin igiel bho̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 2:6 Ya̠a̠, i̠se̠n inyin na̠ ologhom abar wa̠ na̠ a̠sibh O̠karabh O̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠guri tu̠tu̠n ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ga̠i obhel wa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ru bho̠.
2TH 2:7 I̠se̠n bha̠ a̠limon e̠wo̠gi̠na wa̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠we̠le̠ osibh oloko bho̠ na̠ ake̠ ma̠ ogir. Ya̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠sibh a̠limon bho̠ na̠ a̠guri bho̠ ta̠ a̠sibh tu̠tu̠n i̠na ta̠ a̠toka̠n.
2TH 2:8 I̠se̠ kisa̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ osibh d̠o̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom ozu. Ya̠a̠, igiel Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru sa̠ ta̠ a̠pughe ma̠ obhubhulom d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠gigh O̠ni̠ wa̠ osibh d̠o̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠bhin isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠ a̠kunugi i̠na.
2TH 2:9 Eruoma̠ O̠ni̠ wa̠ osibh d̠o̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ ta̠ agi̠ na̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar ta̠ Eru bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien kere kere a̠limon a̠mutioghom relegh, a̠gir ilologia̠n igunugha̠,
2TH 2:10 sa̠ ta̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien kerekere i̠karabh ikoiny a̠gelemeni ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ta̠ ebhe bho̠. Awa ta̠ emugughu ekun, ezin bho̠ awa ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ otula̠n a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠ o̠da obhin b̠o̠ka̠ awa eten.
2TH 2:11 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ afi̠ri̠ma ma̠ a̠limon ola̠ o̠su̠su̠ghu̠d̠i̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an d̠awa b̠o̠ka̠ awa ema̠ra̠ ma̠ igunugha̠ bho̠.
2TH 2:12 Sa̠ ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ osobh ase̠ obhumeni ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠, ya̠a̠ na̠ eba̠ra̠ kuma̠ od̠ighi i̠karabh bho̠.
2TH 2:13 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ kigiel kigiel ebula̠ inyin ogbo ya̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠tula̠n bho̠. Ezin bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aso̠n inyin oten ka̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, d̠a̠ o̠wo̠l oten a̠limon ta̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, wa̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ inyin ta̠ o̠b̠ab̠ala d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ inyin uma̠ra̠ ma̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
2TH 2:14 I̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba d̠o̠yo̠ ya̠ i̠yar u̠gba unigha̠ inyin bho̠ a̠bhelegi inyin, ma̠ inyin o̠te̠i̠ a̠bin d̠inyin d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st.
2TH 2:15 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠kpo̠ ma̠ ologi ma̠ e̠mara d̠a̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ i̠yar u̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin bho̠, ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ d̠i̠yar imite bho̠ bo̠d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ra̠lebh ya̠ i̠yar u̠ge̠ uruom inyin bho̠.
2TH 2:16 Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st na̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar, wa̠ a̠tula̠n i̠yar bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar alu̠kpo̠ ologi ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ na̠ a̠ga̠i eb̠em ologi bho̠,
2TH 2:17 akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi na̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin d̠a̠ ob̠eb̠i ka̠ ob̠eb̠i abar ola̠ inyin na̠ ogir na̠ iya̠ inyin na̠ ofugh.
2TH 3:1 D̠a̠ ipa̠n i̠di̠ar bha̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠gba na̠ onigha̠ inyin a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ ma̠a̠, isiseinye ma̠ enigha̠ i̠yar agu̠o̠ ola̠ Ib̠eb̠i O̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ e̠sasaragi̠an onyen, na̠ a̠nwunom o̠da obhin na̠ edim, agu̠o̠ aro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 3:2 Isiseinye ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni i̠yar d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ id̠im na̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh a̠nwunom, ezin bho̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ta̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ O̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ bho̠.
2TH 3:3 Ya̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠sibh ogua̠n bho̠, ta̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠inyin a̠guri inyin esi eko a̠sigimeni ma̠ O̠karabh O̠ni̠ bho̠.
2TH 3:4 I̠yar onwuna̠ ma̠ alu̠kpo̠ ologi d̠a̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, inyin na̠ ogir agu̠o̠ i̠yar u̠gba unigha̠ inyin bho̠, sa̠ inyin ta̠ o̠ro̠ ma̠ ogir ogir o̠ku̠a nyen.
2TH 3:5 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠rileghom rologi d̠inyin d̠a̠ etula̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ne wa̠ Akrai̠st na̠ a̠nigha̠ bho̠.
2TH 3:6 A̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, i̠yar na̠ obhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ na̠ o̠gba na̠ onigha̠ inyin ma̠a̠, isigima̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ onin ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ya̠ na̠ erugh ado̠l e̠gbu̠o̠r, na̠ ogbo ya̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ i̠yar u̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 3:7 Inyin o̠mar ologhom ma̠a̠, akpe̠ inyin o̠ta ado̠l d̠i̠yar agu̠o̠ i̠yar o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠gbu̠o̠ro̠gbu̠o̠r d̠a̠ igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠.
2TH 3:8 I̠yar ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ od̠e ma̠ inwo nyen. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ i̠yar ugir ogir a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n, ogbosuom a̠ruzu, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ko onigha̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ inyin a̠dol.
2TH 3:9 Bo̠d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de a̠limon opuru inyin o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ onigha̠ i̠yar, ya̠a̠ i̠yar ugir o̠ku̠a b̠o̠ka̠ inyin o̠ta ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh d̠i̠yar.
2TH 3:10 Odi abar eka̠, i̠yar u̠lo̠gh oloko onigha̠ inyin ma̠ igiel bho̠ i̠yar u̠ro̠ na̠ inyin bho̠ ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ola̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir ogir o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ abar d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ a̠d̠e. O̠ni̠ ola̠ ogir d̠o̠ od̠e d̠o̠.”
2TH 3:11 I̠yar na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n ma̠a̠, idi inyin na̠ orugh ado̠l e̠gbu̠o̠r, sa̠ opa̠n abar ola̠ na̠ egir bo̠ a̠ten o̠d̠u̠a esi oten esi na̠ i̠me̠ghe̠nyan.
2TH 3:12 I̠yar na̠ o̠gba na̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠ na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠le̠gh awa d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, ma̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ ekima̠, obhin aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa ogir o̠te̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n ya̠ awa ta̠ ed̠e.
2TH 3:13 Ya̠a̠ inyin a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, ogir ib̠eb̠i o̠tabh d̠o̠ inyin.
2TH 3:14 I̠mare̠ ma̠ ekpon elelegi ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nagha o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠i̠yar, ya̠ i̠yar u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ a̠lebh onon bho̠. O̠ni̠ ko od̠ed̠ia̠n o̠ni̠ ola̠ oku̠a, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na a̠d̠igh ari̠ghe̠l.
2TH 3:15 Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, o̠ni̠ ko oguri i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien, ya̠a̠ ikikiome i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ umor bo̠d̠o̠ u̠marani̠ d̠a̠ onin ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠.
2TH 3:16 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ agu̠o̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ekima̠ bho̠, a̠nigha̠ inyin ekima̠ kigiel kigiel d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal. Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ aro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin.
2TH 3:17 Ami̠ Apo̠l na̠ agu̠o̠, ibhin agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ age̠ ma̠ ibheleguma̠ ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠lebh onon bho̠. Ami̠ na̠ age̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a ma̠ o̠ro̠ elegh d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠lebh d̠ami̠.
2TH 3:18 E̠no̠gho̠man ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st e̠ro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin.
