1TI 1:1 A̠lebh onon ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ Apo̠l, o̠ni̠ogir ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s a̠ru, d̠a̠ i̠to̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar, na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s wa̠ eb̠em ologi d̠i̠yar bho̠,
1TI 1:2 ma̠ onigha̠ oyom A̠timoti, a̠ga̠i o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠. E̠ne̠ghe̠, okpon igbirigbir, na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar bho̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ anwa.
1TI 1:3 Agu̠o̠ ami̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠oyom ma̠ o̠ro̠ d̠a̠ E̠fi̠so̠s, igiel bho̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠ten na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Ame̠sidonia̠ bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ aghaghana ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ igunugha̠ bho̠ ma̠ o̠we̠le̠man ogir o̠ku̠a.
1TI 1:4 Gba ma̠a̠, awa e̠we̠le̠man rasu̠gbagba ezin o̠to̠ na̠ id̠udul ibom ro̠we̠de̠ d̠awa ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠ro̠d̠o̠ bho̠, ya̠ na̠ emutiom raku̠anan ku̠ku̠m, ya̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ enigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ma̠ orugh a̠ghud̠um ologi ima̠ra̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
1TI 1:5 Ezin abar wa̠ u̠tu̠n u̠to̠ ma̠ i̠to̠ i̠nye̠n bho̠ bha̠, od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ odi ta̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ ologi e̠b̠ab̠ala, na̠ ob̠eb̠i eloghoma̠n, na̠ a̠ga̠i ologi ima̠ra̠ a̠tula̠n odi.
1TI 1:6 Idi ogbo na̠ e̠baro̠n e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n e̠gi̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ ibhelebhel a̠fugh.
1TI 1:7 Awa na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠gh oten i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, ya̠a̠ i̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ iya̠ awa na̠ efugh, na̠ ezin asu̠gbagba ya̠ awa na̠ ebhin alu̠kpo̠ ologi na̠ e̠gba bho̠.
1TI 1:8 I̠yar ologhom ma̠a̠ oloko bho̠ a̠bhon, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ orughom agu̠o̠ a̠soran bho̠.
1TI 1:9 I̠yar ologhom nyen ma̠a̠, udin d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ erugh ya̠ igielake̠ omutiom oloko bho̠, ya̠a̠ udin isorogi ma̠ ro̠kpe̠, na̠ iwia̠n ma̠ ra̠dila̠de irileghom, na̠ ighel ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ idighi ma̠ i̠karabh, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ erugh ado̠l i̠te̠i̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ orugh d̠o̠ ma̠ ado̠l igielake̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ abar ola̠ ima̠ra̠ o̠ro̠d̠o̠, na̠ i̠ze̠ ma̠ ronweni na̠ ro̠we̠de̠, na̠ i̠ze̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom,
1TI 1:10 na̠ id̠eme̠ma, na̠ ilobhiri ya̠ na̠ ekod̠uom ilobhiri, na̠ anwani̠ ya̠ na̠ ekod̠uom anwani̠, na̠ ib̠ua̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom, na̠ i̠gba ma̠ igunugha̠, na̠ ronyob̠a̠ igunugha̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ewia̠n a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠,
1TI 1:11 ya̠ i̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Itutumeni iru, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠.
1TI 1:12 Ami̠ na̠ ase̠bh Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar, wa̠ abi̠gh ma̠ ami̠ akpe̠ sa̠ aso̠n ami̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ ogir o̠yo̠ bho̠.
1TI 1:13 D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten, ami̠ ifugh gha̠n a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ i̠na, sa̠ ami̠ igbikimeni ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ ami̠ i̠ki̠ri̠ i̠na. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠kpon ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir agu̠o̠ ami̠ ologhom d̠o̠ ma̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠gir i̠karabh bho̠, ezin bho̠ ami̠ ima̠ra̠ d̠o̠ i̠na.
1TI 1:14 Sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar a̠bhin d̠a̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ na̠ etula̠n, ya̠ i̠wo̠l d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s iru bho̠.
1TI 1:15 Onon a̠ga̠i o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ola̠ akpe̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom o̠da obhin, ma̠a̠: “Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s a̠ru ma̠ i̠se̠n e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ otenemeni id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh.” Sa̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh wa̠ igurom ipu bho̠.
1TI 1:16 Ya̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠kpon ami̠ ma̠ igbirigbir ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s ta̠ a̠rughom ami̠ a̠guri ma̠ agu̠o̠ elegh a̠ma̠ne d̠o̠yo̠, eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh wa̠ a̠gurom a̠pu bho̠ eka̠. Obha̠ na̠ a̠leriom agu̠o̠ i̠di̠ar ta̠ e̠ro̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠, d̠a̠ o̠gu̠man, sa̠ ta̠ ema̠ra̠ i̠na, sa̠ ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul bho̠.
1TI 1:17 I̠se̠n bha̠, edim na̠ isosorogia̠n e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ma̠ O̠li̠le̠ma wa̠ ka̠ kid̠ud̠ul bho̠, wa̠ omugh d̠o̠ bho̠, wa̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien bho̠, wa̠ i̠na ku̠ku̠m aro̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ga̠i bho̠, tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul. Aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
1TI 1:18 O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ A̠timoti, ami̠ na̠ ato̠ ma̠ i̠to̠ i̠nye̠n na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam ma̠ omuzoghod̠iom iwowa̠ ya̠ uwa̠ ugboloma̠ nyam d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten bho̠, bo̠ka̠ igiel anwa i̠ru̠ru̠an, anwa amar a̠we ma̠ e̠gham bho̠.
1TI 1:19 Sibhe ma̠ eloghoma̠n d̠oyom ma̠ akparame̠ni̠, ma̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ologi e̠b̠ab̠ala. Idi ogbo ighel i̠ye̠, sa̠ i̠we̠le̠man o̠nagha iya̠ ologi na̠ agba. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ i̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠awa.
1TI 1:20 Ahi̠me̠ni̠o̠s na̠ Ale̠kzanda bha̠ idi ogbo ya̠ na̠ egir o̠ku̠a d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠inyin. Ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠eton awa alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ Eru bho̠ ma̠ ogbikimeni, b̠o̠ka̠ awa e̠we̠le̠man a̠fugh i̠basi̠ ogboloma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
1TI 2:1 O̠pu̠r abar bho̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠kikiom inyin ma̠a̠, ipuru ma̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠bho̠ro̠gh bho̠, ma̠ esiseiny, ma̠ e̠mara ma̠ eni, ma̠ e̠se̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ egboloma̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠.
1TI 2:2 Isiseinye ma̠ enigha̠ ma̠ Aru̠li̠le̠ma na̠ ipa̠n ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de i̠to̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠yar orugh a̠ghud̠um eb̠okum na̠ ekima̠, na̠ oghila̠n A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ orugh a̠ghud̠um edim.
1TI 2:3 Osiseiny o̠ko̠no̠n a̠bhon, sa̠ a̠d̠igh ologi ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar,
1TI 2:4 wa̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ma̠ oten na̠ ologhom a̠ga̠i a̠ga̠i bho̠.
1TI 2:5 Ezin bho̠ onin A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ onin o̠mara ma̠ enie ku̠ku̠m od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom na̠ A̠zib̠a̠. I̠na Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s,
1TI 2:6 wa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ obhin o̠ta eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ elegh ola̠ umutiom d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ u̠to̠ bho̠.
1TI 2:7 Obha̠ ezin bho̠ u̠so̠n ami̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠-ogir na̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ima̠ra̠ ologi na̠ a̠ga̠i onigha̠ Ibhebhia̠n bho̠. Ami̠ na̠ agba ma̠ ya̠gia̠ga̠i, igunugha̠ d̠o̠.
1TI 2:8 Ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh agu̠o̠ ola̠ kesi kesi ilobhiri a̠nwunom na̠ esiseiny a̠siseiny, awa eb̠egion aru̠gu̠o̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala e̠gi̠o̠m anyu̠, aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ awa ko ogurumia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ rologi, bo̠d̠o̠ ko o̠ku̠anan d̠o̠ ma̠ aku̠anan.
1TI 2:9 Ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh nyen agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwani̠ ta̠ e̠mar ebura̠ ma̠ ibura̠ ya̠ awa ta̠ ed̠igh edim o̠bi̠gh. Awa oguri d̠o̠ ma̠ asi̠ghal d̠awa ma̠ ya̠ ipe ya̠ osorogi adi̠e̠l, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠ke̠le̠gi̠an a̠goli, na̠ i̠ge̠, na̠ i̠ku̠ta, na̠ i̠b̠o̠lo̠, ya̠ ubhin a̠gol bo̠d̠o̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ e̠mu̠ u̠le̠m, ya̠ ibom a̠b̠ua̠.
1TI 2:10 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, bha̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ anwani̠ ya̠ na̠ egir ib̠eb̠i ya̠ izuzua̠n i̠re̠ma agu̠o̠ awa na̠ obuom A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠.
1TI 2:11 Ani̠ebhom aro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m atu̠ghan d̠a̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu.
1TI 2:12 Ami̠ i̠bho̠ro̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ani̠ebhom ta̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ta̠ aragha ma̠ a̠limon a̠rileghom olobhiri o̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ aro̠ b̠o̠b̠o̠m.
1TI 2:13 Iloghome ma̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠d̠ia̠ ale̠m Adam kisa̠ ale̠m Ivu.
1TI 2:14 Adam d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ugelemeni bho̠, ya̠a̠ ani̠ebhom bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠gir i̠karabh.
1TI 2:15 Aro̠ ku ma̠ o̠ku̠a eka̠, i̠na ta̠ a̠ten d̠a̠ i̠mara, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠na a̠bhin ologi ima̠ra̠, na̠ etula̠n, na̠ onyen ologi d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agi̠o̠m d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, d̠a̠ osibhom ozu.
1TI 3:1 Onon a̠kikiom ola̠ a̠d̠igh esi, ma̠a̠: O̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ ebhir oten o̠ni̠ irileghom aso̠si̠, bha̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh ob̠eb̠i ogir.
1TI 3:2 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, e̠kal ali̠o̠m o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ irileghom, a̠bhin onin ani̠, a̠kimeni ma̠ ozu, ato̠to̠gi̠o̠m a̠ma̠rugh, ologhom abar, a̠d̠igh edim, ada ma̠ isuloma̠ a̠bhin na̠ onyen ologi, atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ na̠ e̠mar,
1TI 3:3 o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠d̠amin, oponoma̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ aro̠ ma̠ okima̠kima̠ o̠ni̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠b̠e̠m d̠o̠, o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ e̠d̠o̠gh okpoki.
1TI 3:4 I̠na aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ amar na̠ a̠rileghom eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ e̠nagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠, sa̠ na̠ erugh a̠ma̠rugh ozuruna̠ eghoi.
1TI 3:5 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ orileghom eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠, ka̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠ighi eka̠ a̠loghom agu̠o̠ okponom aso̠si̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
1TI 3:6 I̠na o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ororua̠ o̠ni̠-i̠tu̠o̠no̠m ta̠ Akrai̠st, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na na̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu a̠mel onin emel wa̠ udin usobh ase̠ ubhumeni ma̠ Eru bho̠.
1TI 3:7 Ob̠eb̠i a̠ma̠rugh d̠o̠yo̠ agba i̠na a̠leriom a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠gi̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na na̠ omel a̠d̠igh ari̠ghe̠l, sekina̠ osor e̠te̠ i̠kpati̠ ta̠ eru bho̠.
1TI 3:8 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ ogbo i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠a̠ aso̠si̠, e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ erugh ado̠l ya̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠. Awa o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo igelemeni, bo̠d̠o̠ ro̠d̠a ma̠ a̠min, bo̠d̠o̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠gh o̠te̠i̠ i̠karabh asu̠o̠.
1TI 3:9 Awa ebhin e̠b̠ab̠ala eloghoma̠n esibhom ima̠ra̠ ologi ilologia̠n bho̠.
1TI 3:10 O̠d̠a okpon a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠ku̠a, kisa̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ ogbo i̠to̠to̠gi̠ aso̠si̠ ku̠gba ma̠ e̠kal ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m bo̠.
1TI 3:11 Anwani̠ d̠awa eka̠ erugh ado̠l ya̠ i̠kpe̠ ma̠ iya̠ ta̠ ozuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi, ogbo i̠me̠ghe̠nyan d̠o̠. Awa e̠ro̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ekimeni ma̠ a̠ruzu, sa̠ na̠ ebhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ na̠ egir kabar kabar.
1TI 3:12 O̠ni̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠a̠ aso̠si̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ onin ani̠, aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ amar na̠ erileghom anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ otu d̠o̠yo̠.
1TI 3:13 A̠nwunom ta̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠a̠ aso̠si̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠mar na̠ egir ogir d̠awa. Sa̠ awa ta̠ enwuna̠ ma̠ obom alu̠kpo̠ ologi d̠a̠ ima̠ra̠ ologi d̠a̠ awa d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s.
1TI 3:14 Agu̠o̠ ami̠ na̠ age̠ ma̠ a̠lebh onon na̠ a̠ruom anwa bho̠, bha̠ na̠ ebhir ami̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠r oru ra̠ ozua̠n oyom.
1TI 3:15 Ya̠a̠, ka̠ ami̠ ibia̠ ma̠ oru, agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ a̠loghom agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom i̠kpe̠ ma̠ orugh d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ga̠i bho̠, wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ e̠ko̠ na̠ o̠de̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
1TI 3:16 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠mutiom a̠leriom i̠yar bho̠ obom ilologia̠n: Akrai̠st a̠ru d̠a̠ ipulupul ozu, sa̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba a̠mutiom ma̠a̠, i̠na amar a̠rugh d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠bi̠gh i̠na, sa̠ u̠gba i̠na umutiom d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom, sa̠ a̠nwunom e̠mara̠nwunom bho̠ ima̠ra̠ i̠na, sa̠ ukpobh i̠na ubhuneni d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n.
1TI 4:1 E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ amar agba a̠mutiom ma̠a̠, d̠a̠ rekunuguma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, idi a̠nwunom ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠nagha ma̠ aru̠mu̠gh igunugha̠ na̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ a̠ruru.
1TI 4:2 Wa̠ ibhelebhel i̠gbamigunugha̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ eloghoma̠n bho̠ na̠ asa ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l awa bho̠.
1TI 4:3 Awa ibhin ma̠ o̠walan ilom bha̠ e̠tu̠tu̠, sa̠ na̠ edin od̠e idi ra̠d̠ien ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ale̠m agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ta̠ e̠da ebhin na̠ ali̠se̠bh sa̠ ta̠ eleriom ya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
1TI 4:4 Kabar kabar A̠zib̠a̠ ale̠m, o̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, i̠yar oghel d̠o̠ ma̠ odi abar i̠se̠, ya̠a̠ o̠da obhi̠n na̠ ali̠se̠bh.
1TI 4:5 Ezin bho̠, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠siseiny na̠ e̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.
1TI 4:6 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa a̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ma̠ a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠, bha̠ anwa oten ob̠eb̠i ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠, na̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ anwa ibhin onyen ologi i̠nagha bho̠, imuzo d̠a̠ ozu.
1TI 4:7 Ya̠a̠, ko onwuna̠ ma̠ abar a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ i̠karabh asu̠gbagba na̠ id̠ud̠ul ya̠ emirobh. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ tu̠ghane̠ ma̠ orugh a̠ghud̠um ola̠ ta̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ itutumeni.
1TI 4:8 Oselegi ma̠ ozu d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ta̠ e̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠, ya̠a̠ orugh a̠ma̠rugh oghila̠n A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal ya̠ ta̠ e̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠. Isibhe ma̠ ogua̠n i̠se̠n oghud̠um onon na̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠.
1TI 4:9 Onon a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ola̠ akpe̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠mar o̠da obhin.
1TI 4:10 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠yar na̠ owia̠n na̠ ogir ibom, ezin bho̠ i̠yar na̠ obhin A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠ na̠ ob̠em ologi, i̠na bha̠ Witenemeni eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠, okunukun ogbo ya̠ ima̠ra̠ i̠na bho̠.
1TI 4:11 Kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ agba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n a̠nigha̠ awa, ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa nyen.
1TI 4:12 Ko oma̠ra̠ ka̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠din agu̠o̠ anwa i̠ro̠ ma̠ okubh o̠ni̠ bho̠ a̠kpon anwa aki̠ri̠me̠ni̠. Ya̠a̠, rughe ma̠ ado̠l ya̠ ipa̠n ogbo ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ta̠ e̠ta, d̠a̠ a̠fugh o̠nu̠ na̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar d̠oyom, d̠a̠ etula̠n d̠oyom, d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠oyom, na̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala ologi d̠oyom.
1TI 4:13 Kisa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠ru, bha̠ bhine gha̠n ma̠ obhel a̠sen A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n, kikiome, ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
1TI 4:14 Ko oghel enigha̠ e̠mu̠gh wa̠ od̠i na̠ anwa bho̠, wa̠ unigha̠ nyam igiel bho̠ ikei bho̠ i̠gbamagi̠ ma̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠awa d̠a̠ ozu d̠oyom, iwa̠ igboloma̠ bho̠.
1TI 4:15 Ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, bo̠ka̠ eloloma̠ ogir d̠oyom emite ma̠ ola̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ta̠ abi̠gh
1TI 4:16 Mare̠ ma̠ a̠kpona̠ ma̠ od̠ighi i̠d̠i̠ar d̠oyom na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠oyom. Ro̠ ma̠ ogir ogir i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, ezin bho̠, ka̠ anwa igir o̠ku̠a sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ozu d̠oyom na̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠nagha nyam bho̠.
1TI 5:1 Ko obhin i̠gam a̠kikiom ikei o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠we̠de̠. Kikiome ma̠ ikubh-anwi̠i̠ny agu̠o̠ a̠rumor.
1TI 5:2 Rugha̠ne ma̠ ikei a̠nwunom anwani̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ronweni, ikubh-anwi̠nyan ma̠ agu̠o̠ aru̠marani̠, d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ko o̠pi̠o̠gho̠m d̠o̠ awa d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal.
1TI 5:3 Lo̠ghe̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠ ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠ ga̠i.
1TI 5:4 Ya̠a̠, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ ekpukele ani̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny bo̠d̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny igha̠la̠, bha̠ awa ekponom i̠na, ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠kponom awa, sa̠ ogir o̠ku̠a a̠bhon d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
1TI 5:5 Ya̠a̠, ekpukele ani̠ ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ ekpukele ani̠ ga̠i, ya̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠, bha̠ na̠ a̠bhin A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠b̠em ologi, sa̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠ma̠ne na̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠siseiny a̠siseiny a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n, na̠ a̠puru i̠na ma̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠.
1TI 5:6 Ya̠a̠, ekpukele ani̠ ola̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ e̠me̠me̠m e̠mara̠nwunom onon, bha̠ na̠ a̠mugh, aro̠ ku ma̠ i̠na od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um eka̠.
1TI 5:7 Kikiome awa ma̠ ra̠kikiom i̠nye̠n b̠o̠ka̠ u̠bi̠gh abar e̠kal obhin o̠li̠o̠m awa.
1TI 5:8 Ya̠a̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ okponom ogbo a̠ghisia̠n d̠o̠yo̠, okunukun a̠nwunom eghunotu d̠o̠yo̠, bha̠ o̠ni̠ bho̠ na̠ aku̠a ma̠ ima̠ra̠ ologi bho̠ sa̠ a̠gurom a̠pu ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st.
1TI 5:9 Ko o̠ge̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ekpukele ani̠ ma̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire rekpukele anwani̠ bho̠, a̠ten ola̠ o̠nu̠ ala bho̠ na̠ epel e̠rabharabh (60), ola̠ awal owolom d̠o̠yo̠ ku̠ku̠m, sa̠ od̠e d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠ma.
1TI 5:10 I̠na aro̠ ma̠ ani̠ ola̠ a̠d̠igh edim d̠a̠ a̠misigh eb̠la̠ ogbo sa̠ u̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i ogir d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ amar a̠rughom anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ onyen ologi ola̠ o̠ki̠o̠gho̠m risuloma̠, na̠ otitologh a̠sike a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ alo̠gh gha̠n agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ i̠kparama ado̠l, sa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ obhel a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ogir ib̠eb̠i.
1TI 5:11 Ko o̠lo̠gh a̠rid̠ien rekpukele anwani̠ ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ ikubh, i̠kparakpar rebhiroma̠ ozu d̠awa ta̠ epel iya̠ awa inwuna̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠bho̠ro̠gh omula̠ o̠wal ilom,
1TI 5:12 sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ ebhum ase̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa osibh d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠pu̠r ogua̠n awa bho̠.
1TI 5:13 D̠a̠ onin obhel bho̠, awa ta̠ eten i̠gbu̠o̠ro̠gbu̠o̠r, sa̠ ta̠ erugh rado̠l ya̠ o̠d̠u̠a otu oten otu. Ka̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠gbu̠o̠ro̠gbu̠o̠r ku̠ku̠m, ya̠a̠ ta̠ eten ogbo i̠me̠ghe̠nyan, na̠ ra̠d̠ikelekpum, efughogh i̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠.
1TI 5:14 Oku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ami̠ na̠ a̠kikiom agu̠o̠ ola̠ ikubh rekpukele anwani̠ ta̠ emula̠ e̠wal ilom, e̠maragi̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny, ekponom a̠rutu d̠awa. Sa̠ o̠ni̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien bho̠ ko onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ezin ola̠ odin ofugh i̠karabh ogboloma̠ awa.
1TI 5:15 I̠bi̠ghe̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n d̠a̠ idi awa na̠ e̠baro̠n e̠d̠u̠a na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m Eru bho̠.
1TI 5:16 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠, ani̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ogbo a̠ghisia̠n ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ rekpukele anwani̠, bha̠ i̠na alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠kponom awa. O̠we̠le̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠dol bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ ku̠ku̠m, b̠o̠ka̠ aso̠si̠ bho̠ ekponom a̠ga̠i rekpukele anwani̠ ya̠ i̠kpe̠ bho̠.
1TI 5:17 Ikei ya̠ na̠ e̠mar na̠ erileghom aso̠si̠ bho̠ e̠kpe̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ asu̠wo̠ i̠wal a̠bin, okunukun ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠kparame̠ni̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ na̠ e̠sasaragi̠, sekina̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠.
1TI 5:18 Ezin bho̠, A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Ko o̠gho̠ro̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠kpegi ma̠ o̠nu̠ e̠nam ogir bho̠ ma̠ igiel i̠na na̠ aze̠re̠gi̠ na̠ akagi̠o̠n ikpo ed̠ia̠n bho̠.” Opa̠n esi eka̠ sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, “O̠ni̠ ogir akpe̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ asu̠wo̠ ogir d̠o̠yo̠.”
1TI 5:19 Ko o̠nagha ma̠ iku ola̠ uler ugboloma̠ ma̠ okei-o̠ni̠, a̠ten ka̠ i̠wal o̠ni̠ bo̠d̠o̠ i̠sar o̠ni̠ iru ra̠ i̠gba ma̠ onyob̠a̠ onin o̠nu̠.
1TI 5:20 Ya̠a̠, game̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ egir i̠karabh bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh eb̠la̠ ogbo, bo̠ka̠ a̠d̠igh a̠rugugu a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo.
1TI 5:21 Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin o̠kparakpar okoroko na̠ a̠kikiom anwa d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, na̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ya̠ i̠na na̠ aso̠n bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ atu̠o̠no̠m i̠to̠to̠gi̠ i̠nye̠n, ya̠a̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ abhe̠l odi a̠kpon odi a̠gurumeni.
1TI 5:22 Ko onugia̠n o̠gbamagi̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠ruzu a̠nwunom d̠a̠ o̠so̠n ogbo a̠dila̠de, b̠o̠ka̠ anwa na̠ od̠igh aru̠gi̠an i̠karabh ipa̠n ogbo. Ya̠a̠, rughe ma̠ ado̠l d̠oyom a̠guri d̠a̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala.
1TI 5:23 Ko o̠d̠a ma̠ amu̠m ku̠ku̠m, ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠kara a̠min d̠a̠ ebula̠ okurogh d̠oyom, na̠ rasu̠nwe̠r ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a ma̠ obhel na̠ eten obhel na̠ e̠nwe̠re̠me̠ni̠ nyam bho̠.
1TI 5:24 I̠karabh idi ogbo od̠i ma̠ iya̠ na̠ ologhom na̠ o̠bi̠gh geregere, sa̠ na̠ ebhin awa ka̠ ed̠ighom d̠a̠ ebhum ase̠. Ya̠a̠, i̠karabh idi ogbo na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m awa d̠a̠ aman.
1TI 5:25 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, ib̠eb̠i ogir na̠ e̠ro̠ geregere. Ya̠a̠, ib̠eb̠i ogir ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na bho̠ eka̠, ko orue d̠o̠ o̠wo̠gi̠.
1TI 6:1 Ogbo ya̠ od̠i ma̠ aru̠bana eloghom ma̠a̠ akpe̠ awa ma̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi onigha̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ awa bho̠. O̠ku̠a ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ko ofugh d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠fugh i̠basi̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠i̠yar.
1TI 6:2 Aru̠bana ya̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ awa bho̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠a̠ onin ima̠ra̠ ologi bho̠, okpon d̠o̠ awa e̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠, ezin bho̠ awa a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠awa. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ awa egir epeleni enigha̠ awa, ezin bho̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ asu̠wo̠ ogir d̠awa bho̠ bha̠ ogbo etula̠n ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ onin ima̠ra̠ ologi bho̠. Tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ma̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠awa ma̠ ogir o̠ku̠a.
1TI 6:3 O̠ni̠ ola̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ opa̠n abar ola̠ a̠nwegia̠n na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ igielake̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st, na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ a̠ga̠i ima̠ra̠ ologi d̠i̠yar,
1TI 6:4 bha̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ agaga na̠ abu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu, sa̠ ologhom d̠o̠ bebina̠ abar. I̠na a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ i̠karabh ebhiroma̠ o̠ku̠anan kabar kabar ola̠ ufugh usoroni. Sa̠ obha̠ na̠ a̠mutiom a̠gbokia̠n, na̠ elobhiri, na̠ a̠fugh i̠te̠i̠, na̠ igurumia̠n ologi,
1TI 6:5 na̠ iwia̠n d̠a̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ i̠karabh rologi ya̠ na̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠. Awa ibhin ma̠a̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠a̠ eten o̠wo̠l ogbo e̠li̠la.
1TI 6:6 Ya̠a̠, ado̠l igielake̠ na̠ orugh agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠ni̠ ate̠i̠ ta̠ elegha̠n o̠ni̠, na̠ ebhin ibom asu̠o̠ na̠ eruom o̠ni̠.
1TI 6:7 Abar ola̠ i̠yar ubhin uru d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon bo̠, sa̠ bebina̠ abar ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ orue obhin o̠d̠u̠a bo̠.
1TI 6:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ku̠gba ma̠ i̠yar o̠te̠i̠ ed̠ia̠n od̠e na̠ ibura̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an ma̠ i̠se̠n, bha̠ i̠nye̠n elegha̠n i̠yar.
1TI 6:9 Ya̠a̠, a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ e̠bho̠ro̠gh ogbo e̠li̠la na̠ emel na̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ ad̠agi̠an, na̠ akpati̠an, na̠ a̠d̠izo i̠karabh i̠walama ibhobho i̠kpo̠ ya̠ a̠d̠ugh, ya̠ ta̠ orobh awa od̠ighom d̠a̠ egbika̠ okunugi awa.
1TI 6:10 Ezin bho̠ otula̠n okpoki na̠ a̠mutiom eb̠la̠ i̠karabh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar. Idi ogbo d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ na̠ ewia̠n o̠te̠i̠ bho̠, na̠ ebhe d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ ibom i̠ku̠nu̠.
1TI 6:11 Ya̠a̠, anwa A̠timoti o̠ni̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ghele ma̠ o̠kpo̠ i̠ye̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, wia̠ne ma̠ a̠rugh ado̠l igielake̠, na̠ a̠ghud̠um oghila̠n A̠zib̠a̠, na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠, na̠ etula̠n, na̠ a̠ma̠ne, na̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu.
1TI 6:12 Wia̠ne ma̠ ibom d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ma̠ ate̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhelegi nyam ra̠ a̠d̠ighom bho̠, wa̠ anwa i̠gba imutuma̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh a̠d̠izo ogbo ma̠ anwa ta̠ atu̠o̠no̠m bho̠.
1TI 6:13 Ami̠ na̠ a̠ruom anwa d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar, na̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st wa̠ amara d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Apo̠nti̠o̠s Apai̠let agba ma̠ iya̠gia̠ga̠i a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
1TI 6:14 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠nagha o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ oloko bho̠ b̠o̠ka̠ u̠pi̠e̠ nyam, o̠li̠o̠m d̠o̠ nyam, tu̠tu̠n Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru,
1TI 6:15 d̠a̠ a̠ga̠i obhel wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ itutumeni bho̠, wa̠ i̠na ku̠ku̠m aro̠ ma̠ Wirileghom bho̠, na̠ O̠li̠le̠ma ta̠ Aru̠li̠le̠ma bho̠, na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ bho̠, ta̠ ato̠ bho̠.
1TI 6:16 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, i̠na ku̠ku̠m ola̠ ko omugh d̠o̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ esi e̠b̠alab̠al ola̠ o̠ni̠ ko orue d̠o̠ a̠tua̠n. O̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠d̠ia̠ abi̠gh i̠na bo̠, sa̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠rue abi̠gh i̠na bo̠ nyen. Edim na̠ a̠limon ya̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton na̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠, e̠ro̠ enigha̠ i̠na. Aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
1TI 6:17 Ghaghana ma̠ ogbo ya̠ igbo ma̠ e̠li̠la d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar e̠mara̠nwunom onon bho̠ ma̠a̠, awa o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu bo̠d̠o̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠li̠la ya̠ na̠ ekpokolo eb̠em ologi. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ eb̠em ologi d̠awa aro̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ onyen ologi na̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar e̠nu̠m bho̠.
1TI 6:18 Ggba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ egir ib̠eb̠i, egbo ma̠ ibome e̠li̠la d̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i od̠ighi i̠di̠ar, enwuna̠ ma̠ onyen ologi, e̠ne̠ghe̠ na̠ onyen ologi.
1TI 6:19 Ka̠ awa igir o̠ku̠a bha̠ awa na̠ ekpol e̠li̠la iya̠ awa, ya̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠de̠o̠ma d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠, b̠o̠ka̠ awa e̠te̠i̠ a̠ga̠i a̠ghud̠um bho̠.
1TI 6:20 O A̠timoti, mare̠ ma̠ a̠sibh abar wa̠ ub̠eton u̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom bho̠. Ko o̠nagha ma̠ ibhelebhel a̠fugh, bo̠d̠o̠, i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an na̠ aku̠anan ya̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi ya̠ idi ogbo na̠ ekue na̠ ebhelegi ma̠ “eloghomabar.”
1TI 6:21 Idi ogbo na̠ ebhin e̠re̠ma ma̠ ola̠ na̠ emel e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠. E̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin.
2TI 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l o̠ni̠ogir ta̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st d̠a̠ i̠to̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, wa̠ uruom o̠gba a̠ghud̠um ogua̠n wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s o̠sasaragi̠ bho̠,
2TI 1:2 na̠ age̠ na̠ a̠ruom anwa A̠timoti o̠nyi̠ ed̠igh ologi d̠ami̠. E̠ne̠ghe̠, igbirigbir, na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar e̠ro̠ na̠ anwa.
2TI 1:3 Ami̠ na̠ ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin e̠b̠ab̠ala eloghoma̠n na̠ ako̠l bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ d̠ami̠ igir bho̠. Ami̠ na̠ ka̠ ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ kigiel kigiel ami̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an igboloma̠ ma̠ anwa d̠a̠ ra̠siseiny d̠ami̠ ma̠ a̠d̠uga̠la̠n na̠ etita̠n.
2TI 1:4 Ami̠ na̠ aru̠ru̠an agu̠o̠ anwa ibhin ileghe bho̠ sa̠ na̠ ebhir ami̠ ma̠ o̠bi̠gh oyom, b̠o̠ka̠ ologi d̠ami̠ a̠muzo na̠ ibo ma̠ igiel i̠yar ta̠ ozua̠n.
2TI 1:5 Ami̠ na̠ aru̠ru̠an na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ igielake̠ onweni a̠ko d̠oyom A̠luwis na̠ onweni d̠oyom A̠yunasi̠, sa̠ ami̠ i̠mar ima̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ od̠i nyen d̠a̠ ozu d̠oyom.
2TI 1:6 Obha̠ ezin bho̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠nimeta̠n anwa ma̠ o̠so̠so̠me̠ni̠ enigha̠ wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠b̠eton a̠nigha̠ nyam igiel bho̠ ami̠ i̠gbamagi̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ ozu d̠oyom bho̠.
2TI 1:7 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ onigha̠ d̠o̠ i̠yar e̠mu̠gh a̠rugugu na̠ alu̠ku̠ a̠d̠ien, ya̠a̠, ola̠ a̠limon, na̠ etula̠n, na̠ osibhom ozu.
2TI 1:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ko oghil ari̠ghe̠l ma̠ o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ d̠i̠yar onigha̠ ipa̠n ogbo. Ko odin nyen ma̠a̠ u̠du̠o̠m ami̠ ma̠ ikoli ma̠ ebula̠ o̠yo̠, ma̠ a̠ghil ari̠ghe̠l osen ami̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ bhine ma̠ a̠limon ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam bho̠ ma̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ ami̠ ma̠ a̠gbika̠ ma̠ ebula̠ Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠.
2TI 1:9 A̠zib̠a̠ a̠tenemeni i̠yar sa̠ aso̠n i̠yar ma̠ orugh a̠ghud̠um e̠b̠ab̠ala. Abar ola̠ i̠yar ugir ola̠ akpe̠ i̠yar o̠te̠i̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ i̠nye̠n bo̠, ya̠a̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ okpon igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠. Kisa̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, i̠na ato̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st o̠te̠i̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
2TI 1:10 I̠se̠n bha̠ ubhin eruoma̠ ta̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s oleriom i̠yar e̠ne̠ghe̠ bho̠. I̠na ane̠gi̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ omugh, ma̠ i̠yar o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ya̠ i̠na a̠bhin a̠ruom i̠yar bho̠ o̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um, na̠ ozu ola̠ ko omugh mu.
2TI 1:11 Sa̠ u̠so̠n ami̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ agba ma̠ asu̠gbagba bho̠ asasaragi̠, na̠ o̠ni̠ogir, na̠ o̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠.
2TI 1:12 Obha̠ ezin bho̠ ami̠ na̠ abi̠gh nyen ali̠gam a̠ruzu i̠nye̠n bho̠. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ami̠ id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l, ezin bho̠ ami̠ a̠loghom i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ ami̠ id̠umom bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue a̠kponom abar ola̠ ub̠eton u̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ tu̠tu̠n ta̠ ate̠i̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.
2TI 1:13 Sibhe ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa i̠mu̠gho̠n d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ d̠ami̠ bho̠ ma̠ akparame̠ni̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ya̠ a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠. Bhine d̠a̠ ima̠ra̠ ologi na̠ etula̠n ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s ma̠ a̠gir.
2TI 1:14 Mare̠ ma̠ a̠kponom ob̠eb̠i abar wa̠ ub̠eton u̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom bho̠ d̠a̠ a̠limon ta̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠rugh d̠a̠ rologi d̠a̠ i̠yar bho̠.
2TI 1:15 Anwa a̠loghom ma̠a̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠ d̠a̠ ebhugh Esia̠ na̠ eghel ami̠, sa̠ A̠figelus na̠ Ahe̠mo̠ze̠ne̠s eka̠ id̠igh ani̠.
2TI 1:16 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠kpon igbirigbir Onisiforus na̠ eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa iguri gha̠n i̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠ami̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa odin d̠o̠ ma̠a̠ ami̠ od̠i d̠a̠ ikoli be̠le̠ni̠ eghil ari̠ghe̠l.
2TI 1:17 Igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠ru d̠a̠ A̠rom bho̠, i̠na abho̠ro̠ghan ami̠ kesi kesi tu̠tu̠n i̠na abi̠gh ami̠.
2TI 1:18 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠kpon Onisiforus igbirigbir d̠a̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ obha̠. Anwa a̠loghom e̠mi̠ agu̠o̠ Onisiforus a̠bhin alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠izo re̠kal d̠a̠ E̠fi̠so̠s.
2TI 2:1 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, anwa o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠, kpo̠ ma̠ a̠luzu d̠a̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s bho̠.
2TI 2:2 Bhine ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa i̠mu̠gho̠n ya̠ ami̠ i̠gba d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠d̠izo a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ipa̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ obhin ob̠em ologi ma̠a̠ awa ta̠ erue ani̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ipa̠n a̠nwunom.
2TI 2:3 D̠ighe na̠ ami̠ ma̠ a̠gbika̠ ma̠ egbika̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ob̠eb̠i o̠ni̠e̠gham ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s.
2TI 2:4 O̠ni̠e̠gham na̠ o̠ko̠mo̠gi̠an gha̠n d̠o̠ na̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo-e̠gham, ka̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a bha̠ ko od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠-e̠gham bho̠ ma̠ ologi.
2TI 2:5 Odi abar eka̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠pigia̠n eghil, ko orue d̠o̠ ane̠gi̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ola̠ ta̠ ozuom i̠na ma̠ eghoi, a̠ten ka̠ i̠na atu̠o̠no̠m i̠to̠to̠gi̠ a̠pigia̠n bho̠.
2TI 2:6 Sa̠ od̠i ma̠ ola̠, od̠ighi ma̠ ari̠si̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠wia̠n na̠ a̠gir ogir ibom bho̠, akpe̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠ a̠d̠e ma̠ ed̠ia̠n bho̠.
2TI 2:7 Ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam bho̠. Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam o̠mu̠gho̠nyan eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n.
2TI 2:8 Guri d̠a̠ ologi d̠oyom ma̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st wa̠ ub̠eton d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ ma̠ odi o̠nyi̠ i̠sabh ikpele ta̠ O̠li̠le̠ma A̠devidi. Onon Ob̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba wa̠ ami̠ na̠ agba na̠ asasaragi̠ bho̠.
2TI 2:9 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ ami̠ na̠ abi̠gh ali̠gam ozu na̠ ate̠i̠ esi ola̠ na̠ o̠du̠gi̠ ami̠ ma̠ rikoli ma̠ agu̠o̠ od̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh. Ya̠a̠, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ abar ola̠ ta̠ orue o̠du̠o̠m ikoli d̠o̠.
2TI 2:10 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, ami̠ na̠ a̠ne kabar kabar, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ aso̠n bho̠ e̠te̠i̠ itenemeni d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s na̠ isosorogia̠n ya̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠.
2TI 2:11 Onon o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ola̠ a̠lei abar ola̠ u̠gba ma̠a̠, “Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠yar od̠igh na̠ i̠na omugh, i̠yar ta̠ orugha̠n i̠na nyen.
2TI 2:12 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠yar one ma̠ a̠ma̠ne, bha̠ i̠yar ta̠ od̠igh na̠ i̠na orileghom irileghom d̠o̠yo̠, Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠yar o̠ku̠a i̠na, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ aku̠a i̠yar nyen.
2TI 2:13 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠yar usibh d̠o̠ ma̠ ogua̠n, i̠na od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ a̠sibh ogua̠n, ezin bho̠ i̠na ko orue d̠o̠ aku̠a ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠.”
2TI 2:14 Nimeta̠ne ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, ma̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ akparame̠ni̠ ma̠ agba ma̠ a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠a̠, awa e̠we̠le̠man aku̠anan ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ ikpo a̠fugh. Aku̠anan i̠ye̠ id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ asu̠o̠ enigha̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nagha bho̠.
2TI 2:15 Wia̠ne ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ ada ma̠ anwa a̠bhin agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ogir ola̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ezin ola̠ odin oghil ari̠ghe̠l, ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin ya̠ igielake̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠.
2TI 2:16 Ya̠a̠, ghele ma̠ a̠fugh i̠te̠i̠ na̠ i̠b̠e̠re̠gi̠an ya̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi, ezin bho̠ i̠ye̠ na̠ eb̠uimeni ma̠ i̠karabh d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠, sa̠ na̠ esigimeni ma̠ o̠ni̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
2TI 2:17 Ta̠ obhin o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠awa i̠ye̠ o̠tu̠o̠m e̠ke̠te̠ ola̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠o̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠d̠e na̠ are̠gh d̠a̠ ozu o̠ni̠. Ahi̠me̠ni̠o̠s na̠ A̠filetos na̠ erugh ado̠l i̠ye̠.
2TI 2:18 Awa na̠ emel e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠ga̠i eten bho̠, sa̠ na̠ e̠gba ma̠a̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠ na̠ a̠mite a̠ten, obha̠ sa̠ na̠ api̠e̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ a̠d̠izo ogbo.
2TI 2:19 Ya̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ ade̠ ma̠ o̠kparakpar o̠de̠o̠ma ola̠ ka̠ orue d̠o̠ onu o̠si̠ghe̠, sa̠ u̠ge̠ d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠ a̠loghom ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ o̠yo̠ bho̠.” O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, “Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠sen a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ghel i̠karabh.”
2TI 2:20 D̠a̠ otu ola̠ abu̠gh, a̠d̠ien kere kere i̠di̠ar a̠ma̠rugh otu od̠i, idi ubhin a̠silva̠ o̠le̠m, idi a̠gol, ipa̠n sa̠ ubhin iriren bo̠d̠o̠ i̠do̠gho̠l u̠le̠m. Idi ed̠igh edim, ya̠a̠ idi id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ edim.
2TI 2:21 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni, o̠ni̠ ola̠ ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ma̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh i̠ye̠ bha̠ oten abar edim, ola̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠doni a̠bhin a̠gir a̠d̠ien kere kere ib̠eb̠i ogir.
2TI 2:22 Kpo ma̠ eghil ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ i̠karabh ebhiroma̠ ya̠ na̠ e̠nyagh ikubh a̠nwunom. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ bha̠ra̠nome ma̠ a̠ghud̠um igielake̠, ologi ima̠ra̠, etula̠n na̠ ekima̠, ma̠ a̠bhin a̠rilogha̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ ebhin a̠ga̠i ologi na̠ esen Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠.
2TI 2:23 Si̠ghe̠ ma̠ ozu d̠oyom d̠a̠ raku̠anan ema̠ na̠ iya̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi, ezin bho̠ i̠ye̠ na̠ ekunugiom d̠a̠ o̠b̠e̠m.
2TI 2:24 Ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠b̠u̠man o̠b̠e̠m. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, a̠bhin d̠a̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu na̠ d̠a̠ od̠ighi ib̠eb̠i na̠ e̠mar atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, a̠ne ma̠ a̠nwunom i̠kpalagi̠an.
2TI 2:25 Bhine d̠a̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠damaghan anwa bho̠. Ka̠din A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ a̠rileghom awa ma̠ o̠wo̠l i̠se̠ otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh na̠ o̠mar ologhom eb̠la̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
2TI 2:26 Sa̠ awa ta̠ eloghoma̠n a̠ruzu e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠te̠ akpati̠ ta̠ Eru bho̠, wa̠ akpu̠o̠m awa a̠guri d̠a̠ ekpukpu i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
2TI 3:1 Loghome ma̠a̠ e̠kparama ado̠l ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠.
2TI 3:2 Ezin bho̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ etula̠n a̠ruzu d̠awa na̠ otula̠n ikpoki, ebhubhugha̠, e̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu, efugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠, sa̠ ko o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ onweni na̠ o̠we̠de̠, ko o̠se̠bh d̠o̠ ma̠ ali̠se̠bh, sa̠ ko orugh d̠o̠ ma̠ ado̠l igielake̠.
2TI 3:3 A̠nwunom ta̠ erugh ado̠l ya̠ igbiriri ozu o̠to̠, sa̠ okpon o̠si̠ghe̠ a̠d̠ien ko̠ o̠ro̠ mu̠, ta̠ efugh i̠basi̠, ko osibhom d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ruzu, ta̠ e̠pi̠e̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠pi̠e̠gi̠, sa̠ ta̠ e̠su̠a kabar kabar ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i.
2TI 3:4 Awa ta̠ ewol iwola̠, e̠basi̠ ma̠ i̠basi̠, erugh ado̠l o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ a̠ruzu, etula̠n e̠me̠me̠m e̠mara̠nwunom, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ otula̠n A̠zib̠a̠.
2TI 3:5 Awa ta̠ ekue egir agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ na̠ erugh iya̠ igielake̠, ya̠a̠, na̠ eghel a̠ga̠i a̠limon bho̠. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, sigima̠ ma̠ ozu d̠oyom d̠a̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ o̠ku̠a.
2TI 3:6 Idi awa na̠ e̠b̠o̠i̠ny na̠ ed̠ikighu d̠a̠ a̠rutu a̠nwunom na̠ eponoma̠ ma̠ anwani̠ idudugha̠n ologi ya̠ i̠karabh na̠ e̠ne̠mu̠o̠m bho̠, sa̠ na̠ erileghom awa na̠ ed̠ighom d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ebhiroma̠ i̠karabh.
2TI 3:7 Anwani̠ i̠ye̠ bha̠, eb̠la̠ igiel od̠i d̠a̠ atu̠ghan, ya̠a̠ irue d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
2TI 3:8 A̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ Azane̠s na̠ Azambre̠s i̠damaghan A̠mozizi bho̠, obha̠ agu̠o̠ a̠nwunom i̠nye̠n eka̠ na̠ e̠damaghan a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠. Awa a̠nwunom ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ i̠karabh i̠walama na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ igunugha̠.
2TI 3:9 Ya̠a̠, awa ko obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ esusula̠ d̠awa e̠gi̠ ma̠ egbeiny, ezin bho̠ ko obia̠ d̠o̠ sa̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠loghom a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠ a̠gboloma̠ awa, ma̠ agu̠o̠ imutuma̠ ma̠ Azane̠s na̠ Azambre̠s bho̠.
2TI 3:10 Ya̠a̠, anwa na̠ amar amu̠gho̠nyan atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠ami̠, na̠ a̠ma̠rugh d̠ami̠, na̠ ezin a̠ghud̠um d̠ami̠, na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠ami̠, na̠ a̠ma̠ne d̠ami̠, na̠ etula̠n d̠ami̠, na̠ i̠kparagi̠o̠m d̠ami̠.
2TI 3:11 Anwa a̠loghom a̠ponoma̠ egbika̠ ya̠ i̠te̠i̠ ami̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ali̠gam a̠ruzu ya̠ i̠te̠i̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ Anti̠o̠k, na̠ Ikoni̠o̠m, na̠ A̠listara̠ bho̠. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, ami̠ ane̠, sa̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ a̠tenemeni ami̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ ali̠gam a̠ruzu i̠ye̠.
2TI 3:12 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i, o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ ebhir obhin eb̠la̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ orugh a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s ta̠ abi̠gh a̠ponoma̠ egbika̠.
2TI 3:13 Sa̠ ta̠ a̠mite ma̠ ola̠ i̠karabh a̠nwunom, na̠ ogbo igelemeni ta̠ egurom epeleni, sa̠ ta̠ egelemeni ma̠ a̠nwunom, sa̠ ta̠ ogelemeni awa nyen.
2TI 3:14 Ya̠a̠ anwa, rughe ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar ya̠ anwa i̠tu̠ghan sa̠ anwa i̠mar ima̠ra̠ bho̠ d̠a̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ nyam bho̠.
2TI 3:15 Loghome ma̠a̠, anwa iloghom O̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ka̠ d̠a̠ i̠gbara d̠oyom, ya̠ inigha̠ nyam eloghomabar ya̠ na̠ ebhin itenemeni na̠ eru d̠a̠ o̠wo̠l oten ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠a̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s.
2TI 3:16 A̠zib̠a̠ a̠b̠ugh a̠mutiom eb̠la̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, sa̠ a̠bhon ola̠ obhin o̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, na̠ a̠kikiom, na̠ oselegi i̠di̠ar ya̠ obhon d̠o̠, na̠ atu̠ghan od̠igh e̠mu̠ d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um igielake̠,
2TI 3:17 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ta̠ amar a̠kokod̠ia̠n ogir eb̠la̠ ib̠eb̠i ogir.
2TI 4:1 Ami̠ na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ agba na̠ a̠nigha̠ nyam d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s wa̠ ta̠ a̠sobh ase̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um na̠ imumugh bho̠, na̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠mula̠ a̠ru ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠li̠le̠ma d̠a̠ irileghom d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠:
2TI 4:2 Gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ obhel. Bhine d̠a̠ a̠ma̠ne na̠ a̠kikiom ma̠ a̠rubhugiom, na̠ o̠nyagh ra̠to, o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ rologi a̠nwunom.
2TI 4:3 Obhel na̠ a̠ru ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ko o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ awa ta̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠karabh rebhiroma̠ ologi d̠awa, sa̠ ta̠ eko ma̠ a̠ruzu d̠awa ekitineni na̠ ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ ta̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ awa ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ na̠ ebhir awa ma̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n.
2TI 4:4 Sa̠ awa ta̠ etiba̠ra̠ e̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ a̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠ sa̠ ta̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m asu̠gbagba id̠ud̠ul ya̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ esi.
2TI 4:5 Ya̠a̠ anwa, kimeni ma̠ ozu d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar, ma̠ a̠ne ma̠ egbika̠, ma̠ aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ o̠d̠u̠a esi oten esi, ma̠ a̠gir ogir wa̠ ubhelegi nyam ogir bho̠ ma̠ a̠muzoghod̠iom.
2TI 4:6 I̠se̠n bha̠ na̠ ozu ma̠ asi̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠min i̠ko̠l, sa̠ obhel wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠b̠etina̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom onon bho̠ na̠ a̠tua̠n.
2TI 4:7 Ami̠ na̠ a̠we ma̠ ob̠eb̠i elobhiri, ami̠ na̠ amar a̠ghil eghil bho̠ ka̠ kunugiom, ami̠ na̠ a̠sibhom ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠ ka̠ a̠kunugiom.
2TI 4:8 O̠ku̠a bha̠ i̠se̠n na̠ oguri ma̠ eghoi ane̠gi̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ osisa̠n ami̠, wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ amu̠kpe̠ ola̠ ta̠ oleriom d̠a̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osobh Ase̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, ami̠ a̠rugh iya̠ igielake̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠, osobhmase̠ igielake̠ bho̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, amu̠kpe̠ bho̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ enigha̠ ami̠ ku̠ku̠m, ya̠a̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ enigha̠ ani̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ itula̠n eruoma̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.
2TI 4:9 Wia̠ne ma̠ anu̠r a̠ru d̠ami̠ ma̠ obhel ola̠ ko obia̠ d̠o̠,
2TI 4:10 ezin bho̠ Ade̠mas na̠ a̠ba̠ra̠ ma̠ e̠mara̠nwunom amu̠m onon, sa̠ na̠ awe̠le̠man ami̠ a̠ten agi̠ d̠a̠ Ate̠saloni̠ka, A̠krise̠ns na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Agalesia̠, ya̠a̠ Atai̠to̠s na̠ agi̠ d̠a̠ Adalmatia̠.
2TI 4:11 A̠luk ku̠ku̠m od̠i na̠ ami̠. Te̠ye̠ ma̠ Amaki̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ anwa a̠ru, ezin bho̠ i̠na ta̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ ogir d̠ami̠.
2TI 4:12 Ami̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠dila̠de a̠limon d̠ami̠ a̠ruom Ata̠i̠siku̠s oten o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ E̠fi̠so̠s.
2TI 4:13 Igiel anwa na̠ a̠ru, bhine ma̠ akapa anyu̠ d̠ami̠ wa̠ od̠i na̠ Akarpu̠s d̠a̠ A̠troa̠s bho̠. B̠arame̠ na̠ ra̠d̠ire bho̠, okunukun iya̠ ozu i̠nam bho̠.
2TI 4:14 Ale̠kzanda o̠le̠ma i̠d̠i̠ar a̠rukurogh bho̠ a̠gir i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠izo re̠kal. Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ akpe̠ i̠na ma̠ ogir ya̠ i̠na a̠gir bho̠.
2TI 4:15 Anwa eka̠ kpona̠ ma̠ a̠sigima̠ i̠na, ezin bho̠ i̠na adamaghan i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠i̠yar ibom.
2TI 4:16 O̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ agba d̠ami̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠pu̠r igiel wa̠ ami̠ i̠gba ma̠ o̠nu̠ d̠a̠ iku wa̠ uler ami̠ bho̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ighel ami̠, ya̠a̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠siseiny ma̠a̠ o̠wal d̠o̠ o̠lo̠gh d̠a̠ i̠karabh d̠awa.
2TI 4:17 Ya̠a̠, Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ aro̠ na̠ ami̠ sa̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ akparame̠ni̠ ami̠, ma̠ o̠gba Ib̠eb̠i Asu̠gbagba bho̠ omuzoghod̠iom onigha̠ eb̠la̠ Ibhebhia̠n bho̠. Sa̠ a̠tenemeni ami̠ d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ odughunub̠agu̠ bho̠.
2TI 4:18 Ya̠ga̠i, Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni ami̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠karabh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar, a̠guri ami̠ ma̠ ola̠ eko ka̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ irileghom ote̠nai̠ny d̠o̠yo̠. Itutumeni e̠ro̠ enigha̠ i̠na ad̠u̠a ma̠ amu̠m a̠ten amu̠m. Aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a.
2TI 4:19 Pura̠ne ma̠ A̠priska na̠ A̠kwila̠, na̠ eghun otu ta̠ Onisiforus.
2TI 4:20 E̠rasto̠s aro̠ d̠a̠ Ako̠ri̠nt, ya̠a̠ ami̠ i̠we̠le̠man A̠trofimo̠s d̠a̠ A̠militus ezin bho̠ ozu d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ obhon d̠o̠.
2TI 4:21 Wia̠ne ma̠ anu̠r a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ ami̠ kisa̠ ta̠ ate̠i̠ obhel eb̠okum bho̠. A̠yubulus, na̠ Apu̠de̠ns, na̠ Alai̠no̠s, na̠ A̠kilodia̠, na̠ eb̠la̠ a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ bho̠ epura̠n anwa nyen.
2TI 4:22 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ aro̠ na̠ e̠mu̠gh d̠oyom. E̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ e̠ro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin.
TIT 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, o̠ni̠ogir ta̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st na̠ age̠ ma̠ a̠lebh onon na̠ a̠ruom anwa. Na̠ oruom ami̠ ma̠ o̠kpo̠me̠ni̠ rologi ima̠ra̠ ta̠ ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ aso̠n bho̠, ma̠ od̠ighi agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ e̠mar e̠mu̠gho̠nyan a̠ga̠i a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ ta̠ etutumeni ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
TIT 1:2 Ta̠ awo̠l i̠se̠ sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ eb̠em ologi a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ igunugha̠ bho̠, a̠gua̠n kisa̠ e̠mara̠nwunom a̠mite bho̠.
TIT 1:3 D̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar a̠muzoghod̠iom a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ uloghom o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ i̠na ato̠ a̠guri bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton ogir bho̠ alo̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ o̠gba omutiom, d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ i̠na a̠ruom ami̠ bho̠.
TIT 1:4 Ami̠ Apo̠l na̠ age̠ na̠ a̠ruom anwa Atai̠to̠s, a̠ga̠i o̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ onin ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠. E̠no̠gho̠man na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ bho̠ na̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st Witenemeni d̠i̠yar e̠ro̠ na̠ anwa.
TIT 1:5 Ami̠ i̠we̠le̠man anwa d̠a̠ ekpe A̠kriti ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ anwa ta̠ a̠selegi ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ ogir bho̠ omunieni, na̠ o̠so̠n ikei omutiom ke̠ma ke̠ma ma̠ agu̠o̠ ami̠ i̠to̠ inigha̠ nyam bho̠.
TIT 1:6 Okei aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ abar o̠li̠o̠m o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, owolom ta̠ onin ani̠ ku̠ku̠m, anwi̠i̠ny d̠o̠yo̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st na̠ iya̠ ta̠ obhin ob̠em ologi, iya̠ i̠karabh ya̠ ob̠ologiom o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠, iya̠ orugh d̠o̠ ma̠ ado̠l i̠te̠i̠, bo̠d̠o̠ o̠b̠agh d̠o̠ ma̠ e̠mu̠.
TIT 1:7 Agu̠o̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠rileghom aso̠si̠ na̠ a̠kponom otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, i̠na na̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ onwuna̠ e̠kal abar ola̠ o̠li̠o̠m, ya̠a̠ aro̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ob̠a̠ra̠motu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. I̠na ko o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ozu, ko o̠nu̠r d̠o̠ agam i̠gam, o̠d̠a ma̠ a̠min d̠o̠, o̠ni̠ a̠ponoma̠ d̠o̠. I̠na ko ogba̠gba̠ra̠gha̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo e̠li̠la ma̠ awai̠.
TIT 1:8 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, i̠na aro̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ a̠bhin onyen ologi na̠ a̠d̠ighom isuloma̠, sa̠ a̠ba̠ra̠ ma̠ a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠sibhom ozu, o̠ni̠ igielake̠, o̠ni̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala, sa̠ na̠ a̠gir iya̠ i̠kpe̠ d̠a̠ obhel wa̠ a̠sora̠n bho̠.
TIT 1:9 I̠na na̠ a̠sibh a̠ga̠i o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ u̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠na bho̠ akparame̠ni̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠rue a̠bhin a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ bho̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi ipa̠n ogbo, na̠ oselegi amu̠gho̠nyan ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠damaghan bho̠.
TIT 1:10 Ezin bho̠, a̠d̠izo awa na̠ e̠pagi̠raghan, sa̠ na̠ efugh iya̠ i̠te̠i̠ na̠ egelemeni ma̠ igelemeni, okunukun d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io awa ogbo ya̠ na̠ etia̠ ma̠ ipo bho̠.
TIT 1:11 Ya̠a̠, akpe̠ ma̠ okpegi aru̠nu̠ d̠awa, ezin bho̠ awa na̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ osora̠n d̠o̠, sa̠ na̠ e̠pi̠e̠gi̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ eghun a̠rutu, ma̠ ebula̠ ikpoki.
TIT 1:12 Odi owil ola̠ A̠kriti na̠ agu̠o̠ eka̠ agba ma̠a̠, “A̠nwunom A̠kriti na̠ e̠gba ma̠ igunugha̠ kigiel kigiel, ibom id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh ya̠ na̠ e̠basi̠o̠m a̠nwunom, na̠ i̠gbu̠o̠ro̠gbu̠o̠r i̠d̠o̠gho̠d̠o̠gh.”
TIT 1:13 Asu̠gbagba bho̠ ya̠gia̠ga̠i. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, game̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ awa ma̠ ibom bo̠ka̠ rologi ima̠ra̠ d̠awa e̠ghu̠a.
TIT 1:14 Ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ko o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh id̠ud̠ul na̠ asi̠b̠o̠m Ogbo A̠zu bho̠, na̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ eghel ya̠gia̠ga̠i bho̠.
TIT 1:15 Kabar kabar ab̠ab̠ala d̠awa ogbo ya̠ i̠b̠ab̠ala bho̠; ya̠a̠, d̠awa ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠pi̠o̠gho̠m sa̠ od̠umom d̠o̠ bho̠, abar e̠b̠ab̠ala ola̠ od̠i na̠ awa bo̠, ya̠a̠, rologi d̠awa na̠ egbiriri a̠ruzu d̠awa na̠ e̠pi̠an.
TIT 1:16 Awa na̠ e̠re̠ma ma̠a̠ awa eloghom A̠zib̠a̠, ya̠a̠ rod̠ighi i̠di̠ar d̠awa na̠ eghel i̠na. Eghenegia̠n awa, i̠b̠agh ma̠ aru̠mu̠ ya̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠, ya̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir bebina̠ abar ola̠ aro̠ ma̠ ob̠eb̠i.
TIT 2:1 Ya̠a̠ anwa, tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ isora̠n o̠ro̠ a̠ga̠i atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
TIT 2:2 Kikiome ma̠ ikei ilobhiri a̠nwunom bho̠ ma̠ awa ekimeni ma̠ a̠ruzu, ed̠igh edim, esibhom a̠ruzu, e̠ghu̠a d̠a̠ ima̠ra̠ ologi, enwuna̠ ma̠ etula̠n, na̠ a̠ma̠ne.
TIT 2:3 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, kikiome ma̠ iguda̠ anwani̠ bho̠ ma̠ orugh ado̠l d̠awa o̠gu̠b̠e̠ni̠ a̠ma̠rugh anwani̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala. Awa o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo isorogiom, bo̠d̠o̠ re̠bana ta̠ a̠min, ya̠a̠, awa e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i i̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠.
TIT 2:4 Sa̠ awa ta̠ ebhin i̠se̠ e̠tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ikubh anwani̠ bho̠ ma̠ otula̠n a̠riwolom na̠ anwi̠i̠ny d̠awa,
TIT 2:5 na̠ osibhom a̠ruzu d̠awa, na̠ orugh ado̠l e̠b̠ab̠ala, na̠ ogir ogir d̠a̠ a̠rutu d̠awa, na̠ ogir ib̠eb̠i, na̠ ozuruna̠ eghoi onigha̠ a̠riwolom d̠awa, b̠o̠ka̠ o̠ni̠ na̠ ofugh a̠fugh i̠basi̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
TIT 2:6 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, kpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi anwi̠i̠ny oyel bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ta̠ esibhom a̠ruzu d̠awa d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar.
TIT 2:7 A̠ma̠rugh d̠oyom ebhon d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ e̠bi̠gh e̠ta. Bhine d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um igielake̠ na̠ edim, ma̠ a̠leriom ma̠ agu̠o̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ d̠oyom a̠lei abar ate̠i̠.
TIT 2:8 Ro̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠oyom ebhon e̠ro̠ ma̠ iya̠ ko orue d̠o̠ o̠bi̠gh o̠pi̠e̠, b̠o̠ka̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠damaghan bho̠ ed̠igh ari̠ghe̠l, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ awa ko o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠karabh ola̠ ofugh ogboloma̠ i̠yar.
TIT 2:9 Re̠bana bho̠ ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ awa bho̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar iya̠ isora̠n. Awa o̠kpalatu̠an d̠o̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ inwuna̠ awa bho̠,
TIT 2:10 bo̠d̠o̠ oniniom d̠o̠ awa. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, awa erugh a̠ghud̠um igielake̠ iya̠ ta̠ obhin awa ob̠em ologi, b̠o̠ka̠ eb̠la̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar bho̠ ed̠igh e̠b̠e̠l enigha̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar.
TIT 2:11 Ezin bho̠, A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠leriom e̠ne̠ghe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin itenemeni na̠ a̠ruom eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom bho̠.
TIT 2:12 E̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ na̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ i̠yar ogin a̠ma̠rugh ya̠ ko onigha̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ itutumeni, na̠ i̠karabh e̠ralma e̠mara̠nwunom, ya̠a̠ i̠yar osibhom a̠ruzu d̠i̠yar, orugh a̠ma̠rugh igielake̠ d̠a̠ amu̠m onon.
TIT 2:13 D̠a̠ a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ i̠yar na̠ ogon itutumeni eb̠em ologi bho̠ na̠ eruoma̠ isosorogia̠n ta̠ Obom A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st
TIT 2:14 wa̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ obhin o̠ta i̠yar o̠si̠ghe̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere i̠karabh, na̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ i̠yar oguri a̠nwunom iyo̠yo̠, ya̠ ta̠ ebhir ogir ib̠eb̠i.
TIT 2:15 Tu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n, ma̠ akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠nagha nyam bho̠, ma̠ a̠bhin eb̠la̠ a̠limon d̠oyom ma̠ a̠selegi ma̠ a̠risi ya̠ awa na̠ erima̠. Ko orugh agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠kpon anwa aki̠ri̠me̠ni̠.
TIT 3:1 Nemeta̠ne awa, ma̠ awa ezuruna̠ ma̠ eghoi enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo irileghom na̠ ra̠dila̠de i̠to̠, e̠nagha ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠awa, ema̠ra̠ ma̠ obhin onyen ologi ogir ib̠eb̠i d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal.
TIT 3:2 Awa o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠ni̠ e̠pi̠e̠, o̠b̠u̠man d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠b̠e̠m, ya̠a̠ awa erugh ado̠l ekima̠, na̠ a̠ma̠rugh o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ozu egboloma̠ ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠.
TIT 3:3 Ezin bho̠, d̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten, abar ola̠ i̠yar u̠mu̠gho̠nyan na̠ o̠ri̠la d̠o̠. I̠yar u̠b̠agh aru̠mu̠, sa̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere i̠karabh e̠ralma, na̠ e̠ralma ipulupul ozu na̠ ipesi, na̠ i̠karabh i̠walama, i̠le̠ge̠ i̠yar ka̠ id̠ighom re̠bana, ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar urugh ado̠l igurumia̠n ologi na̠ a̠gbokia̠n, na̠ o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien, sa̠ odi a̠ghir ologi ma̠ odi.
TIT 3:4 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Witenemeni d̠i̠yar a̠leriom i̠yar okpon igbirigbir na̠ etula̠n d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠,
TIT 3:5 sa̠ i̠yar u̠te̠i̠ itenemeni d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠. Na̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠o̠ d̠a̠ ib̠eb̠i ya̠ i̠yar ugir, ya̠a̠ ad̠u̠a ku d̠a̠ igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠ sa̠ i̠na a̠tenemeni i̠yar. I̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠titol i̠karabh d̠i̠yar, sa̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar omom i̠mara, na̠ omom a̠ghud̠um.
TIT 3:6 I̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st Witenemeni d̠i̠yar a̠bhin onyen ologi a̠zuom i̠yar E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠,
TIT 3:7 ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ igbirigbir d̠o̠yo̠, ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar na̠ onwuna̠ ma̠ eb̠em ologi od̠e ad̠i̠a a̠ghud̠um kid̠ud̠ul.
TIT 3:8 Onon a̠ga̠i o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠, sa̠ ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh anwa ma̠ o̠gba o̠kparame̠ni̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ema̠ra̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ta̠ ebhin eb̠la̠ rologi d̠awa egir ib̠eb̠i. I̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n ebhon sa̠ ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ asu̠o̠ inigha̠ ko̠ni̠ ko̠ni̠.
TIT 3:9 Ya̠a̠ anwa, sigima̠ ma̠ raku̠anan obhobho i̠kpo̠, na̠ i̠re̠ma imitia̠n, na̠ o̠b̠e̠m, na̠ aku̠anan ya̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠. Ezin bho̠, i̠ye̠ asu̠o̠ bo̠, sa̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ ogir ema̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠.
TIT 3:10 Kikiome ma̠ o̠go̠me̠ma, ma̠ onin bo̠d̠o̠ i̠wal igiel, ka̠ a̠ten i̠se̠, sigima̠ i̠na.
TIT 3:11 Loghome ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ o̠ku̠a na̠ a̠mel ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠karabh d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ esobh ase̠ ebhumeni i̠na.
TIT 3:12 Igiel ami̠ iruom Ate̠mas bo̠d̠o̠ Atai̠kiku̠s oru d̠oyom, bha̠ nugia̠ne ma̠ a̠ru ra̠ ate̠i̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ A̠nikopolis, ezin bho̠ ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ i̠se̠ ma̠ obhel okogoro bho̠.
TIT 3:13 Wia̠ne ma̠ anu̠r alo̠gh agu̠o̠ ma̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Aze̠nas o̠ni̠ oloko bho̠, na̠ Apo̠lo̠s ma̠ d̠a̠ e̠gi̠ d̠awa, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ abar ko o̠kparama d̠o̠ awa.
TIT 3:14 Akpe̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠i̠yar o̠tu̠ghan agu̠o̠ obhin obhel d̠awa ogir ib̠eb̠i ogir, b̠o̠ka̠ awa e̠te̠i̠ a̠ga̠i i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ awa ma̠ o̠te̠i̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ o̠ro̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ko omum d̠o̠ ma̠ imuma̠.
TIT 3:15 Eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ od̠i na̠ ami̠ ma̠ enen bho̠ epura̠n anwa. Pura̠ne ma̠ eb̠la̠ ra̠tologha̠n ya̠ itula̠n i̠yar bho̠, ya̠ awa na̠ i̠yar unwuna̠ ma̠ onin ologi ima̠ra̠ bho̠. E̠no̠gho̠man ta̠ A̠zib̠a e̠ro̠ na̠ eb̠la̠ inyin.
PHM 1:1 Ami̠ Apo̠l o̠ni̠ ikoli ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s, na̠ A̠timoti umor d̠i̠yar na̠ o̠ge̠ na̠ oruom anwa A̠filimo̠n wa̠ na̠ i̠yar uma̠ra̠ ma̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ i̠yar na̠ a̠gir bho̠,
PHM 1:2 na̠ u̠marani̠ d̠i̠yar Afi̠a, na̠ Aki̠pu̠s wa̠ na̠ i̠yar na̠ owe ma̠ e̠gham bho̠, na̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠igh aso̠si̠ d̠a̠ otu d̠oyom bho̠.
PHM 1:3 E̠ne̠ghe̠ na̠ ekima̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar na̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st e̠ro̠ na̠ inyin.
PHM 1:4 Ami̠ na̠ ase̠bh A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠gboloma̠ nyam kigiel kigiel ola̠ ami̠ i̠ru̠ru̠an anwa d̠a̠ a̠siseiny d̠ami̠,
PHM 1:5 ezin bho̠, ami̠ na̠ amu̠gho̠n agu̠o̠ anwa na̠ a̠tula̠n eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a, na̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ wa̠ anwa inwuna̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ A̠zizo̠s bho̠.
PHM 1:6 A̠siseiny d̠ami̠ bha̠, a̠ghisia̠n wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io d̠i̠yar ogbo-ima̠ra̠ ta̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠mar o̠mu̠gho̠nyan eb̠la̠ e̠no̠gho̠man ya̠ na̠ i̠te̠i̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um, d̠a̠ ebula̠ Akrai̠st bho̠.
PHM 1:7 Umor d̠ami̠, etula̠n d̠oyom na̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ ibom a̠libhon ologi, akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠ami̠. Sa̠ anwa na̠ ame̠me̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
PHM 1:8 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, ami̠ ka̠ ibhin agu̠o̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ umor d̠oyom d̠a̠ Akrai̠st bho̠, akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi akparame̠ni̠ a̠ruom anwa ma̠ ogir i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠kpe̠ nyam ogir bho̠,
PHM 1:9 kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ ami̠ na̠ ale̠gh ale̠gha ma̠ anwa d̠a̠ ebula̠ etula̠n. Ami̠ okei-o̠ni̠ Apo̠l, o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s na̠ amara bho̠, wa̠ udin i̠na u̠lo̠gh ikoli ma̠ i̠se̠n nyen bho̠.
PHM 1:10 Ami̠ na̠ a̠siseiny anwa na̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ Onisimo̠s, wa̠ ra̠ a̠ten o̠nyi̠ ola̠ ami̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ o̠we̠de̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ u̠du̠o̠m ami̠ d̠a̠ ikoli bho̠.
PHM 1:11 Obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten, i̠na na̠ olei d̠o̠ ma̠ abar d̠a̠ a̠misigh d̠oyom, ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n i̠na na̠ a̠ten o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠lei abar d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ i̠wal i̠yar.
PHM 1:12 Ami̠ na̠ a̠mulumeni i̠na wa̠ ed̠igh ologi d̠ami̠ bho̠, na̠ a̠ruom anwa.
PHM 1:13 Nab̠o̠, ebhir ami̠ ma̠ oguri o̠yo̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠bhin esi d̠oyom alo̠gh agu̠o̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n u̠du̠o̠m ami̠ ma̠ ikoli d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠gba ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠.
PHM 1:14 Ya̠a̠, ami̠ i̠bho̠ro̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ oponoma̠ oyom ma̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ onigha̠ ami̠, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ ad̠u̠a d̠a̠ onyen ologi d̠oyom na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠ru.
PHM 1:15 Ka̠din Onisimo̠s abagi̠na nyam ekud̠i obhel b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na a̠mula̠ a̠ru ra̠ a̠d̠igh na̠ anwa aro̠ ma̠ owewegh obhel,
PHM 1:16 i̠se̠n bha̠, agu̠o̠ e̠bana d̠o̠, a̠pel e̠bana. D̠ami̠ bha̠ i̠na umor ed̠igh ologi d̠a̠ Akrai̠st, ya̠a̠, d̠oyom bha̠ i̠na o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠pel o̠ku̠a, ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ na̠ agu̠o̠ umor d̠a̠ Akrai̠st.
PHM 1:17 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠ anwa ibhin ami̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ i̠b̠aragu̠ma d̠oyom, bha̠ d̠a̠ ma̠ Onisimo̠s a̠bhin onin agu̠o̠ anwa ta̠ ada ami̠ a̠bhin bho̠.
PHM 1:18 Ku̠gba ma̠ i̠na a̠gir i̠karabh a̠gboloma̠ nyam, bo̠d̠o̠ a̠d̠igh o̠mu̠gh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠oyom, bha̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ e̠mu̠ d̠ami̠.
PHM 1:19 Ami̠ Apo̠l na̠ agu̠o̠ ibhin agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ age̠ ma̠a̠, ami̠ ta̠ akpe̠ nyam a̠mulumeni. Ami̠ i̠bho̠ro̠gh d̠o̠ ma̠ onemeta̠n oyom ma̠a̠, a̠ghud̠um d̠oyom bha̠ o̠mu̠gh ola̠ anwa id̠igh d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ nyen.
PHM 1:20 Ob̠eb̠i umor ed̠igh ologi d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ onin ima̠ra̠ ologi d̠a̠ Akrai̠st, gire ma̠ abar onon a̠nigha̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ ebula̠ Akrai̠st, ma̠ ame̠me̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi d̠ami̠.
PHM 1:21 Agu̠o̠ ami̠ na̠ age̠ na̠ a̠ruom anwa bho̠, ami̠ ima̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ anwa ta̠ a̠gir abar wa̠ ami̠ na̠ abho̠ro̠gh anwa ma̠ ogir bho̠, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠gir a̠peleni ma̠ o̠ku̠a nyen.
PHM 1:22 O̠b̠aragi̠o̠m i̠se̠, tu̠ghu̠mane̠ ma̠ otu-esul a̠guri ma̠ a̠sisa̠n ami̠, ezin bho̠ ami̠ na̠ a̠b̠em ologi ma̠a̠ ta̠ o̠wo̠ran ra̠siseiny d̠inyin omutiom ami̠ onigha̠ inyin.
PHM 1:23 Epafras wa̠ od̠i na̠ ami̠ d̠a̠ ikoli d̠a̠ ebula̠ Akrai̠st A̠zizo̠s bho̠, agba ma̠a̠ ami̠ ipura̠n anwa.
PHM 1:24 Amaki̠, na̠ Ari̠staku̠s, na̠ Ade̠mas, na̠ A̠luk, ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠igh na̠ ami̠ na̠ egir bho̠ eka̠ epura̠n anwa.
PHM 1:25 E̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ Wa̠nwuna̠ i̠yar A̠zizo̠s Akrai̠st aro̠ na̠ inyin.
HEB 1:1 D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠ten, A̠zib̠a̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ aru̠nu̠ a̠riwil bho̠ agba ma̠ a̠d̠izo i̠di̠ar a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ d̠i̠yar ma̠ a̠d̠izo igiel,
HEB 1:2 ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n d̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ ekunuguma̠ i̠nye̠n, i̠na na̠ a̠bhin O̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ agba ma̠ i̠di̠ar na̠ a̠nigha̠ i̠yar. A̠zib̠a̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ O̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠, wa̠ i̠na a̠b̠eton eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar a̠nigha̠ bho̠, ale̠m eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠a̠ a̠de na̠ e̠nai̠ny.
HEB 1:3 O̠nyi̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠mutioghom e̠b̠alab̠al isosorogia̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠le̠m d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠bhin ibom a̠limon o̠nu̠ o̠kpe̠ d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ a̠sibh eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ od̠i d̠a̠ e̠ma ra̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ a̠guri. Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ i̠yar d̠a̠ i̠karabh bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agi̠ ka̠ aro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon a̠pu bho̠.
HEB 1:4 O̠nyi̠ bho̠ abu̠gh a̠pu ma̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠d̠ien wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠ghol i̠na bho̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu ma̠ ita̠ awa bho̠.
HEB 1:5 D̠a̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, ka̠ oken wa̠ I̠na a̠fugh a̠nigha̠ ma̠a̠: “Anwa O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠; anwa na̠ a̠ten O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠ ma̠ a̠didon.” Bo̠d̠o̠ sa̠ a̠fugh ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ O̠we̠de̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ a̠ten O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠”?
HEB 1:6 Ya̠a̠, igiel bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin o̠kpana o̠nyi̠ d̠o̠yo̠ a̠ru d̠a̠ e̠ma ra̠ a̠nwunom bho̠, sa̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Eb̠la̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ e̠ko̠l i̠na.”
HEB 1:7 I̠na agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “I̠na na̠ a̠tenemeni awa ma̠ itileduom d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ aru̠mu̠gh, sa̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu d̠o̠yo̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ re̠ba anya.”
HEB 1:8 Ya̠a̠, d̠a̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠ sa̠ I̠na agba ma̠a̠, “E A̠zib̠a̠, a̠dila̠de irileghom d̠oyom ta̠ ad̠u̠a ma̠ id̠ud̠ul a̠ten id̠ud̠ul, sa̠ anwa ta̠ a̠rileghom a̠nwunom d̠oyom d̠a̠ igielake̠.
HEB 1:9 Anwa a̠ba̠ra̠ ma̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala sa̠ i̠karabh na̠ eghir anwa ma̠ ologi. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠oyom bho̠, aso̠n anwa a̠doni, a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠libhon ologi ya̠ id̠igh edim ipu ma̠ ita̠ ipa̠n ogbo.”
HEB 1:10 I̠na ab̠aram agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Anwa, Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠, i̠le̠m a̠de bho̠ d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠, sa̠ ro̠b̠u̠ghu̠b̠u̠gh bho̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ ogir a̠limon d̠oyom.
HEB 1:11 Awa ta̠ ekun, ya̠a̠ anwa ta̠ aro̠ kid̠ud̠ul. Awa ta̠ e̠ghu̠r eten igba̠iny ka̠ a̠rukpe ibura̠.
HEB 1:12 Anwa ta̠ a̠kporokpor awa ma̠ agu̠o̠ akapa, sa̠ ta̠ obhin awa onwegina̠ ka̠ a̠rukpe ibura̠ nyen. Ya̠a̠, anwa ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ onin agu̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ ekunuguma ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ rala d̠oyom.
HEB 1:13 Orileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ nyen ke̠re̠, ma̠ ola̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠a̠, “Ro̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ d̠ami̠ tu̠tu̠n ami̠ ta̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ogbo o̠lo̠gi̠an a̠d̠ien d̠oyom okpokpolom o̠gbam a̠sike d̠inyin.”
HEB 1:14 O̠ku̠a ka̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠ro̠ eka̠? Awa aru̠mu̠gh, sa̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ rob̠a̠ra̠motu ya̠ na̠ egir na̠ enigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ itenemeni bho̠.
HEB 2:1 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, akpe̠ i̠yar o̠mar o̠nagha i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠yar umel o̠d̠u̠a.
HEB 2:2 Ezin bho̠ a̠duom wa̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ i̠gba imutiom bho̠ ya̠gia̠ga̠i, sa̠ na̠ osobh ase̠ ya̠ igielake̠ na̠ ogboloma̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠pi̠o̠gho̠m bho̠, na̠ iya̠ o̠nagha d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ bho̠.
HEB 2:3 I̠yar ta̠ od̠ighi eka̠ omiza̠n ku̠gba ma̠ i̠yar oghel obom ogir itenemeni ola̠ o̠ku̠a? Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠d̠ia̠ agba ma̠ ogir itenemeni onon a̠mutiom, sa̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠ ibhin ra̠ i̠gba inigha̠ i̠yar ma̠ iya̠gia̠ga̠i.
HEB 2:4 Sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhin relegh, na̠ ilologia̠n na̠ a̠d̠ien kere kere ogir ilologia̠n, na̠ atu̠gi̠ re̠ne̠ghe̠ E̠mu̠gh E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, a̠muzoghod̠iom asu̠gbagba d̠awa d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
HEB 2:5 I̠na na̠ onigha̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠ orileghom e̠ma ra̠ a̠nwunom, wa̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠gba na̠ ogboloma̠ bho̠.
HEB 2:6 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, u̠gba ma̠ odi esi d̠a̠ ra̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “ ‘O̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ka̠ ere ma̠ ola̠ anwa na̠ aru̠ru̠an na̠ a̠gboloma̠, bo̠d̠o̠ ka̠ i̠na o̠nyi̠ ta̠ o̠ni̠ ke̠re̠ ma̠ ola̠ anwa na̠ a̠kponom’?
HEB 2:7 Anwa i̠le̠m i̠na aki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠ki̠ki̠ra a̠pu ma̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ anwa ibhin eghoi isosorogia̠n na̠ edim izuom i̠na,
HEB 2:8 iguri ma̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar d̠a̠ ekpukpu a̠sike d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ orileghom.’ ” U̠ge̠ ma̠a̠, ‘eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar,’ o̠ku̠a na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ abar ola̠ usigimeni bo̠. Ya̠a̠, i̠yar ta̠ o̠bi̠gh d̠o̠ ka̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ na̠ orileghom eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar i̠se̠n.
HEB 2:9 Ya̠a̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠bi̠gh A̠zizo̠s wa, ekud̠i obhel sa̠ uguri ma̠ a̠dila̠de ola̠ aki̠r a̠pu ma̠ ita̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ d̠a̠ igbirigbir ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠na a̠gbika̠ a̠mugh ebula̠ i̠yar. I̠se̠n i̠yar na̠ o̠bi̠gh ka̠ na̠ ozuom i̠na ma̠ eghoi isosorogia̠n na̠ edim, d̠a̠ ebula̠ egbika̠ omugh d̠o̠yo̠.
HEB 2:10 A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ ale̠m eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠, ato̠ ma̠ obhin a̠d̠izo anwi̠i̠ny od̠ighom d̠a̠ isosorogia̠n d̠o̠yo̠. Sa̠ a̠bhon agu̠o̠ i̠na ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s amado̠n bho̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ egbika̠ ya̠ A̠zizo̠s atu̠n otenemeni awa a̠gbika̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠.
HEB 2:11 O̠ku̠a bha̠ i̠se̠n, A̠zizo̠s na̠ ogbo ya̠ i̠na na̠ ab̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a bho̠, na̠ eten anwi̠i̠ny onin eghun. Obha̠ ezin bho̠ i̠na od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l obhelegi awa ma̠ a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
HEB 2:12 Ezin bho̠ i̠na agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ta̠ a̠sen ib̠eb̠i ya̠ d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien d̠oyom bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ da̠mi̠. Ami̠ ta̠ amo̠r aso̠r a̠tutumeni nyam d̠a̠ a̠kokod̠ia̠n a̠nwunom bho̠.”
HEB 2:13 O̠lo̠gho̠m i̠se̠ sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “Eb̠em ologi d̠ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠.” Sa̠ a̠mula̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ od̠i ma̠ i̠se̠n na̠ anwi̠i̠ny ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠nigha̠ ami̠ bho̠.”
HEB 2:14 Ebula̠ agu̠o̠ anwi̠i̠ny ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ inwuna̠ ma̠ asi̠ na̠ ipulupul bho̠, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ten o̠ni̠ ola̠ asi̠ na̠ ipulupul. I̠na a̠gir o̠ku̠a ma̠ o̠wo̠l d̠a̠ omugh d̠o̠yo̠ o̠pi̠e̠gi̠ a̠limon ta̠ Eru bho̠, wa̠ na̠ a̠sibh a̠limon omugh bho̠.
HEB 2:15 Ogir o̠ko̠no̠n a̠d̠ighi kisa̠ i̠na a̠rue a̠tenemeni ma̠ ogbo ya̠, d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠awa, i̠ro̠ ma̠ igoni d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠ku̠nu̠ omugh bho̠.
HEB 2:16 Ya̠gia̠ga̠i i̠na na̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun ta̠ Ebraham, ya̠a̠ itileduom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠o̠.
HEB 2:17 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ u̠le̠m i̠na u̠gu̠b̠e̠ni̠ ma̠ a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ re̠kal, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na a̠bhin d̠a̠ igbirigbir na̠ iya̠ igielake̠ aro̠ ma̠ We̠mu̠ Okur d̠i̠yar d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Sa̠ na̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ ola̠ a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ itulugia̠n na̠ okpon i̠karabh o̠si̠ghe̠ a̠d̠ien.
HEB 2:18 I̠se̠n i̠na na̠ a̠rue na̠ alo̠gh agu̠o̠ na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ad̠agi̠an i̠te̠i̠, ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠gbika̠ sa̠ ad̠agi̠an i̠te̠i̠ i̠na nyen.
HEB 3:1 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, inyin a̠rumor na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠ami̠, ogbo ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ab̠aram a̠bhelegi a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ e̠gi̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠. Iloghoma̠ne ma̠ A̠zizo̠s wa̠ i̠yar na̠ osen bho̠ ma̠a̠, i̠na wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ afi̠ri̠ma ma̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ni̠ ogir na̠ We̠mu̠ Okur ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠i̠yar bho̠.
HEB 3:2 I̠na a̠rugh ado̠l igielake̠ d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ aso̠n i̠na bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠mozizi a̠gir igiel bho̠ ub̠eton eb̠la̠ eghun otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ unigha̠ i̠na ma̠ orileghom bho̠.
HEB 3:3 Ya̠a̠, akpe̠ ma̠ o̠bu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ A̠zizo̠s opu A̠mozizi, a̠d̠ien agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lo ma̠ otu bho̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu ma̠ otu wa̠ i̠na a̠lo bho̠.
HEB 3:4 Ezin bho̠, eb̠la̠ a̠rutu ya̠ od̠i bho̠, o̠ni̠ na̠ a̠lo ma̠ odi i̠se̠. Ya̠a̠, A̠zib̠a̠ a̠lo kabar kabar.
HEB 3:5 A̠mozizi ob̠a̠ra̠motu ola̠ a̠rugh ya̠ igielake̠ d̠a̠ otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. Ogir d̠o̠yo̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ elegh egboloma̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ta̠ agba a̠mutiom d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠.
HEB 3:6 Ya̠a̠, Akrai̠st a̠bhin d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de O̠nyi̠ na̠ a̠rileghom otu ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ igielake̠. I̠yar eghun otu d̠o̠yo̠ ku̠gba ma̠ i̠yar o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ d̠i̠yar, d̠a̠ abar wa̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠tu̠n na̠ obo d̠a̠ eb̠em ologi bho̠.
HEB 3:7 O̠ku̠a bha̠ od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ E̠mu̠gh Etu̠tu̠ bho̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ inyin u̠mu̠gho̠n okoroko d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠didon,
HEB 3:8 o̠ni̠ ko o̠kparame̠ni̠ ma̠ rologi d̠inyin agu̠o̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul d̠inyin iwia̠n a̠limon ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ sa̠ i̠d̠agi̠an i̠na d̠a̠ e̠ghana bho̠.
HEB 3:9 Awa i̠d̠agi̠an ami̠ d̠a̠ ebla̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠bi̠gh i̠di̠ar ya̠ ami̠ igir
HEB 3:10 d̠a̠ eruba̠l ala bho̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ ologi d̠ami̠ agam a̠nigha̠ ma̠ amu̠m obha̠ ifugh ma̠a̠, ‘Rologi d̠awa na̠ e̠ru̠ru̠an ipa̠n eb̠la̠ igiel, sa̠ awa na̠ e̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ na̠ egboloma̠ ma̠ i̠to̠ d̠ami̠.’
HEB 3:11 Sa̠ d̠a̠ i̠gam d̠ami̠, sa̠ ami̠ igurugia̠n ma̠a̠, awa ko o̠gi̠ d̠o̠ ka̠ ed̠igh ed̠e ma̠ e̠nu̠m d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠ami̠.
HEB 3:12 A̠rumor d̠ami̠ na̠ aru̠marani̠ d̠ami̠, o̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni, o̠ni̠ inyin onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠karabh ologi na̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ o̠d̠u̠a d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠.
HEB 3:13 Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠, odi akpo̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ologi ta̠ odi ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠, d̠a̠ i̠to̠ e̠mu̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠karabh igelemeni ma̠ o̠ni̠ inyin ma̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
HEB 3:14 O̠ku̠a na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, eb̠la̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ od̠e ma̠ e̠nu̠m ogir ta̠ Akrai̠st, ku̠gba ma̠a̠ i̠yar osibh o̠pu̠r ima̠ra̠ ologi d̠i̠yar o̠kparame̠ni̠, tu̠tu̠n ta̠ ate̠i̠ ekunuguma̠ bho̠.
HEB 3:15 I̠ru̠ru̠ane̠ ma̠ iya̠ u̠gba d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠: “Igiel inyin u̠mu̠gho̠n okoroko d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ a̠didon, o̠ni̠ ko o̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul d̠inyin, ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa iwia̠n a̠limon ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ igurumeni ma̠ ologi d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠.”
HEB 3:16 Ya̠a̠, wa̠ a̠nyen ogbo ya̠ i̠mu̠gho̠n okoroko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, ku̠ku̠m eka̠ sa̠ iwia̠n a̠limon d̠o̠yo̠ igurumeni ma̠ ologi bho̠? Eb̠la̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ A̠mozizi a̠rileghom a̠mutiom d̠a̠ Izipt bho̠.
HEB 3:17 Wa̠ a̠nyen ogbo ya̠ i̠na agam i̠gam a̠nigha̠ ma̠ eruba̠l rala bho̠? I̠nye̠ ogbo ya̠ igir i̠karabh sa̠ imugughu, sa̠ regua̠de d̠awa i̠ro̠ i̠b̠o̠r d̠a̠ e̠ghana bho̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠?
HEB 3:18 Ya̠a̠, wa̠ a̠nyen ogbo ya̠ agba a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na a̠gurugia̠n ma̠a̠, “Awa ko o̠gi̠ d̠o̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠ami̠” bho̠? Ogbo ya̠ i̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ inigha̠ i̠na bho̠ d̠o̠ ke̠re̠?
HEB 3:19 O̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠bi̠gh ma̠ agbo̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ awa oma̠ra̠ d̠o̠ bho̠, sa̠ awa orue d̠o̠ ma̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠o̠yo̠.
HEB 4:1 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠sibh ogua̠n wa̠ i̠na a̠gua̠n ma̠a̠, i̠yar ta̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠. Ku̠ku̠m eka̠, i̠yar ta̠ okpona̠, b̠o̠ka̠ bebena̠ o̠ni̠ inyin na̠ o̠pi̠o̠m (omel ad̠u̠a) ma̠ ola̠ i̠na ko o̠te̠i̠ d̠o̠ a̠d̠igh.
HEB 4:2 O̠lo̠gho̠m i̠se̠, i̠yar na̠ o̠mu̠gho̠n ani̠ ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba ya̠ u̠gba unigha̠ i̠yar bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠. Ya̠a̠, id̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ asu̠o̠ enigha̠ awa ma̠ igiel bho̠ awa i̠mu̠gho̠n bho̠, ezin bho̠ awa inwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ wa̠ o̠da asu̠gbagba bho̠ obhin.
HEB 4:3 I̠yar ogbo ya̠ na̠ oma̠ra̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n bho̠ na̠ o̠te̠i̠ od̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gua̠n bho̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “Ami̠ ibhin d̠a̠ i̠gam a̠gurugia̠n ma̠a̠, awa ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠ami̠.” A̠zib̠a̠ a̠kunugiom o̠le̠m i̠di̠ar ka̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na alem e̠ma ra̠nwunom awe̠le̠ bho̠; ku̠ku̠m eka̠, i̠na agba ma̠ o̠ku̠a a̠mutiom.
HEB 4:4 I̠na agba ma̠ odi esi d̠a̠ A̠d̠ire E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ oleghemeni od̠ua̠l a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Igiel bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ale̠m i̠di̠ar a̠kunugiom bho̠, sa̠ i̠na a̠sira̠ ma̠ epobh oleghemeni od̠ua̠l a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.”
HEB 4:5 D̠a̠ onin esi obha̠ sa̠ i̠na agba a̠numeta̠n ma̠a̠, “Awa ko od̠igh d̠o̠ d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh d̠ami̠.”
HEB 4:6 Agu̠o̠ na̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ idi ogbo ta̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh bho̠, sa ogbo ya̠ ud̠ia̠ u̠gba ma̠ ib̠eb̠i asu̠gbagba bho̠ unigha̠ bho̠ ko od̠igh d̠o̠, d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ awa i̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ i̠we̠le̠ ma̠ o̠da obhin bho̠,
HEB 4:7 sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠nwe a̠gua̠n opa̠n a̠d̠a̠ma̠ ola̠ i̠yar ta̠ orue od̠igh. “A̠didon” a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠. D̠a̠ obhel ola̠ na̠ a̠bia̠ ma̠ o̠gu̠man, sa̠ i̠na awo̠l d̠a̠ o̠nu̠ ta̠ A̠devidi agba a̠mutiom agu̠o̠ i̠na agba ma̠ i̠se bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Ka̠ inyin u̠mu̠gho̠n okoroko ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ma̠ a̠didon, o̠ni̠ ko o̠b̠agh e̠mu̠ ma̠ e̠we̠le̠man o̠nagha.”
HEB 4:8 Aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ A̠zosu̠a a̠rileghom awa ka̠ a̠d̠ighom d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh nab̠o̠, A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ ifugh d̠o̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ onon d̠a̠ obhel o̠gu̠man.
HEB 4:9 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, na̠ oguri ma̠ A̠d̠a̠ma̠ Osira̠-epobh osisa̠n a̠nwunom ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
HEB 4:10 O̠ku̠a bha̠, o̠ni̠ ola̠ ta̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ e̠b̠e̠l a̠d̠igh a̠d̠e d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, o̠ni̠ bho̠ eka̠ ta̠ a̠gir ogir o̠yo̠ a̠sira̠ ma̠ epobh, ma̠ agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gir bho̠.
HEB 4:11 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, owia̠n od̠igh d̠a̠ esi osira̠ epobh obha̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠e̠l, b̠o̠ka̠ o̠ni̠ i̠yar na̠ omugh a̠bhe d̠a̠ ebula̠ ab̠agh e̠mu̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ awa.
HEB 4:12 Ezin bho̠, o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um sa̠ na̠ a̠lol, sa̠ a̠sibh a̠pu ma̠ ab̠e̠ge̠re̠ (ogidi i̠wal-aman). Sa̠ na̠ a̠gu na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ eloghoma̠n ozu na̠ e̠mu̠gh o̠ni̠, ma̠ o̠bagi̠o̠n awa d̠a̠ re̠tu̠tu̠la na̠ ali̠si̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠rue na̠ agba ma̠ e̠wo̠gi̠na i̠ru̠ruan na̠ i̠walama ologi.
HEB 4:13 Bebina̠ abar ola̠ u̠le̠m usoroni d̠a̠ a̠de onon, ola̠ awo̠gi̠na d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bo̠. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠, na̠ ob̠ugh kabarkabar omutiom e̠ma, d̠a̠ a̠misigh o̠ni̠ wa̠ i̠yar ta̠ o̠gba ma̠ ado̠l d̠i̠yar onigha̠ bho̠.
HEB 4:14 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, o̠kpaghano̠m id̠umom d̠i̠yar. Ezin bho̠, i̠yar onwuna̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, obom We̠mu̠ Okur wa̠ na̠ a̠bhun d̠a̠ ote̠nai̠ny bho̠.
HEB 4:15 I̠yar unwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ We̠mu̠ Okur ola̠ orue d̠o̠ ma̠ okpon i̠yar igbirigbir d̠a̠ rasu̠nwe̠r d̠i̠yar. Ya̠a̠, i̠yar unwuna̠ ma̠ We̠mu̠ Okur ola̠ a̠d̠izo re̠kal ad̠agi̠an i̠te̠i̠ agu̠o̠ na̠ e̠te̠i̠ i̠yar i̠se̠n bho̠, ku̠ku̠m eka̠ i̠na na̠ omel d̠o̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
HEB 4:16 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, obhin d̠a̠ alu̠kpo̠ ologi od̠igh d̠a̠ a̠lukpesi e̠ne̠ghe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠yar o̠te̠i̠ okpon igbirigbir na̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠, d̠a̠ obhel i̠kparama ado̠l.
HEB 5:1 Na̠ okpon d̠a̠ esa̠d̠io a̠nwunom bho̠ na̠ o̠so̠n ghan we̠mu̠ rokur, b̠o̠ka̠ i̠na amara ma̠ eni d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ako̠l i̠ko̠l akpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ ya̠ otenemeni awa d̠a̠ i̠karabh.
HEB 5:2 Agu̠o̠ i̠na eka̠ na̠ a̠dugh a̠ludugh bho̠, sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rue na̠ a̠bhin odudugha̠n ologi na̠ a̠kpon ogbo ya̠ ologhoma̠n d̠o̠ sa̠ na̠ egir i̠karabh bho̠.
HEB 5:3 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ i̠na ta̠ akpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ i̠karabh d̠o̠yo̠, na̠ i̠karabh a̠nwunom bho̠.
HEB 5:4 O̠ni̠ ola̠ i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ a̠rue ate̠i̠ a̠d̠ien a̠dila̠de edim onon bo̠, a̠ten ka̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠bhelegi i̠na ma̠ agu̠o̠ a̠bhelegi ma̠ Ero̠n bho̠.
HEB 5:5 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ Akrai̠st na̠ agu̠o̠ o̠re̠ma d̠o̠ ma̠ alu̠bu̠gh a̠ten we̠mu̠ rokur. Kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ bha̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ka̠ agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Anwa O̠nyi̠ d̠ami̠. Ob̠eton a̠didon, ami̠ na̠ a̠ten o̠we̠de̠ d̠oyom.”
HEB 5:6 Onin agu̠o̠ bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ agba ma̠ opa̠n esi ma̠a̠, “Anwa okur ola̠ ta̠ aro̠ tu̠tu̠n ka̠ id̠ud̠ul, ola̠ a̠d̠ien e̠mar ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lki̠ze̠de̠k.
HEB 5:7 D̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom, i̠na a̠siseiny a̠siseiny, a̠puru ma̠ okpon igbirigbir, a̠leghe ma̠ ed̠i agba ma̠ igbir a̠nigha̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ wa̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠limon otenemeni o̠yo̠ d̠a̠ omugh bho̠. Sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ awo̠ran i̠na d̠a̠ ebula̠ o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ o̠zu igielake̠ d̠o̠yo̠.
HEB 5:8 Ebla̠ agu̠o̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ Onyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ eka̠, i̠na a̠bhin egbika̠ ya̠ i̠na a̠gbika̠ bho̠ atu̠ghan o̠ki̠ri̠me̠ni̠ o̠zu.
HEB 5:9 Igiel bho̠ na̠ o̠b̠ab̠a̠le̠ni̠ i̠na o̠mado̠n bho̠, sa̠ i̠na aro̠ ma̠ eten wa̠ ogbo ya̠ id̠umom i̠na ta̠ e̠wol e̠te̠i̠ a̠ghud̠um ka̠ id̠ud̠ul bho̠.
HEB 5:10 Sa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠guri i̠na ma̠ a̠dila̠de we̠mu̠ rokur, ola̠ a̠d̠ien e̠mar ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lki̠ze̠de̠k.
HEB 5:11 I̠di̠ar ya̠ o̠gba ogboloma̠ o̠yo̠ a̠b̠utu, ya̠a̠ ta̠ akpar ogba o̠si̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ onigha̠ inyin, ezin bho̠ i̠nyin na̠ o̠b̠o̠ri̠o̠m o̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar.
HEB 5:12 Obhel amar aro̠ a̠nigha̠ inyin oten ogbo atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n, ya̠a̠ od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ ola̠ opa̠n o̠ni̠ ta̠ a̠mula̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ inyin i̠pu̠r ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar imutuma̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠. O̠ku̠a̠ bha̠ inyin na̠ oten ogbo ya̠ ta̠ onigha̠ amu̠mam amu̠mam, kpe̠le̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ ikpo ed̠ia̠n.
HEB 5:13 Ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ amam amu̠mam od̠id̠ia̠ ma̠ o̠gbara o̠nyi̠, ola̠ ta̠ o̠mu̠gho̠nyan d̠o̠ ma̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala.
HEB 5:14 Ya̠a̠, ikpo ed̠ia̠n i̠ro̠ inigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠ikighu ma̠ aru̠mu̠, ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠ghan e̠ku̠ro̠m sa̠ na̠ erue na̠ eloghom a̠nwegia̠n ta̠ i̠karabh na̠ ib̠eb̠i.
HEB 6:1 O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni, owia̠n eloghom abar d̠i̠yar d̠a̠ Akrai̠st a̠pel ya̠ i̠yar u̠tu̠ghan d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r ob̠eton bho̠. Omula̠ d̠o̠ o̠gi̠ d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de ola̠ na̠ a̠puru ma̠ okpon i̠karabh o̠si̠ghe̠ a̠d̠ien, d̠a̠ ebula̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar ya̠ eb̠em ologi o̠to̠ d̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠;
HEB 6:2 na̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ ozu, na̠ o̠gbamagi̠ aru̠gu̠o̠, na̠ ob̠etina̠ d̠a̠ omugh, na̠ ebhum ase̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ bho̠.
HEB 6:3 Akpe̠ i̠yar ogir o̠ku̠a, d̠a̠ okpon igbirigbir ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
HEB 6:4 Ta̠ akpar ogbo ya̠ na̠ ed̠ia̠ e̠ro̠ d̠a̠ e̠b̠alab̠al bho̠ e̠d̠e̠d̠i̠ma ma̠ e̠ne̠ghe̠ ote̠nai̠ny, sa̠ id̠e̠d̠ia̠n na̠ Ob̠eb̠i E̠mu̠gh bho̠,
HEB 6:5 e̠bi̠gh e̠no̠gho̠man o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ ra̠limon amu̠m wa̠ na̠ a̠ru bho̠,
HEB 6:6 ma̠ orue otiba̠ra̠ d̠a̠ i̠karabh ku̠gba ma̠ awa emel e̠d̠u̠a. O̠ku̠a bha̠ awa na̠ enwe na̠ egigh o̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ d̠a̠ e̠mi̠gi̠re̠ni̠an oriren bho̠, na̠ e̠lo̠gi̠ i̠na ma̠ ari̠ghe̠l na̠ emutiom e̠ma.
HEB 6:7 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ a̠tutumeni ma̠ a̠de wa̠ na̠ a̠mibh gha̠n amu̠m o̠lo̠bha wa̠ na̠ a̠ba̠ra̠ ma̠ o̠lo̠bho̠m o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ na̠ a̠b̠om ib̠eb̠i ed̠ia̠n na̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ ogbo ya̠ igbebh bho̠.
HEB 6:8 Ya̠a̠, a̠de ola̠ a̠d̠igh ib̠ub̠ulom na̠ ralai̠-agbo̠gi̠ri̠ bha̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠ a̠de, ola̠ na̠ orogi sa̠ ta̠ o̠bhu̠gi̠ d̠a̠ ekunuguma̠.
HEB 6:9 Ib̠eb̠i ra̠tologha̠n d̠i̠yar, eb̠la̠ agu̠o̠ o̠nu̠o̠kpe̠ d̠i̠yar aro̠ ma̠ o̠ku̠a bho̠ eka̠, i̠yar uma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠ inyin ta̠ o̠te̠i̠ ibom e̠no̠gho̠man ya̠ uguri usisa̠n ogbo ya̠ na̠ otenemeni bho̠.
HEB 6:10 A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ ipa̠n a̠gir ipa̠n. I̠na ko oweleta̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ ogir d̠inyin, na̠ agu̠o̠ inyin na̠ obhin na̠ otula̠n a̠d̠ien d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ma̠ o̠lo̠gh agu̠o̠ ya̠ inyin na̠ o̠lo̠gh na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ ogbo-ogir d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, sa̠ inyin od̠id̠ia̠ na̠ ogir o̠ku̠a bho̠.
HEB 6:11 Na̠ ebhir i̠yar o̠bi̠gh ma̠a̠, ko̠ni̠ko̠ni̠ inyin na̠ a̠bhin d̠a̠ onin onyen ologi bho̠ na̠ a̠gir ya̠ o̠te̠i̠ imuzoghod̠iom eb̠em ologi d̠o̠yo̠ tu̠tu̠n ekunuguma̠ bho̠.
HEB 6:12 I̠yar u̠bho̠ro̠gh d̠o̠ inyin o̠gbu̠o̠r, ya̠a̠ i̠ta ma̠ ogbo ya̠ ibhin d̠a̠ ologi ima̠ra̠ na̠ a̠ma̠ne i̠te̠i̠ i̠d̠i̠ar ya̠ ugua̠n uguri bho̠.
HEB 6:13 Igiel bho̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gua̠n a̠nigha̠ ma̠ Ebraham bho̠, i̠na na̠ agu̠o̠ a̠sibhigha̠n d̠a̠ ebula̠ agu̠o̠ o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠pu i̠na o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ bho̠,
HEB 6:14 agba ma̠a̠, “D̠a̠ itutumeni, ami̠ ta̠ a̠tutumeni nyam ga̠i, d̠a̠ i̠mara sa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ighi ma̠ o̠la anwa ta̠ amaragi̠an a̠b̠utu anwi̠i̠ny.
HEB 6:15 Igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠ne a̠b̠ara̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na ate̠i̠ abar wa̠ uguan unigha̠ i̠na bho̠.
HEB 6:16 A̠nwunom na̠ ebhin a̠d̠ien o̠ni̠ ola̠ a̠pu awa na̠ esibhigha̠, sa̠ eb̠la̠ raku̠anan d̠awa na̠ ekun agu̠o̠ ola̠ i̠zo̠ bho̠ ta̠ amara.
HEB 6:17 A̠zib̠a̠ abho̠ro̠gh o̠mar oleriom ogbo ya̠ ta̠ e̠te̠i̠ abar wa̠ i̠na a̠gua̠n a̠nigha̠ awa bho̠, ma̠ i̠na na̠ onwe gha̠n o̠nu̠ d̠a̠ i̠to̠ d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ a̠d̠ia̠n i̠zo̠ alo̠gho̠m.
HEB 6:18 A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gir o̠ku̠a ma̠ agu̠o̠ ola̠, ta̠ awo̠l d̠a̠ i̠wal i̠di̠ar ya̠ onwegia̠n gha̠n sa̠ i̠mara ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ na̠ o̠gba d̠o̠ ma̠ igunugha̠. Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, akpe̠ i̠yar ogbo ya̠ na̠ od̠igh ed̠oghotu d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ d̠o̠yo̠ bho̠, ma̠ osibh abar eb̠em ologi wa̠ uguri usisa̠n i̠yar bho̠ o̠kparame̠ni̠.
HEB 6:19 Eb̠em ologi onon wa̠ i̠yar unwuna̠ bho̠, bha̠ a̠limon wa̠ na̠ a̠sibh rologi d̠i̠yar na̠ akparame̠ni̠ na̠ a̠guri d̠a̠ eko bho̠. Na̠ awo̠l na̠ a̠ten e̠nu̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ a̠lukpesi e̠tu̠tu̠ d̠a̠ otuta̠zib̠a̠,
HEB 6:20 esi wa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠d̠ia̠ agi̠ ka̠ a̠d̠igh d̠a̠ ebula̠ i̠yar bho̠. I̠se̠n i̠na na̠ a̠ten we̠mu̠ rokur kid̠ud̠ul, d̠a̠ a̠d̠ien ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lkize̠de̠k.
HEB 7:1 Ame̠lkize̠de̠k onon aro̠ ma̠ o̠li̠le̠ma Asale̠m na̠ okur ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ Wagi̠manyu̠ A̠pu bho̠. I̠na a̠mutuma̠ ma̠ Ebraham a̠tutumeni, ma̠ igiel bho̠ Ebraham ane̠gi̠me̠ni̠ ma̠ aru̠lala e̠ma bho̠ sa̠ na̠ a̠mula̠ na̠ a̠yel bho̠,
HEB 7:2 sa̠ Ebraham a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh d̠a̠ eb̠la̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠bhin bho̠. O̠pu̠r ezin a̠d̠ien ta̠ Ame̠lkizede̠k bha̠ “o̠li̠le̠ma e̠b̠ab̠ala”, opa̠n ezin sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ “o̠li̠le̠ma ekima̠.”
HEB 7:3 I̠na o̠wede̠ bo̠ onweni bo̠, o̠la-imitia̠n ibom ro̠we̠de̠ na̠ ronweni id̠ud̠ul bo̠, i̠na na̠ onwuna̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ obhel eru a̠ghud̠um na̠ obhel oyel nyen, ya̠a̠ u̠le̠m i̠na o̠gu̠b̠e̠ni̠ ma̠ O̠nyi̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠, sa̠ aro̠ ma̠ okur tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul.
HEB 7:4 Ikpone ma̠ ed̠ighom e̠mi̠ alu̠bu̠gh d̠o̠yo̠; aga̠i Ebraham wa̠ aro̠ ma̠ obom o̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul bho̠ eka̠, a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠ odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh d̠a̠ i̠di̠ar ya̠ ilei abar ipu d̠a̠ ologi i̠di̠ar ya̠ i̠na a̠bhin bho̠.
HEB 7:5 Oloko bho̠ a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠limon anwi̠i̠ny imitia̠n ta̠ A̠livai̠ ya̠ id̠igh rokur bho̠, ma̠ obhin odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ a̠nwunom bho̠. O̠ku̠a na̠ a̠ma̠ra̠ ma̠a̠, awa na̠ ebhin d̠a̠ aru̠gu̠o̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ anwi̠i̠ny a̠rughun Izre̠l agu̠o̠ awa, ya̠ i̠ro̠ ani̠ ma̠ imitia̠n ta̠ Ebraham bho̠.
HEB 7:6 Ame̠lkize̠de̠k na̠ omite̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ o̠la ta̠ A̠livai̠, ku̠ku̠m eka̠ i̠na a̠bhin odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh bho̠ d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ ta̠ Ebraham a̠tutumeni i̠na o̠ni̠ wa̠ rogua̠n ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ i̠ro̠ inigha̠ bho̠.
HEB 7:7 Ologhom ma̠a̠ o̠ni̠ wa̠ a̠lei abar a̠pu bho̠ na̠ a̠tutumeni gha̠n o̠ni̠ wa̠ aki̠r a̠pu i̠na bho̠, aku̠anan bo̠no̠bo̠.
HEB 7:8 D̠a̠ e̠kal wa̠ igboloma̠ ma̠ rokur bho̠, bha̠ a̠nwunom ya̠ ta̠ emugughu na̠ ebhin odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh bho̠; ya̠a̠ d̠a̠ opa̠n e̠kal, bha̠ i̠na wa̠ u̠gba umutiom ma̠ od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um bho̠ na̠ a̠bhin.
HEB 7:9 D̠a̠ agu̠o̠ o̠gba bha̠, aga̠i A̠levai̠ wa̠ na̠ a̠bhin odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh bho̠ eka̠, awo̠l d̠a̠ Ebraham akpe̠ ghan odi a̠bin d̠a̠ atu̠gi̠ a̠d̠iobh bho̠,
HEB 7:10 ezin bho̠ A̠livai̠ od̠id̠ia̠ d̠a̠ eghun obom o̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ igiel bho̠ Ame̠lkize̠de̠k ate̠i̠ Ebraham bho̠.
HEB 7:11 Ku̠gba ma̠a̠, a̠nwunom ta̠ erue e̠wo̠l d̠a̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ ta̠ rokur ya̠ i̠ro̠ ma̠ imitia̠n ta̠ A̠livai̠ bho̠ e̠te̠i̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala, ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠nye̠ i̠gbo̠ d̠a̠ oloko bho̠ imite bho̠, ka̠ ezin wa̠ opa̠n okur ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lkize̠de̠k ta̠ a̠mite a̠ru bho̠, ola̠ obhin d̠o̠ ma̠ ita̠ Ero̠n bho̠, ka̠ ere?
HEB 7:12 Ezin bho̠, igiel a̠dila̠de okur bho̠ a̠nwegia̠n, bha̠ oloko bho̠ eka̠ ta̠ awegia̠n nyen.
HEB 7:13 O̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ o̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ ogboloma̠ bho̠, a̠mite d̠a̠ opa̠n ebhugh. Ebhugh d̠o̠yo̠ ta̠ od̠ia̠ d̠o̠ emutiom o̠ni̠ ola̠ na̠ aro̠ ato̠to̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ d̠a̠ enwen bho̠.
HEB 7:14 O̠mar ologhom ma̠a̠, Wa̠nwuna̠ wa̠ na̠ o̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n na̠ ogboloma̠ bho̠ a̠mite d̠a̠ eghun ta̠ A̠zuda̠, sa̠ A̠mozizi na̠ osen d̠o̠ ma̠ eghun obha̠ a̠gboloma̠ ma̠ a̠dila̠de okur.
HEB 7:15 Ta̠ o̠mar o̠mu̠gho̠nyan abar wa̠ i̠yar u̠gba bho̠, ma̠ agu̠o̠ opa̠n okur ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lkize̠de̠k na̠ a̠mite bho̠,
HEB 7:16 i̠na wa̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de okur, ola̠ o̠tu̠o̠no̠m d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ oloko e̠ma-ra̠nwunom o̠ri̠lo̠me̠ni̠, ya̠a̠ ubhin d̠a̠ a̠limon a̠ghud̠um wa̠ ekunuguma̠ o̠to̠ bho̠.
HEB 7:17 U̠gba d̠a̠ a̠d̠ire e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ omutiom ma̠a̠, “Anwa ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ okur tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul, ola̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar ta̠ Ame̠lkize̠de̠k.”
HEB 7:18 Na̠ ogbogion ugba̠iny oloko bho̠, ezin bho̠ odudugha̠n na̠ obhobho i̠kpo̠ abar.
HEB 7:19 Ezin bho̠, abar ola̠ oloko bho̠ a̠rue ma̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ bo̠, ya̠a̠ na̠ omutiom eb̠em ologi ola̠ a̠bhon a̠pu, ola̠ ta̠ o̠wo̠l o̠te̠i̠ A̠zib̠a̠.
HEB 7:20 O̠tu̠o̠no̠m i̠se̠ bha̠, i̠na na̠ od̠igh d̠o̠ ma̠ okur ola̠ A̠zib̠a̠ od̠ia̠n d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠zo̠ a̠gboloma̠, ya̠a̠ ubhin d̠o̠ ma̠ i̠zo̠ o̠lo̠gi̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom iyed̠i ma̠ rokur.
HEB 7:21 Ya̠a̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠d̠ia̠n i̠zo̠ alo̠gh i̠na ma̠ okur agba a̠nigha̠ i̠na ma̠a̠, “Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠sibhigha̠ sa̠ i̠na ko onwe d̠o̠ ma̠ o̠nu̠. Anwa ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ okur tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul.”
HEB 7:22 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a, sa̠ A̠zizo̠s a̠ten o̠ni̠ wa̠ na̠ amara ma̠ eni na̠ a̠leriom ma̠a̠ omom i̠zo̠ bho̠ a̠bhon a̠pu.
HEB 7:23 Opa̠n a̠nwegia̠n od̠i, ezin bho̠, a̠d̠izo rokur iyed̠i imugughu d̠a̠ egum sa̠ i̠ro̠ d̠o̠ d̠a̠ a̠dila̠de bho̠ egir e̠gi̠o̠m d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠.
HEB 7:24 Agu̠o̠ A̠zizo̠s od̠i d̠a̠ a̠ghud̠um tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul bho̠, bha̠ ogir okur d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ okunugiom d̠o̠.
HEB 7:25 Ebula̠ o̠ku̠a sa̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rue na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ ogbo ya̠ na̠ e̠wo̠l d̠o̠yo̠ ma̠ o̠te̠i̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠. Ezin bho̠ i̠na na̠ a̠rugh a̠ghud̠um o̠mara eni onigha̠ awa d̠a̠ a̠misigh ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ kigiel kigiel.
HEB 7:26 O̠ku̠a bha̠ i̠na we̠mu̠ okur ola̠ igielake̠ na̠ e̠b̠ab̠ala, o̠ni̠ abar o̠li̠o̠m o̠to̠ na̠ i̠karabh o̠to̠. Uguri i̠na osigimeni ma̠ id̠ighi ma̠ i̠karabh, sa̠ ub̠eton i̠na u̠gi̠o̠m anyu̠ upeleni ma̠ re̠nai̠ny bho̠.
HEB 7:27 I̠na bo̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur iyed̠i. A̠dila̠de okur d̠o̠yo̠ na̠ opuru d̠o̠ i̠na ma̠ o̠kpe̠gi̠ ralu̠kpe̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠ ka̠d̠a̠ma̠, ya̠ od̠ia̠ obhin otenemeni i̠karabh d̠o̠yo̠, sa̠ i̠na ta̠ akpe̠gi̠ ma̠ iya̠ otenemeni i̠karabh a̠nwunom bho̠. I̠na a̠nigha̠ ma̠ a̠ghud̠um d̠o̠yo̠ a̠bhin akpe̠ ma̠ i̠karabh d̠awa ma̠ onin ogbudon sa̠ a̠munia̠n i̠se̠.
HEB 7:28 Ogbo aru̠mu̠ rokur ya̠ oloko bho̠ na̠ alo̠gi̠ bho̠ idudugha̠n d̠a̠ re̠kal, ya̠a̠ i̠zo̠ wa̠ a̠ru ma̠ o̠gu̠man bho̠ aso̠n i̠na O̠nyi̠ bho̠, wa̠ na̠ o̠b̠ab̠alame̠ni̠ oguri tu̠tu̠n kid̠ud̠ul bho̠.
HEB 8:1 Onon e̠mu̠ abar wa̠ i̠yar na̠ o̠gba bho̠. I̠yar unwuna̠ ma̠ we̠mu̠ okur ola̠ od̠i ma̠ a̠dila̠de d̠a̠ od̠iom agu̠o̠ a̠lukpesi ta̠ Wa̠lei Abar A̠pu bho̠ d̠a̠ renai̠ny.
HEB 8:2 I̠na ob̠a̠ra̠motu e̠b̠ab̠ala d̠a̠ a̠lukpesi e̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠ na̠ a̠ga̠i otu-akpu̠ru̠ wa̠ A̠zib̠a̠ a̠gim bho̠, wa̠ o̠nyi̠o̠mo̠ro̠ni̠ ogim d̠o̠ bho̠.
HEB 8:3 We̠mu̠ okur we̠mu̠ okur ola̠ u̠so̠n na̠ a̠bhin gha̠n i̠di̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ na̠ i̠nam i̠ko̠l na̠ ako̠l i̠ko̠l. O̠ku̠a a̠d̠ighi be̠le̠ni̠, sa̠ a̠bhon we̠mu̠ okur onon onwuna̠ ani̠ abar ola̠ obhin o̠kpe̠ alu̠kpe̠.
HEB 8:4 Aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ i̠na od̠i d̠a̠ e̠mara̠nwunom nab̠o̠, i̠na ka̠ id̠igh d̠o̠ na̠ od̠igh okur, ezin bho̠ rokur ya̠ na̠ e̠tu̠o̠no̠m oloko bho̠ na̠ ebhin i̠di̠ar e̠ne̠ghe̠ na̠ e̠kpe̠ ma̠ alu̠kpe̠ od̠i.
HEB 8:5 I̠ko̠l d̠awa od̠i ka̠ o̠ru̠ran abar ola̠ na̠ egir na̠ e̠gu̠b̠e̠ni̠ ma̠ od̠ighi i̠di̠ar ote̠nai̠ny. Obha̠ ezin bho̠ u̠kparame̠ni̠ ukikiom A̠mozizi ma̠ igiel bho̠ i̠na na̠ ra̠ ogim otu-akpu̠ru̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠ ma̠a̠, “Mare̠ ma̠ a̠kpon a̠gir kabar kabar agu̠b̠e̠ni̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ uleriom anwa d̠a̠ igu bho̠.”
HEB 8:6 Ya̠a̠ i̠se̠n, na̠ onigha̠ ma̠ A̠zizo̠s opa̠n a̠d̠ien ed̠ighiom i̠di̠ar okur ya̠ ilei abar ipu ma̠ ita̠ awa. Od̠i ma̠ agu̠o̠ rogua̠n d̠a̠ i̠zo̠ wa̠ i̠na na̠ amara eni bho̠, ibhon ipu ma̠ ita̠ oloko bho̠.
HEB 8:7 I̠se̠ ma̠ abar ola̠ api̠an d̠a̠ o̠pu̠r i̠zo̠ bho̠ na̠ o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ na̠b̠o̠, ezin ola̠ o̠tu̠n omutiom wa̠leghemeni i̠wal bho̠ ka̠ i̠ro̠ d̠o̠.
HEB 8:8 Agu̠o̠ A̠zib̠a̠ abi̠gh ma̠ awa na̠ egir na̠ e̠pi̠e̠ bho̠, sa̠ i̠na agba ma̠a̠, “I̠nagha! Ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ na̠ eru ma̠ igiel ami̠ ta̠ a̠mutiom omom i̠zo̠ a̠d̠ia̠n na̠ a̠nwunom Izre̠l na̠ a̠nwunom A̠zuda̠.
HEB 8:9 Obha̠ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠ ma̠ agu̠o̠ i̠zo̠ wa̠ ami̠ id̠ia̠n na̠ ibom ro̠we̠de̠ id̠ud̠ul d̠awa bho̠, ma̠ igiel bho̠ ami̠ isibh awa d̠a̠ agu̠o̠ irileghom imutiom d̠a̠ Izipt bho̠. Igiel obha̠, awa i̠b̠agh aru̠mu̠ e̠we̠le̠man obhin d̠a̠ igielake̠ okoko i̠zo̠ bho̠, sa̠ ami̠ ighel awa.”
HEB 8:10 Wa̠nwuna̠ bho̠ na̠ agba ma̠a̠, “Onon i̠zo̠ wa̠ ami̠ ta̠ a̠d̠ia̠n na̠ a̠nwunom Izre̠l ma̠a̠, ‘D̠a̠ ra̠d̠a̠ma̠ i̠nye̠, ami̠ ta̠ alo̠gi̠ ma̠ roloko d̠ami̠ d̠a̠ rologi d̠awa, age̠ d̠a̠ rekpo ologi d̠awa. Ami̠ ta̠ aro̠ ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠ da̠wa, sa̠ awa ta̠ e̠ro̠ ma̠ a̠nwunom d̠ami̠.’
HEB 8:11 o̠ni̠ awa ola̠ ta̠ atu̠ghu̠me̠ni̠, bo̠d̠o̠ agba a̠nigha̠ ma̠ opa̠n o̠nyi̠ eghun ma̠a̠, ‘Loghome ma̠ A̠zib̠a̠,’ ko o̠ro̠ d̠o̠, ezin bho̠ eb̠la̠ awa ta̠ eloghom ami̠, i̠gbara na̠ ikei.
HEB 8:12 Ami̠ ta̠ a̠kpon i̠karabh d̠awa asi̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien, sa̠ ami̠ ko o̠ru̠ru̠an mu ma̠ i̠karabh od̠ighi i̠di̠ar d̠awa.”
HEB 8:13 Agu̠o̠ i̠na na̠ agba ma̠a̠ omom i̠zo̠ onon a̠bhon a̠pu bho̠, bha̠ i̠na na̠ a̠tenemeni ma̠ o̠pu̠r bho̠ ma̠ ugba̠iny. Ologhom ma̠a̠, abar ola̠ na̠ a̠ten ugba̠iny sa̠ ko orue mu orughom ma̠a̠, na̠ a̠tua̠n ebhi abar bho̠ ma̠ oghur oten.
HEB 9:1 O̠pu̠r i̠zo̠ bho̠ a̠nwuna̠ ma̠ i̠to̠to̠gi̠ na̠ a̠lukpesi ola̠ o̠ro̠ o̠ko̠l i̠ko̠l.
HEB 9:2 Otu-akpu̠ru̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ aro̠ ma̠ ola̠ ugim. O̠pu̠r e̠kpe̠ bho̠ ubhelegi ma̠ A̠lukpesi E̠tu̠tu̠, esi ola̠ uguri ma̠ o̠lo̠ ato̠di̠ na̠ akpata ola̠ u̠gbamagi̠ ikpokpogh abre̠di̠.
HEB 9:3 D̠a̠ aman wa̠leghemeni i̠wal ukpe wa̠ ubhin usobhom A̠lukpesi E̠tu̠tu̠ bho̠, bha̠ opa̠n e̠kpe̠ od̠i ma̠ ola̠ ubhelegi ma̠a̠ Obom A̠lukpesi E̠tu̠tu̠,
HEB 9:4 esi bho̠ enwen i̠tani̠ ed̠u-e̠nu̠nu̠ ola̠ ubhin a̠gol u̠le̠m, na̠ obom igba̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ ola̠ ubhin a̠gol ukelema̠ ma̠ eb̠la̠ ozu sa̠ ud̠ighom okpa̠ko ola̠ ubhin a̠gol u̠le̠m od̠i bho̠. U̠b̠aram na̠ okpeti ta̠ Ero̠n wa̠ na̠ aghu̠r bho̠, na̠ ipopola̠ ro̠gbi̠o̠ma ya̠ u̠ge̠ ma̠ oloko bho̠ od̠ighom d̠a̠ ologi obom igba̠ ta̠ A̠zib̠a̠ bho̠,
HEB 9:5 sa̠ Itileduom isosorogia̠n od̠i d̠a̠ anyu̠ bho̠ na̠ eghughuom a̠lukpesi wa̠ na̠ okpon i̠karabh na̠ o̠si̠ghe̠ ma̠ a̠d̠ien bho̠. Ya̠a̠ i̠yar ko orue d̠o̠ o̠gba ma̠ i̠di̠ar i̠nye̠n o̠si̠se̠ghe̠ni̠ ma̠ i̠se̠n.
HEB 9:6 Igiel na̠ o̠mar o̠to̠to̠gi̠ ma̠ i̠di̠ar bho̠ oguri ma̠ o̠ko̠no̠n, sa̠ rokur bho̠ na̠ e̠gi̠ ka̠ ed̠igh d̠a̠ e̠kpe̠ wa̠ d̠a̠ ed̠ia̠ bho̠ na̠ egir gha̠n ogir ya̠ a̠d̠a̠ma̠ bho̠.
